Walamm*a* dakhaloo min *h*aythu amarahum aboohum m*a* k*a*na yughnee AAanhum mina All*a*hi min shayin ill*a* *ha*jatan fee nafsi yaAAqooba qa*da*h*a* wainnahu la*th*oo AAilmin lim*a* AAallamn*a*hu wal*a*kinna akthara a**l**nn*a*si l*a* yaAAlamoon**a**

## 12:69

Walamm*a* dakhaloo AAal*a* yoosufa *a*w*a* ilayhi akh*a*hu q*a*la innee an*a* akhooka fal*a* tabtais bim*a* k*a*noo yaAAmaloon**a**

## 12:70

Falamm*a* jahhazahum bijah*a*zihim jaAAala a**l**ssiq*a*yata fee ra*h*li akheehi thumma a*thth*ana mua*thth*inun ayyatuh*a* alAAeeru innakum las*a*riqoon**a**

## 12:71

Q*a*loo waaqbaloo AAalayhim m*atha* tafqidoon**a**

## 12:72

Q*a*loo nafqidu *s*uw*a*AAa almaliki waliman j*a*a bihi *h*imlu baAAeerin waan*a* bihi zaAAeem**un**

## 12:73

Q*a*loo ta**A**ll*a*hi laqad AAalimtum m*a* jin*a* linufsida fee alar*d*i wam*a* kunn*a* s*a*riqeen**a**

## 12:74

Q*a*loo fam*a* jaz*a*ohu in kuntum k*ath*ibeen**a**

## 12:75

Q*a*loo jaz*a*ohu man wujida fee ra*h*lihi fahuwa jaz*a*ohu ka*tha*lika najzee a**l****thth***a*limeen**a**

## 12:76

Fabadaa biawAAiyatihim qabla wiAA*a*i akheehi thumma istakhrajah*a* min wiAA*a*i akheehi ka*tha*lika kidn*a* liyoosufa m*a* k*a*na liyakhu*th*a akh*a*hu fee deeni almaliki ill*a* an yash*a*a All*a*hu narfaAAu daraj*a*tin man nash*a*o wafawqa kulli *th*ee AAilmin AAaleem**un**

## 12:77

Q*a*loo in yasriq faqad saraqa akhun lahu min qablu faasarrah*a* yoosufu fee nafsihi walam yubdih*a* lahum q*a*la antum sharrun mak*a*nan wa**A**ll*a*hu aAAlamu bim*a* ta*s*ifoon**a**

## 12:78

Q*a*loo y*a* ayyuh*a* alAAazeezu inna lahu aban shaykhan kabeeran fakhu*th* a*h*adan*a* mak*a*nahu inn*a* nar*a*ka mina almu*h*sineen**a**

## 12:79

Q*a*la maAA*ath*a All*a*hi an nakhu*th*a ill*a* man wajadn*a* mat*a*AAan*a* AAindahu inn*a* i*th*an l&#x61;**th***a*limoon**a**

## 12:80

Falamm*a* istayasoo minhu khala*s*oo najiyyan q*a*la kabeeruhum alam taAAlamoo anna ab*a*kum qad akha*th*a AAalaykum mawthiqan mina All*a*hi wamin qablu m*a* farra*t*tum fee yoosufa falan abra*h*a alar*d*a *h*att*a* ya*th*ana lee abee aw ya*h*kuma All*a*hu lee wahuwa khayru al*ha*kimeen**a**

## 12:81

IrjiAAoo il*a* abeekum faqooloo y*a* ab*a*n*a* inna ibnaka saraqa wam*a* shahidn*a* ill*a* bim*a* AAalimn*a* wam*a* kunn*a* lilghaybi *ha*f&#x69;**th**&#x65;en**a**

## 12:82

Wa**i**sali alqaryata allatee kunn*a* feeh*a* wa**a**lAAeera allatee aqbaln*a* feeh*a* wainn*a* la*sa*diqoon**a**

## 12:83

Q*a*la bal sawwalat lakum anfusukum amran fa*s*abrun jameelun AAas*a* All*a*hu an yatiyanee bihim jameeAAan innahu huwa alAAaleemu al*h*akeem**u**

## 12:84

Watawall*a* AAanhum waq*a*la y*a* asaf*a* AAal*a* yoosufa wa**i**bya*dd*at AAayn*a*hu mina al*h*uzni fahuwa k&#x61;**th**&#x65;em**un**

## 12:85

Q*a*loo ta**A**ll*a*hi taftao ta*th*kuru yoosufa *h*att*a* takoona *h*ara*d*an aw takoona mina alh*a*likeen**a**

## 12:86

Q*a*la innam*a* ashkoo baththee wa*h*uznee il*a* All*a*hi waaAAlamu mina All*a*hi m*a* l*a* taAAlamoon**a**

## 12:87

Y*a* baniyya i*th*haboo fata*h*assasoo min yoosufa waakheehi wal*a* tayasoo min raw*h*i All*a*hi innahu l*a* yayasu min raw*h*i All*a*hi ill*a* alqawmu alk*a*firoon**a**

## 12:88

Falamm*a* dakhaloo AAalayhi q*a*loo y*a* ayyuh*a* alAAazeezu massan*a* waahlan*a* a**l***dd*urru wajin*a* bibi*da*AAatin muzj*a*tin faawfi lan*a* alkayla wata*s*addaq AAalayn*a* inna All*a*ha yajzee almuta*s*addiqeen**a**

## 12:89

Q*a*la hal AAalimtum m*a* faAAaltum biyoosufa waakheehi i*th* antum j*a*hiloon**a**

## 12:90

Q*a*loo ainnaka laanta yoosufa q*a*la an*a* yoosufu wah*atha* akhee qad manna All*a*hu AAalayn*a* innahu man yattaqi waya*s*bir fainna All*a*ha l*a* yu*d*eeAAu ajra almu*h*sineen**a**

## 12:91

Q*a*loo ta**A**ll*a*hi laqad *a*tharaka All*a*hu AAalayn*a* wain kunn*a* lakh*at*ieen**a**

## 12:92

Q*a*la l*a* tathreeba AAalaykumu alyawma yaghfiru All*a*hu lakum wahuwa ar*h*amu a**l**rr*ah*imeen**a**

## 12:93

I*th*haboo biqamee*s*ee h*atha* faalqoohu AAal*a* wajhi abee yati ba*s*eeran watoonee biahlikum ajmaAAeen**a**

## 12:94

Walamm*a* fa*s*alati alAAeeru q*a*la aboohum innee laajidu ree*h*a yoosufa lawl*a* an tufannidoon**i**

## 12:95

Q*a*loo ta**A**ll*a*hi innaka lafee *d*al*a*lika alqadeem**i**

## 12:96

Falamm*a* an j*a*a albasheeru alq*a*hu AAal*a* wajhihi fa**i**rtadda ba*s*eeran q*a*la alam aqul lakum innee aAAlamu mina All*a*hi m*a* l*a* taAAlamoon**a**

## 12:97

Q*a*loo y*a* ab*a*n*a* istaghfir lan*a* *th*unooban*a* inn*a* kunn*a* kh*at*ieen**a**

## 12:98

Q*a*la sawfa astaghfiru lakum rabbee innahu huwa alghafooru a**l**rra*h*eem**u**

## 12:99

Falamm*a* dakhaloo AAal*a* yoosufa *a*w*a* ilayhi abawayhi waq*a*la odkhuloo mi*s*ra in sh*a*a All*a*hu *a*mineen**a**

## 12:100

WarafaAAa abawayhi AAal*a* alAAarshi wakharroo lahu sujjadan waq*a*la y*a* abati h*atha* taweelu ruy*a*ya min qablu qad jaAAalah*a* rabbee *h*aqqan waqad a*h*sana bee i*th* akhrajanee mina a**l**ssijni waj*a*a bikum mina albadwi min baAAdi an nazagha a**l**shshay*ta*nu baynee wabayna ikhwatee inna rabbee la*t*eefun lim*a* yash*a*o innahu huwa alAAaleemu al*h*akeem**u**

## 12:101

Rabbi qad *a*taytanee mina almulki waAAallamtanee min taweeli ala*ha*deethi f*at*ira a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i anta waliyyee fee a**l**dduny*a* wa**a**l*a*khirati tawaffanee musliman waal*h*iqnee bi**al***ssa*li*h*een**a**

## 12:102

*Tha*lika min anb*a*i alghaybi noo*h*eehi ilayka wam*a* kunta ladayhim i*th* ajmaAAoo amrahum wahum yamkuroon**a**

## 12:103

Wam*a* aktharu a**l**nn*a*si walaw *h*ara*s*ta bimumineen**a**

## 12:104

Wam*a* tasaluhum AAalayhi min ajrin in huwa ill*a* *th*ikrun lilAA*a*lameen**a**

## 12:105

Wakaayyin min *a*yatin fee a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i yamurroona AAalayh*a* wahum AAanh*a* muAAri*d*oon**a**

## 12:106

Wam*a* yuminu aktharuhum bi**A**ll*a*hi ill*a* wahum mushrikoon**a**

## 12:107

Afaaminoo an tatiyahum gh*a*shiyatun min AAa*tha*bi All*a*hi aw tatiyahumu a**l**ss*a*AAatu baghtatan wahum l*a* yashAAuroon**a**

## 12:108

Qul h*ath*ihi sabeelee adAAoo il*a* All*a*hi AAal*a* ba*s*eeratin an*a* wamani ittabaAAanee wasub*ha*na All*a*hi wam*a* an*a* mina almushrikeen**a**

## 12:109

Wam*a* arsaln*a* min qablika ill*a* rij*a*lan noo*h*ee ilayhim min ahli alqur*a* afalam yaseeroo fee alar*d*i faya&#x6E;**th**&#x75;roo kayfa k*a*na AA*a*qibatu alla*th*eena min qablihim walad*a*ru al*a*khirati khayrun lilla*th*eena ittaqaw afal*a* taAAqiloon**a**

## 12:110

*H*att*a* i*tha* istayasa a**l**rrusulu w&#x61;**th**&#x61;nnoo annahum qad ku*th*iboo j*a*ahum na*s*run*a* fanujjiya man nash*a*o wal*a* yuraddu basun*a* AAani alqawmi almujrimeen**a**

## 12:111

Laqad k*a*na fee qa*s*a*s*ihim AAibratun liolee alalb*a*bi m*a* k*a*na *h*adeethan yuftar*a* wal*a*kin ta*s*deeqa alla*th*ee bayna yadayhi wataf*s*eela kulli shayin wahudan wara*h*matan liqawmin yuminoon**a**

## 13:1

Alifl*a*mmeemr*a* tilka *a*y*a*tu alkit*a*bi wa**a**lla*th*ee onzila ilayka min rabbika al*h*aqqu wal*a*kinna akthara a**l**nn*a*si l*a* yuminoon**a**

## 13:2

All*a*hu alla*th*ee rafaAAa a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti bighayri AAamadin tarawnah*a* thumma istaw*a* AAal*a* alAAarshi wasakhkhara a**l**shshamsa wa**a**lqamara kullun yajree liajalin musamman yudabbiru alamra yufa*ss*ilu al*a*y*a*ti laAAallakum biliq*a*i rabbikum tooqinoon**a**

## 13:3

Wahuwa alla*th*ee madda alar*d*a wajaAAala feeh*a* raw*a*siya waanh*a*ran wamin kulli a**l**ththamar*a*ti jaAAala feeh*a* zawjayni ithnayni yughshee allayla a**l**nnah*a*ra inna fee *tha*lika la*a*y*a*tin liqawmin yatafakkaroon**a**

## 13:4

Wafee alar*d*i qi*t*aAAun mutaj*a*wir*a*tun wajann*a*tun min aAAn*a*bin wazarAAun wanakheelun *s*inw*a*nun waghayru *s*inw*a*nin yusq*a* bim*a*in w*ah*idin wanufa*dd*ilu baAA*d*ah*a* AAal*a* baAA*d*in fee alokuli inna fee *tha*lika la*a*y*a*tin liqawmin yaAAqiloon**a**

## 13:5

Wain taAAjab faAAajabun qawluhum ai*tha* kunn*a* tur*a*ban ainn*a* lafee khalqin jadeedin ol*a*ika alla*th*eena kafaroo birabbihim waol*a*ika alaghl*a*lu fee aAAn*a*qihim waol*a*ika a*s**ha*bu a**l**nn*a*ri hum feeh*a* kh*a*lidoon**a**

## 13:6

WayastaAAjiloonaka bi**al**ssayyiati qabla al*h*asanati waqad khalat min qablihimu almathul*a*tu wainna rabbaka la*th*oo maghfiratin li**l**nn*a*si AAal*a* **th**&#x75;lmihim wainna rabbaka lashadeedu alAAiq*a*b**i**

## 13:7

Wayaqoolu alla*th*eena kafaroo lawl*a* onzila AAalayhi *a*yatun min rabbihi innam*a* anta mun*th*irun walikulli qawmin h*a*d**in**

## 13:8

All*a*hu yaAAlamu m*a* ta*h*milu kullu onth*a* wam*a* taghee*d*u alar*ha*mu wam*a* tazd*a*du wakullu shayin AAindahu bimiqd*a*r**in**

## 13:9

AA*a*limu alghaybi wa**al**shshah*a*dati alkabeeru almutaAA*a*l**i**

## 13:10

Saw*a*on minkum man asarra alqawla waman jahara bihi waman huwa mustakhfin bi**a**llayli was*a*ribun bi**al**nnah*a*r**i**

## 13:11

Lahu muAAaqqib*a*tun min bayni yadayhi wamin khalfihi ya*h*f&#x61;**th**&#x6F;onahu min amri All*a*hi inna All*a*ha l*a* yughayyiru m*a* biqawmin *h*att*a* yughayyiroo m*a* bianfusihim wai*tha* ar*a*da All*a*hu biqawmin sooan fal*a* maradda lahu wam*a* lahum min doonihi min w*a*l**in**

## 13:12

Huwa alla*th*ee yureekumu albarqa khawfan wa*t*amaAAan wayunshio a**l**ssa*ha*ba a**l**ththiq*a*l**a**

## 13:13

Wayusabbi*h*u a**l**rraAAdu bi*h*amdihi wa**a**lmal*a*ikatu min kheefatihi wayursilu a**l***ss*aw*a*AAiqa fayu*s*eebu bih*a* man yash*a*o wahum yuj*a*diloona fee All*a*hi wahuwa shadeedu almi*ha*l**i**

## 13:14

Lahu daAAwatu al*h*aqqi wa**a**lla*th*eena yadAAoona min doonihi l*a* yastajeeboona lahum bishayin ill*a* kab*a*si*t*i kaffayhi il*a* alm*a*i liyablugha f*a*hu wam*a* huwa bib*a*lighihi wam*a* duAA*a*o alk*a*fireena ill*a* fee *d*al*a*l**in**

## 13:15

Walill*a*hi yasjudu man fee a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i *t*awAAan wakarhan w&#x61;**th**&#x69;l*a*luhum bi**a**lghuduwwi wa**a**l*asa*l**i**

## 13:16

Qul man rabbu a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i quli All*a*hu qul afa**i**ttakha*th*tum min doonihi awliy*a*a l*a* yamlikoona lianfusihim nafAAan wal*a* *d*arran qul hal yastawee alaAAm*a* wa**a**lba*s*eeru am hal tastawee a**l****thth**&#x75;lum*a*tu wa**al**nnooru am jaAAaloo lill*a*hi shurak*a*a khalaqoo kakhalqihi fatash*a*baha alkhalqu AAalayhim quli All*a*hu kh*a*liqu kulli shayin wahuwa alw*ah*idu alqahh*a*r**u**

## 13:17

Anzala mina a**l**ssam*a*i m*a*an fas*a*lat awdiyatun biqadarih*a* fa**i***h*tamala a**l**ssaylu zabadan r*a*biyan wamimm*a* yooqidoona AAalayhi fee a**l**nn*a*ri ibtigh*a*a *h*ilyatin aw mat*a*AAin zabadun mithluhu ka*tha*lika ya*d*ribu All*a*hu al*h*aqqa wa**a**lb*at*ila faamm*a* a**l**zzabadu faya*th*habu juf*a*an waamm*a* m*a* yanfaAAu a**l**nn*a*sa fayamkuthu fee alar*d*i ka*tha*lika ya*d*ribu All*a*hu alamth*a*l**a**

## 13:18

Lilla*th*eena istaj*a*boo lirabbihimu al*h*usn*a* wa**a**lla*th*eena lam yastajeeboo lahu law anna lahum m*a* fee alar*d*i jameeAAan wamithlahu maAAahu la**i**ftadaw bihi ol*a*ika lahum sooo al*h*is*a*bi wamaw*a*hum jahannamu wabisa almih*a*d**u**

## 13:19

Afaman yaAAlamu annam*a* onzila ilayka min rabbika al*h*aqqu kaman huwa aAAm*a* innam*a* yata*th*akkaru oloo alalb*a*b**i**

## 13:20

Alla*th*eena yoofoona biAAahdi All*a*hi wal*a* yanqu*d*oona almeeth*a*q**a**

## 13:21

Wa**a**lla*th*eena ya*s*iloona m*a* amara All*a*hu bihi an yoo*s*ala wayakhshawna rabbahum wayakh*a*foona sooa al*h*is*a*b**i**

## 13:22

Wa**a**lla*th*eena *s*abaroo ibtigh*a*a wajhi rabbihim waaq*a*moo a**l***ss*al*a*ta waanfaqoo mimm*a* razaqn*a*hum sirran waAAal*a*niyatan wayadraoona bi**a**l*h*asanati a**l**ssayyiata ol*a*ika lahum AAuqb*a* a**l**dd*a*r**i**

## 13:23

Jann*a*tu AAadnin yadkhuloonah*a* waman *s*ala*h*a min *a*b*a*ihim waazw*a*jihim wa*th*urriyy*a*tihim wa**a**lmal*a*ikatu yadkhuloona AAalayhim min kulli b*a*b**in**

## 13:24

Sal*a*mun AAalaykum bim*a* *s*abartum faniAAma AAuqb*a* a**l**dd*a*r**i**

## 13:25

Wa**a**lla*th*eena yanqu*d*oona AAahda All*a*hi min baAAdi meeth*a*qihi wayaq*t*aAAoona m*a* amara All*a*hu bihi an yoo*s*ala wayufsidoona fee alar*d*i ol*a*ika lahumu allaAAnatu walahum sooo a**l**dd*a*r**i**

## 13:26

All*a*hu yabsu*t*u a**l**rrizqa liman yash*a*o wayaqdiru wafari*h*oo bi**a**l*h*ay*a*ti a**l**dduny*a* wam*a* al*h*ay*a*tu a**l**dduny*a* fee al*a*khirati ill*a* mat*a*AA**un**

## 13:27

Wayaqoolu alla*th*eena kafaroo lawl*a* onzila AAalayhi *a*yatun min rabbihi qul inna All*a*ha yu*d*illu man yash*a*o wayahdee ilayhi man an*a*b**a**

## 13:28

Alla*th*eena *a*manoo wata*t*mainnu quloobuhum bi*th*ikri All*a*hi al*a* bi*th*ikri All*a*hi ta*t*mainnu alquloob**u**

## 13:29

Alla*th*eena *a*manoo waAAamiloo a**l***ssa*li*ha*ti *t*oob*a* lahum wa*h*usnu ma*a*b**in**

## 13:30

Ka*tha*lika arsaln*a*ka fee ommatin qad khalat min qablih*a* omamun litatluwa AAalayhimu alla*th*ee aw*h*ayn*a* ilayka wahum yakfuroona bi**al**rra*h*m*a*ni qul huwa rabbee l*a* il*a*ha ill*a* huwa AAalayhi tawakkaltu wailayhi mat*a*b**i**

## 13:31

Walaw anna qur*a*nan suyyirat bihi aljib*a*lu aw qu*tt*iAAat bihi alar*d*u aw kullima bihi almawt*a* bal lill*a*hi alamru jameeAAan afalam yayasi alla*th*eena *a*manoo an law yash*a*o All*a*hu lahad*a* a**l**nn*a*sa jameeAAan wal*a* yaz*a*lu alla*th*eena kafaroo tu*s*eebuhum bim*a* *s*anaAAoo q*a*riAAatun aw ta*h*ullu qareeban min d*a*rihim *h*att*a* yatiya waAAdu All*a*hi inna All*a*ha l*a* yukhlifu almeeAA*a*d**a**

## 13:32

Walaqadi istuhzia birusulin min qablika faamlaytu lilla*th*eena kafaroo thumma akha*th*tuhum fakayfa k*a*na AAiq*a*b**i**

## 13:33

Afaman huwa q*a*imun AAal*a* kulli nafsin bim*a* kasabat wajaAAaloo lill*a*hi shurak*a*a qul sammoohum am tunabbioonahu bim*a* l*a* yaAAlamu fee alar*d*i am b&#x69;**th***a*hirin mina alqawli bal zuyyina lilla*th*eena kafaroo makruhum wa*s*uddoo AAani a**l**ssabeeli waman yu*d*lili All*a*hu fam*a* lahu min h*a*d**in**

## 13:34

Lahum AAa*tha*bun fee al*h*ay*a*ti a**l**dduny*a* walaAAa*tha*bu al*a*khirati ashaqqu wam*a* lahum mina All*a*hi min w*a*q**in**

## 13:35

Mathalu aljannati allatee wuAAida almuttaqoona tajree min ta*h*tih*a* alanh*a*ru okuluh*a* d*a*imun w&#x61;**th**&#x69;lluh*a* tilka AAuqb*a* alla*th*eena ittaqaw waAAuqb*a* alk*a*fireena a**l**nn*a*r**u**

## 13:36

Wa**a**lla*th*eena *a*tayn*a*humu alkit*a*ba yafra*h*oona bim*a* onzila ilayka wamina ala*h*z*a*bi man yunkiru baAA*d*ahu qul innam*a* omirtu an aAAbuda All*a*ha wal*a* oshrika bihi ilayhi adAAoo wailayhi ma*a*b**i**

## 13:37

Waka*tha*lika anzaln*a*hu *h*ukman AAarabiyyan walaini ittabaAAta ahw*a*ahum baAAda m*a* j*a*aka mina alAAilmi m*a* laka mina All*a*hi min waliyyin wal*a* w*a*q**in**

## 13:38

Walaqad arsaln*a* rusulan min qablika wajaAAaln*a* lahum azw*a*jan wa*th*urriyyatan wam*a* k*a*na lirasoolin an yatiya bi*a*yatin ill*a* bii*th*ni All*a*hi likulli ajalin kit*a*b**un**

## 13:39

Yam*h*oo All*a*hu m*a* yash*a*o wayuthbitu waAAindahu ommu alkit*a*b**i**

## 13:40

Wain m*a* nuriyannaka baAA*d*a alla*th*ee naAAiduhum aw natawaffayannaka fainnam*a* AAalayka albal*a*ghu waAAalayn*a* al*h*is*a*b**u**

## 13:41

Awalam yaraw ann*a* natee alar*d*a nanqu*s*uh*a* min a*t*r*a*fih*a* wa**A**ll*a*hu ya*h*kumu l*a* muAAaqqiba li*h*ukmihi wahuwa sareeAAu al*h*is*a*b**i**

## 13:42

Waqad makara alla*th*eena min qablihim falill*a*hi almakru jameeAAan yaAAlamu m*a* taksibu kullu nafsin wasayaAAlamu alkuff*a*ru liman AAuqb*a* a**l**dd*a*r**i**

## 13:43

Wayaqoolu alla*th*eena kafaroo lasta mursalan qul kaf*a* bi**A**ll*a*hi shaheedan baynee wabaynakum waman AAindahu AAilmu alkit*a*b**i**

## 14:1

Alifl*a*mr*a* kit*a*bun anzaln*a*hu ilayka litukhrija a**l**nn*a*sa mina a**l****thth**&#x75;lum*a*ti il*a* a**l**nnoori bii*th*ni rabbihim il*a* *s*ir*at*i alAAazeezi al*h*ameed**i**

## 14:2

All*a*hi alla*th*ee lahu m*a* fee a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wam*a* fee alar*d*i wawaylun lilk*a*fireena min AAa*tha*bin shadeed**in**

## 14:3

Alla*th*eena yasta*h*ibboona al*h*ay*a*ta a**l**dduny*a* AAal*a* al*a*khirati waya*s*uddoona AAan sabeeli All*a*hi wayabghoonah*a* AAiwajan ol*a*ika fee *d*al*a*lin baAAeed**in**

## 14:4

Wam*a* arsaln*a* min rasoolin ill*a* bilis*a*ni qawmihi liyubayyina lahum fayu*d*illu All*a*hu man yash*a*o wayahdee man yash*a*o wahuwa alAAazeezu al*h*akeem**u**

## 14:5

Walaqad arsaln*a* moos*a* bi*a*y*a*tin*a* an akhrij qawmaka mina a**l****thth**&#x75;lum*a*ti il*a* a**l**nnoori wa*th*akkirhum biayy*a*mi All*a*hi inna fee *tha*lika la*a*y*a*tin likulli *s*abb*a*rin shakoor**in**

## 14:6

Wai*th* q*a*la moos*a* liqawmihi o*th*kuroo niAAmata All*a*hi AAalaykum i*th* anj*a*kum min *a*li firAAawna yasoomoonakum sooa alAAa*tha*bi wayu*th*abbi*h*oona abn*a*akum wayasta*h*yoona nis*a*akum wafee *tha*likum bal*a*on min rabbikum AA&#x61;**th**&#x65;em**un**

## 14:7

Wai*th* taa*thth*ana rabbukum lain shakartum laazeedannakum walain kafartum inna AAa*tha*bee lashadeed**un**

## 14:8

Waq*a*la moos*a* in takfuroo antum waman fee alar*d*i jameeAAan fainna All*a*ha laghaniyyun *h*ameed**un**

## 14:9

Alam yatikum nabao alla*th*eena min qablikum qawmi noo*h*in waAA*a*din wathamooda wa**a**lla*th*eena min baAAdihim l*a* yaAAlamuhum ill*a* All*a*hu j*a*athum rusuluhum bi**a**lbayyin*a*ti faraddoo aydiyahum fee afw*a*hihim waq*a*loo inn*a* kafarn*a* bim*a* orsiltum bihi wainn*a* lafee shakkin mimm*a* tadAAoonan*a* ilayhi mureeb**un**

## 14:10

Q*a*lat rusuluhum afee All*a*hi shakkun f*at*iri a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i yadAAookum liyaghfira lakum min *th*unoobikum wayuakhkhirakum il*a* ajalin musamman q*a*loo in antum ill*a* basharun mithlun*a* tureedoona an ta*s*uddoon*a* AAamm*a* k*a*na yaAAbudu *a*b*a*on*a* fatoon*a* bisul*ta*nin mubeen**in**

## 14:11

Q*a*lat lahum rusuluhum in na*h*nu ill*a* basharun mithlukum wal*a*kinna All*a*ha yamunnu AAal*a* man yash*a*o min AAib*a*dihi wam*a* k*a*na lan*a* an natiyakum bisul*ta*nin ill*a* bii*th*ni All*a*hi waAAal*a* All*a*hi falyatawakkali almuminoon**a**

## 14:12

Wam*a* lan*a* all*a* natawakkala AAal*a* All*a*hi waqad had*a*n*a* subulan*a* walana*s*biranna AAal*a* m*a* *ath*aytumoon*a* waAAal*a* All*a*hi falyatawakkali almutawakkiloon**a**

## 14:13

Waq*a*la alla*th*eena kafaroo lirusulihim lanukhrijannakum min ar*d*in*a* aw lataAAoodunna fee millatin*a* faaw*ha* ilayhim rabbuhum lanuhlikanna a**l****thth***a*limeen**a**

## 14:14

Walanuskinannakumu alar*d*a min baAAdihim *tha*lika liman kh*a*fa maq*a*mee wakh*a*fa waAAeed**i**

## 14:15

Wa**i**stafta*h*oo wakh*a*ba kullu jabb*a*rin AAaneed**in**

## 14:16

Min war*a*ihi jahannamu wayusq*a* min m*a*in *s*adeed**in**

## 14:17

YatajarraAAuhu wal*a* yak*a*du yuseeghuhu wayateehi almawtu min kulli mak*a*nin wam*a* huwa bimayyitin wamin war*a*ihi AAa*tha*bun ghale&#x65;**th****un**

## 14:18

Mathalu alla*th*eena kafaroo birabbihim aAAm*a*luhum karam*a*din ishtaddat bihi a**l**rree*h*u fee yawmin AA*as*ifin l*a* yaqdiroona mimm*a* kasaboo AAal*a* shayin *tha*lika huwa a**l***dd*al*a*lu albaAAeed**u**

## 14:19

Alam tara anna All*a*ha khalaqa a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*a bi**a**l*h*aqqi in yasha yu*th*hibkum wayati bikhalqin jadeed**in**

## 14:20

Wam*a* *tha*lika AAal*a* All*a*hi biAAazeez**in**

## 14:21

Wabarazoo lill*a*hi jameeAAan faq*a*la a**l***dd*uAAaf*a*o lilla*th*eena istakbaroo inn*a* kunn*a* lakum tabaAAan fahal antum mughnoona AAann*a* min AAa*tha*bi All*a*hi min shayin q*a*loo law had*a*n*a* All*a*hu lahadayn*a*kum saw*a*on AAalayn*a* ajaziAAn*a* am *s*abarn*a* m*a* lan*a* min ma*h*ee*s***in**

## 14:22

Waq*a*la a**l**shshay*ta*nu lamm*a* qu*d*iya alamru inna All*a*ha waAAadakum waAAda al*h*aqqi wawaAAadtukum faakhlaftukum wam*a* k*a*na liya AAalaykum min sul*ta*nin ill*a* an daAAawtukum fa**i**stajabtum lee fal*a* taloomoonee waloomoo anfusakum m*a* an*a* bimu*s*rikhikum wam*a* antum bimu*s*rikhiyya innee kafartu bim*a* ashraktumooni min qablu inna a**l****thth***a*limeena lahum AAa*tha*bun aleem**un**

## 14:23

Waodkhila alla*th*eena *a*manoo waAAamiloo a**l***ssa*li*ha*ti jann*a*tin tajree min ta*h*tih*a* alanh*a*ru kh*a*lideena feeh*a* bii*th*ni rabbihim ta*h*iyyatuhum feeh*a* sal*a*m**un**

## 14:24

Alam tara kayfa *d*araba All*a*hu mathalan kalimatan *t*ayyibatan kashajaratin *t*ayyibatin a*s*luh*a* th*a*bitun wafarAAuh*a* fee a**l**ssam*a***i**

## 14:25

Tutee okulah*a* kulla *h*eenin bii*th*ni rabbih*a* waya*d*ribu All*a*hu alamth*a*la li**l**nn*a*si laAAallahum yata*th*akkaroon**a**

## 14:26

Wamathalu kalimatin khabeethatin kashajaratin khabeethatin ijtuththat min fawqi alar*d*i m*a* lah*a* min qar*a*r**in**

## 14:27

Yuthabbitu All*a*hu alla*th*eena *a*manoo bi**a**lqawli a**l**thth*a*biti fee al*h*ay*a*ti a**l**dduny*a* wafee al*a*khirati wayu*d*illu All*a*hu a**l****thth***a*limeena wayafAAalu All*a*hu m*a* yash*a***o**

## 14:28

Alam tara il*a* alla*th*eena baddaloo niAAmata All*a*hi kufran waa*h*alloo qawmahum d*a*ra albaw*a*r**i**

## 14:29

Jahannama ya*s*lawnah*a* wabisa alqar*a*r**u**

## 14:30

WajaAAaloo lill*a*hi and*a*dan liyu*d*illoo AAan sabeelihi qul tamattaAAoo fainna ma*s*eerakum il*a* a**l**nn*a*r**i**

## 14:31

Qul liAAib*a*diya alla*th*eena *a*manoo yuqeemoo a**l***ss*al*a*ta wayunfiqoo mimm*a* razaqn*a*hum sirran waAAal*a*niyatan min qabli an yatiya yawmun l*a* bayAAun feehi wal*a* khil*a*l**un**

## 14:32

All*a*hu alla*th*ee khalaqa a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*a waanzala mina a**l**ssam*a*i m*a*an faakhraja bihi mina a**l**ththamar*a*ti rizqan lakum wasakhkhara lakumu alfulka litajriya fee alba*h*ri biamrihi wasakhkhara lakumu alanh*a*r**a**

## 14:33

Wasakhkhara lakumu a**l**shshamsa wa**a**lqamara d*a*ibayni wasakhkhara lakumu allayla wa**al**nnah*a*r**a**

## 14:34

Wa*a*t*a*kum min kulli m*a* saaltumoohu wain taAAuddoo niAAmata All*a*hi l*a* tu*hs*ooh*a* inna alins*a*na l&#x61;**th**&#x61;loomun kaff*a*r**un**

## 14:35

Wai*th* q*a*la ibr*a*heemu rabbi ijAAal h*atha* albalada *a*minan wa**o**jnubnee wabaniyya an naAAbuda ala*s*n*a*m**a**

## 14:36

Rabbi innahunna a*d*lalna katheeran mina a**l**nn*a*si faman tabiAAanee fainnahu minnee waman AAa*sa*nee fainnaka ghafoorun ra*h*eem**un**

## 14:37

Rabban*a* innee askantu min *th*urriyyatee biw*a*din ghayri *th*ee zarAAin AAinda baytika almu*h*arrami rabban*a* liyuqeemoo a**l***ss*al*a*ta fa**i**jAAal afidatan mina a**l**nn*a*si tahwee ilayhim wa**o**rzuqhum mina a**l**ththamar*a*ti laAAallahum yashkuroon**a**

## 14:38

Rabban*a* innaka taAAlamu m*a* nukhfee wam*a* nuAAlinu wam*a* yakhf*a* AAal*a* All*a*hi min shayin fee alar*d*i wal*a* fee a**l**ssam*a***i**

## 14:39

Al*h*amdu lill*a*hi alla*th*ee wahaba lee AAal*a* alkibari ism*a*AAeela wais*ha*qa inna rabbee lasameeAAu a**l**dduAA*a***i**

## 14:40

Rabbi ijAAalnee muqeema a**l***ss*al*a*ti wamin *th*urriyyatee rabban*a* wtaqabbal duAA*a***i**

## 14:41

Rabban*a* ighfir lee waliw*a*lidayya walilmumineena yawma yaqoomu al*h*is*a*b**u**

## 14:42

Wal*a* ta*h*sabanna All*a*ha gh*a*filan AAamm*a* yaAAmalu a**l****thth***a*limoona innam*a* yuakhkhiruhum liyawmin tashkha*s*u feehi alab*sa*r**u**

## 14:43

Muh*t*iAAeena muqniAAee ruoosihim l*a* yartaddu ilayhim *t*arfuhum waafidatuhum haw*a***on**

## 14:44

Waan*th*iri a**l**nn*a*sa yawma yateehimu alAAa*tha*bu fayaqoolu alla*th*eena **th**&#x61;lamoo rabban*a* akhkhirn*a* il*a* ajalin qareebin nujib daAAwataka wanattabiAAi a**l**rrusula awalam takoonoo aqsamtum min qablu m*a* lakum min zaw*a*l**in**

## 14:45

Wasakantum fee mas*a*kini alla*th*eena **th**&#x61;lamoo anfusahum watabayyana lakum kayfa faAAaln*a* bihim wa*d*arabn*a* lakumu alamth*a*l**a**

## 14:46

Waqad makaroo makrahum waAAinda All*a*hi makruhum wain k*a*na makruhum litazoola minhu aljib*a*l**u**

## 14:47

Fal*a* ta*h*sabanna All*a*ha mukhlifa waAAdihi rusulahu inna All*a*ha AAazeezun *th*oo intiq*a*m**in**

## 14:48

Yawma tubaddalu alar*d*u ghayra alar*d*i wa**al**ssam*a*w*a*tu wabarazoo lill*a*hi alw*ah*idi alqahh*a*r**i**

## 14:49

Watar*a* almujrimeena yawmai*th*in muqarraneena fee ala*s*f*a*d**i**

## 14:50

Sar*a*beeluhum min qa*t*r*a*nin wataghsh*a* wujoohahumu a**l**nn*a*r**u**

## 14:51

Liyajziya All*a*hu kulla nafsin m*a* kasabat inna All*a*ha sareeAAu al*h*is*a*b**i**

## 14:52

H*atha* bal*a*ghun li**l**nn*a*si waliyun*th*aroo bihi waliyaAAlamoo annam*a* huwa il*a*hun w*ah*idun waliya*thth*akkara oloo alalb*a*b**i**

## 15:1

Alifl*a*mr*a* tilka *a*y*a*tu alkit*a*bi waqur*a*nin mubeen**in**

## 15:2

Rubam*a* yawaddu alla*th*eena kafaroo law k*a*noo muslimeen**a**

## 15:3

*Th*arhum yakuloo wayatamattaAAoo wayulhihimu alamalu fasawfa yaAAlamoon**a**

## 15:4

Wam*a* ahlakn*a* min qaryatin ill*a* walah*a* kit*a*bun maAAloom**un**

## 15:5

M*a* tasbiqu min ommatin ajalah*a* wam*a* yastakhiroon**a**

## 15:6

Waq*a*loo y*a* ayyuh*a* alla*th*ee nuzzila AAalayhi a**l***thth*ikru innaka lamajnoon**un**

## 15:7

Law m*a* tateen*a* bi**a**lmal*a*ikati in kunta mina a**l***ssa*diqeen**a**

## 15:8

M*a* nunazzilu almal*a*ikata ill*a* bi**a**l*h*aqqi wam*a* k*a*noo i*th*an mu&#x6E;**th**&#x61;reen**a**

## 15:9

Inn*a* na*h*nu nazzaln*a* a**l***thth*ikra wainn*a* lahu la*ha*f&#x69;**th**&#x6F;on**a**

## 15:10

Walaqad arsaln*a* min qablika fee shiyaAAi alawwaleen**a**

## 15:11

Wam*a* yateehim min rasoolin ill*a* k*a*noo bihi yastahzioon**a**

## 15:12

Ka*tha*lika naslukuhu fee quloobi almujrimeen**a**

## 15:13

L*a* yuminoona bihi waqad khalat sunnatu alawwaleen**a**

## 15:14

Walaw fata*h*n*a* AAalayhim b*a*ban mina a**l**ssam*a*i f&#x61;**th**&#x61;lloo feehi yaAArujoon**a**

## 15:15

Laq*a*loo innam*a* sukkirat ab*sa*run*a* bal na*h*nu qawmun mas*h*ooroon**a**

## 15:16

Walaqad jaAAaln*a* fee a**l**ssam*a*i buroojan wazayyann*a*h*a* li**l**nn*a***th**&#x69;reen**a**

## 15:17

Wa*h*af&#x69;**th**&#x6E;*a*h*a* min kulli shay*ta*nin rajeem**in**

## 15:18

Ill*a* mani istaraqa a**l**ssamAAa faatbaAAahu shih*a*bun mubeen**un**

## 15:19

Wa**a**lar*d*a madadn*a*h*a* waalqayn*a* feeh*a* raw*a*siya waanbatn*a* feeh*a* min kulli shayin mawzoon**in**

## 15:20

WajaAAaln*a* lakum feeh*a* maAA*a*yisha waman lastum lahu bir*a*ziqeen**a**

## 15:21

Wain min shayin ill*a* AAindan*a* khaz*a*inuhu wam*a* nunazziluhu ill*a* biqadarin maAAloom**in**

## 15:22

Waarsaln*a* a**l**rriy*ah*a law*a*qi*h*a faanzaln*a* mina a**l**ssam*a*i m*a*an faasqayn*a*kumoohu wam*a* antum lahu bikh*a*zineen**a**

## 15:23

Wainn*a* lana*h*nu nu*h*yee wanumeetu wana*h*nu alw*a*rithoon**a**

## 15:24

Walaqad AAalimn*a* almustaqdimeena minkum walaqad AAalimn*a* almustakhireen**a**

## 15:25

Wainna rabbaka huwa ya*h*shuruhum innahu *h*akeemun AAaleem**un**

## 15:26

Walaqad khalaqn*a* alins*a*na min *s*al*sa*lin min *h*amain masnoon**in**

## 15:27

Wa**a**lj*a*nna khalaqn*a*hu min qablu min n*a*ri a**l**ssamoom**i**

## 15:28

Wai*th* q*a*la rabbuka lilmal*a*ikati innee kh*a*liqun basharan min *s*al*sa*lin min *h*amain masnoon**in**

## 15:29

Fai*tha* sawwaytuhu wanafakhtu feehi min roo*h*ee faqaAAoo lahu s*a*jideen**a**

## 15:30

Fasajada almal*a*ikatu kulluhum ajmaAAoon**a**

## 15:31

Ill*a* ibleesa ab*a* an yakoona maAAa a**l**ss*a*jideen**a**

## 15:32

Q*a*la y*a* ibleesu m*a* laka all*a* takoona maAAa a**l**ss*a*jideen**a**

## 15:33

Q*a*la lam akun liasjuda libasharin khalaqtahu min *s*al*sa*lin min *h*amain masnoon**in**

## 15:34

Q*a*la fa**o**khruj minh*a* fainnaka rajeem**un**

## 15:35

Wainna AAalayka allaAAnata il*a* yawmi a**l**ddeen**i**

## 15:36

Q*a*la rabbi faa&#x6E;**th**&#x69;rnee il*a* yawmi yubAAathoon**a**

## 15:37

Q*a*la fainnaka mina almu&#x6E;**th**&#x61;reen**a**

## 15:38

Il*a* yawmi alwaqti almaAAloom**i**

## 15:39

Q*a*la rabbi bim*a* aghwaytanee laozayyinanna lahum fee alar*d*i walaoghwiyannahum ajmaAAeen**a**

## 15:40

Ill*a* AAib*a*daka minhumu almukhla*s*een**a**

## 15:41

Q*a*la h*atha* *s*ir*at*un AAalayya mustaqeem**un**

## 15:42

Inna AAib*a*dee laysa laka AAalayhim sul*ta*nun ill*a* mani ittabaAAaka mina algh*a*ween**a**

## 15:43

Wainna jahannama lamawAAiduhum ajmaAAeen**a**

## 15:44

Lah*a* sabAAatu abw*a*bin likulli b*a*bin minhum juzon maqsoom**un**

## 15:45

Inna almuttaqeena fee jann*a*tin waAAuyoon**in**

## 15:46

Odkhulooh*a* bisal*a*min *a*mineen**a**

## 15:47

WanazaAAn*a* m*a* fee *s*udoorihim min ghillin ikhw*a*nan AAal*a* sururin mutaq*a*bileen**a**

## 15:48

L*a* yamassuhum feeh*a* na*s*abun wam*a* hum minh*a* bimukhrajeen**a**

## 15:49

Nabbi AAib*a*dee annee an*a* alghafooru a**l**rra*h*eem**u**

## 15:50

Wa anna AAa*tha*bee huwa alAAa*tha*bu alaleem**u**

## 15:51

Wanabbihum AAan *d*ayfi ibr*a*heem**a**

## 15:52

I*th* dakhaloo AAalayhi faq*a*loo sal*a*man q*a*la inn*a* minkum wajiloon**a**

## 15:53

Q*a*loo l*a* tawjal inn*a* nubashshiruka bighul*a*min AAaleem**in**

## 15:54

Q*a*la abashshartumoonee AAal*a* an massaniya alkibaru fabima tubashshiroon**i**

## 15:55

Q*a*loo bashsharn*a*ka bi**a**l*h*aqqi fal*a* takun mina alq*a*ni*t*een**a**

## 15:56

Q*a*la waman yaqna*t*u min ra*h*mati rabbihi ill*a* a**l***dda*lloon**a**

## 15:57

Q*a*la fam*a* kha*t*bukum ayyuh*a* almursaloon**a**

## 15:58

Q*a*loo inn*a* orsiln*a* il*a* qawmin mujrimeen**a**

## 15:59

Ill*a* *a*la loo*t*in inn*a* lamunajjoohum ajmaAAeen**a**

## 15:60

Ill*a* imraatahu qaddarn*a* innah*a* lamina algh*a*bireen**a**

## 15:61

Falamm*a* j*a*a *a*la loo*t*in almursaloon**a**

## 15:62

Q*a*la innakum qawmun munkaroon**a**

## 15:63

Q*a*loo bal jin*a*ka bim*a* k*a*noo feehi yamtaroon**a**

## 15:64

Waatayn*a*ka bi**a**l*h*aqqi wainn*a* la*sa*diqoon**a**

## 15:65

Faasri biahlika biqi*t*AAin mina allayli wa**i**ttabiAA adb*a*rahum wal*a* yaltafit minkum a*h*adun wa**i**m*d*oo *h*aythu tumaroon**a**

## 15:66

Waqa*d*ayn*a* ilayhi *tha*lika alamra anna d*a*bira h*a*ol*a*i maq*t*ooAAun mu*s*bi*h*een**a**

## 15:67

Waj*a*a ahlu almadeenati yastabshiroon**a**

## 15:68

Q*a*la inna h*a*ol*a*i *d*ayfee fal*a* taf*d*a*h*oon**i**

## 15:69

Wa**i**ttaqoo All*a*ha wal*a* tukhzoon**i**

## 15:70

Q*a*loo awalam nanhaka AAani alAA*a*lameen**a**

## 15:71

Q*a*la h*a*ol*a*i ban*a*tee in kuntum f*a*AAileen**a**

## 15:72

LaAAamruka innahum lafee sakratihim yaAAmahoona

## 15:73

Faakha*th*athumu a**l***ss*ay*h*atu mushriqeen**a**

## 15:74

FajaAAaln*a* AA*a*liyah*a* s*a*filah*a* waam*t*arn*a* AAalayhim *h*ij*a*ratan min sijjeel**in**

## 15:75

Inna fee *tha*lika la*a*y*a*tin lilmutawassimeen**a**

## 15:76

Wainnah*a* labisabeelin muqeem**in**

## 15:77

Inna fee *tha*lika la*a*yatan lilmumineen**a**

## 15:78

Wain k*a*na a*s**ha*bu alaykati l&#x61;**th***a*limeen**a**

## 15:79

Fa**i**ntaqamn*a* minhum wainnahum*a* labiim*a*min mubeen**in**

## 15:80

Walaqad ka*thth*aba a*s**ha*bu al*h*ijri almursaleen**a**

## 15:81

Wa*a*tayn*a*hum *a*y*a*tin*a* fak*a*noo AAanh*a* muAAri*d*een**a**

## 15:82

Wak*a*noo yan*h*itoona mina aljib*a*li buyootan *a*mineen**a**

## 15:83

Faakha*th*athumu a**l***ss*ay*h*atu mu*s*bi*h*een**a**

## 15:84

Fam*a* aghn*a* AAanhum m*a* k*a*noo yaksiboon**a**

## 15:85

Wam*a* khalaqn*a* a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*a wam*a* baynahum*a* ill*a* bi**a**l*h*aqqi wainna a**l**ss*a*AAata la*a*tiyatun fa**i***s*fa*h*i a**l***ss*af*h*a aljameel**a**

## 15:86

Inna rabbaka huwa alkhall*a*qu alAAaleem**u**

## 15:87

Walaqad *a*tayn*a*ka sabAAan mina almath*a*nee wa**a**lqur*a*na alAA&#x61;**th**&#x65;em**a**

## 15:88

L*a* tamuddanna AAaynayka il*a* m*a* mattaAAn*a* bihi azw*a*jan minhum wal*a* ta*h*zan AAalayhim wa**i**khfi*d* jan*ah*aka lilmumineen**a**

## 15:89

Waqul innee an*a* a**l**nna*th*eeru almubeen**u**

## 15:90

Kam*a* anzaln*a* AAal*a* almuqtasimeen**a**

## 15:91

Alla*th*eena jaAAaloo alqur*a*na AAi*d*een**a**

## 15:92

Fawarabbika lanasalannahum ajmaAAeen**a**

## 15:93

AAamm*a* k*a*noo yaAAmaloon**a**

## 15:94

Fa**i***s*daAA bim*a* tumaru waaAAri*d* AAani almushrikeen**a**

## 15:95

Inn*a* kafayn*a*ka almustahzieen**a**

## 15:96

Alla*th*eena yajAAaloona maAAa All*a*hi il*a*han *a*khara fasawfa yaAAlamoon**a**

## 15:97

Walaqad naAAlamu annaka ya*d*eequ *s*adruka bim*a* yaqooloon**a**

## 15:98

Fasabbi*h* bi*h*amdi rabbika wakun mina a**l**ss*a*jideen**a**

## 15:99

Wa**o**AAbud rabbaka *h*att*a* yatiyaka alyaqeen**u**

## 16:1

At*a* amru All*a*hi fal*a* tastaAAjiloohu sub*ha*nahu wataAA*a*l*a* AAamm*a* yushrikoon**a**

## 16:2

Yunazzilu almal*a*ikata bi**al**rroo*h*i min amrihi AAal*a* man yash*a*o min AAib*a*dihi an an*th*iroo annahu l*a* il*a*ha ill*a* an*a* fa**i**ttaqoon**i**

## 16:3

Khalaqa a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*a bi**a**l*h*aqqi taAA*a*l*a* AAamm*a* yushrikoon**a**

## 16:4

Khalaqa alins*a*na min nu*t*fatin fai*tha* huwa kha*s*eemun mubeen**un**

## 16:5

Wa**a**lanAA*a*ma khalaqah*a* lakum feeh*a* difon waman*a*fiAAu waminh*a* takuloon**a**

## 16:6

Walakum feeh*a* jam*a*lun *h*eena turee*h*oona wa*h*eena tasra*h*oon**a**

## 16:7

Wata*h*milu athq*a*lakum il*a* baladin lam takoonoo b*a*ligheehi ill*a* bishiqqi alanfusi inna rabbakum laraoofun ra*h*eem**un**

## 16:8

Wa**a**lkhayla wa**a**lbigh*a*la wa**a**l*h*ameera litarkabooh*a* wazeenatan wayakhluqu m*a* l*a* taAAlamoon**a**

## 16:9

WaAAal*a* All*a*hi qa*s*du a**l**ssabeeli waminh*a* j*a*irun walaw sh*a*a lahad*a*kum ajmaAAeen**a**

## 16:10

Huwa alla*th*ee anzala mina a**l**ssam*a*i m*a*an lakum minhu shar*a*bun waminhu shajarun feehi tuseemoon**a**

## 16:11

Yunbitu lakum bihi a**l**zzarAAa wa**al**zzaytoona wa**al**nnakheela wa**a**laAAn*a*ba wamin kulli a**l**ththamar*a*ti inna fee *tha*lika la*a*yatan liqawmin yatafakkaroon**a**

## 16:12

Wasakhkhara lakumu allayla wa**al**nnah*a*ra wa**al**shshamsa wa**a**lqamara wa**al**nnujoomu musakhkhar*a*tun biamrihi inna fee *tha*lika la*a*y*a*tin liqawmin yaAAqiloon**a**

## 16:13

Wam*a* *th*araa lakum fee alar*d*i mukhtalifan alw*a*nuhu inna fee *tha*lika la*a*yatan liqawmin ya*thth*akkaroon**a**

## 16:14

Wahuwa alla*th*ee sakhkhara alba*h*ra litakuloo minhu la*h*man *t*ariyyan watastakhrijoo minhu *h*ilyatan talbasoonah*a* watar*a* alfulka maw*a*khira feehi walitabtaghoo min fa*d*lihi walaAAallakum tashkuroon**a**

## 16:15

Waalq*a* fee alar*d*i raw*a*siya an tameeda bikum waanh*a*ran wasubulan laAAallakum tahtadoon**a**

## 16:16

WaAAal*a*m*a*tin wabi**al**nnajmi hum yahtadoon**a**

## 16:17

Afaman yakhluqu kaman l*a* yakhluqu afal*a* ta*th*akkaroon**a**

## 16:18

Wain taAAuddoo niAAmata All*a*hi l*a* tu*hs*ooh*a* inna All*a*ha laghafoorun ra*h*eem**un**

## 16:19

Wa**A**ll*a*hu yaAAlamu m*a* tusirroona wam*a* tuAAlinoon**a**

## 16:20

Wa**a**lla*th*eena yadAAoona min dooni All*a*hi l*a* yakhluqoona shayan wahum yukhlaqoon**a**

## 16:21

Amw*a*tun ghayru a*h*y*a*in wam*a* yashAAuroona ayy*a*na yubAAathoon**a**

## 16:22

Il*a*hukum il*a*hun w*ah*idun fa**a**lla*th*eena l*a* yuminoona bi**a**l*a*khirati quloobuhum munkiratun wahum mustakbiroon**a**

## 16:23

L*a* jarama anna All*a*ha yaAAlamu m*a* yusirroona wam*a* yuAAlinoona innahu l*a* yu*h*ibbu almustakbireen**a**

## 16:24

Wai*tha* qeela lahum m*atha* anzala rabbukum q*a*loo as*at*eeru alawwaleen**a**

## 16:25

Liya*h*miloo awz*a*rahum k*a*milatan yawma alqiy*a*mati wamin awz*a*ri alla*th*eena yu*d*illoonahum bighayri AAilmin al*a* s*a*a m*a* yaziroon**a**

## 16:26

Qad makara alla*th*eena min qablihim faat*a* All*a*hu buny*a*nahum mina alqaw*a*AAidi fakharra AAalayhimu a**l**ssaqfu min fawqihim waat*a*humu alAAa*tha*bu min *h*aythu l*a* yashAAuroon**a**

## 16:27

Thumma yawma alqiy*a*mati yukhzeehim wayaqoolu ayna shurak*a*iya alla*th*eena kuntum tush*a*qqoona feehim q*a*la alla*th*eena ootoo alAAilma inna alkhizya alyawma wa**al**ssooa AAal*a* alk*a*fireen**a**

## 16:28

Alla*th*eena tatawaff*a*humu almal*a*ikatu **th***a*limee anfusihim faalqawoo a**l**ssalama m*a* kunn*a* naAAmalu min sooin bal*a* inna All*a*ha AAaleemun bim*a* kuntum taAAmaloon**a**

## 16:29

Fa**o**dkhuloo abw*a*ba jahannama kh*a*lideena feeh*a* falabisa mathw*a* almutakabbireen**a**

## 16:30

Waqeela lilla*th*eena ittaqaw m*atha* anzala rabbukum q*a*loo khayran lilla*th*eena a*h*sanoo fee h*ath*ihi a**l**dduny*a* *h*asanatun walad*a*ru al*a*khirati khayrun walaniAAma d*a*ru almuttaqeen**a**

## 16:31

Jann*a*tu AAadnin yadkhuloonah*a* tajree min ta*h*tih*a* alanh*a*ru lahum feeh*a* m*a* yash*a*oona ka*tha*lika yajzee All*a*hu almuttaqeen**a**

## 16:32

Alla*th*eena tatawaff*a*humu almal*a*ikatu *t*ayyibeena yaqooloona sal*a*mun AAalaykumu odkhuloo aljannata bim*a* kuntum taAAmaloon**a**

## 16:33

Hal ya&#x6E;**th**&#x75;roona ill*a* an tatiyahumu almal*a*ikatu aw yatiya amru rabbika ka*tha*lika faAAala alla*th*eena min qablihim wam*a* **th**&#x61;lamahumu All*a*hu wal*a*kin k*a*noo anfusahum y&#x61;**th**&#x6C;imoon**a**

## 16:34

Faa*sa*bahum sayyi*a*tu m*a* AAamiloo wa*ha*qa bihim m*a* k*a*noo bihi yastahzioon**a**

## 16:35

Waq*a*la alla*th*eena ashrakoo law sh*a*a All*a*hu m*a* AAabadn*a* min doonihi min shayin na*h*nu wal*a* *a*b*a*on*a* wal*a* *h*arramn*a* min doonihi min shayin ka*tha*lika faAAala alla*th*eena min qablihim fahal AAal*a* a**l**rrusuli ill*a* albal*a*ghu almubeen**u**

## 16:36

Walaqad baAAathn*a* fee kulli ommatin rasoolan ani oAAbudoo All*a*ha wa**i**jtaniboo a**l***tta*ghoota faminhum man had*a* All*a*hu waminhum man *h*aqqat AAalayhi a**l***dd*al*a*latu faseeroo fee alar*d*i fa**o**&#x6E;**th**&#x75;roo kayfa k*a*na AA*a*qibatu almuka*thth*ibeen**a**

## 16:37

In ta*h*ri*s* AAal*a* hud*a*hum fainna All*a*ha l*a* yahdee man yu*d*illu wam*a* lahum min n*as*ireen**a**

## 16:38

Waaqsamoo bi**A**ll*a*hi jahda aym*a*nihim l*a* yabAAathu All*a*hu man yamootu bal*a* waAAdan AAalayhi *h*aqqan wal*a*kinna akthara a**l**nn*a*si l*a* yaAAlamoon**a**

## 16:39

Liyubayyina lahumu alla*th*ee yakhtalifoona feehi waliyaAAlama alla*th*eena kafaroo annahum k*a*noo k*ath*ibeen**a**

## 16:40

Innam*a* qawlun*a* lishayin i*tha* aradn*a*hu an naqoola lahu kun fayakoon**u**

## 16:41

Wa**a**lla*th*eena h*a*jaroo fee All*a*hi min baAAdi m*a* **th**&#x75;limoo lanubawwiannahum fee a**l**dduny*a* *h*asanatan walaajru al*a*khirati akbaru law k*a*noo yaAAlamoon**a**

## 16:42

Alla*th*eena *s*abaroo waAAal*a* rabbihim yatawakkaloon**a**

## 16:43

Wam*a* arsaln*a* min qablika ill*a* rij*a*lan noo*h*ee ilayhim fa**i**saloo ahla a**l***thth*ikri in kuntum l*a* taAAlamoon**a**

## 16:44

Bi**a**lbayyin*a*ti wa**al**zzuburi waanzaln*a* ilayka a**l***thth*ikra litubayyina li**l**nn*a*si m*a* nuzzila ilayhim walaAAallahum yatafakkaroon**a**

## 16:45

Afaamina alla*th*eena makaroo a**l**ssayyi*a*ti an yakhsifa All*a*hu bihimu alar*d*a aw yatiyahumu alAAa*tha*bu min *h*aythu l*a* yashAAuroon**a**

## 16:46

Aw yakhu*th*ahum fee taqallubihim fam*a* hum bimuAAjizeen**a**

## 16:47

Aw yakhu*th*ahum AAal*a* takhawwufin fainna rabbakum laraoofun ra*h*eem**un**

## 16:48

Awa lam yaraw il*a* m*a* khalaqa All*a*hu min shayin yatafayyao **th**&#x69;l*a*luhu AAani alyameeni wa**al**shsham*a*ili sujjadan lill*a*hi wahum d*a*khiroon**a**

## 16:49

Walill*a*hi yasjudu m*a* fee a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wam*a* fee alar*d*i min d*a*bbatin wa**a**lmal*a*ikatu wahum l*a* yastakbiroon**a**

## 16:50

Yakh*a*foona rabbahum min fawqihim wayafAAaloona m*a* yumaroon**a**

## 16:51

Waq*a*la All*a*hu l*a* tattakhi*th*oo il*a*hayni ithnayni innam*a* huwa il*a*hun w*ah*idun faiyy*a*ya fa**i**rhaboon**i**

## 16:52

Walahu m*a* fee a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i walahu a**l**ddeenu w*as*iban afaghayra All*a*hi tattaqoon**a**

## 16:53

Wam*a* bikum min niAAmatin famina All*a*hi thumma i*tha* massakumu a**l***dd*urru failayhi tajaroon**a**

## 16:54

Thumma i*tha* kashafa a**l***dd*urra AAankum i*tha* fareequn minkum birabbihim yushrikoon**a**

## 16:55

Liyakfuroo bim*a* *a*tayn*a*hum fatamattaAAoo fasawfa taAAlamoon**a**

## 16:56

WayajAAaloona lim*a* l*a* yaAAlamoona na*s*eeban mimm*a* razaqn*a*hum ta**A**ll*a*hi latusalunna AAamm*a* kuntum taftaroon**a**

## 16:57

WayajAAaloona lill*a*hi alban*a*ti sub*ha*nahu walahum m*a* yashtahoon**a**

## 16:58

Wai*tha* bushshira a*h*aduhum bi**a**lonth*a* **th**&#x61;lla wajhuhu muswaddan wahuwa k&#x61;**th**&#x65;em**un**

## 16:59

Yataw*a*r*a* mina alqawmi min sooi m*a* bushshira bihi ayumsikuhu AAal*a* hoonin am yadussuhu fee a**l**ttur*a*bi al*a* s*a*a m*a* ya*h*kumoon**a**

## 16:60

Lilla*th*eena l*a* yuminoona bi**a**l*a*khirati mathalu a**l**ssawi walill*a*hi almathalu alaAAl*a* wahuwa alAAazeezu al*h*akeem**u**

## 16:61

Walaw yu*a*khi*th*u All*a*hu a**l**nn*a*sa b&#x69;**th**&#x75;lmihim m*a* taraka AAalayh*a* min d*a*bbatin wal*a*kin yuakhkhiruhum il*a* ajalin musamman fai*tha* j*a*a ajaluhum l*a* yastakhiroona s*a*AAatan wal*a* yastaqdimoon**a**

## 16:62

WayajAAaloona lill*a*hi m*a* yakrahoona wata*s*ifu alsinatuhumu alka*th*iba anna lahumu al*h*usn*a* l*a* jarama anna lahumu a**l**nn*a*ra waannahum mufra*t*oon**a**

## 16:63

Ta**A**ll*a*hi laqad arsaln*a* il*a* omamin min qablika fazayyana lahumu a**l**shshay*ta*nu aAAm*a*lahum fahuwa waliyyuhumu alyawma walahum AAa*tha*bun aleem**un**

## 16:64

Wam*a* anzaln*a* AAalayka alkit*a*ba ill*a* litubayyina lahumu alla*th*ee ikhtalafoo feehi wahudan wara*h*matan liqawmin yuminoon**a**

## 16:65

Wa**A**ll*a*hu anzala mina a**l**ssam*a*i m*a*an faa*h*y*a* bihi alar*d*a baAAda mawtih*a* inna fee *tha*lika la*a*yatan liqawmin yasmaAAoon**a**

## 16:66

Wainna lakum fee alanAA*a*mi laAAibratan nusqeekum mimm*a* fee bu*t*oonihi min bayni farthin wadamin labanan kh*a*li*s*an s*a*ighan li**l**shsh*a*ribeen**a**

## 16:67

Wamin thamar*a*ti a**l**nnakheeli wa**a**laAAn*a*bi tattakhi*th*oona minhu sakaran warizqan *h*asanan inna fee *tha*lika la*a*yatan liqawmin yaAAqiloon**a**

## 16:68

Waaw*ha* rabbuka il*a* a**l**nna*h*li ani ittakhi*th*ee mina aljib*a*li buyootan wamina a**l**shshajari wamimm*a* yaAArishoon**a**

## 16:69

Thumma kulee min kulli a**l**ththamar*a*ti fa**o**slukee subula rabbiki *th*ululan yakhruju min bu*t*oonih*a* shar*a*bun mukhtalifun alw*a*nuhu feehi shif*a*on li**l**nn*a*si inna fee *tha*lika la*a*yatan liqawmin yatafakkaroon**a**

## 16:70

Wa**A**ll*a*hu khalaqakum thumma yatawaff*a*kum waminkum man yuraddu il*a* ar*th*ali alAAumuri likay l*a* yaAAlama baAAda AAilmin shayan inna All*a*ha AAaleemun qadeer**un**

## 16:71

Wa**A**ll*a*hu fa*dd*ala baAA*d*akum AAal*a* baAA*d*in fee a**l**rrizqi fam*a* alla*th*eena fu*dd*iloo bir*a*ddee rizqihim AAal*a* m*a* malakat aym*a*nuhum fahum feehi saw*a*on afabiniAAmati All*a*hi yaj*h*adoon**a**

## 16:72

Wa**A**ll*a*hu jaAAala lakum min anfusikum azw*a*jan wajaAAala lakum min azw*a*jikum baneena wa*h*afadatan warazaqakum mina a**l***tt*ayyib*a*ti afabi**a**lb*at*ili yuminoona wabiniAAmati All*a*hi hum yakfuroon**a**

## 16:73

WayaAAbudoona min dooni All*a*hi m*a* l*a* yamliku lahum rizqan mina a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i shayan wal*a* yasta*t*eeAAoon**a**

## 16:74

Fal*a* ta*d*riboo lill*a*hi alamth*a*la inna All*a*ha yaAAlamu waantum l*a* taAAlamoon**a**

## 16:75

*D*araba All*a*hu mathalan AAabdan mamlookan l*a* yaqdiru AAal*a* shayin waman razaqn*a*hu minn*a* rizqan *h*asanan fahuwa yunfiqu minhu sirran wajahran hal yastawoona al*h*amdu lill*a*hi bal aktharuhum l*a* yaAAlamoon**a**

## 16:76

Wa*d*araba All*a*hu mathalan rajulayni a*h*aduhum*a* abkamu l*a* yaqdiru AAal*a* shayin wahuwa kallun AAal*a* mawl*a*hu aynam*a* yuwajjihhu l*a* yati bikhayrin hal yastawee huwa waman yamuru bi**a**lAAadli wahuwa AAal*a* *s*ir*at*in mustaqeem**in**

## 16:77

Walill*a*hi ghaybu a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i wam*a* amru a**l**ss*a*AAati ill*a* kalam*h*i alba*s*ari aw huwa aqrabu inna All*a*ha AAal*a* kulli shayin qadeer**un**

## 16:78

Wa**A**ll*a*hu akhrajakum min bu*t*ooni ommah*a*tikum l*a* taAAlamoona shayan wajaAAala lakumu a**l**ssamAAa wa**a**lab*sa*ra wa**a**lafidata laAAallakum tashkuroon**a**

## 16:79

Alam yaraw il*a* a**l***tt*ayri musakhkhar*a*tin fee jawwi a**l**ssam*a*i m*a* yumsikuhunna ill*a* All*a*hu inna fee *tha*lika la*a*y*a*tin liqawmin yuminoon**a**

## 16:80

Wa**A**ll*a*hu jaAAala lakum min buyootikum sakanan wajaAAala lakum min juloodi alanAA*a*mi buyootan tastakhiffoonah*a* yawma **th**&#x61;AAnikum wayawma iq*a*matikum wamin a*s*w*a*fih*a* waawb*a*rih*a* waashAA*a*rih*a* ath*a*than wamat*a*AAan il*a* *h*een**in**

## 16:81

Wa**A**ll*a*hu jaAAala lakum mimm*a* khalaqa **th**&#x69;l*a*lan wajaAAala lakum mina aljib*a*li akn*a*nan wajaAAala lakum sar*a*beela taqeekumu al*h*arra wasar*a*beela taqeekum basakum ka*tha*lika yutimmu niAAmatahu AAalaykum laAAallakum tuslimoon**a**

## 16:82

Fain tawallaw fainnam*a* AAalayka albal*a*ghu almubeen**u**

## 16:83

YaAArifoona niAAmata All*a*hi thumma yunkiroonah*a* waaktharuhumu alk*a*firoon**a**

## 16:84

Wayawma nabAAathu min kulli ommatin shaheedan thumma l*a* yu*th*anu lilla*th*eena kafaroo wal*a* hum yustaAAtaboon**a**

## 16:85

Wai*tha* ra*a* alla*th*eena **th**&#x61;lamoo alAAa*tha*ba fal*a* yukhaffafu AAanhum wal*a* hum yu&#x6E;**th**&#x61;roon**a**

## 16:86

Wai*tha* ra*a* alla*th*eena ashrakoo shurak*a*ahum q*a*loo rabban*a* h*a*ol*a*i shurak*a*on*a* alla*th*eena kunn*a* nadAAoo min doonika faalqaw ilayhimu alqawla innakum lak*ath*iboon**a**

## 16:87

Waalqaw il*a* All*a*hi yawmai*th*in a**l**ssalama wa*d*alla AAanhum m*a* k*a*noo yaftaroon**a**

## 16:88

Alla*th*eena kafaroo wa*s*addoo AAan sabeeli All*a*hi zidn*a*hum AAa*tha*ban fawqa alAAa*tha*bi bim*a* k*a*noo yufsidoon**a**

## 16:89

Wayawma nabAAathu fee kulli ommatin shaheedan AAalayhim min anfusihim wajin*a* bika shaheedan AAal*a* h*a*ol*a*i wanazzaln*a* AAalayka alkit*a*ba tiby*a*nan likulli shayin wahudan wara*h*matan wabushr*a* lilmuslimeen**a**

## 16:90

Inna All*a*ha yamuru bi**a**lAAadli wa**a**li*h*s*a*ni waeet*a*i *th*ee alqurb*a* wayanh*a* AAani alfa*h*sh*a*i wa**a**lmunkari wa**a**lbaghyi yaAA&#x69;**th**&#x75;kum laAAallakum ta*th*akkaroon**a**

## 16:91

Waawfoo biAAahdi All*a*hi i*tha* AA*a*hadtum wal*a* tanqu*d*oo alaym*a*na baAAda tawkeedih*a* waqad jaAAaltumu All*a*ha AAalaykum kafeelan inna All*a*ha yaAAlamu m*a* tafAAaloon**a**

## 16:92

Wal*a* takoonoo ka**a**llatee naqa*d*at ghazlah*a* min baAAdi quwwatin ank*a*than tattakhi*th*oona aym*a*nakum dakhalan baynakum an takoona ommatun hiya arb*a* min ommatin innam*a* yablookumu All*a*hu bihi walayubayyinanna lakum yawma alqiy*a*mati m*a* kuntum feehi takhtalifoon**a**

## 16:93

Walaw sh*a*a All*a*hu lajaAAalakum ommatan w*ah*idatan wal*a*kin yu*d*illu man yash*a*o wayahdee man yash*a*o walatusalunna AAamm*a* kuntum taAAmaloon**a**

## 16:94

Wal*a* tattakhi*th*oo aym*a*nakum dakhalan baynakum fatazilla qadamun baAAda thubootih*a* wata*th*ooqoo a**l**ssooa bim*a* *s*adadtum AAan sabeeli All*a*hi walakum AAa*tha*bun AA&#x61;**th**&#x65;em**un**

## 16:95

Wal*a* tashtaroo biAAahdi All*a*hi thamanan qaleelan innam*a* AAinda All*a*hi huwa khayrun lakum in kuntum taAAlamoon**a**

## 16:96

M*a* AAindakum yanfadu wam*a* AAinda All*a*hi b*a*qin walanajziyanna alla*th*eena *s*abaroo ajrahum bia*h*sani m*a* k*a*noo yaAAmaloon**a**

## 16:97

Man AAamila *sa*li*h*an min *th*akarin aw onth*a* wahuwa muminun falanu*h*yiyannahu *h*ay*a*tan *t*ayyibatan walanajziyannahum ajrahum bia*h*sani m*a* k*a*noo yaAAmaloon**a**

## 16:98

Fai*tha* qarata alqur*a*na fa**i**staAAi*th* bi**A**ll*a*hi mina a**l**shshay*ta*ni a**l**rrajeem**i**

## 16:99

Innahu laysa lahu sul*ta*nun AAal*a* alla*th*eena *a*manoo waAAal*a* rabbihim yatawakkaloon**a**

## 16:100

Innam*a* sul*ta*nuhu AAal*a* alla*th*eena yatawallawnahu wa**a**lla*th*eena hum bihi mushrikoon**a**

## 16:101

Wai*tha* baddaln*a* *a*yatan mak*a*na *a*yatin wa**A**ll*a*hu aAAlamu bim*a* yunazzilu q*a*loo innam*a* anta muftarin bal aktharuhum l*a* yaAAlamoon**a**

## 16:102

Qul nazzalahu roo*h*u alqudusi min rabbika bi**a**l*h*aqqi liyuthabbita alla*th*eena *a*manoo wahudan wabushr*a* lilmuslimeen**a**

## 16:103

Walaqad naAAlamu annahum yaqooloona innam*a* yuAAallimuhu basharun lis*a*nu alla*th*ee yul*h*idoona ilayhi aAAjamiyyun wah*atha* lis*a*nun AAarabiyyun mubeen**un**

## 16:104

Inna alla*th*eena l*a* yuminoona bi*a*y*a*ti All*a*hi l*a* yahdeehimu All*a*hu walahum AAa*tha*bun aleem**un**

## 16:105

Innam*a* yaftaree alka*th*iba alla*th*eena l*a* yuminoona bi*a*y*a*ti All*a*hi waol*a*ika humu alk*ath*iboon**a**

## 16:106

Man kafara bi**A**ll*a*hi min baAAdi eem*a*nihi ill*a* man okriha waqalbuhu mu*t*mainnun bi**a**leem*a*ni wal*a*kin man shara*h*a bi**a**lkufri *s*adran faAAalayhim gha*d*abun mina All*a*hi walahum AAa*tha*bun AA&#x61;**th**&#x65;em**un**

## 16:107

*Tha*lika biannahumu ista*h*abboo al*h*ay*a*ta a**l**dduny*a* AAal*a* al*a*khirati waanna All*a*ha l*a* yahdee alqawma alk*a*fireen**a**

## 16:108

Ol*a*ika alla*th*eena *t*abaAAa All*a*hu AAal*a* quloobihim wasamAAihim waab*sa*rihim waol*a*ika humu algh*a*filoon**a**

## 16:109

L*a* jarama annahum fee al*a*khirati humu alkh*a*siroon**a**

## 16:110

Thumma inna rabbaka lilla*th*eena h*a*jaroo min baAAdi m*a* futinoo thumma j*a*hadoo wa*s*abaroo inna rabbaka min baAAdih*a* laghafoorun ra*h*eem**un**

## 16:111

Yawma tatee kullu nafsin tuj*a*dilu AAan nafsih*a* watuwaff*a* kullu nafsin m*a* AAamilat wahum l*a* y&#x75;**th**&#x6C;amoon**a**

## 16:112

Wa*d*araba All*a*hu mathalan qaryatan k*a*nat *a*minatan mu*t*mainnatan yateeh*a* rizquh*a* raghadan min kulli mak*a*nin fakafarat bianAAumi All*a*hi faa*tha*qah*a* All*a*hu lib*a*sa aljooAAi wa**a**lkhawfi bim*a* k*a*noo ya*s*naAAoon**a**

## 16:113

Walaqad j*a*ahum rasoolun minhum faka*thth*aboohu faakha*th*ahumu alAAa*tha*bu wahum **th***a*limoon**a**

## 16:114

Fakuloo mimm*a* razaqakumu All*a*hu *h*al*a*lan *t*ayyiban wa**o**shkuroo niAAmata All*a*hi in kuntum iyy*a*hu taAAbudoon**a**

## 16:115

Innam*a* *h*arrama AAalaykumu almaytata wa**al**ddama wala*h*ma alkhinzeeri wam*a* ohilla lighayri All*a*hi bihi famani i*dt*urra ghayra b*a*ghin wal*a* AA*a*din fainna All*a*ha ghafoorun ra*h*eem**un**

## 16:116

Wal*a* taqooloo lim*a* ta*s*ifu alsinatukumu alka*th*iba h*atha* *h*al*a*lun wah*atha* *h*ar*a*mun litaftaroo AAal*a* All*a*hi alka*th*iba inna alla*th*eena yaftaroona AAal*a* All*a*hi alka*th*iba l*a* yufli*h*oon**a**

## 16:117

Mat*a*AAun qaleelun walahum AAa*tha*bun aleem**un**

## 16:118

WaAAal*a* alla*th*eena h*a*doo *h*arramn*a* m*a* qa*s*a*s*n*a* AAalayka min qablu wam*a* **th**&#x61;lamn*a*hum wal*a*kin k*a*noo anfusahum y&#x61;**th**&#x6C;imoon**a**

## 16:119

Thumma inna rabbaka lilla*th*eena AAamiloo a**l**ssooa bijah*a*latin thumma t*a*boo min baAAdi *tha*lika waa*s*la*h*oo inna rabbaka min baAAdih*a* laghafoorun ra*h*eem**un**

## 16:120

Inna ibr*a*heema k*a*na ommatan q*a*nitan lill*a*hi *h*aneefan walam yaku mina almushrikeen**a**

## 16:121

Sh*a*kiran lianAAumihi ijtab*a*hu wahad*a*hu il*a* *s*ir*at*in mustaqeem**in**

## 16:122

Wa*a*tayn*a*hu fee a**l**dduny*a* *h*asanatan wainnahu fee al*a*khirati lamina a**l***ssa*li*h*een**a**

## 16:123

Thumma aw*h*ayn*a* ilayka ani ittabiAA millata ibr*a*heema *h*aneefan wam*a* k*a*na mina almushrikeen**a**

## 16:124

Innam*a* juAAila a**l**ssabtu AAal*a* alla*th*eena ikhtalafoo feehi wainna rabbaka laya*h*kumu baynahum yawma alqiy*a*mati feem*a* k*a*noo feehi yakhtalifoon**a**

## 16:125

OdAAu il*a* sabeeli rabbika bi**a**l*h*ikmati wa**a**lmawAA&#x69;**th**&#x61;ti al*h*asanati waj*a*dilhum bi**a**llatee hiya a*h*sanu inna rabbaka huwa aAAlamu biman *d*alla AAan sabeelihi wahuwa aAAlamu bi**a**lmuhtadeen**a**

## 16:126

Wain AA*a*qabtum faAA*a*qiboo bimithli m*a* AAooqibtum bihi walain *s*abartum lahuwa khayrun li**l***ssa*bireen**a**

## 16:127

Wa**i***s*bir wam*a* *s*abruka ill*a* bi**A**ll*a*hi wal*a* ta*h*zan AAalayhim wal*a* taku fee *d*ayqin mimm*a* yamkuroon**a**

## 16:128

Inna All*a*ha maAAa alla*th*eena ittaqaw wa**a**lla*th*eena hum mu*h*sinoon**a**

## 17:1

Sub*ha*na alla*th*ee asr*a* biAAabdihi laylan mina almasjidi al*h*ar*a*mi il*a* almasjidi alaq*sa* alla*th*ee b*a*rakn*a* *h*awlahu linuriyahu min *a*y*a*tin*a* innahu huwa a**l**ssameeAAu alba*s*eer**u**

## 17:2

Wa*a*tayn*a* moos*a* alkit*a*ba wajaAAaln*a*hu hudan libanee isr*a*eela all*a* tattakhi*th*oo min doonee wakeel*a***n**

## 17:3

*Th*urriyyata man *h*amaln*a* maAAa noo*h*in innahu k*a*na AAabdan shakoor*a***n**

## 17:4

Waqa*d*ayn*a* il*a* banee isr*a*eela fee alkit*a*bi latufsidunna fee alar*d*i marratayni walataAAlunna AAuluwwan kabeer*a***n**

## 17:5

Fai*tha* j*a*a waAAdu ool*a*hum*a* baAAathn*a* AAalaykum AAib*a*dan lan*a* olee basin shadeedin faj*a*soo khil*a*la a**l**ddiy*a*ri wak*a*na waAAdan mafAAool*a***n**

## 17:6

Thumma radadn*a* lakumu alkarrata AAalayhim waamdadn*a*kum biamw*a*lin wabaneena wajaAAaln*a*kum akthara nafeer*a***n**

## 17:7

In a*h*santum a*h*santum lianfusikum wain asatum falah*a* fai*tha* j*a*a waAAdu al*a*khirati liyasoooo wujoohakum waliyadkhuloo almasjida kam*a* dakhaloohu awwala marratin waliyutabbiroo m*a* AAalaw tatbeer*a***n**

## 17:8

AAas*a* rabbukum an yar*h*amakum wain AAudtum AAudn*a* wajaAAaln*a* jahannama lilk*a*fireena *h*a*s*eer*a***n**

## 17:9

Inna h*atha* alqur*a*na yahdee lillatee hiya aqwamu wayubashshiru almumineena alla*th*eena yaAAmaloona a**l***ssa*li*ha*ti anna lahum ajran kabeer*a***n**

## 17:10

Waanna alla*th*eena l*a* yuminoona bi**a**l*a*khirati aAAtadn*a* lahum AAa*tha*ban aleem*a***n**

## 17:11

WayadAAu alins*a*nu bi**al**shsharri duAA*a*ahu bi**a**lkhayri wak*a*na alins*a*nu AAajool*a***n**

## 17:12

WajaAAaln*a* allayla wa**al**nnah*a*ra *a*yatayni fama*h*awn*a* *a*yata allayli wajaAAaln*a* *a*yata a**l**nnah*a*ri mub*s*iratan litabtaghoo fa*d*lan min rabbikum walitaAAlamoo AAadada a**l**ssineena wa**a**l*h*is*a*ba wakulla shayin fa*ss*aln*a*hu taf*s*eel*a***n**

## 17:13

Wakulla ins*a*nin alzamn*a*hu *ta*irahu fee AAunuqihi wanukhriju lahu yawma alqiy*a*mati kit*a*ban yalq*a*hu manshoor*a***n**

## 17:14

Iqra kit*a*baka kaf*a* binafsika alyawma AAalayka *h*aseeb*a***n**

## 17:15

Mani ihtad*a* fainnam*a* yahtadee linafsihi waman *d*alla fainnam*a* ya*d*illu AAalayh*a* wal*a* taziru w*a*ziratun wizra okhr*a* wam*a* kunn*a* muAAa*thth*ibeena *h*att*a* nabAAatha rasool*a***n**

## 17:16

Wai*tha* aradn*a* an nuhlika qaryatan amarn*a* mutrafeeh*a* fafasaqoo feeh*a* fa*h*aqqa AAalayh*a* alqawlu fadammarn*a*h*a* tadmeer*a***n**

## 17:17

Wakam ahlakn*a* mina alqurooni min baAAdi noo*h*in wakaf*a* birabbika bi*th*unoobi AAib*a*dihi khabeeran ba*s*eer*a***n**

## 17:18

Man k*a*na yureedu alAA*a*jilata AAajjaln*a* lahu feeh*a* m*a* nash*a*o liman nureedu thumma jaAAaln*a* lahu jahannama ya*s*l*a*h*a* ma*th*mooman mad*h*oor*a***n**

## 17:19

Waman ar*a*da al*a*khirata wasaAA*a* lah*a* saAAyah*a* wahuwa muminun faol*a*ika k*a*na saAAyuhum mashkoor*a***n**

## 17:20

Kullan numiddu h*a*ol*a*i wah*a*ol*a*i min AAa*ta*i rabbika wam*a* k*a*na AAa*ta*o rabbika ma*h***th**&#x6F;or*a***n**

## 17:21

O&#x6E;**th**&#x75;r kayfa fa*dd*aln*a* baAA*d*ahum AAal*a* baAA*d*in walal*a*khiratu akbaru daraj*a*tin waakbaru taf*d*eel*a***n**

## 17:22

L*a* tajAAal maAAa All*a*hi il*a*han *a*khara fataqAAuda ma*th*mooman makh*th*ool*a***n**

## 17:23

Waqa*da* rabbuka all*a* taAAbudoo ill*a* iyy*a*hu wabi**a**lw*a*lidayni i*h*s*a*nan imm*a* yablughanna AAindaka alkibara a*h*aduhum*a* aw kil*a*hum*a* fal*a* taqul lahum*a* offin wal*a* tanharhum*a* waqul lahum*a* qawlan kareem*a***n**

## 17:24

Wa**i**khfi*d* lahum*a* jan*ah*a a**l***thth*ulli mina a**l**rra*h*mati waqul rabbi ir*h*amhum*a* kam*a* rabbay*a*nee *s*agheer*a***n**

## 17:25

Rabbukum aAAlamu bim*a* fee nufoosikum in takoonoo *sa*li*h*eena fainnahu k*a*na lilaww*a*beena ghafoor*a***n**

## 17:26

Wa*a*ti *tha* alqurb*a* *h*aqqahu wa**a**lmiskeena wa**i**bna a**l**ssabeeli wal*a* tuba*thth*ir tab*th*eer*a***n**

## 17:27

Inna almuba*thth*ireena k*a*noo ikhw*a*na a**l**shshay*at*eeni wak*a*na a**l**shshay*ta*nu lirabbihi kafoor*a***n**

## 17:28

Waimm*a* tuAAri*d*anna AAanhumu ibtigh*a*a ra*h*matin min rabbika tarjooh*a* faqul lahum qawlan maysoor*a***n**

## 17:29

Wal*a* tajAAal yadaka maghloolatan il*a* AAunuqika wal*a* tabsu*t*h*a* kulla albas*t*i fataqAAuda malooman ma*h*soor*a***n**

## 17:30

Inna rabbaka yabsu*t*u a**l**rrizqa liman yash*a*o wayaqdiru innahu k*a*na biAAib*a*dihi khabeeran ba*s*eer*a***n**

## 17:31

Wal*a* taqtuloo awl*a*dakum khashyata iml*a*qin na*h*nu narzuquhum waiyy*a*kum inna qatlahum k*a*na khi*t*an kabeer*a***n**

## 17:32

Wal*a* taqraboo a**l**zzin*a* innahu k*a*na f*ah*ishatan was*a*a sabeel*a***n**

## 17:33

Wal*a* taqtuloo a**l**nnafsa allatee *h*arrama All*a*hu ill*a* bi**a**l*h*aqqi waman qutila m&#x61;**th**&#x6C;ooman faqad jaAAaln*a* liwaliyyihi sul*ta*nan fal*a* yusrif fee alqatli innahu k*a*na man*s*oor*a***n**

## 17:34

Wal*a* taqraboo m*a*la alyateemi ill*a* bi**a**llatee hiya a*h*sanu *h*att*a* yablugha ashuddahu waawfoo bi**a**lAAahdi inna alAAahda k*a*na masool*a***n**

## 17:35

Waawfoo alkayla i*tha* kiltum wazinoo bi**a**lqis*ta*si almustaqeemi *tha*lika khayrun waa*h*sanu taweel*a***n**

## 17:36

Wal*a* taqfu m*a* laysa laka bihi AAilmun inna a**l**ssamAAa wa**a**lba*s*ara wa**a**lfu*a*da kullu ol*a*ika k*a*na AAanhu masool*a***n**

## 17:37

Wal*a* tamshi fee alar*d*i mara*h*an innaka lan takhriqa alar*d*a walan tablugha aljib*a*la *t*ool*a***n**

## 17:38

Kullu *tha*lika k*a*na sayyiohu AAinda rabbika makrooh*a***n**

## 17:39

*Tha*lika mimm*a* aw*ha* ilayka rabbuka mina al*h*ikmati wal*a* tajAAal maAAa All*a*hi il*a*han *a*khara fatulq*a* fee jahannama malooman mad*h*oor*a***n**

## 17:40

Afaa*s*f*a*kum rabbukum bi**a**lbaneena wa**i**ttakha*th*a mina almal*a*ikati in*a*than innakum lataqooloona qawlan AA&#x61;**th**&#x65;em*a***n**

## 17:41

Walaqad *s*arrafn*a* fee h*atha* alqur*a*ni liya*thth*akkaroo wam*a* yazeeduhum ill*a* nufoor*a***n**

## 17:42

Qul law k*a*na maAAahu *a*lihatun kam*a* yaqooloona i*th*an la**i**btaghaw il*a* *th*ee alAAarshi sabeel*a***n**

## 17:43

Sub*ha*nahu wataAA*a*l*a* AAamm*a* yaqooloona AAuluwwan kabeer*a***n**

## 17:44

Tusabbi*h*u lahu a**l**ssam*a*w*a*tu a**l**ssabAAu wa**a**lar*d*u waman feehinna wain min shayin ill*a* yusabbi*h*u bi*h*amdihi wal*a*kin l*a* tafqahoona tasbee*h*ahum innahu k*a*na *h*aleeman ghafoor*a***n**

## 17:45

Wai*tha* qarata alqur*a*na jaAAaln*a* baynaka wabayna alla*th*eena l*a* yuminoona bi**a**l*a*khirati *h*ij*a*ban mastoor*a***n**

## 17:46

WajaAAaln*a* AAal*a* quloobihim akinnatan an yafqahoohu wafee *atha*nihim waqran wai*tha* *th*akarta rabbaka fee alqur*a*ni wa*h*dahu wallaw AAal*a* adb*a*rihim nufoor*a***n**

## 17:47

Na*h*nu aAAlamu bim*a* yastamiAAoona bihi i*th* yastamiAAoona ilayka wai*th* hum najw*a* i*th* yaqoolu a**l****thth***a*limoona in tattabiAAoona ill*a* rajulan mas*h*oor*a***n**

## 17:48

O&#x6E;**th**&#x75;r kayfa *d*araboo laka alamth*a*la fa*d*alloo fal*a* yasta*t*eeAAoona sabeel*a***n**

## 17:49

Waq*a*loo ai*tha* kunn*a* AA&#x69;**th***a*man waruf*a*tan ainn*a* lamabAAoothoona khalqan jadeed*a***n**

## 17:50

Qul koonoo *h*ij*a*ratan aw *h*adeed*a***n**

## 17:51

Aw khalqan mimm*a* yakburu fee *s*udoorikum fasayaqooloona man yuAAeedun*a* quli alla*th*ee fa*t*arakum awwala marratin fasayunghi*d*oona ilayka ruoosahum wayaqooloona mat*a* huwa qul AAas*a* an yakoona qareeb*a***n**

## 17:52

Yawma yadAAookum fatastajeeboona bi*h*amdihi wat&#x61;**th**&#x75;nnoona in labithtum ill*a* qaleel*a***n**

## 17:53

Waqul liAAib*a*dee yaqooloo allatee hiya a*h*sanu inna a**l**shshay*ta*na yanzaghu baynahum inna a**l**shshay*ta*na k*a*na lilins*a*ni AAaduwwan mubeen*a***n**

## 17:54

Rabbukum aAAlamu bikum in yasha yar*h*amkum aw in yasha yuAAa*thth*ibkum wam*a* arsaln*a*ka AAalayhim wakeel*a***n**

## 17:55

Warabbuka aAAlamu biman fee a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i walaqad fa*dd*aln*a* baAA*d*a a**l**nnabiyyeena AAal*a* baAA*d*in wa*a*tayn*a* d*a*wooda zaboor*a***n**

## 17:56

Quli odAAu alla*th*eena zaAAamtum min doonihi fal*a* yamlikoona kashfa a**l***dd*urri AAankum wal*a* ta*h*weel*a***n**

## 17:57

Ol*a*ika alla*th*eena yadAAoona yabtaghoona il*a* rabbihimu alwaseelata ayyuhum aqrabu wayarjoona ra*h*matahu wayakh*a*foona AAa*tha*bahu inna AAa*tha*ba rabbika k*a*na ma*hth*oor*a***n**

## 17:58

Wain min qaryatin ill*a* na*h*nu muhlikooh*a* qabla yawmi alqiy*a*mati aw muAAa*thth*ibooh*a* AAa*tha*ban shadeedan k*a*na *tha*lika fee alkit*a*bi mas*t*oor*a***n**

## 17:59

Wam*a* manaAAan*a* an nursila bi**a**l*a*y*a*ti ill*a* an ka*thth*aba bih*a* alawwaloona wa*a*tayn*a* thamooda a**l**nn*a*qata mub*s*iratan f&#x61;**th**&#x61;lamoo bih*a* wam*a* nursilu bi**a**l*a*y*a*ti ill*a* takhweef*a***n**

## 17:60

Wai*th* quln*a* laka inna rabbaka a*hat*a bi**al**nn*a*si wam*a* jaAAaln*a* a**l**rruy*a* allatee arayn*a*ka ill*a* fitnatan li**l**nn*a*si wa**al**shshajarata almalAAoonata fee alqur*a*ni wanukhawwifuhum fam*a* yazeeduhum ill*a* *t*ughy*a*nan kabeer*a***n**

## 17:61

Wai*th* quln*a* lilmal*a*ikati osjudoo li*a*dama fasajadoo ill*a* ibleesa q*a*la aasjudu liman khalaqta *t*een*a***n**

## 17:62

Q*a*la araaytaka h*atha* alla*th*ee karramta AAalayya lain akhkhartani il*a* yawmi alqiy*a*mati laa*h*tanikanna *th*urriyyatahu ill*a* qaleel*a***n**

## 17:63

Q*a*la i*th*hab faman tabiAAaka minhum fainna jahannama jaz*a*okum jaz*a*an mawfoor*a***n**

## 17:64

Wa**i**stafziz mani ista*t*aAAta minhum bi*s*awtika waajlib AAalayhim bikhaylika warajlika wash*a*rikhum fee alamw*a*li wa**a**lawl*a*di waAAidhum wam*a* yaAAiduhumu a**l**shshay*ta*nu ill*a* ghuroor*a***n**

## 17:65

Inna AAib*a*dee laysa laka AAalayhim sul*ta*nun wakaf*a* birabbika wakeel*a***n**

## 17:66

Rabbukumu alla*th*ee yuzjee lakumu alfulka fee alba*h*ri litabtaghoo min fa*d*lihi innahu k*a*na bikum ra*h*eem*a***n**

## 17:67

Wai*tha* massakumu a**l***dd*urru fee alba*h*ri *d*alla man tadAAoona ill*a* iyy*a*hu falamm*a* najj*a*kum il*a* albarri aAAra*d*tum wak*a*na alins*a*nu kafoor*a***n**

## 17:68

Afaamintum an yakhsifa bikum j*a*niba albarri aw yursila AAalaykum *has*iban thumma l*a* tajidoo lakum wakeel*a***n**

## 17:69

Am amintum an yuAAeedakum feehi t*a*ratan okhr*a* fayursila AAalaykum q*as*ifan mina a**l**rree*h*i fayughriqakum bim*a* kafartum thumma l*a* tajidoo lakum AAalayn*a* bihi tabeeAA*a***n**

## 17:70

Walaqad karramn*a* banee *a*dama wa*h*amaln*a*hum fee albarri wa**a**lba*h*ri warazaqn*a*hum mina a**l***tt*ayyib*a*ti wafa*dd*aln*a*hum AAal*a* katheerin mimman khalaqn*a* taf*d*eel*a***n**

## 17:71

Yawma nadAAoo kulla on*a*sin biim*a*mihim faman ootiya kit*a*bahu biyameenihi faol*a*ika yaqraoona kit*a*bahum wal*a* y&#x75;**th**&#x6C;amoona fateel*a***n**

## 17:72

Waman k*a*na fee h*ath*ihi aAAm*a* fahuwa fee al*a*khirati aAAm*a* waa*d*allu sabeel*a***n**

## 17:73

Wain k*a*doo layaftinoonaka AAani alla*th*ee aw*h*ayn*a* ilayka litaftariya AAalayn*a* ghayrahu wai*th*an la**i**ttakha*th*ooka khaleel*a***n**

## 17:74

Walawl*a* an thabbatn*a*ka laqad kidta tarkanu ilayhim shayan qaleel*a***n**

## 17:75

I*th*an laa*th*aqn*a*ka *d*iAAfa al*h*ay*a*ti wa*d*iAAfa almam*a*ti thumma l*a* tajidu laka AAalayn*a* na*s*eer*a***n**

## 17:76

Wain k*a*doo layastafizzoonaka mina alar*d*i liyukhrijooka minh*a* wai*th*an l*a* yalbathoona khil*a*faka ill*a* qaleel*a***n**

## 17:77

Sunnata man qad arsaln*a* qablaka min rusulin*a* wal*a* tajidu lisunnatin*a* ta*h*weel*a***n**

## 17:78

Aqimi a**l***ss*al*a*ta lidulooki a**l**shshamsi il*a* ghasaqi allayli waqur*a*na alfajri inna qur*a*na alfajri k*a*na mashhood*a***n**

## 17:79

Wamina allayli fatahajjad bihi n*a*filatan laka AAas*a* an yabAAathaka rabbuka maq*a*man ma*h*mood*a***n**

## 17:80

Waqul rabbi adkhilnee mudkhala *s*idqin waakhrijnee mukhraja *s*idqin wa**i**jAAal lee min ladunka sul*ta*nan na*s*eer*a***n**

## 17:81

Waqul j*a*a al*h*aqqu wazahaqa alb*at*ilu inna alb*at*ila k*a*na zahooq*a***n**

## 17:82

Wanunazzilu mina alqur*a*ni m*a* huwa shif*a*on wara*h*matun lilmumineena wal*a* yazeedu a**l****thth***a*limeena ill*a* khas*a*r*a***n**

## 17:83

Wai*tha* anAAamn*a* AAal*a* alins*a*ni aAAra*d*a wana*a* bij*a*nibihi wai*tha* massahu a**l**shsharru k*a*na yaoos*a***n**

## 17:84

Qul kullun yaAAmalu AAal*a* sh*a*kilatihi farabbukum aAAlamu biman huwa ahd*a* sabeel*a***n**

## 17:85

Wayasaloonaka AAani a**l**rroo*h*i quli a**l**rroo*h*u min amri rabbee wam*a* ooteetum mina alAAilmi ill*a* qaleel*a***n**

## 17:86

Walain shin*a* lana*th*habanna bi**a**lla*th*ee aw*h*ayn*a* ilayka thumma l*a* tajidu laka bihi AAalayn*a* wakeel*a***n**

## 17:87

Ill*a* ra*h*matan min rabbika inna fa*d*lahu k*a*na AAalayka kabeer*a***n**

## 17:88

Qul laini ijtamaAAati alinsu wa**a**ljinnu AAal*a* an yatoo bimithli h*atha* alqur*a*ni l*a* yatoona bimithlihi walaw k*a*na baAA*d*uhum libaAA*d*in **th**&#x61;heer*a***n**

## 17:89

Walaqad *s*arrafn*a* li**l**nn*a*si fee h*atha* alqur*a*ni min kulli mathalin faab*a* aktharu a**l**nn*a*si ill*a* kufoor*a***n**

## 17:90

Waq*a*loo lan numina laka *h*att*a* tafjura lan*a* mina alar*d*i yanbooAA*a***n**

## 17:91

Aw takoona laka jannatun min nakheelin waAAinabin fatufajjira alanh*a*ra khil*a*lah*a* tafjeer*a***n**

## 17:92

Aw tusqi*t*a a**l**ssam*a*a kam*a* zaAAamta AAalayn*a* kisafan aw tatiya bi**A**ll*a*hi wa**a**lmal*a*ikati qabeel*a***n**

## 17:93

Aw yakoona laka baytun min zukhrufin aw tarq*a* fee a**l**ssam*a*i walan numina liruqiyyika *h*att*a* tunazzila AAalayn*a* kit*a*ban naqraohu qul sub*ha*na rabbee hal kuntu ill*a* basharan rasool*a***n**

## 17:94

Wam*a* manaAAa a**l**nn*a*sa an yuminoo i*th* j*a*ahumu alhud*a* ill*a* an q*a*loo abaAAatha All*a*hu basharan rasool*a***n**

## 17:95

Qul law k*a*na fee alar*d*i mal*a*ikatun yamshoona mu*t*mainneena lanazzaln*a* AAalayhim mina a**l**ssam*a*i malakan rasool*a***n**

## 17:96

Qul kaf*a* bi**A**ll*a*hi shaheedan baynee wabaynakum innahu k*a*na biAAib*a*dihi khabeeran ba*s*eer*a***n**

## 17:97

Waman yahdi All*a*hu fahuwa almuhtadi waman yu*d*lil falan tajida lahum awliy*a*a min doonihi wana*h*shuruhum yawma alqiy*a*mati AAal*a* wujoohihim AAumyan wabukman wa*s*umman maw*a*hum jahannamu kullam*a* khabat zidn*a*hum saAAeer*a***n**

## 17:98

*Tha*lika jaz*a*ohum biannahum kafaroo bi*a*y*a*tin*a* waq*a*loo ai*tha* kunn*a* AA&#x69;**th***a*man waruf*a*tan ainn*a* lamabAAoothoona khalqan jadeed*a***n**

## 17:99

Awalam yaraw anna All*a*ha alla*th*ee khalaqa a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*a q*a*dirun AAal*a* an yakhluqa mithlahum wajaAAala lahum ajalan l*a* rayba feehi faab*a* a**l****thth***a*limoona ill*a* kufoor*a***n**

## 17:100

Qul law antum tamlikoona khaz*a*ina ra*h*mati rabbee i*th*an laamsaktum khashyata alinf*a*qi wak*a*na alins*a*nu qatoor*a***n**

## 17:101

Walaqad *a*tayn*a* moos*a* tisAAa *a*y*a*tin bayyin*a*tin fa**i**sal banee isr*a*eela i*th* j*a*ahum faq*a*la lahu firAAawnu innee la&#x61;**th**&#x75;nnuka y*a* moos*a* mas*h*oor*a***n**

## 17:102

Q*a*la laqad AAalimta m*a* anzala h*a*ol*a*i ill*a* rabbu a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i ba*sa*ira wainnee la&#x61;**th**&#x75;nnuka y*a* firAAawnu mathboor*a***n**

## 17:103

Faar*a*da an yastafizzahum mina alar*d*i faaghraqn*a*hu waman maAAahu jameeAA*a***n**

## 17:104

Waquln*a* min baAAdihi libanee isr*a*eela oskunoo alar*d*a fai*tha* j*a*a waAAdu al*a*khirati jin*a* bikum lafeef*a***n**

## 17:105

Wabi**a**l*h*aqqi anzaln*a*hu wabi**a**l*h*aqqi nazala wam*a* arsaln*a*ka ill*a* mubashshiran wana*th*eer*a***n**

## 17:106

Waqur*a*nan faraqn*a*hu litaqraahu AAal*a* a**l**nn*a*si AAal*a* mukthin wanazzaln*a*hu tanzeel*a***n**

## 17:107

Qul *a*minoo bihi aw l*a* tuminoo inna alla*th*eena ootoo alAAilma min qablihi i*tha* yutl*a* AAalayhim yakhirroona lila*th*q*a*ni sujjad*a***n**

## 17:108

Wayaqooloona sub*ha*na rabbin*a* in k*a*na waAAdu rabbin*a* lamafAAool*a***n**

## 17:109

Wayakhirroona lila*th*q*a*ni yabkoona wayazeeduhum khushooAA*a***n**

## 17:110

Quli odAAoo All*a*ha awi odAAoo a**l**rra*h*m*a*na ayyan m*a* tadAAoo falahu alasm*a*o al*h*usn*a* wal*a* tajhar bi*s*al*a*tika wal*a* tukh*a*fit bih*a* wa**i**btaghi bayna *tha*lika sabeel*a***n**

## 17:111

Waquli al*h*amdu lill*a*hi alla*th*ee lam yattakhi*th* waladan walam yakun lahu shareekun fee almulki walam yakun lahu waliyyun mina a**l***thth*ulli wakabbirhu takbeer*a***n**

## 18:1

Al*h*amdu lill*a*hi alla*th*ee anzala AAal*a* AAabdihi alkit*a*ba walam yajAAal lahu AAiwaj*a***n**

## 18:2

Qayyiman liyun*th*ira basan shadeedan min ladunhu wayubashshira almumineena alla*th*eena yaAAmaloona a**l***ssa*li*ha*ti anna lahum ajran *h*asan*a***n**

## 18:3

M*a*kitheena feehi abad*a***n**

## 18:4

Wayun*th*ira alla*th*eena q*a*loo ittakha*th*a All*a*hu walad*a***n**

## 18:5

M*a* lahum bihi min AAilmin wal*a* li*a*b*a*ihim kaburat kalimatan takhruju min afw*a*hihim in yaqooloona ill*a* ka*th*ib*a***n**

## 18:6

FalaAAallaka b*a*khiAAun nafsaka AAal*a* *a*th*a*rihim in lam yuminoo bih*atha* al*h*adeethi asaf*a***n**

## 18:7

Inn*a* jaAAaln*a* m*a* AAal*a* alar*d*i zeenatan lah*a* linabluwahum ayyuhum a*h*sanu AAamal*a***n**

## 18:8

Wainn*a* laj*a*AAiloona m*a* AAalayh*a* *s*aAAeedan juruz*a***n**

## 18:9

Am *h*asibta anna a*s**ha*ba alkahfi wa**al**rraqeemi k*a*noo min *a*y*a*tin*a* AAajab*a***n**

## 18:10

I*th* aw*a* alfityatu il*a* alkahfi faq*a*loo rabban*a* *a*tin*a* min ladunka ra*h*matan wahayyi lan*a* min amrin*a* rashad*a***n****

## 18:11

Fa*d*arabn*a* AAal*a* *atha*nihim fee alkahfi sineena AAadad*a***n**

## 18:12

Thumma baAAathn*a*hum linaAAlama ayyu al*h*izbayni a*hsa* lim*a* labithoo amad*a***n**

## 18:13

Na*h*nu naqu*ss*u AAalayka nabaahum bi**a**l*h*aqqi innahum fityatun *a*manoo birabbihim wazidn*a*hum hud*a***n**

## 18:14

Waraba*t*n*a* AAal*a* quloobihim i*th* q*a*moo faq*a*loo rabbun*a* rabbu a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i lan nadAAuwa min doonihi il*a*han laqad quln*a* i*th*an sha*t*a*ta***n**

## 18:15

H*a*ol*a*i qawmun*a* ittakha*th*oo min doonihi *a*lihatan lawl*a* yatoona AAalayhim bisul*ta*nin bayyinin faman &#x61;**th**&#x6C;amu mimmani iftar*a* AAal*a* All*a*hi ka*th*ib*a***n**

## 18:16

Wai*th*i iAAtazaltumoohum wam*a* yaAAbudoona ill*a* All*a*ha fawoo il*a* alkahfi yanshur lakum rabbukum min ra*h*matihi wayuhayyi lakum min amrikum mirfaq*a***n**

## 18:17

Watar*a* a**l**shshamsa i*tha* *t*alaAAat taz*a*waru AAan kahfihim *tha*ta alyameeni wai*tha* gharabat taqri*d*uhum *tha*ta a**l**shshim*a*li wahum fee fajwatin minhu *tha*lika min *a*y*a*ti All*a*hi man yahdi All*a*hu fahuwa almuhtadi waman yu*d*lil falan tajida lahu waliyyan murshid*a***n**

## 18:18

Wata*h*sabuhum ayq*a***th**&#x61;n wahum ruqoodun wanuqallibuhum *tha*ta alyameeni wa*tha*ta a**l**shshim*a*li wakalbuhum b*a*si*t*un *th*ir*a*AAayhi bi**a**lwa*s*eedi lawi i*tt*alaAAta AAalayhim lawallayta minhum fir*a*ran walamulita minhum ruAAb*a***n**

## 18:19

Waka*tha*lika baAAathn*a*hum liyatas*a*aloo baynahum q*a*la q*a*ilun minhum kam labithtum q*a*loo labithn*a* yawman aw baAA*d*a yawmin q*a*loo rabbukum aAAlamu bim*a* labithtum fa**i**bAAathoo a*h*adakum biwariqikum h*ath*ihi il*a* almadeenati falya&#x6E;**th**&#x75;r ayyuh*a* azk*a* *t*aAA*a*man falyatikum birizqin minhu walyatala*tt*af wal*a* yushAAiranna bikum a*h*ad*a***n**

## 18:20

Innahum in y&#x61;**th**&#x68;aroo AAalaykum yarjumookum aw yuAAeedookum fee millatihim walan tufli*h*oo i*th*an abad*a***n**

## 18:21

Waka*tha*lika aAAtharn*a* AAalayhim liyaAAlamoo anna waAAda All*a*hi *h*aqqun waanna a**l**s*a*AAata l*a* rayba feeh*a* i*th* yatan*a*zaAAoona baynahum amrahum faq*a*loo ibnoo AAalayhim buny*a*nan rabbuhum aAAlamu bihim q*a*la alla*th*eena ghalaboo AAal*a* amrihim lanattakhi*th*anna AAalayhim masjid*a***n**

## 18:22

Sayaqooloona thal*a*thatun r*a*biAAuhum kalbuhum wayaqooloona khamsatun s*a*disuhum kalbuhum rajman bi**a**lghaybi wayaqooloona sabAAatun wath*a*minuhum kalbuhum qul rabbee aAAlamu biAAiddatihim m*a* yaAAlamuhum ill*a* qaleelun fal*a* tum*a*ri feehim ill*a* mir*a*an **th***a*hiran wal*a* tastafti feehim minhum a*h*ad*a***n**

## 18:23

Wal*a* taqoolanna lishayin innee f*a*AAilun *tha*lika ghad*a***n**

## 18:24

Ill*a* an yash*a*a All*a*hu wa**o***th*kur rabbaka i*tha* naseeta waqul AAas*a* an yahdiyani rabbee liaqraba min h*atha* rashad*a***n**

## 18:25

Walabithoo fee kahfihim thal*a*tha miatin sineena wa**i**zd*a*doo tisAA*a***n**

## 18:26

Quli All*a*hu aAAlamu bim*a* labithoo lahu ghaybu a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i ab*s*ir bihi waasmiAA m*a* lahum min doonihi min waliyyin wal*a* yushriku fee *h*ukmihi a*h*ad*a***n**

## 18:27

Wa**o**tlu m*a* oo*h*iya ilayka min kit*a*bi rabbika l*a* mubaddila likalim*a*tihi walan tajida min doonihi multa*h*ad*a***n**

## 18:28

Wa**i***s*bir nafsaka maAAa alla*th*eena yadAAoona rabbahum bi**a**lghad*a*ti wa**a**lAAashiyyi yureedoona wajhahu wal*a* taAAdu AAayn*a*ka AAanhum tureedu zeenata al*h*ay*a*ti a**l**dduny*a* wal*a* tu*t*iAA man aghfaln*a* qalbahu AAan *th*ikrin*a* wa**i**ttabaAAa haw*a*hu wak*a*na amruhu furu*ta***n**

## 18:29

Waquli al*h*aqqu min rabbikum faman sh*a*a falyumin waman sh*a*a falyakfur inn*a* aAAtadn*a* li**l****thth***a*limeena n*a*ran a*hat*a bihim sur*a*diquh*a* wain yastagheethoo yugh*a*thoo bim*a*in ka**a**lmuhli yashwee alwujooha bisa a**l**shshar*a*bu was*a*at murtafaq*a***n**

## 18:30

Inna alla*th*eena *a*manoo waAAamiloo a**l***ssa*li*ha*ti inn*a* l*a* nu*d*eeAAu ajra man a*h*sana AAamal*a***n**

## 18:31

Ol*a*ika lahum jann*a*tu AAadnin tajree min ta*h*tihimu alanh*a*ru yu*h*allawna feeh*a* min as*a*wira min *th*ahabin way**a**lbasoona thiy*a*ban khu*d*ran min sundusin waistabraqin muttakieena feeh*a* AAal*a* alar*a*iki niAAma a**l**ththaw*a*bu wa*h*asunat murtafaq*a***n**

## 18:32

Wa**i***d*rib lahum mathalan rajulayni jaAAaln*a* lia*h*adihim*a* jannatayni min aAAn*a*bin wa*h*afafn*a*hum*a* binakhlin wajaAAaln*a* baynahum*a* zarAA*a***n**

## 18:33

Kilt*a* aljannatayni *a*tat okulah*a* walam t&#x61;**th**&#x6C;im minhu shayan wafajjarn*a* khil*a*lahum*a* nahar*a***n**

## 18:34

Wak*a*na lahu thamarun faq*a*la li*sah*ibihi wahuwa yu*ha*wiruhu an*a* aktharu minka m*a*lan waaAAazzu nafar*a***n**

## 18:35

Wadakhala jannatahu wahuwa **th***a*limun linafsihi q*a*la m*a* &#x61;**th**&#x75;nnu an tabeeda h*ath*ihi abad*a***n**

## 18:36

Wam*a* &#x61;**th**&#x75;nnu a**l**ss*a*AAata q*a*imatan walain rudidtu il*a* rabbee laajidanna khayran minh*a* munqalab*a***n**

## 18:37

Q*a*la lahu *sah*ibuhu wahuwa yu*ha*wiruhu akafarta bi**a**lla*th*ee khalaqaka min tur*a*bin thumma min nu*t*fatin thumma saww*a*ka rajul*a***n**

## 18:38

L*a*kinna huwa All*a*hu rabbee wal*a* oshriku birabbee a*h*ad*a***n**

## 18:39

Walawl*a* i*th* dakhalta jannataka qulta m*a* sh*a*a All*a*hu l*a* quwwata ill*a* bi**A**ll*a*hi in tarani an*a* aqalla minka m*a*lan wawalad*a***n**

## 18:40

FaAAas*a* rabbee an yutiyani khayran min jannatika wayursila AAalayh*a* *h*usb*a*nan mina a**l**ssam*a*i fatu*s*bi*h*a *s*aAAeedan zalaq*a***n**

## 18:41

Aw yu*s*bi*h*a m*a*oh*a* ghawran falan tasta*t*eeAAa lahu *t*alab*a***n**

## 18:42

Wao*h*ee*t*a bithamarihi faa*s*ba*h*a yuqallibu kaffayhi AAal*a* m*a* anfaqa feeh*a* wahiya kh*a*wiyatun AAal*a* AAurooshih*a* wayaqoolu y*a* laytanee lam oshrik birabbee a*h*ad*a***n**

## 18:43

Walam takun lahu fiatun yan*s*uroonahu min dooni All*a*hi wam*a* k*a*na munta*s*ir*a***n**

## 18:44

Hun*a*lika alwal*a*yatu lill*a*hi al*h*aqqi huwa khayrun thaw*a*ban wakhayrun AAuqb*a***n**

## 18:45

Wa**i***d*rib lahum mathala al*h*ay*a*ti a**l**dduny*a* kam*a*in anzaln*a*hu mina a**l**ssam*a*i fa**i**khtala*t*a bihi nab*a*tu alar*d*i faa*s*ba*h*a hasheeman ta*th*roohu a**l**rriy*ah*u wak*a*na All*a*hu AAal*a* kulli shayin muqtadir*a***n**

## 18:46

Alm*a*lu wa**a**lbanoona zeenatu al*h*ay*a*ti a**l**dduny*a* wa**a**lb*a*qiy*a*tu a**l***ssa*li*ha*tu khayrun AAinda rabbika thaw*a*ban wakhayrun amal*a***n**

## 18:47

Wayawma nusayyiru aljib*a*la watar*a* alar*d*a b*a*rizatan wa*h*asharn*a*hum falam nugh*a*dir minhum a*h*ad*a***n**

## 18:48

WaAAuri*d*oo AAal*a* rabbika *s*affan laqad jitumoon*a* kam*a* khalaqn*a*kum awwala marratin bal zaAAamtum allan najAAala lakum mawAAid*a***n**

## 18:49

Wawu*d*iAAa alkit*a*bu fatar*a* almujrimeena mushfiqeena mimm*a* feehi wayaqooloona y*a* waylatan*a* m*a* lih*atha* alkit*a*bi l*a* yugh*a*diru *s*agheeratan wal*a* kabeeratan ill*a* a*hsa*h*a* wawajadoo m*a* AAamiloo *had*iran wal*a* y&#x61;**th**&#x6C;imu rabbuka a*h*ad*a***n**

## 18:50

Wai*th* quln*a* lilmal*a*ikati osjudoo li*a*dama fasajadoo ill*a* ibleesa k*a*na mina aljinni fafasaqa AAan amri rabbihi afatattakhi*th*oonahu wa*th*urriyyatahu awliy*a*a min doonee wahum lakum AAaduwwun bisa li**l****thth***a*limeena badal*a***n**

## 18:51

M*a* ashhadtuhum khalqa a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i wal*a* khalqa anfusihim wam*a* kuntu muttakhi*th*a almu*d*illeena AAa*d*ud*a***n**

## 18:52

Wayawma yaqoolu n*a*doo shurak*a*iya alla*th*eena zaAAamtum fadaAAawhum falam yastajeeboo lahum wajaAAaln*a* baynahum mawbiq*a***n**

## 18:53

Wara*a* almujrimoona a**l**nn*a*ra f&#x61;**th**&#x61;nnoo annahum muw*a*qiAAooh*a* walam yajidoo AAanh*a* ma*s*rif*a***n**

## 18:54

Walaqad *s*arrafn*a* fee h*atha* alqur*a*ni li**l**nn*a*si min kulli mathalin wak*a*na alins*a*nu akthara shayin jadal*a***n**

## 18:55

Wam*a* manaAAa a**l**nn*a*sa an yuminoo i*th* j*a*ahumu alhud*a* wayastaghfiroo rabbahum ill*a* an tatiyahum sunnatu alawwaleena aw yatiyahumu alAAa*tha*bu qubul*a***n**

## 18:56

Wam*a* nursilu almursaleena ill*a* mubashshireena wamun*th*ireena wayuj*a*dilu alla*th*eena kafaroo bi**a**lb*at*ili liyud*h*i*d*oo bihi al*h*aqqa wa**i**ttakha*th*oo *a*y*a*tee wam*a* on*th*iroo huzuw*a***n**

## 18:57

Waman &#x61;**th**&#x6C;amu mimman *th*ukkira bi*a*y*a*ti rabbihi faaAAra*d*a AAanh*a* wanasiya m*a* qaddamat yad*a*hu inn*a* jaAAaln*a* AAal*a* quloobihim akinnatan an yafqahoohu wafee *atha*nihim waqran wain tadAAuhum il*a* alhud*a* falan yahtadoo i*th*an abad*a***n**

## 18:58

Warabbuka alghafooru *th*oo a**l**rra*h*mati law yu*a*khi*th*uhum bim*a* kasaboo laAAajjala lahumu alAAa*tha*ba bal lahum mawAAidun lan yajidoo min doonihi mawil*a***n**

## 18:59

Watilka alqur*a* ahlakn*a*hum lamm*a* **th**&#x61;lamoo wajaAAaln*a* limahlikihim mawAAid*a***n**

## 18:60

Wai*th* q*a*la moos*a* lifat*a*hu l*a* abra*h*u *h*att*a* ablugha majmaAAa alba*h*rayni aw am*d*iya *h*uqub*a***n**

## 18:61

Falamm*a* balagh*a* majmaAAa baynihim*a* nasiy*a* *h*ootahum*a* fa**i**ttakha*th*a sabeelahu fee alba*h*ri sarab*a***n**

## 18:62

Falamm*a* j*a*waz*a* q*a*la lifat*a*hu *a*tin*a* ghad*a*an*a* laqad laqeen*a* min safarin*a* h*atha* na*s*ab*a***n**

## 18:63

Q*a*la araayta i*th* awayn*a* il*a* a**l***ss*akhrati fainnee naseetu al*h*oota wam*a* ans*a*neehu ill*a* a**l**shshay*ta*nu an a*th*kurahu wa**i**ttakha*th*a sabeelahu fee alba*h*ri AAajab*a***n**

## 18:64

Q*a*la *tha*lika m*a* kunn*a* nabghi fa**i**rtadd*a* AAal*a* *a*th*a*rihim*a* qa*s*a*sa***n**

## 18:65

Fawajad*a* AAabdan min AAib*a*din*a* *a*tayn*a*hu ra*h*matan min AAindin*a* waAAallamn*a*hu min ladunn*a* AAilm*a***n**

## 18:66

Q*a*la lahu moos*a* hal attabiAAuka AAal*a* an tuAAallimani mimm*a* AAullimta rushd*a***n**

## 18:67

Q*a*la innaka lan tasta*t*eeAAa maAAiya *s*abr*a***n**

## 18:68

Wakayfa ta*s*biru AAal*a* m*a* lam tu*h*i*t* bihi khubr*a***n**

## 18:69

Q*a*la satajidunee in sh*a*a All*a*hu *sa*biran wal*a* aAA*s*ee laka amr*a***n**

## 18:70

Q*a*la faini ittabaAAtanee fal*a* tasalnee AAan shayin *h*att*a* o*h*ditha laka minhu *th*ikr*a***n**

## 18:71

Fa**i**n*t*alaq*a* *h*att*a* i*tha* rakib*a* fee a**l**ssafeenati kharaqah*a* q*a*la akharaqtah*a* litughriqa ahlah*a* laqad jita shayan imr*a***n**

## 18:72

Q*a*la alam aqul innaka lan tasta*t*eeAAa maAAiya *s*abr*a***n**

## 18:73

Q*a*la l*a* tu*a*khi*th*nee bim*a* naseetu wal*a* turhiqnee min amree AAusr*a***n**

## 18:74

Fa**i**n*t*alaq*a* *h*att*a* i*tha* laqiy*a* ghul*a*man faqatalahu q*a*la aqatalta nafsan zakiyyatan bighayri nafsin laqad jita shayan nukr*a***n**

## 18:75

Q*a*la alam aqul laka innaka lan tasta*t*eeAAa maAAiya *s*abr*a***n**

## 18:76

Q*a*la in saaltuka AAan shayin baAAdah*a* fal*a* tu*sah*ibnee qad balaghta min ladunnee AAu*th*r*a***n**

## 18:77

Fa**i**n*t*alaq*a* *h*att*a* i*tha* atay*a* ahla qaryatin ista*t*AAam*a* ahlah*a* faabaw an yu*d*ayyifoohum*a* fawajad*a* feeh*a* jid*a*ran yureedu an yanqa*dd*a faaq*a*mahu q*a*la law shita la**i**ttakha*th*ta AAalayhi ajr*a***n**

## 18:78
