Q*a*la h*atha* fir*a*qu baynee wabaynika saonabbioka bitaweeli m*a* lam tasta*t*iAA AAalayhi *s*abr*a***n**

## 18:79

Amm*a* a**l**ssafeenatu fak*a*nat limas*a*keena yaAAmaloona fee alba*h*ri faaradtu an aAAeebah*a* wak*a*na war*a*ahum malikun yakhu*th*u kulla safeenatin gha*s*b*a***n**

## 18:80

Waamm*a* alghul*a*mu fak*a*na abaw*a*hu muminayni fakhasheen*a* an yurhiqahum*a* *t*ughy*a*nan wakufr*a***n**

## 18:81

Faaradn*a* an yubdilahum*a* rabbuhum*a* khayran minhu zak*a*tan waaqraba ru*h*m*a***n**

## 18:82

Waamm*a* aljid*a*ru fak*a*na lighul*a*mayni yateemayni fee almadeenati wak*a*na ta*h*tahu kanzun lahum*a* wak*a*na aboohum*a* *sa*li*h*an faar*a*da rabbuka an yablugh*a* ashuddahum*a* wayastakhrij*a* kanzahum*a* ra*h*matan min rabbika wam*a* faAAaltuhu AAan amree *tha*lika taweelu m*a* lam tas*t*iAA AAalayhi *s*abr*a***n**

## 18:83

Wayasaloonaka AAan *th*ee alqarnayni qul saatloo AAalaykum minhu *th*ikr*a***n**

## 18:84

Inn*a* makkann*a* lahu fee alar*d*i wa*a*tayn*a*hu min kulli shayin sabab*a***n**

## 18:85

FaatbaAAa sabab*a***n**

## 18:86

*H*att*a* i*tha* balagha maghriba a**l**shshamsi wajadah*a* taghrubu fee AAaynin *h*amiatin wawajada AAindah*a* qawman quln*a* y*a* *tha* alqarnayni imm*a* an tuAAa*thth*iba waimm*a* an tattakhi*th*a feehim *h*usn*a***n**

## 18:87

Q*a*la amm*a* man **th**&#x61;lama fasawfa nuAAa*thth*ibuhu thumma yuraddu il*a* rabbihi fayuAAa*thth*ibuhu AAa*tha*ban nukr*a***n**

## 18:88

Waamm*a* man *a*mana waAAamila *sa*li*h*an falahu jaz*a*an al*h*usn*a* wasanaqoolu lahu min amrin*a* yusr*a***n**

## 18:89

Thumma atbaAAa sabab*a***n**

## 18:90

*H*att*a* i*tha* balagha ma*t*liAAa a**l**shshamsi wajadah*a* ta*t*luAAu AAal*a* qawmin lam najAAal lahum min doonih*a* sitr*a***n**

## 18:91

Ka*tha*lika waqad a*h*a*t*n*a* bim*a* ladayhi khubr*a***n**

## 18:92

Thumma atbaAAa sabab*a***n**

## 18:93

*H*att*a* i*tha* balagha bayna a**l**ssaddayni wajada min doonihim*a* qawman l*a* yak*a*doona yafqahoona qawl*a***n**

## 18:94

Q*a*loo y*a* *tha* alqarnayni inna yajooja wamajooja mufsidoona fee alar*d*i fahal najAAalu laka kharjan AAal*a* an tajAAala baynan*a* wabaynahum sadd*a***n**

## 18:95

Q*a*la m*a* makkannee feehi rabbee khayrun faaAAeenoonee biquwwatin ajAAal baynakum wabaynahum radm*a***n**

## 18:96

*A*toonee zubara al*h*adeedi *h*att*a* i*tha* s*a*w*a* bayna a**l***s*adafayni q*a*la onfukhoo *h*att*a* i*tha* jaAAalahu n*a*ran q*a*la *a*toonee ofrigh AAalayhi qi*t*r*a***n**

## 18:97

Fam*a* is*ta*AAoo an y&#x61;**th**&#x68;aroohu wam*a* ista*ta*AAoo lahu naqb*a***n**

## 18:98

Q*a*la h*atha* ra*h*matun min rabbee fai*tha* j*a*a waAAdu rabbee jaAAalahu dakk*a*a wak*a*na waAAdu rabbee *h*aqq*a***n**

## 18:99

Watarakn*a* baAA*d*ahum yawmai*th*in yamooju fee baAA*d*in wanufikha fee a**l***ss*oori fajamaAAn*a*hum jamAA*a***n**

## 18:100

WaAAara*d*n*a* jahannama yawmai*th*in lilk*a*fireena AAar*da***n**

## 18:101

Alla*th*eena k*a*nat aAAyunuhum fee ghi*ta*in AAan *th*ikree wak*a*noo l*a* yasta*t*eeAAoona samAA*a***n**

## 18:102

Afa*h*asiba alla*th*eena kafaroo an yattakhi*th*oo AAib*a*dee min doonee awliy*a*a inn*a* aAAtadn*a* jahannama lilk*a*fireena nuzul*a***n**

## 18:103

Qul hal nunabbiokum bi**a**lakhsareena aAAm*a*l*a***n**

## 18:104

Alla*th*eena *d*alla saAAyuhum fee al*h*ay*a*ti a**l**dduny*a* wahum ya*h*saboona annahum yu*h*sinoona *s*unAA*a***n**

## 18:105

Ol*a*ika alla*th*eena kafaroo bi*a*y*a*ti rabbihim waliq*a*ihi fa*h*abi*t*at aAAm*a*luhum fal*a* nuqeemu lahum yawma alqiy*a*mati wazn*a***n**

## 18:106

*Tha*lika jaz*a*ohum jahannamu bim*a* kafaroo wa**i**ttakha*th*oo *a*y*a*tee warusulee huzuw*a***n**

## 18:107

Inna alla*th*eena *a*manoo waAAamiloo a**l***ssa*li*ha*ti k*a*nat lahum jann*a*tu alfirdawsi nuzul*a***n**

## 18:108

Kh*a*lideena feeh*a* l*a* yabghoona AAanh*a* *h*iwal*a***n**

## 18:109

Qul law k*a*na alba*h*ru mid*a*dan likalim*a*ti rabbee lanafida alba*h*ru qabla an tanfada kalim*a*tu rabbee walaw jin*a* bimithlihi madad*a***n**

## 18:110

Qul innam*a* an*a* basharun mithlukum yoo*ha* ilayya annam*a* il*a*hukum il*a*hun w*ah*idun faman k*a*na yarjoo liq*a*a rabbihi falyaAAmal AAamalan *sa*li*h*an wal*a* yushrik biAAib*a*dati rabbihi a*h*ad*a***n**

## 19:1

K*a*fh*a*y*a*AAayn*sa*d

## 19:2

*Th*ikru ra*h*mati rabbika AAabdahu zakariyy*a*

## 19:3

I*th* n*a*d*a* rabbahu nid*a*an khafiyy*a***n**

## 19:4

Q*a*la rabbi innee wahana alAA&#x61;**th**&#x6D;u minnee wa**i**shtaAAala a**l**rrasu shayban walam akun biduAA*a*ika rabbi shaqiyy*a***n**

## 19:5

Wainnee khiftu almaw*a*liya min war*a*ee wak*a*nati imraatee AA*a*qiran fahab lee min ladunka waliyy*a***n**

## 19:6

Yarithunee wayarithu min *a*li yaAAqooba wa**i**jAAalhu rabbi ra*d*iyy*a***n**

## 19:7

Y*a* zakariyy*a* inn*a* nubashshiruka bighul*a*min ismuhu ya*h*y*a* lam najAAal lahu min qablu samiyy*a***n**

## 19:8

Q*a*la rabbi ann*a* yakoonu lee ghul*a*mun wak*a*nati imraatee AA*a*qiran waqad balaghtu mina alkibari AAitiyy*a***n**

## 19:9

Q*a*la ka*tha*lika q*a*la rabbuka huwa AAalayya hayyinun waqad khalaqtuka min qablu walam taku shay*a***n**

## 19:10

Q*a*la rabbi ijAAal lee *a*yatan q*a*la *a*yatuka all*a* tukallima a**l**nn*a*sa thal*a*tha lay*a*lin sawiyy*a***n**

## 19:11

Fakharaja AAal*a* qawmihi mina almi*h*r*a*bi faaw*ha* ilayhim an sabbi*h*oo bukratan waAAashiyy*a***n**

## 19:12

Y*a* ya*h*y*a* khu*th*i alkit*a*ba biquwwatin wa*a*tayn*a*hu al*h*ukma *s*abiyy*a***n**

## 19:13

Wa*h*an*a*nan min ladunn*a* wazak*a*tan wak*a*na taqiyy*a***n**

## 19:14

Wabarran biw*a*lidayhi walam yakun jabb*a*ran AAa*s*iyy*a***n**

## 19:15

Wasal*a*mun AAalayhi yawma wulida wayawma yamootu wayawma yubAAathu *h*ayy*a***n**

## 19:16

Wa**o***th*kur fee alkit*a*bi maryama i*th*i intaba*th*at min ahlih*a* mak*a*nan sharqiyy*a***n**

## 19:17

Fa**i**ttakha*th*at min doonihim *h*ij*a*ban faarsaln*a* ilayh*a* roo*h*an*a* fatamaththala lah*a* basharan sawiyy*a***n**

## 19:18

Q*a*lat innee aAAoo*th*u bi**al**rra*h*m*a*ni minka in kunta taqiyy*a***n**

## 19:19

Q*a*la innam*a* an*a* rasoolu rabbiki liahaba laki ghul*a*man zakiyy*a***n**

## 19:20

Q*a*lat ann*a* yakoonu lee ghul*a*mun walam yamsasnee basharun walam aku baghiyy*a***n**

## 19:21

Q*a*la ka*tha*liki q*a*la rabbuki huwa AAalayya hayyinun walinajAAalahu *a*yatan li**l**nn*a*si wara*h*matan minn*a* wak*a*na amran maq*d*iyy*a***n**

## 19:22

Fa*h*amalathu fa**i**ntaba*th*at bihi mak*a*nan qa*s*iyy*a***n**

## 19:23

Faaj*a*ah*a* almakh*ad*u il*a* ji*th*AAi a**l**nnakhlati q*a*lat y*a* laytanee mittu qabla h*atha* wakuntu nasyan mansiyy*a***n**

## 19:24

Fan*a*d*a*h*a* min ta*h*tih*a* all*a* ta*h*zanee qad jaAAala rabbuki ta*h*taki sariyy*a***n**

## 19:25

Wahuzzee ilayki biji*th*AAi a**l**nnakhlati tus*a*qi*t* AAalayki ru*t*aban janiyy*a***n**

## 19:26

Fakulee wa**i**shrabee waqarree AAaynan faimm*a* tarayinna mina albashari a*h*adan faqoolee innee na*th*artu li**l**rra*h*m*a*ni *s*awman falan okallima alyawma insiyy*a***n**

## 19:27

Faatat bihi qawmah*a* ta*h*miluhu q*a*loo y*a* maryamu laqad jiti shayan fariyy*a***n**

## 19:28

Y*a* okhta h*a*roona m*a* k*a*na abooki imraa sawin wam*a* k*a*nat ommuki baghiyy*a***n**

## 19:29

Faash*a*rat ilayhi q*a*loo kayfa nukallimu man k*a*na fee almahdi *s*abiyy*a***n**

## 19:30

Q*a*la innee AAabdu All*a*hi *a*t*a*niya alkit*a*ba wajaAAalanee nabiyy*a***n**

## 19:31

WajaAAalanee mub*a*rakan ayna m*a* kuntu waaw*sa*nee bi**al***ss*al*a*ti wa**al**zzak*a*ti m*a* dumtu *h*ayy*a***n**

## 19:32

Wabarran biw*a*lidatee walam yajAAalnee jabb*a*ran shaqiyy*a***n**

## 19:33

Wa**al**ssal*a*mu AAalayya yawma wulidtu wayawma amootu wayawma obAAathu *h*ayy*a***n**

## 19:34

*Tha*lika AAees*a* ibnu maryama qawla al*h*aqqi alla*th*ee feehi yamtaroon**a**

## 19:35

M*a* k*a*na lill*a*hi an yattakhi*th*a min waladin sub*ha*nahu i*tha* qa*da* amran fainnam*a* yaqoolu lahu kun fayakoon**u**

## 19:36

Wainna All*a*ha rabbee warabbukum fa**o**AAbudoohu h*atha* *s*ir*at*un mustaqeem**un**

## 19:37

Fa**i**khtalafa ala*h*z*a*bu min baynihim fawaylun lilla*th*eena kafaroo min mashhadi yawmin AA&#x61;**th**&#x65;em**in**

## 19:38

AsmiAA bihim waab*s*ir yawma yatoonan*a* l*a*kini a**l****thth***a*limoona alyawma fee *d*al*a*lin mubeen**in**

## 19:39

Waan*th*irhum yawma al*h*asrati i*th* qu*d*iya alamru wahum fee ghaflatin wahum l*a* yuminoon**a**

## 19:40

Inn*a* na*h*nu narithu alar*d*a waman AAalayh*a* wailayn*a* yurjaAAoon**a**

## 19:41

Wa**o***th*kur fee alkit*a*bi ibr*a*heema innahu k*a*na *s*iddeeqan nabiyy*a***n**

## 19:42

I*th* q*a*la liabeehi y*a* abati lima taAAbudu m*a* l*a* yasmaAAu wal*a* yub*s*iru wal*a* yughnee AAanka shay*a***n**

## 19:43

Y*a* abati innee qad j*a*anee mina alAAilmi m*a* lam yatika fa**i**ttabiAAnee ahdika *s*ir*at*an sawiyy*a***n**

## 19:44

Y*a* abati l*a* taAAbudi a**l**shshay*ta*na inna a**l**shshay*ta*na k*a*na li**l**rra*h*m*a*ni AAa*s*iyy*a***n**

## 19:45

Y*a* abati innee akh*a*fu an yamassaka AAa*tha*bun mina a**l**rra*h*m*a*ni fatakoona li**l**shshya*ta*ni waliyy*a***n**

## 19:46

Q*a*la ar*a*ghibun anta AAan *a*lihatee y*a* ibr*a*heemu lain lam tantahi laarjumannaka wa**o**hjurnee maliyy*a***n**

## 19:47

Q*a*la sal*a*mun AAalayka saastaghfiru laka rabbee innahu k*a*na bee *h*afiyy*a***n**

## 19:48

WaaAAtazilukum wam*a* tadAAoona min dooni All*a*hi waadAAoo rabbee AAas*a* all*a* akoona biduAA*a*i rabbee shaqiyy*a***n**

## 19:49

Falamm*a* iAAtazalahum wam*a* yaAAbudoona min dooni All*a*hi wahabn*a* lahu is*ha*qa wayaAAqooba wakullan jaAAaln*a* nabiyy*a***n**

## 19:50

Wawahabn*a* lahum min ra*h*matin*a* wajaAAaln*a* lahum lis*a*na *s*idqin AAaliyy*a***n**

## 19:51

Wa**o***th*kur fee alkit*a*bi moos*a* innahu k*a*na mukhla*s*an wak*a*na rasoolan nabiyy*a***n**

## 19:52

Wan*a*dayn*a*hu min j*a*nibi a**l***tt*oori alaymani waqarrabn*a*hu najiyy*a***n**

## 19:53

Wawahabn*a* lahu min ra*h*matin*a* akh*a*hu h*a*roona nabiyy*a***n**

## 19:54

Wa**o***th*kur fee alkit*a*bi ism*a*AAeela innahu k*a*na *sa*diqa alwaAAdi wak*a*na rasoolan nabiyy*a***n**

## 19:55

Wak*a*na yamuru ahlahu bi**al***ss*al*a*ti wa**al**zzak*a*ti wak*a*na AAinda rabbihi mar*d*iyy*a***n**

## 19:56

Wa**o***th*kur fee alkit*a*bi idreesa innahu k*a*na *s*iddeeqan nabiyy*a***n**

## 19:57

WarafaAAn*a*hu mak*a*nan AAaliyy*a***n**

## 19:58

Ol*a*ika alla*th*eena anAAama All*a*hu AAalayhim mina a**l**nnabiyyeena min *th*urriyyati *a*dama wamimman *h*amaln*a* maAAa noo*h*in wamin *th*urriyyati ibr*a*heema waisr*a*eela wamimman hadayn*a* wa**i**jtabayn*a* i*tha* tutl*a* AAalayhim *a*y*a*tu a**l**rra*h*m*a*ni kharroo sujjadan wabukiyy*a***n**

## 19:59

Fakhalafa min baAAdihim khalfun a*da*AAoo a**l***ss*al*a*ta wa**i**ttabaAAoo a**l**shshahaw*a*ti fasawfa yalqawna ghayy*a***n**

## 19:60

Ill*a* man t*a*ba wa*a*mana waAAamila *sa*li*h*an faol*a*ika yadkhuloona aljannata wal*a* y&#x75;**th**&#x6C;amoona shay*a***n**

## 19:61

Jann*a*ti AAadnin allatee waAAada a**l**rra*h*m*a*nu AAib*a*dahu bi**al**ghaybi innahu k*a*na waAAduhu matiyy*a***n**

## 19:62

L*a* yasmaAAoona feeh*a* laghwan ill*a* sal*a*man walahum rizquhum feeh*a* bukratan waAAashiyy*a***n**

## 19:63

Tilka aljannatu allatee noorithu min AAib*a*din*a* man k*a*na taqiyy*a***n**

## 19:64

Wam*a* natanazzalu ill*a* biamri rabbika lahu m*a* bayna aydeen*a* wam*a&#x20;*&#x6B;halfan*a* wam*a* bayna *tha*lika wam*a* k*a*na rabbuka nasiyy*a***n**

## 19:65

Rabbu a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i wam*a* baynahum*a* fa**o**AAbudhu wa**i***st*abir liAAib*a*datihi hal taAAlamu lahu samiyy*a***n**

## 19:66

Wayaqoolu alins*a*nu ai*tha* m*a* mittu lasawfa okhraju *h*ayy*a***n**

## 19:67

Awal*a* ya*th*kuru alins*a*nu ann*a* khalaqn*a*hu min qablu walam yaku shay*a***n**

## 19:68

Fawarabbika lana*h*shurannahum wa**al**shshay*at*eena thumma lanu*hd*irannahum *h*awla jahannama jithiyy*a***n**

## 19:69

Thumma lananziAAanna min kulli sheeAAatin ayyuhum ashaddu AAal*a* a**l**rra*h*m*a*ni AAitiyy*a***n**

## 19:70

Thumma lana*h*nu aAAlamu bi**a**lla*th*eena hum awl*a* bih*a* *s*iliyy*a***n**

## 19:71

Wain minkum ill*a* w*a*riduh*a* k*a*na AAal*a* rabbika *h*atman maq*d*iyy*a***n**

## 19:72

Thumma nunajjee alla*th*eena ittaqaw wana*th*aru a**l****thth***a*limeena feeh*a* jithiyy*a***n**

## 19:73

Wai*tha* tutl*a* AAalayhim *a*y*a*tun*a* bayyin*a*tin q*a*la alla*th*eena kafaroo lilla*th*eena *a*manoo ayyu alfareeqayni khayrun maq*a*man waa*h*sanu nadiyy*a***n**

## 19:74

Wakam ahlakn*a* qablahum min qarnin hum a*h*sanu ath*a*than wariy*a***n**

## 19:75

Qul man k*a*na fee a**l***dd*al*a*lati falyamdud lahu a**l**rra*h*m*a*nu maddan *h*att*a* i*tha* raaw m*a* yooAAadoona imm*a* alAAa*tha*ba waimm*a* a**l**ss*a*AAata fasayaAAlamoona man huwa sharrun mak*a*nan waa*d*AAafu jund*a***n**

## 19:76

Wayazeedu All*a*hu alla*th*eena ihtadaw hudan wa**a**lb*a*qiy*a*tu a**l***ssa*li*ha*tu khayrun AAinda rabbika thaw*a*ban wakhayrun maradd*a***n**

## 19:77

Afaraayta alla*th*ee kafara bi*a*y*a*tin*a* waq*a*la laootayanna m*a*lan wawalad*a***n**

## 19:78

A*tt*alaAAa alghayba ami ittakha*th*a AAinda a**l**rra*h*m*a*ni AAahd*a***n**

## 19:79

Kall*a* sanaktubu m*a* yaqoolu wanamuddu lahu mina alAAa*tha*bi madd*a***n**

## 19:80

Wanarithuhu m*a* yaqoolu wayateen*a* fard*a***n**

## 19:81

Wa**i**ttakha*th*oo min dooni All*a*hi *a*lihatan liyakoonoo lahum AAizz*a***n**

## 19:82

Kall*a* sayakfuroona biAAib*a*datihim wayakoonoona AAalayhim *d*idd*a***n**

## 19:83

Alam tara ann*a* arsaln*a* a**l**shshay*at*eena AAal*a* alk*a*fireena taozzuhum azz*a***n**

## 19:84

Fal*a* taAAjal AAalayhim innam*a* naAAuddu lahum AAadd*a***n**

## 19:85

Yawma na*h*shuru almuttaqeena il*a* a**l**rra*h*m*a*ni wafd*a***n**

## 19:86

Wanasooqu almujrimeena il*a* jahannama wird*a***n**

## 19:87

L*a* yamlikoona a**l**shshaf*a*AAata ill*a* mani ittakha*th*a AAinda a**l**rra*h*m*a*ni AAahd*a***n**

## 19:88

Waq*a*loo ittakha*th*a a**l**rra*h*m*a*nu walad*a***n**

## 19:89

Laqad jitum shayan idd*a***n**

## 19:90

Tak*a*du a**l**ssam*a*w*a*tu yatafa*tt*arna minhu watanshaqqu alar*d*u watakhirru aljib*a*lu hadd*a***n**

## 19:91

An daAAaw li**l**rra*h*m*a*ni walad*a***n**

## 19:92

Wam*a* yanbaghee li**l**rra*h*m*a*ni an yattakhi*th*a walad*a***n**

## 19:93

In kullu man fee a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i ill*a* *a*tee a**l**rra*h*m*a*ni AAabd*a***n**

## 19:94

Laqad a*hsa*hum waAAaddahum AAadd*a***n**

## 19:95

Wakulluhum *a*teehi yawma alqiy*a*mati fard*a***n**

## 19:96

Inna alla*th*eena *a*manoo waAAamiloo a**l***ssa*li*ha*ti sayajAAalu lahumu a**l**rra*h*m*a*nu wudd*a***n**

## 19:97

Fainnam*a* yassarn*a*hu bilis*a*nika litubashshira bihi almuttaqeena watun*th*ira bihi qawman ludd*a***n**

## 19:98

Wakam ahlakn*a* qablahum min qarnin hal tu*h*issu minhum min a*h*adin aw tasmaAAu lahum rikz*a***n**

## 20:1

*Ta*h*a*

## 20:2

M*a* anzaln*a* AAalayka alqur*a*na litashq*a*

## 20:3

Ill*a* ta*th*kiratan liman yakhsh*a*

## 20:4

Tanzeelan mimman khalaqa alar*d*a wa**al**ssam*a*w*a*ti alAAul*a*

## 20:5

A**l**rra*h*m*a*nu AAal*a* alAAarshi istaw*a*

## 20:6

Lahu m*a* fee a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wam*a* fee alar*d*i wam*a* baynahum*a* wam*a* ta*h*ta a**l**ththar*a*

## 20:7

Wain tajhar bi**a**lqawli fainnahu yaAAlamu a**l**ssirra waakhf*a*

## 20:8

All*a*hu l*a* il*a*ha ill*a* huwa lahu alasm*a*o al*h*usn*a*

## 20:9

## 20:10

I*th* ra*a* n*a*ran faq*a*la liahlihi omkuthoo innee *a*nastu n*a*ran laAAallee *a*teekum minh*a* biqabasin aw ajidu AAal*a* a**l**nn*a*ri hud*a***n**

## 20:11

Falamm*a* at*a*h*a* noodiya y*a* moos*a*

## 20:12

Innee an*a* rabbuka fa**i**khlaAA naAAlayka innaka bi**a**lw*a*di almuqaddasi *t*uw*a***n**

## 20:13

## 20:14

## 20:15

Inna a**l**ss*a*AAata *a*tiyatun ak*a*du okhfeeh*a* litujz*a* kullu nafsin bim*a* tasAA*a*

## 20:16

Fal*a* ya*s*uddannaka AAanh*a* man l*a* yuminu bih*a* wa**i**ttabaAAa haw*a*hu fatard*a*

## 20:17

Wam*a* tilka biyameenika y*a* moos*a*

## 20:18

Q*a*la hiya AAa*sa*ya atawakkao AAalayh*a* waahushshu bih*a* AAal*a* ghanamee waliya feeh*a* ma*a*ribu okhr*a*

## 20:19

Q*a*la alqih*a* y*a* moos*a*

## 20:20

Faalq*a*h*a* fai*tha* hiya *h*ayyatun tasAA*a*

## 20:21

Q*a*la khu*th*h*a* wal*a* takhaf sanuAAeeduh*a* seeratah*a* alool*a*

## 20:22

## 20:23

Linuriyaka min *a*y*a*tin*a* alkubr*a*

## 20:24

I*th*hab il*a* firAAawna innahu *t*agh*a*

## 20:25

Q*a*la rabbi ishra*h* lee *s*adree

## 20:26

## 20:27

## 20:28

Yafqahoo qawlee

## 20:29

## 20:30

H*a*roona akhee

## 20:31
