## 20:32

Waashrikhu fee amree

## 20:33

Kay nusabbi*h*aka katheer*a***n**

## 20:34

Wana*th*kuraka katheer*a***n**

## 20:35

Innaka kunta bin*a* ba*s*eer*a***n**

## 20:36

Q*a*la qad ooteeta sulaka y*a* moos*a*

## 20:37

Walaqad manann*a* AAalayka marratan okhr*a*

## 20:38

I*th* aw*h*ayn*a* il*a* ommika m*a* yoo*ha*

## 20:39

Ani iq*th*ifeehi fee a**l**tt*a*booti fa**i**q*th*ifeehi fee alyammi falyulqihi alyammu bi**al**ss*ah*ili yakhu*th*hu AAaduwwun lee waAAaduwwun lahu waalqaytu AAalayka ma*h*abbatan minnee walitu*s*naAAa AAal*a* AAaynee

## 20:40

I*th* tamshee okhtuka fataqoolu hal adullukum AAal*a* man yakfuluhu farajaAAn*a*ka il*a* ommika kay taqarra AAaynuh*a* wal*a* ta*h*zana waqatalta nafsan fanajjayn*a*ka mina alghammi wafatann*a*ka futoonan falabithta sineena fee ahli madyana thumma jita AAal*a* qadarin y*a* moos*a*

## 20:41

Wa**i***st*anaAAtuka linafsee

## 20:42

I*th*hab anta waakhooka bi*a*y*a*tee wal*a* taniy*a* fee *th*ikree

## 20:43

I*th*hab*a* il*a* firAAawna innahu *t*agh*a*

## 20:44

Faqool*a* lahu qawlan layyinan laAAallahu yata*th*akkaru aw yakhsh*a*

## 20:45

Q*a*l*a* rabban*a* innan*a* nakh*a*fu an yafru*t*a AAalayn*a* aw an ya*t*gh*a*

## 20:46

Q*a*la l*a* takh*a*f*a* innanee maAAakum*a* asmaAAu waar*a*

## 20:47

Fatiy*a*hu faqool*a* inn*a* rasool*a* rabbika faarsil maAAan*a* banee isr*a*eela wal*a* tuAAa*thth*ibhum qad jin*a*ka bi*a*yatin min rabbika wa**al**ssal*a*mu AAal*a* mani ittabaAAa alhud*a*

## 20:48

Inn*a* qad oo*h*iya ilayn*a* anna alAAa*tha*ba AAal*a* man ka*thth*aba watawall*a*

## 20:49

Q*a*la faman rabbukum*a* y*a* moos*a*

## 20:50

Q*a*la rabbun*a* alla*th*ee aAA*ta* kulla shayin khalqahu thumma had*a*

## 20:51

Q*a*la fam*a* b*a*lu alqurooni alool*a*

## 20:52

Q*a*la AAilmuh*a* AAinda rabbee fee kit*a*bin l*a* ya*d*illu rabbee wal*a* yans*a*

## 20:53

Alla*th*ee jaAAala lakumu alar*d*a mahdan wasalaka lakum feeh*a* subulan waanzala mina a**l**ssam*a*i m*a*an faakhrajn*a* bihi azw*a*jan min nab*a*tin shatt*a*

## 20:54

Kuloo wa**i**rAAaw anAA*a*makum inna fee *tha*lika la*a*y*a*tin liolee a**l**nnuh*a*

## 20:55

Minh*a* khalaqn*a*kum wafeeh*a* nuAAeedukum waminh*a* nukhrijukum t*a*ratan okhr*a*

## 20:56

Walaqad arayn*a*hu *a*y*a*tin*a* kullah*a* faka*thth*aba waab*a*

## 20:57

Q*a*la ajitan*a* litukhrijan*a* min ar*d*in*a* bisi*h*rika y*a* moos*a*

## 20:58

Falanatiyannaka bisi*h*rin mithlihi fa**i**jAAal baynan*a* wabaynaka mawAAidan l*a* nukhlifuhu na*h*nu wal*a* anta mak*a*nan suw*a***n**

## 20:59

Q*a*la mawAAidukum yawmu a**l**zzeenati waan yu*h*shara a**l**nn*a*su *d*u*ha***n**

## 20:60

Fatawall*a* firAAawnu fajamaAAa kaydahu thumma at*a*

## 20:61

Q*a*la lahum moos*a* waylakum l*a* taftaroo AAal*a* All*a*hi ka*th*iban fayus*h*itakum biAAa*tha*bin waqad kh*a*ba mani iftar*a*

## 20:62

Fatan*a*zaAAoo amrahum baynahum waasarroo a**l**nnajw*a*

## 20:63

Q*a*loo in h*atha*ni las*ah*ir*a*ni yureed*a*ni an yukhrij*a*kum min ar*d*ikum bisi*h*rihim*a* waya*th*hab*a* bi*t*areeqatikumu almuthl*a*

## 20:64

FaajmiAAoo kaydakum thumma itoo *s*affan waqad afla*h*a alyawma mani istaAAl*a*

## 20:65

Q*a*loo y*a* moos*a* imm*a* an tulqiya waimm*a* an nakoona awwala man alq*a*

## 20:66

Q*a*la bal alqoo fai*tha* *h*ib*a*luhum waAAi*s*iyyuhum yukhayyalu ilayhi min si*h*rihim annah*a* tasAA*a*

## 20:67

Faawjasa fee nafsihi kheefatan moos*a*

## 20:68

Quln*a* l*a* takhaf innaka anta alaAAl*a*

## 20:69

Waalqi m*a* fee yameenika talqaf m*a* *s*anaAAoo innam*a* *s*anaAAoo kaydu s*ah*irin wal*a* yufli*h*u a**l**ss*ah*iru *h*aythu at*a*

## 20:70

Faolqiya a**l**ssa*h*aratu sujjadan q*a*loo *a*mann*a* birabbi h*a*roona wamoos*a*

## 20:71

Q*a*la *a*mantum lahu qabla an *ath*ana lakum innahu lakabeerukumu alla*th*ee AAallamakumu a**l**ssi*h*ra falaoqa*tt*iAAanna aydiyakum waarjulakum min khil*a*fin walao*s*allibannakum fee ju*th*ooAAi a**l**nnakhli walataAAlamunna ayyun*a* ashaddu AAa*tha*ban waabq*a*

## 20:72

Q*a*loo lan nuthiraka AAal*a* m*a* j*a*an*a* mina albayyin*a*ti wa**a**lla*th*ee fa*t*aran*a* fa**i**q*d*i m*a* anta q*ad*in innam*a* taq*d*ee h*ath*ihi al*h*ay*a*ta a**l**dduny*a*

## 20:73

Inn*a* *a*mann*a* birabbin*a* liyaghfira lan*a* kha*ta*y*a*n*a* wam*a* akrahtan*a* AAalayhi mina a**l**ssi*h*ri wa**A**ll*a*hu khayrun waabq*a*

## 20:74

Innahu man yati rabbahu mujriman fainna lahu jahannama l*a* yamootu feeh*a* wal*a* ya*h*y*a*

## 20:75

Waman yatihi muminan qad AAamila a**l***ssa*li*ha*ti faol*a*ika lahumu a**l**ddaraj*a*tu alAAul*a*

## 20:76

Jann*a*tu AA*a*dnin tajree min ta*h*tih*a* alanh*a*ru kh*a*lideena feeh*a* wa*tha*lika jaz*a*o man tazakk*a*

## 20:77

Walaqad aw*h*ayn*a* il*a* moos*a* an asri biAAib*a*dee fa**i***d*rib lahum *t*areeqan fee alba*h*ri yabasan l*a* takh*a*fu darakan wal*a* takhsh*a*

## 20:78

FaatbaAAahum firAAawnu bijunoodihi faghashiyahum mina alyammi m*a* ghashiyahum

## 20:79

Waa*d*alla firAAawnu qawmahu wam*a* had*a*

## 20:80

Y*a* banee isr*a*eela qad anjayn*a*kum min AAaduwwikum waw*a*AAadn*a*kum j*a*niba a**l***tt*oori alaymana wanazzaln*a* AAalaykumu almanna wa**al**ssalw*a*

## 20:81

Kuloo min *t*ayyib*a*ti m*a* razaqn*a*kum wal*a* ta*t*ghaw feehi faya*h*illa AAalaykum gha*d*abee waman ya*h*lil AAalayhi gha*d*abee faqad haw*a*

## 20:82

Wainnee laghaff*a*run liman t*a*ba wa*a*mana waAAamila *sa*li*h*an thumma ihtad*a*

## 20:83

Wam*a* aAAjalaka AAan qawmika y*a* moos*a*

## 20:84

Q*a*la hum ol*a*i AAal*a* atharee waAAajiltu ilayka rabbi litar*da*

## 20:85

Q*a*la fainn*a* qad fatann*a* qawmaka min baAAdika waa*d*allahumu a**l**ss*a*miriy**yu**

## 20:86

FarajaAAa moos*a* il*a* qawmihi gha*d*b*a*na asifan q*a*la y*a* qawmi alam yaAAidkum rabbukum waAAdan *h*asanan afa*ta*la AAalaykumu alAAahdu am aradtum an ya*h*illa AAalaykum gha*d*abun min rabbikum faakhlaftum mawAAidee

## 20:87

Q*a*loo m*a* akhlafn*a* mawAAidaka bimalkin*a* wal*a*kinn*a* *h*ummiln*a* awz*a*ran min zeenati alqawmi faqa*th*afn*a*h*a* faka*tha*lika alq*a* a**l**ss*a*miriy**yu**

## 20:88

Faakhraja lahum AAijlan jasadan lahu khuw*a*run faq*a*loo h*atha* il*a*hukum wail*a*hu moos*a* fanasiy**a**

## 20:89

Afal*a* yarawna all*a* yarjiAAu ilayhim qawlan wal*a* yamliku lahum *d*arran wal*a* nafAA*a***n**

## 20:90

Walaqad q*a*la lahum h*a*roonu min qablu y*a* qawmi innam*a* futintum bihi wainna rabbakumu a**l**rra*h*m*a*nu fa**i**ttabiAAoonee waa*t*eeAAoo amree

## 20:91

Q*a*loo lan nabra*h*a AAalayhi AA*a*kifeena *h*att*a* yarjiAAa ilayn*a* moos*a*

## 20:92

Q*a*la y*a* h*a*roonu m*a* manaAAaka i*th* raaytahum *d*alloo

## 20:93

All*a* tattabiAAani afaAAa*s*ayta amree

## 20:94

Q*a*la ya bna omma l*a* takhu*th* bili*h*yatee wal*a* birasee innee khasheetu an taqoola farraqta bayna banee isr*a*eela walam tarqub qawlee

## 20:95

Q*a*la fam*a* kha*t*buka y*a* s*a*miriy**yu**

## 20:96

Q*a*la ba*s*urtu bim*a* lam yab*s*uroo bihi faqaba*d*tu qab*d*atan min athari a**l**rrasooli fanaba*th*tuh*a* waka*tha*lika sawwalat lee nafsee

## 20:97

Q*a*la fa**i***th*hab fainna laka fee al*h*ay*a*ti an taqoola l*a* mis*a*sa wainna laka mawAAidan lan tukhlafahu wa**o**&#x6E;**th**&#x75;r il*a* il*a*hika alla*th*ee **th**&#x61;lta AAalayhi AA*a*kifan lanu*h*arriqannahu thumma lanansifannahu fee alyammi nasf*a***n**

## 20:98

Innam*a* il*a*hukumu All*a*hu alla*th*ee l*a* il*a*ha ill*a* huwa wasiAAa kulla shayin AAilm*a***n**

## 20:99

Ka*tha*lika naqu*ss*u AAalayka min anb*a*i m*a* qad sabaqa waqad *a*tayn*a*ka min ladunn*a* thikra**n**

## 20:100

Man aAAra*d*a AAanhu fainnahu ya*h*milu yawma alqiy*a*mati wizr*a***n**

## 20:101

Kh*a*lideena feehi was*a*a lahum yawma alqiy*a*mati *h*iml*a***n**

## 20:102

Yawma yunfakhu fee a**l***ss*oori wana*h*shuru almujrimeena yawmai*th*in zurq*a***n**

## 20:103

Yatakh*a*fatoona baynahum in labithtum ill*a* AAashr*a***n**

## 20:104

Na*h*nu aAAlamu bim*a* yaqooloona i*th* yaqoolu amthaluhum *t*areeqatan in labithtum ill*a* yawm*a***n**

## 20:105

Wayasaloonaka AAani aljib*a*li faqul yansifuh*a* rabbee nasf*a***n**

## 20:106

Faya*th*aruh*a* q*a*AAan *s*af*s*af*a***n**

## 20:107

L*a* tar*a* feeh*a* AAiwajan wal*a* amt*a***n**

## 20:108

Yawmai*th*in yattabiAAoona a**l**dd*a*AAiya l*a* AAiwaja lahu wakhashaAAati ala*s*w*a*tu li**l**rra*h*m*a*ni fal*a* tasmaAAu ill*a* hams*a***n**

## 20:109

Yawmai*th*in l*a* tanfaAAu a**l**shshaf*a*AAatu ill*a* man a*th*ina lahu a**l**rra*h*m*a*nu wara*d*iya lahu qawl*a***n**

## 20:110

YaAAlamu m*a* bayna aydeehim wam*a* khalfahum wal*a* yu*h*ee*t*oona bihi AAilm*a***n**

## 20:111

WaAAanati alwujoohu lil*h*ayyi alqayyoomi waqad kh*a*ba man *h*amala **th**&#x75;lm*a***n**

## 20:112

Waman yaAAmal mina a**l***ssa*li*ha*ti wahuwa muminun fal*a* yakh*a*fu **th**&#x75;lman wal*a* ha*d*m*a***n**

## 20:113

Waka*tha*lika anzaln*a*hu qur*a*nan AAarabiyyan wa*s*arrafn*a* feehi mina alwaAAeedi laAAallahum yattaqoona aw yu*h*dithu lahum *th*ikr*a***n**

## 20:114

FataAA*a*l*a* All*a*hu almaliku al*h*aqqu wal*a* taAAjal bi**a**lqur*a*ni min qabli an yuq*da* ilayka wa*h*yuhu waqul rabbi zidnee AAilm*a***n**

## 20:115

Walaqad AAahidn*a* il*a* *a*dama min qablu fanasiya walam najid lahu AAazm*a***n**

## 20:116

Wai*th* quln*a* lilmal*a*ikati osjudoo li*a*dama fasajadoo ill*a* ibleesa ab*a*

## 20:117

Faquln*a* y*a* *a*damu inna h*atha* AAaduwwun laka walizawjika fal*a* yukhrijannakum*a* mina aljannati fatashq*a*

## 20:118

Inna laka all*a* tajooAAa feeh*a* wal*a* taAAr*a*

## 20:119

Waannaka l*a* t&#x61;**th**&#x6D;ao feeh*a* wal*a* ta*dha*

## 20:120

Fawaswasa ilayhi a**l**shshay*ta*nu q*a*la y*a* *a*damu hal adulluka AAal*a* shajarati alkhuldi wamulkin l*a* yabl*a*

## 20:121

Faakal*a* minh*a* fabadat lahum*a* saw*a*tuhum*a* wa*t*afiq*a* yakh*s*if*a*ni AAalayhim*a* min waraqi aljannati waAAa*sa* *a*damu rabbahu faghaw*a*

## 20:122

Thumma ijtab*a*hu rabbuhu fat*a*ba AAalayhi wahad*a*

## 20:123

Q*a*la ihbi*ta* minh*a* jameeAAan baAA*d*ukum libaAA*d*in AAaduwwun faimm*a* yatiyannakum minnee hudan famani ittabaAAa hud*a*ya fal*a* ya*d*illu wal*a* yashq*a*

## 20:124

Waman aAAra*d*a AAan *th*ikree fainna lahu maAAeeshatan *d*ank*a***n** wana*h*shuruhu yawma alqiy*a*mati aAAm*a***n**

## 20:125

Q*a*la rabbi lima *h*ashartanee aAAm*a* waqad kuntu ba*s*eer*a***n**

## 20:126

Q*a*la ka*tha*lika atatka *a*y*a*tun*a* fanaseetah*a* waka*tha*lika alyawma tuns*a*

## 20:127

Waka*tha*lika najzee man asrafa walam yumin bi*a*y*a*ti rabbihi walaAAa*tha*bu al*a*khirati ashaddu waabq*a*

## 20:128

Afalam yahdi lahum kam ahlakn*a* qablahum mina alqurooni yamshoona fee mas*a*kinihim inna fee *tha*lika la*a*y*a*tin liolee a**l**nnuh*a*

## 20:129

Walawl*a* kalimatun sabaqat min rabbika lak*a*na liz*a*man waajalun musamm*a***n**

## 20:130

Fa**i***s*bir AAal*a* m*a* yaqooloona wasabbi*h* bi*h*amdi rabbika qabla *t*ulooAAi a**l**shshamsi waqabla ghuroobih*a* wamin *a*n*a*i allayli fasabbi*h* waa*t*r*a*fa a**l**nnah*a*ri laAAallaka tar*da*

## 20:131

Wal*a* tamuddanna AAaynayka il*a* m*a* mattaAAn*a* bihi azw*a*jan minhum zahrata al*h*ay*a*ti a**l**dduny*a* linaftinahum feehi warizqu rabbika khayrun waabq*a*

## 20:132

Wamur ahlaka bi**al***ss*al*a*ti wa**i***st*abir AAalayh*a* l*a* nasaluka rizqan na*h*nu narzuquka wa**a**lAA*a*qibatu li**l**ttaqw*a*

## 20:133

Waq*a*loo lawl*a* yateen*a* bi*a*yatin min rabbihi awalam tatihim bayyinatu m*a* fee a**l***ss*u*h*ufi alool*a*

## 20:134

Walaw ann*a* ahlakn*a*hum biAAa*tha*bin min qablihi laq*a*loo rabban*a* lawl*a* arsalta ilayn*a* rasoolan fanattabiAAa *a*y*a*tika min qabli an na*th*illa wanakhz*a*

## 20:135

Qul kullun mutarabbi*s*un fatarabba*s*oo fasataAAlamoona man a*s**ha*bu a**l***ss*ir*at*i a**l**ssawiyyi wamani ihtad*a*

## 21:1

Iqtaraba li**l**nn*a*si *h*is*a*buhum wahum fee ghaflatin muAAri*d*oon**a**

## 21:2

M*a* yateehim min *th*ikrin min rabbihim mu*h*dathin ill*a* istamaAAoohu wahum yalAAaboon**a**

## 21:3

L*a*hiyatan quloobuhum waasarroo a**l**nnajw*a* alla*th*eena **th**&#x61;lamoo hal h*atha* ill*a* basharun mithlukum afatatoona a**l**ssi*h*ra waantum tub*s*iroon**a**

## 21:4

Q*a*la rabbee yaAAlamu alqawla fee a**l**ssam*a*i wa**a**lar*d*i wahuwa a**l**ssameeAAu alAAaleem**u**

## 21:5

Bal q*a*loo a*d*gh*a*thu a*h*l*a*min bali iftar*a*hu bal huwa sh*a*AAirun falyatin*a* bi*a*yatin kam*a* orsila alawwaloon**a**

## 21:6

M*a* *a*manat qablahum min qaryatin ahlakn*a*h*a* afahum yuminoon**a**

## 21:7

Wam*a* arsaln*a* qablaka ill*a* rij*a*lan noo*h*ee ilayhim fa**i**saloo ahla a**l***thth*ikri in kuntum l*a* taAAlamoon**a**

## 21:8

Wam*a* jaAAaln*a*hum jasadan l*a* yakuloona a**l***tt*aAA*a*ma wam*a* k*a*noo kh*a*lideen**a**

## 21:9

Thumma *s*adaqn*a*humu alwaAAda faanjayn*a*hum waman nash*a*o waahlakn*a* almusrifeen**a**

## 21:10

Laqad anzaln*a* ilaykum kit*a*ban feehi *th*ikrukum afal*a* taAAqiloon**a**

## 21:11

Wakam qa*s*amn*a* min qaryatin k*a*nat **th***a*limatan waanshan*a* baAAdah*a* qawman *a*khareen**a**

## 21:12

Falamm*a* a*h*assoo basan*a* i*tha* hum minh*a* yarku*d*oon**a**

## 21:13

L*a* tarku*d*oo wa**i**rjiAAoo il*a* m*a* otriftum feehi wamas*a*kinikum laAAallakum tusaloon**a**

## 21:14

Q*a*loo y*a* waylan*a* inn*a* kunn*a* **th***a*limeen**a**

## 21:15

Fam*a* z*a*lat tilka daAAw*a*hum *h*att*a* jaAAaln*a*hum *h*a*s*eedan kh*a*mideen**a**

## 21:16

Wam*a* khalaqn*a* a**l**ssam*a*a wa**a**lar*d*a wam*a* baynahum*a* l*a*AAibeen**a**

## 21:17

Law aradn*a* an nattakhi*th*a lahwan la**i**ttakha*th*n*a*hu min ladunn*a* in kunn*a* f*a*AAileen**a**

## 21:18

Bal naq*th*ifu bi**a**l*h*aqqi AAal*a* alb*at*ili fayadmaghuhu fai*tha* huwa z*a*hiqun walakumu alwaylu mimm*a* ta*s*ifoon**a**

## 21:19

Walahu man fee a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i waman AAindahu l*a* yastakbiroona AAan AAib*a*datihi wal*a* yasta*h*siroon**a**

## 21:20

Yusabbi*h*oona allayla wa**al**nnah*a*ra l*a* yafturoon**a**

## 21:21

Ami ittakha*th*oo *a*lihatan mina alar*d*i hum yunshiroon**a**

## 21:22

Law k*a*na feehim*a* *a*lihatun ill*a* All*a*hu lafasadat*a* fasub*ha*na All*a*hi rabbi alAAarshi AAamm*a* ya*s*ifoon**a**

## 21:23

L*a* yusalu AAamm*a* yafAAalu wahum yusaloon**a**

## 21:24

Ami ittakha*th*oo min doonihi *a*lihatan qul h*a*too burh*a*nakum h*atha* *th*ikru man maAAiya wa*th*ikru man qablee bal aktharuhum l*a* yaAAlamoona al*h*aqqa fahum muAAri*d*oon**a**

## 21:25

Wam*a* arsaln*a* min qablika min rasoolin ill*a* noo*h*ee ilayhi annahu l*a* il*a*ha ill*a* an*a* fa**o**AAbudoon**i**

## 21:26

Waq*a*loo ittakha*th*a a**l**rra*h*m*a*nu waladan sub*ha*nahu bal AAib*a*dun mukramoon**a**

## 21:27

L*a* yasbiqoonahu bi**a**lqawli wahum biamrihi yaAAmaloon**a**

## 21:28

YaAAlamu m*a* bayna aydeehim wam*a* khalfahum wal*a* yashfaAAoona ill*a* limani irta*da* wahum min khashyatihi mushfiqoon**a**

## 21:29

Waman yaqul minhum innee il*a*hun min doonihi fa*tha*lika najzeehi jahannama ka*tha*lika najzee a**l****thth***a*limeen**a**

## 21:30

Awalam yar*a* alla*th*eena kafaroo anna a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*a k*a*nat*a* ratqan fafataqn*a*hum*a* wajaAAaln*a* mina alm*a*i kulla shayin *h*ayyin afal*a* yuminoon**a**

## 21:31

WajaAAaln*a* fee alar*d*i raw*a*siya an tameeda bihim wajaAAaln*a* feeh*a&#x20;*&#x66;ij*a*jan subulan laAAallahum yahtadoon**a**

## 21:32

WajaAAaln*a* a**l**ssam*a*a saqfan ma*h*fo&#x6F;**th**&#x61;n wahum AAan *a*y*a*tih*a* muAAri*d*oon**a**

## 21:33

Wahuwa alla*th*ee khalaqa allayla wa**al**nnah*a*ra wa**al**shshamsa wa**a**lqamara kullun fee falakin yasba*h*oon**a**

## 21:34

Wam*a* jaAAaln*a* libasharin min qablika alkhulda afain mitta fahumu alkh*a*lidoon**a**

## 21:35

Kullu nafsin *tha*iqatu almawti wanablookum bi**al**shsharri wa**a**lkhayri fitnatan wailayn*a* turjaAAoon**a**

## 21:36

Wai*tha* ra*a*ka alla*th*eena kafaroo in yattakhi*th*oonaka ill*a* huzuwan ah*atha* alla*th*ee ya*th*kuru *a*lihatakum wahum bi*th*ikri a**l**rra*h*m*a*ni hum k*a*firoon**a**

## 21:37

Khuliqa alins*a*nu min AAajalin saoreekum *a*y*a*tee fal*a* tastaAAjiloon**a**

## 21:38

Wayaqooloona mat*a* h*atha* alwaAAdu in kuntum *sa*diqeen**a**

## 21:39

Law yaAAlamu alla*th*eena kafaroo *h*eena l*a* yakuffoona AAan wujoohihimu a**l**nn*a*ra wal*a* AAan **th**&#x75;hoorihim wal*a* hum yun*s*aroon**a**

## 21:40

Bal tateehim baghtatan fatabhatuhum fal*a* yasta*t*eeAAoona raddah*a* wal*a* hum yu&#x6E;**th**&#x61;roon**a**

## 21:41

Walaqadi istuhzia birusulin min qablika fa*ha*qa bi**a**lla*th*eena sakhiroo minhum m*a* k*a*noo bihi yastahzioon**a**

## 21:42

Qul man yaklaokum bi**a**llayli wa**al**nnah*a*ri mina a**l**rra*h*m*a*ni bal hum AAan *th*ikri rabbihim muAAri*d*oon**a**

## 21:43

Am lahum *a*lihatun tamnaAAuhum min doonin*a* l*a* yasta*t*eeAAoona na*s*ra anfusihim wal*a* hum minn*a* yu*sh*aboon**a**

## 21:44

Bal mattaAAn*a* h*a*ol*a*i wa*a*b*a*ahum *h*att*a* *ta*la AAalayhimu alAAumuru afal*a* yarawna ann*a* natee alar*d*a nanqu*s*uh*a* min a*t*r*a*fih*a* afahumu algh*a*liboon**a**

## 21:45

Qul innam*a* on*th*irukum bi**a**lwa*h*yi wal*a* yasmaAAu a**l***ss*ummu a**l**dduAA*a*a i*tha* m*a* yun*th*aroon**a**

## 21:46

Walain massathum naf*h*atun min AAa*tha*bi rabbika layaqoolunna y*a&#x20;*&#x77;aylan*a* inn*a* kunn*a* **th***a*limeen**a**

## 21:47

Wana*d*aAAu almaw*a*zeena alqis*t*a liyawmi alqiy*a*mati fal*a* t&#x75;**th**&#x6C;amu nafsun shayan wain k*a*na mithq*a*la *h*abbatin min khardalin atayn*a* bih*a* wakaf*a* bin*a* *ha*sibeen**a**

## 21:48

Walaqad *a*tayn*a* moos*a* wah*a*roona alfurq*a*na wa*d*iy*a*an wa*th*ikran lilmuttaqeen**a**

## 21:49

Alla*th*eena yakhshawna rabbahum bi**a**lghaybi wahum mina a**l**ss*a*AAati mushfiqoon**a**

## 21:50

Wah*atha* *th*ikrun mub*a*rakun anzaln*a*hu afaantum lahu munkiroon**a**

## 21:51

Walaqad *a*tayn*a* ibr*a*heema rushdahu min qablu wakunn*a* bihi AA*a*limeen**a**

## 21:52

I*th* q*a*la liabeehi waqawmihi m*a* h*ath*ihi a**l**ttam*a*theelu allatee antum lah*a* AA*a*kifoon**a**

## 21:53

Q*a*loo wajadn*a* *a*b*a*an*a* lah*a* AA*a*bideen**a**

## 21:54

Q*a*la laqad kuntum antum wa*a*b*a*okum fee *d*al*a*lin mubeen**in**

## 21:55

Q*a*loo ajitan*a* bi**a**l*h*aqqi am anta mina all*a*AAibeen**a**

## 21:56

Q*a*la bal rabbukum rabbu a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i alla*th*ee fa*t*arahunna waan*a* AAal*a* *tha*likum mina a**l**shsh*a*hideen**a**

## 21:57

Wata**A**ll*a*hi laakeedanna a*s*n*a*makum baAAda an tuwalloo mudbireen**a**

## 21:58

FajaAAalahum ju*thath*an ill*a* kabeeran lahum laAAallahum ilayhi yarjiAAoon**a**

## 21:59

Q*a*loo man faAAala h*atha* bi*a*lihatin*a* innahu lamina a**l****thth***a*limeen**a**

## 21:60

Q*a*loo samiAAn*a* fatan ya*th*kuruhum yuq*a*lu lahu ibr*a*heem**u**

## 21:61

Q*a*loo fatoo bihi AAal*a* aAAyuni a**l**nn*a*si laAAallahum yashhadoon**a**

## 21:62

Q*a*loo aanta faAAalta h*atha* bi*a*lihatin*a* y*a* ibr*a*heem**u**

## 21:63

Q*a*la bal faAAalahu kabeeruhum h*atha* fa**i**saloohum in k*a*noo yan*t*iqoon**a**

## 21:64

FarajaAAoo il*a* anfusihim faq*a*loo innakum antumu a**l****thth***a*limoon**a**

## 21:65

Thumma nukisoo AAal*a* ruoosihim laqad AAalimta m*a* h*a*ol*a*i yan*t*iqoon**a**

## 21:66

Q*a*la afataAAbudoona min dooni All*a*hi m*a* l*a* yanfaAAukum shayan wal*a* ya*d*urrukum

## 21:67

Offin lakum walim*a* taAAbudoona min dooni All*a*hi afal*a* taAAqiloon**a**

## 21:68

Q*a*loo *h*arriqoohu wa**o**n*s*uroo *a*lihatakum in kuntum f*a*AAileen**a**

## 21:69

Quln*a* y*a* n*a*ru koonee bardan wasal*a*man AAal*a* ibr*a*heem**a**

## 21:70

Waar*a*doo bihi kaydan fajaAAaln*a*humu alakhsareen**a**

## 21:71

Wanajjayn*a*hu waloo*t*an il*a* alar*d*i allatee b*a*rakn*a* feeh*a* lilAA*a*lameen**a**

## 21:72

Wawahabn*a* lahu is*ha*qa wayaAAqooba n*a*filatan wakullan jaAAaln*a* *sa*li*h*een**a**

## 21:73

WajaAAaln*a*hum aimmatan yahdoona biamrin*a* waaw*h*ayn*a* ilayhim fiAAla alkhayr*a*ti waiq*a*ma a**l***ss*al*a*ti waeet*a*a a**l**zzak*a*ti wak*a*noo lan*a* AA*a*bideen**a**

## 21:74

Waloo*t*an *a*tayn*a*hu *h*ukman waAAilman wanajjayn*a*hu mina alqaryati allatee k*a*nat taAAmalu alkhab*a*itha innahum k*a*noo qawma sawin f*a*siqeen**a**

## 21:75

Waadkhaln*a*hu fee ra*h*matin*a* innahu mina a**l***ssa*li*h*een**a**

## 21:76

Wanoo*h*an i*th* n*a*d*a* min qablu fa**i**stajabn*a* lahu fanajjayn*a*hu waahlahu mina alkarbi alAA&#x61;**th**&#x65;em**i**

## 21:77

Wana*s*arn*a*hu mina alqawmi alla*th*eena ka*thth*aboo bi*a*y*a*tin*a* innahum k*a*noo qawma sawin faaghraqn*a*hum ajmaAAeen**a**

## 21:78

Wad*a*wooda wasulaym*a*na i*th* ya*h*kum*a*ni fee al*h*arthi i*th* nafashat feehi ghanamu alqawmi wakunn*a* li*h*ukmihim sh*a*hideen**a**

## 21:79

Fafahhamn*a*h*a* sulaym*a*na wakullan *a*tayn*a* *h*ukman waAAilman wasakhkharn*a* maAAa d*a*wooda aljib*a*la yusabbi*h*na wa**al***tt*ayra wakunn*a* f*a*AAileen**a**

## 21:80

WaAAallamn*a*hu *s*anAAata laboosin lakum litu*hs*inakum min basikum fahal antum sh*a*kiroon**a**

## 21:81

Walisulaym*a*na a**l**rree*h*a AA*as*ifatan tajree biamrihi il*a* alar*d*i allatee b*a*rakn*a* feeh*a* wakunn*a* bikulli shayin AA*a*limeen**a**

## 21:82

Wamina a**l**shshay*at*eeni man yaghoo*s*oona lahu wayaAAmaloona AAamalan doona *tha*lika wakunn*a* lahum *ha*f&#x69;**th**&#x65;en**a**

## 21:83

Waayyooba i*th* n*a*d*a* rabbahu annee massaniya a**l***dd*urru waanta ar*h*amu a**l**rr*ah*imeen**a**

## 21:84

Fa**i**stajabn*a* lahu fakashafn*a* m*a* bihi min *d*urrin wa*a*tayn*a*hu ahlahu wamithlahum maAAahum ra*h*matan min AAindin*a* wa*th*ikr*a* lilAA*a*bideen**a**

## 21:85

Waism*a*AAeela waidreesa wa*tha* alkifli kullun mina a**l***ssa*bireen**a**

## 21:86

Waadkhaln*a*hum fee ra*h*matin*a* innahum mina a**l***ssa*li*h*een**a**

## 21:87

Wa*tha* a**l**nnooni i*th* *th*ahaba mugh*ad*iban f&#x61;**th**&#x61;nna an lan naqdira AAalayhi fan*a*d*a* fee a**l****thth**&#x75;lum*a*ti an l*a* il*a*ha ill*a* anta sub*ha*naka innee kuntu mina a**l****thth***a*limeen**a**

## 21:88

Fa**i**stajabn*a* lahu wanajjayn*a*hu mina alghammi waka*tha*lika nunjee almumineen**a**

## 21:89

Wazakariyy*a* i*th* n*a*d*a* rabbahu rabbi l*a* ta*th*arnee fardan waanta khayru alw*a*ritheen**a**

## 21:90

Fa**i**stajabn*a* lahu wawahabn*a* lahu ya*h*y*a* waa*s*la*h*n*a* lahu zawjahu innahum k*a*noo yus*a*riAAoona fee alkhayr*a*ti wayadAAoonan*a* raghaban warahaban wak*a*noo lan*a* kh*a*shiAAeen**a**

## 21:91

Wa**a**llatee a*hs*anat farjah*a* fanafakhn*a* feeh*a* min roo*h*in*a* wajaAAaln*a*h*a* wa**i**bnah*a* *a*yatan lilAA*a*lameen**a**

## 21:92

Inna h*ath*ihi ommatukum ommatan w*ah*idatan waan*a* rabbukum faoAAbudoon**i**

## 21:93

Wataqa*tt*aAAoo amrahum baynahum kullun ilayn*a* r*a*jiAAoon**a**

## 21:94

Faman yaAAmal mina a**l***ssa*li*ha*ti wahuwa muminun fal*a* kufr*a*na lisaAAyihi wainn*a* lahu k*a*tiboon**a**

## 21:95

Wa*h*ar*a*mun AAal*a* qaryatin ahlakn*a*h*a* annahum l*a* yarjiAAoon**a**

## 21:96

*H*att*a* i*tha* futi*h*at yajooju wamajooju wahum min kulli *h*adabin yansiloon**a**

## 21:97

Wa**i**qtaraba alwaAAdu al*h*aqqu fai*tha* hiya sh*a*khi*s*atun ab*sa*ru alla*th*eena kafaroo y*a* waylan*a* qad kunn*a* fee ghaflatin min h*atha* bal kunn*a* **th***a*limeen**a**

## 21:98

Innakum wam*a* taAAbudoona min dooni All*a*hi *h*a*s*abu jahannama antum lah*a* w*a*ridoon**a**

## 21:99

Law k*a*na h*a*ol*a*i *a*lihatan m*a* waradooh*a* wakullun feeh*a* kh*a*lidoon**a**

## 21:100

Lahum feeh*a* zafeerun wahum feeh*a* l*a* yasmaAAoon**a**

## 21:101

Inna alla*th*eena sabaqat lahum minn*a* al*h*usn*a* ol*a*ika AAanh*a&#x20;*&#x6D;ubAAadoon**a**

## 21:102

L*a* yasmaAAoona *h*aseesah*a* wahum fee m*a* ishtahat anfusuhum kh*a*lidoon**a**

## 21:103

L*a* ya*h*zunuhumu alfazaAAu alakbaru watatalaqq*a*humu almal*a*ikatu h*atha* yawmukumu alla*th*ee kuntum tooAAadoon**a**

## 21:104

Yawma na*t*wee a**l**ssam*a*a ka*t*ayyi a**l**ssijlli lilkutubi kam*a* badan*a* awwala khalqin nuAAeeduhu waAAdan AAalayn*a* inn*a* kunn*a* f*a*AAileen**a**

## 21:105

Walaqad katabn*a* fee a**l**zzaboori min baAAdi a**l***thth*ikri anna alar*d*a yarithuh*a* AAib*a*diya a**l***ssa*li*h*oon**a**

## 21:106

Inna fee h*atha* labal*a*ghan liqawmin AA*a*bideen**a**

## 21:107

Wam*a* arsaln*a*ka ill*a* ra*h*matan lilAA*a*lameen**a**

## 21:108

Qul innam*a* yoo*ha* ilayya annam*a* il*a*hukum il*a*hun w*ah*idun fahal antum muslimoon**a**

## 21:109

Fain tawallaw faqul *ath*antukum AAal*a* saw*a*in wain adree aqareebun am baAAeedun m*a* tooAAadoon**a**

## 21:110

Innahu yaAAlamu aljahra mina alqawli wayaAAlamu m*a* taktumoon**a**

## 21:111

Wain adree laAAallahu fitnatun lakum wamat*a*AAun il*a* *h*een**in**

## 21:112

Q*a*la rabbi o*h*kum bi**a**l*h*aqqi warabbun*a* a**l**rra*h*m*a*nu almustaAA*a*nu AAal*a* m*a* ta*s*ifoon**a**

## 22:1

Y*a* ayyuh*a* a**l**nn*a*su ittaqoo rabbakum inna zalzalata a**l**ss*a*AAati shayon AA&#x61;**th**&#x65;em**un**

## 22:2

Yawma tarawnah*a* ta*th*halu kullu mur*d*iAAatin AAamm*a* ar*d*aAAat wata*d*aAAu kullu *tha*ti *h*amlin *h*amlah*a* watar*a* a**l**nn*a*sa suk*a*r*a* wam*a* hum bisuk*a*r*a* wal*a*kinna AAa*tha*ba All*a*hi shadeed**un**

## 22:3

Wamina a**l**nn*a*si man yuj*a*dilu fee All*a*hi bighayri AAilmin wayattabiAAu kulla shay*ta*nin mareed**in**

## 22:4

Kutiba AAalayhi annahu man tawall*a*hu faannahu yu*d*illuhu wayahdeehi il*a* AAa*tha*bi a**l**ssaAAeer**i**

## 22:5

Y*a* ayyuh*a* a**l**nn*a*su in kuntum fee raybin mina albaAAthi fainn*a* khalaqn*a*kum min tur*a*bin thumma min nu*t*fatin thumma min AAalaqatin thumma min mu*d*ghatin mukhallaqatin waghayri mukhallaqatin linubayyina lakum wanuqirru fee alar*ha*mi m*a* nash*a*o il*a* ajalin musamman thumma nukhrijukum *t*iflan thumma litablughoo ashuddakum waminkum man yutawaff*a* waminkum man yuraddu il*a* ar*th*ali alAAumuri likayl*a* yaAAlama min baAAdi AAilmin shayan watar*a* alar*d*a h*a*midatan fai*tha* anzaln*a* AAalayh*a* alm*a*a ihtazzat warabat waanbatat min kulli zawjin baheej**in**

## 22:6

*Tha*lika bianna All*a*ha huwa al*h*aqqu waannahu yu*h*yee almawt*a* waannahu AAal*a* kulli shayin qadeer**un**

## 22:7

Waanna a**l**ss*a*AAata *a*tiyatun l*a* rayba feeh*a* waanna All*a*ha yabAAathu man fee alquboor**i**

## 22:8

Wamina a**l**nn*a*si man yuj*a*dilu fee All*a*hi bighayri AAilmin wal*a* hudan wal*a* kit*a*bin muneer**in**

## 22:9

Th*a*niya AAi*t*fihi liyu*d*illa AAan sabeeli All*a*hi lahu fee a**l**dduny*a* khizyun wanu*th*eequhu yawma alqiy*a*mati AAa*tha*ba al*h*areeq**i**

## 22:10

*Tha*lika bim*a* qaddamat yad*a*ka waanna All*a*ha laysa b&#x69;**th**&#x61;ll*a*min lilAAabeed**i**

## 22:11

Wamina a**l**nn*a*si man yaAAbudu All*a*ha AAal*a* *h*arfin fain a*sa*bahu khayrun i*t*maanna bihi wain a*sa*bathu fitnatun inqalaba AAal*a* wajhihi khasira a**l**dduny*a* wa**a**l*a*khirata *tha*lika huwa alkhusr*a*nu almubeen**u**

## 22:12

YadAAoo min dooni All*a*hi m*a* l*a* ya*d*urruhu wam*a* l*a* yanfaAAuhu *tha*lika huwa a**l***dd*al*a*lu albaAAeed**u**

## 22:13

YadAAoo laman *d*arruhu aqrabu min nafAAihi labisa almawl*a* walabisa alAAasheer**u**

## 22:14

Inna All*a*ha yudkhilu alla*th*eena *a*manoo waAAamiloo a**l***ssa*li*ha*ti jann*a*tin tajree min ta*h*tih*a* alanh*a*ru inna All*a*ha yafAAalu m*a* yureed**u**

## 22:15

Man k*a*na y&#x61;**th**&#x75;nnu an lan yan*s*urahu All*a*hu fee a**l**dduny*a* wa**a**l*a*khirati falyamdud bisababin il*a* a**l**ssam*a*i thumma liyaq*t*aAA falya&#x6E;**th**&#x75;r hal yu*th*hibanna kayduhu m*a* yaghe&#x65;**th****u**

## 22:16

Waka*tha*lika anzaln*a*hu *a*y*a*tin bayyin*a*tin waanna All*a*ha yahdee man yureed**u**

## 22:17

Inna alla*th*eena *a*manoo wa**a**lla*th*eena h*a*doo wa**al***ssa*bieena wa**al**nna*sa*r*a* wa**a**lmajoosa wa**a**lla*th*eena ashrakoo inna All*a*ha yaf*s*ilu baynahum yawma alqiy*a*mati inna All*a*ha AAal*a* kulli shayin shaheed**un**

## 22:18

Alam tara anna All*a*ha yasjudu lahu man fee a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti waman fee alar*d*i wa**al**shshamsu wa**a**lqamaru wa**al**nnujoomu wa**a**ljib*a*lu wa**al**shshajaru wa**al**ddaw*a*bbu wakatheerun mina a**l**nn*a*si wakatheerun *h*aqqa AAalayhi alAAa*tha*bu waman yuhini All*a*hu fam*a* lahu min mukrimin inna All*a*ha yafAAalu m*a* yash*a***o**

## 22:19

H*atha*ni kha*s*m*a*ni ikhta*s*amoo fee rabbihim fa**a**lla*th*eena kafaroo qu*tt*iAAat lahum thiy*a*bun min n*a*rin yu*s*abbu min fawqi ruoosihimu al*h*ameem**u**

## 22:20

Yu*s*haru bihi m*a* fee bu*t*oonihim wa**a**ljulood**u**

## 22:21

Walahum maq*a*miAAu min *h*adeed**in**

## 22:22

Kullam*a* ar*a*doo an yakhrujoo minh*a* min ghammin oAAeedoo feeh*a* wa*th*ooqoo AAa*tha*ba al*h*areeq**i**

## 22:23

Inna All*a*ha yudkhilu alla*th*eena *a*manoo waAAamiloo a**l***ssa*li*ha*ti jann*a*tin tajree min ta*h*tih*a* alanh*a*ru yu*h*allawna feeh*a* min as*a*wira min *th*ahabin waluluan walib*a*suhum feeh*a* *h*areer**un**

## 22:24

Wahudoo il*a* a**l***tt*ayyibi mina alqawli wahudoo il*a* *s*ir*at*i al*h*ameed**i**

## 22:25

Inna alla*th*eena kafaroo waya*s*uddoona AAan sabeeli All*a*hi wa**a**lmasjidi al*h*ar*a*mi alla*th*ee jaAAaln*a*hu li**l**nn*a*si saw*a*an alAA*a*kifu feehi wa**a**lb*a*di waman yurid feehi biil*ha*din b&#x69;**th**&#x75;lmin nu*th*iqhu min AAa*tha*bin aleem**in**

## 22:26

Wai*th* bawwan*a* liibr*a*heema mak*a*na albayti an l*a* tushrik bee shayan wa*t*ahhir baytiya li**l***tta*ifeena wa**a**lq*a*imeena wa**al**rrukkaAAi a**l**ssujood**i**

## 22:27

Waa*thth*in fee a**l**nn*a*si bi**a**l*h*ajji yatooka rij*a*lan waAAal*a* kulli *da*mirin yateena min kulli fajjin AAameeq**in**

## 22:28

Liyashhadoo man*a*fiAAa lahum waya*th*kuroo isma All*a*hi fee ayy*a*min maAAloom*a*tin AAal*a* m*a* razaqahum min baheemati alanAA*a*mi fakuloo minh*a* waa*t*AAimoo alb*a*isa alfaqeer**a**

## 22:29

Thumma lyaq*d*oo tafathahum walyoofoo nu*th*oorahum walya*tt*awwafoo bi**a**lbayti alAAateeq**i**

## 22:30

*Tha*lika waman yuAA&#x61;**thth**&#x69;m *h*urum*a*ti All*a*hi fahuwa khayrun lahu AAinda rabbihi wao*h*illat lakumu alanAA*a*mu ill*a* m*a* yutl*a* AAalaykum fa**i**jtaniboo a**l**rrijsa mina alawth*a*ni wa**i**jtaniboo qawla a**l**zzoor**i**

## 22:31

*H*unaf*a*a lill*a*hi ghayra mushrikeena bihi waman yushrik bi**A**ll*a*hi fakaannam*a* kharra mina a**l**ssam*a*i fatakh*t*afuhu a**l***tt*ayru aw tahwee bihi a**l**rree*h*u fee mak*a*nin sa*h*eeq**in**

## 22:32

*Tha*lika waman yuAA&#x61;**thth**&#x69;m shaAA*a*ira All*a*hi fainnah*a* min taqw*a* alquloob**i**

## 22:33

Lakum feeh*a* man*a*fiAAu il*a* ajalin musamman thumma ma*h*illuh*a* il*a* albayti alAAateeq**i**

## 22:34

Walikulli ommatin jaAAaln*a* mansakan liya*th*kuroo isma All*a*hi AAal*a* m*a* razaqahum min baheemati alanAA*a*mi fail*a*hukum il*a*hun w*ah*idun falahu aslimoo wabashshiri almukhbiteen**a**

## 22:35

Alla*th*eena i*tha* *th*ukira All*a*hu wajilat quloobuhum wa**al***ssa*bireena AAal*a* m*a* a*sa*bahum wa**a**lmuqeemee a**l***ss*al*a*ti wamimm*a* razaqn*a*hum yunfiqoon**a**

## 22:36

Wa**a**lbudna jaAAaln*a*h*a* lakum min shaAA*a*iri All*a*hi lakum feeh*a* khayrun fa**o***th*kuroo isma All*a*hi AAalayh*a* *s*aw*a*ffa fai*tha* wajabat junoobuh*a* fakuloo minh*a* waa*t*AAimoo alq*a*niAAa wa**a**lmuAAtarra ka*tha*lika sakhkharn*a*h*a* lakum laAAallakum tashkuroon**a**

## 22:37

Lan yan*a*la All*a*ha lu*h*oomuh*a* wal*a* dim*a*oh*a* wal*a*kin yan*a*luhu a**l**ttaqw*a* minkum ka*tha*lika sakhkharah*a* lakum litukabbiroo All*a*ha AAal*a* m*a* had*a*kum wabashshiri almu*h*sineen**a**

## 22:38

Inna All*a*ha yud*a*fiAAu AAani alla*th*eena *a*manoo inna All*a*ha l*a* yu*h*ibbu kulla khaww*a*nin kafoor**in**

## 22:39

O*th*ina lilla*th*eena yuq*a*taloona biannahum **th**&#x75;limoo wainna All*a*ha AAal*a* na*s*rihim laqadeer**un**

## 22:40

Alla*th*eena okhrijoo min diy*a*rihim bighayri *h*aqqin ill*a* an yaqooloo rabbun*a* All*a*hu walawl*a* dafAAu All*a*hi a**l**nn*a*sa baAA*d*ahum bibaAA*d*in lahuddimat *s*aw*a*miAAu wabiyaAAun wa*s*alaw*a*tun wamas*a*jidu yu*th*karu feeh*a* ismu All*a*hi katheeran walayan*s*uranna All*a*hu man yan*s*uruhu inna All*a*ha laqawiyyun AAazeez**un**

## 22:41

Alla*th*eena in makkann*a*hum fee alar*d*i aq*a*moo a**l***ss*al*a*ta wa*a*tawoo a**l**zzak*a*ta waamaroo bi**a**lmaAAroofi wanahaw AAani almunkari walill*a*hi AA*a*qibatu alomoor**i**

## 22:42

Wain yuka*thth*ibooka faqad ka*thth*abat qablahum qawmu noo*h*in waAA*a*dun wathamood**u**

## 22:43

Waqawmu ibr*a*heema waqawmu loo*t***in**

## 22:44

Waa*s**ha*bu madyana waku*thth*iba moos*a* faamlaytu lilk*a*fireena thumma akha*th*tuhum fakayfa k*a*na nakeer**i**

## 22:45

Fakaayyin min qaryatin ahlakn*a*h*a* wahiya **th***a*limatun fahiya kh*a*wiyatun AAal*a* AAurooshih*a* wabirin muAAa*tt*alatin waqa*s*rin masheed**in**

## 22:46

Afalam yaseeroo fee alar*d*i fatakoona lahum quloobun yaAAqiloona bih*a* aw *atha*nun yasmaAAoona bih*a* fainnah*a* l*a* taAAm*a* alab*sa*ru wal*a*kin taAAm*a* alquloobu allatee fee a**l***ss*udoor**i**

## 22:47

WayastaAAjiloonaka bi**a**lAAa*tha*bi walan yukhlifa All*a*hu waAAdahu wainna yawman AAinda rabbika kaalfi sanatin mimm*a* taAAuddoon**a**

## 22:48

Wakaayyin min qaryatin amlaytu lah*a* wahiya **th***a*limatun thumma akha*th*tuh*a* wailayya alma*s*eer**u**

## 22:49

Qul y*a* ayyuh*a* a**l**nn*a*su innam*a* an*a* lakum na*th*eerun mubeen**un**

## 22:50

Fa**a**lla*th*eena *a*manoo waAAamiloo a**l***ssa*li*ha*ti lahum maghfiratun warizqun kareem**un**

## 22:51

Wa**a**lla*th*eena saAAaw fee *a*y*a*tin*a* muAA*a*jizeena ol*a*ika a*s**ha*bu alja*h*eem**i**

## 22:52

Wam*a* arsaln*a* min qablika min rasoolin wal*a* nabiyyin ill*a* i*tha* tamann*a* alq*a* a**l**shshay*ta*nu fee omniyyatihi fayansakhu All*a*hu m*a* yulqee a**l**shshay*ta*nu thumma yu*h*kimu All*a*hu *a*y*a*tihi wa**A**ll*a*hu AAaleemun *h*akeem**un**

## 22:53

LiyajAAala m*a* yulqee a**l**shshay*ta*nu fitnatan lilla*th*eena fee quloobihim mara*d*un wa**a**lq*a*siyati quloobuhum wainna a**l****thth***a*limeena lafee shiq*a*qin baAAeed**in**

## 22:54

WaliyaAAlama alla*th*eena ootoo alAAilma annahu al*h*aqqu min rabbika fayuminoo bihi fatukhbita lahu quloobuhum wainna All*a*ha lah*a*di alla*th*eena *a*manoo il*a* *s*ir*at*in mustaqeem**in**

## 22:55

Wal*a* yaz*a*lu alla*th*eena kafaroo fee miryatin minhu *h*att*a* tatiyahumu a**l**ss*a*AAatu baghtatan aw yatiyahum AAa*tha*bu yawmin AAaqeem**in**

## 22:56

Almulku yawmai*th*in lill*a*hi ya*h*kumu baynahum fa**a**lla*th*eena *a*manoo waAAamiloo a**l***ssa*li*ha*ti fee jann*a*ti a**l**nnaAAeem**i**

## 22:57

Wa**a**lla*th*eena kafaroo waka*thth*aboo bi*a*y*a*tin*a* faol*a*ika lahum AAa*tha*bun muheen**un**

## 22:58

Wa**a**lla*th*eena h*a*jaroo fee sabeeli All*a*hi thumma qutiloo aw m*a*too layarzuqannahumu All*a*hu rizqan *h*asanan wainna All*a*ha lahuwa khayru a**l**rr*a*ziqeen**a**

## 22:59

Layudkhilannahum mudkhalan yar*d*awnahu wainna All*a*ha laAAaleemun *h*aleem**un**

## 22:60

*Tha*lika waman AA*a*qaba bimithli m*a* AAooqiba bihi thumma bughiya AAalayhi layan*s*urannahu All*a*hu inna All*a*ha laAAafuwwun ghafoor**un**

## 22:61

*Tha*lika bianna All*a*ha yooliju allayla fee a**l**nnah*a*ri wayooliju a**l**nnah*a*ra fee allayli waanna All*a*ha sameeAAun ba*s*eer**un**

## 22:62

*Tha*lika bianna All*a*ha huwa al*h*aqqu waanna m*a* yadAAoona min doonihi huwa alb*at*ilu waanna All*a*ha huwa alAAaliyyu alkabeer**u**

## 22:63

Alam tara anna All*a*ha anzala mina a**l**ssam*a*i m*a*an fatu*s*bi*h*u alar*d*u mukh*d*arratan inna All*a*ha la*t*eefun khabeer**un**

## 22:64

Lahu m*a* fee a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wam*a* fee alar*d*i wainna All*a*ha lahuwa alghaniyyu al*h*ameed**u**

## 22:65

Alam tara anna All*a*ha sakhkhara lakum m*a* fee alar*d*i wa**a**lfulka tajree fee alba*h*ri biamrihi wayumsiku a**l**ssam*a*a an taqaAAa AAal*a* alar*d*i ill*a* bii*th*nihi inna All*a*ha bi**al**nn*a*si laraoofun ra*h*eem**un**

## 22:66

Wahuwa alla*th*ee a*h*y*a*kum thumma yumeetukum thumma yu*h*yeekum inna alins*a*na lakafoor**un**

## 22:67

Likulli ommatin jaAAaln*a* mansakan hum n*a*sikoohu fal*a* yun*a*ziAAunnaka fee alamri wa**o**dAAu il*a* rabbika innaka laAAal*a* hudan mustaqeem**in**

## 22:68

Wain j*a*dalooka faquli All*a*hu aAAlamu bim*a* taAAmaloon**a**

## 22:69

All*a*hu ya*h*kumu baynakum yawma alqiy*a*mati feem*a* kuntum feehi takhtalifoon**a**

## 22:70

Alam taAAlam anna All*a*ha yaAAlamu m*a* fee a**l**ssam*a*i wa**a**lar*d*i inna *tha*lika fee kit*a*bin inna *tha*lika AAal*a* All*a*hi yaseer**un**

## 22:71

WayaAAbudoona min dooni All*a*hi m*a* lam yunazzil bihi sul*ta*nan wam*a* laysa lahum bihi AAilmun wam*a* li**l****thth***a*limeena min na*s*eer**in**

## 22:72

Wai*tha* tutl*a* AAalayhim *a*y*a*tun*a* bayyin*a*tin taAArifu fee wujoohi alla*th*eena kafaroo almunkara yak*a*doona yas*t*oona bi**a**lla*th*eena yatloona AAalayhim *a*y*a*tin*a* qul afaonabbiokum bisharrin min *tha*likum a**l**nn*a*ru waAAadah*a* All*a*hu alla*th*eena kafaroo wabisa alma*s*eer**u**

## 22:73

Y*a* ayyuh*a* a**l**nn*a*su *d*uriba mathalun fa**i**stamiAAoo lahu inna alla*th*eena tadAAoona min dooni All*a*hi lan yakhluqoo *th*ub*a*ban walawi ijtamaAAoo lahu wain yaslubuhumu a**l***thth*ub*a*bu shayan l*a* yastanqi*th*oohu minhu *d*aAAufa a**l***tta*libu wa**a**lma*t*loob**u**

## 22:74

M*a* qadaroo All*a*ha *h*aqqa qadrihi inna All*a*ha laqawiyyun AAazeez**un**

## 22:75

All*a*hu ya*st*afee mina almal*a*ikati rusulan wamina a**l**nn*a*si inna All*a*ha sameeAAun ba*s*eer**un**

## 22:76

YaAAlamu m*a* bayna aydeehim wam*a* khalfahum wail*a* All*a*hi turjaAAu alomoor**u**

## 22:77

Y*a* ayyuh*a* alla*th*eena *a*manoo irkaAAoo wa**o**sjudoo wa**o**AAbudoo rabbakum wa**i**fAAaloo alkhayra laAAallakum tufli*h*oon**a**

## 22:78

Waj*a*hidoo fee All*a*hi *h*aqqa jih*a*dihi huwa ijtab*a*kum wam*a* jaAAala AAalaykum fee a**l**ddeeni min *h*arajin millata abeekum ibr*a*heema huwa samm*a*kumu almuslimeena min qablu wafee h*atha* liyakoona a**l**rrasoolu shaheedan AAalaykum watakoonoo shuhad*a*a AAal*a* a**l**nn*a*si faaqeemoo a**l***ss*al*a*ta wa*a*too a**l**zzak*a*ta wa**i**AAta*s*imoo bi**A**ll*a*hi huwa mawl*a*kum faniAAma almawl*a* waniAAma a**l**nna*s*eer**u**

## 23:1

Qad afla*h*a almuminoon**a**

## 23:2

Alla*th*eena hum fee *s*al*a*tihim kh*a*shiAAoon**a**

## 23:3

Wa**a**lla*th*eena hum AAani allaghwi muAAri*d*oon**a**

## 23:4

Wa**a**lla*th*eena hum li**l**zzak*a*ti f*a*AAiloon**a**

## 23:5

Wa**a**lla*th*eena hum lifuroojihim *ha*f&#x69;**th**&#x6F;on**a**

## 23:6

Ill*a* AAal*a* azw*a*jihim aw m*a* malakat aym*a*nuhum fainnahum ghayru maloomeen**a**

## 23:7

Famani ibtagh*a* war*a*a *tha*lika faol*a*ika humu alAA*a*doon**a**

## 23:8

Wa**a**lla*th*eena hum liam*a*n*a*tihim waAAahdihim r*a*AAoon**a**

## 23:9

Wa**a**lla*th*eena hum AAal*a* *s*alaw*a*tihim yu*ha*f&#x69;**th**&#x6F;on**a**

## 23:10

Ol*a*ika humu alw*a*rithoon**a**

## 23:11

Alla*th*eena yarithoona alfirdawsa hum feeh*a* kh*a*lidoon**a**

## 23:12

Walaqad khalaqn*a* alins*a*na min sul*a*latin min *t*een**in**

## 23:13

Thumma jaAAaln*a*hu nu*t*fatan fee qar*a*rin makeen**in**

## 23:14

Thumma khalaqn*a* a**l**nnu*t*fata AAalaqatan fakhalaqn*a* alAAalaqata mu*d*ghatan fakhalaqn*a* almu*d*ghata AA&#x69;**th***a*man fakasawn*a* alAA&#x69;**th***a*ma la*h*man thumma anshan*a*hu khalqan *a*khara fatab*a*raka All*a*hu a*h*sanu alkh*a*liqeen**a**

## 23:15

Thumma innakum baAAda *tha*lika lamayyitoon**a**

## 23:16

Thumma innakum yawma alqiy*a*mati tubAAathoon**a**

## 23:17

Walaqad khalaqn*a* fawqakum sabAAa *t*ar*a*iqa wam*a* kunn*a* AAani alkhalqi gh*a*fileen**a**

## 23:18

Waanzaln*a* mina a**l**ssam*a*i m*a*an biqadarin faaskann*a*hu fee alar*d*i wainn*a* AAal*a* *th*ah*a*bin bihi laq*a*diroon**a**

## 23:19

Faanshan*a* lakum bihi jann*a*tin min nakheelin waaAAn*a*bin lakum feeh*a* faw*a*kihu katheeratun waminh*a* takuloon**a**

## 23:20

Washajaratan takhruju min *t*oori sayn*a*a tanbutu bi**al**dduhni wa*s*ibghin lil*a*kileen**a**

## 23:21

Wainna lakum fee alanAA*a*mi laAAibratan nusqeekum mimm*a* fee bu*t*oonih*a* walakum feeh*a* man*a*fiAAu katheeratun waminh*a* takuloon**a**

## 23:22

WaAAalayh*a* waAAal*a* alfulki tu*h*maloon**a**

## 23:23

Walaqad arsaln*a* noo*h*an il*a* qawmihi faq*a*la y*a* qawmi oAAbudoo All*a*ha m*a* lakum min il*a*hin ghayruhu afal*a* tattaqoon**a**

## 23:24

Faq*a*la almalao alla*th*eena kafaroo min qawmihi m*a* h*atha* ill*a* basharun mithlukum yureedu an yatafa*dd*ala AAalaykum walaw sh*a*a All*a*hu laanzala mal*a*ikatan m*a* samiAAn*a* bih*atha* fee *a*b*a*in*a* alawwaleen**a**

## 23:25

In huwa ill*a* rajulun bihi jinnatun fatarabba*s*oo bihi *h*att*a* *h*een**in**

## 23:26

Q*a*la rabbi on*s*urnee bim*a* ka*thth*aboon**i**

## 23:27

Faaw*h*ayn*a* ilayhi ani i*s*naAAi alfulka biaAAyunin*a* wawa*h*yin*a* fai*tha* j*a*a amrun*a* waf*a*ra a**l**ttannooru fa**o**sluk feeh*a* min kullin zawjayni ithnayni waahlaka ill*a* man sabaqa AAalayhi alqawlu minhum wal*a* tukh*at*ibnee fee alla*th*eena **th**&#x61;lamoo innahum mughraqoon**a**

## 23:28

Fai*tha* istawayta anta waman maAAaka AAal*a* alfulki faquli al*h*amdu lill*a*hi alla*th*ee najj*a*n*a* mina alqawmi a**l****thth***a*limeen**a**

## 23:29

Waqul rabbi anzilnee munzalan mub*a*rakan waanta khayru almunzileen**a**

## 23:30

Inna fee *tha*lika la*a*y*a*tin wain kunn*a* lamubtaleen**a**

## 23:31

Thumma anshan*a* min baAAdihim qarnan *a*khareen**a**

## 23:32

Faarsaln*a* feehim rasoolan minhum ani oAAbudoo All*a*ha m*a* lakum min il*a*hin ghayruhu afal*a* tattaqoon**a**

## 23:33

Waq*a*la almalao min qawmihi alla*th*eena kafaroo waka*thth*aboo biliq*a*i al*a*khirati waatrafn*a*hum fee al*h*ay*a*ti a**l**dduny*a* m*a* h*atha* ill*a* basharun mithlukum yakulu mimm*a* takuloona minhu wayashrabu mimm*a* tashraboon**a**

## 23:34

Walain a*t*aAAtum basharan mithlakum innakum i*th*an lakh*a*siroon**a**

## 23:35

AyaAAidukum annakum i*tha* mittum wakuntum tur*a*ban waAA&#x69;**th***a*man annakum mukhrajoon**a**

## 23:36

Hayh*a*ta hayh*a*ta lim*a* tooAAadoon**a**

## 23:37

In hiya ill*a* *h*ay*a*tun*a* a**l**dduny*a* namootu wana*h*y*a* wam*a* na*h*nu bimabAAootheen**a**

## 23:38

In huwa ill*a* rajulun iftar*a* AAal*a* All*a*hi ka*th*iban wam*a* na*h*nu lahu bimumineen**a**

## 23:39

Q*a*la rabbi on*s*urnee bim*a* ka*thth*aboon**i**

## 23:40

Q*a*la AAamm*a* qaleelin layu*s*bi*h*unna n*a*dimeen**a**

## 23:41

Faakha*th*athumu a**l***ss*ay*h*atu bi**a**l*h*aqqi fajaAAaln*a*hum ghuth*a*an fabuAAdan lilqawmi a**l****thth***a*limeen**a**

## 23:42

Thumma anshan*a* min baAAdihim quroonan *a*khareen**a**

## 23:43

M*a* tasbiqu min ommatin ajalah*a* wam*a* yastakhiroon**a**

## 23:44

Thumma arsaln*a* rusulan*a* tatr*a* kulla m*a* j*a*a ommatan rasooluh*a* ka*thth*aboohu faatbaAAn*a* baAA*d*ahum baAA*d*an wajaAAaln*a*hum a*ha*deetha fabuAAdan liqawmin l*a* yuminoon**a**

## 23:45

Thumma arsaln*a* moos*a* waakh*a*hu h*a*roona bi*a*y*a*tin*a* wasul*ta*nin mubeen**in**

## 23:46

Il*a* firAAawna wamalaihi fa**i**stakbaroo wak*a*noo qawman AA*a*leen**a**

## 23:47

Faq*a*loo anuminu libasharayni mithlin*a* waqawmuhum*a* lan*a* AA*a*bidoon**a**

## 23:48

Faka*thth*aboohum*a* fak*a*noo mina almuhlakeen**a**

## 23:49

Walaqad *a*tayn*a* moos*a* alkit*a*ba laAAallahum yahtadoon**a**

## 23:50

WajaAAaln*a* ibna maryama waommahu *a*yatan wa*a*wayn*a*hum*a* il*a* rabwatin *tha*ti qar*a*rin wamaAAeen**in**

## 23:51

Y*a* ayyuh*a* a**l**rrusulu kuloo mina a**l***tt*ayyib*a*ti wa**i**AAmaloo *sa*li*h*an innee bim*a* taAAmaloona AAaleem**un**

## 23:52

Wainna h*ath*ihi ommatukum ommatan w*ah*idatan waan*a* rabbukum fa**i**ttaqoon**i**

## 23:53

Fataqa*tt*aAAoo amrahum baynahum zuburan kullu *h*izbin bim*a* ladayhim fari*h*oon**a**

## 23:54

Fa*th*arhum fee ghamratihim *h*att*a* *h*een**in**

## 23:55

Aya*h*saboona annam*a* numidduhum bihi min m*a*lin wabaneen**a**

## 23:56

Nus*a*riAAu lahum fee alkhayr*a*ti bal l*a* yashAAuroon**a**

## 23:57

Inna alla*th*eena hum min khashyati rabbihim mushfiqoon**a**

## 23:58

Wa**a**lla*th*eena hum bi*a*y*a*ti rabbihim yuminoon**a**

## 23:59

Wa**a**lla*th*eena hum birabbihim l*a* yushrikoon**a**

## 23:60

Wa**a**lla*th*eena yutoona m*a* *a*taw waquloobuhum wajilatun annahum il*a* rabbihim r*a*jiAAoon**a**

## 23:61

Ol*a*ika yus*a*riAAoona fee alkhayr*a*ti wahum lah*a* s*a*biqoon**a**

## 23:62

Wal*a* nukallifu nafsan ill*a* wusAAah*a* waladayn*a* kit*a*bun yan*t*iqu bi**a**l*h*aqqi wahum l*a* y&#x75;**th**&#x6C;amoon**a**

## 23:63

Bal quloobuhum fee ghamratin min h*atha* walahum aAAm*a*lun min dooni *tha*lika hum lah*a* AA*a*miloon**a**

## 23:64

*H*att*a* i*tha* akha*th*n*a* mutrafeehim bi**a**lAAa*tha*bi i*tha* hum yajaroon**a**

## 23:65

L*a* tajaroo alyawma innakum minn*a* l*a* tun*s*aroon**a**

## 23:66

Qad k*a*nat *a*y*a*tee tutl*a* AAalaykum fakuntum AAal*a* aAAq*a*bikum tanki*s*oon**a**

## 23:67

Mustakbireena bihi s*a*miran tahjuroon**a**

## 23:68

Afalam yaddabbaroo alqawla am j*a*ahum m*a* lam yati *a*b*a*ahumu alawwaleen**a**

## 23:69

Am lam yaAArifoo rasoolahum fahum lahu munkiroon**a**

## 23:70

Am yaqooloona bihi jinnatun bal j*a*ahum bi**a**l*h*aqqi waaktharuhum lil*h*aqqi k*a*rihoon**a**

## 23:71

Walawi ittabaAAa al*h*aqqu ahw*a*ahum lafasadati a**l**ssam*a*w*a*tu wa**a**lar*d*u waman feehinna bal atayn*a*hum bi*th*ikrihim fahum AAan *th*ikrihim muAAri*d*oon**a**

## 23:72

Am tasaluhum kharjan fakhar*a*ju rabbika khayrun wahuwa khayru a**l**rr*a*ziqeen**a**

## 23:73

Wainnaka latadAAoohum il*a* *s*ir*at*in mustaqeem**in**

## 23:74

Wainna alla*th*eena l*a* yuminoona bi**a**l*a*khirati AAani a**l***ss*ir*at*i lan*a*kiboon**a**

## 23:75

Walaw ra*h*imn*a*hum wakashafn*a* m*a* bihim min *d*urrin lalajjoo fee *t*ughy*a*nihim yaAAmahoon**a**

## 23:76

Walaqad akha*th*n*a*hum bi**a**lAAa*tha*bi fam*a* istak*a*noo lirabbihim wam*a* yata*d*arraAAoon**a**

## 23:77

*H*att*a* i*tha* fata*h*n*a* AAalayhim b*a*ban *tha* AAa*tha*bin shadeedin i*tha* hum feehi mublisoon**a**

## 23:78

Wahuwa alla*th*ee anshaa lakumu a**l**ssamAAa wa**a**lab*sa*ra wa**a**lafidata qaleelan m*a* tashkuroon**a**

## 23:79

Wahuwa alla*th*ee *th*araakum fee alar*d*i wailayhi tu*h*sharoon**a**

## 23:80

Wahuwa alla*th*ee yu*h*yee wayumeetu walahu ikhtil*a*fu allayli wa**al**nnah*a*ri afal*a* taAAqiloon**a**

## 23:81

Bal q*a*loo mithla m*a* q*a*la alawwaloon**a**

## 23:82

Q*a*loo ai*tha* mitn*a* wakunn*a* tur*a*ban waAA&#x69;**th***a*man ainn*a* lamabAAoothoon**a**

## 23:83

Laqad wuAAidn*a* na*h*nu wa*a*b*a*on*a* h*atha* min qablu in h*atha* ill*a* as*at*eeru alawwaleen**a**

## 23:84

Qul limani alar*d*u waman feeh*a* in kuntum taAAlamoon**a**

## 23:85

Sayaqooloona lill*a*hi qul afal*a* ta*th*akkaroon**a**

## 23:86

Qul man rabbu a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti a**l**ssabAAi warabbu alAAarshi alAA&#x61;**th**&#x65;em**i**

## 23:87

Sayaqooloona lill*a*hi qul afal*a* tattaqoon**a**

## 23:88

Qul man biyadihi malakootu kulli shayin wahuwa yujeeru wal*a* yuj*a*ru AAalayhi in kuntum taAAlamoon**a**

## 23:89

Sayaqooloona lill*a*hi qul faann*a* tus*h*aroon**a**

## 23:90

Bal atayn*a*hum bi**a**l*h*aqqi wainnahum lak*ath*iboon**a**

## 23:91

M*a* ittakha*th*a All*a*hu min waladin wam*a* k*a*na maAAahu min il*a*hin i*th*an la*th*ahaba kullu il*a*hin bim*a* khalaqa walaAAal*a* baAA*d*uhum AAal*a* baAA*d*in sub*ha*na All*a*hi AAamm*a* ya*s*ifoon**a**

## 23:92

AA*a*limi alghaybi wa**al**shshah*a*dati fataAA*a*l*a* AAamm*a* yushrikoon**a**

## 23:93

Qul rabbi imm*a* turiyannee m*a* yooAAadoon**a**

## 23:94

Rabbi fal*a* tajAAalnee fee alqawmi a**l****thth***a*limeen**a**

## 23:95

Wainn*a* AAal*a* an nuriyaka m*a* naAAiduhum laq*a*diroon**a**

## 23:96

IdfaAA bi**a**llatee hiya a*h*sanu a**l**ssayyiata na*h*nu aAAlamu bim*a* ya*s*ifoon**a**

## 23:97

Waqul rabbi aAAoo*th*u bika min hamaz*a*ti a**l**shshay*at*een**i**

## 23:98

WaaAAoo*th*u bika rabbi an ya*hd*uroon**i**

## 23:99

*H*att*a* i*tha* j*a*a a*h*adahumu almawtu q*a*la rabbi irjiAAoon**i**

## 23:100

LaAAallee aAAmalu *sa*li*h*an feem*a* taraktu kall*a* innah*a* kalimatun huwa q*a*iluh*a* wamin war*a*ihim barzakhun il*a* yawmi yubAAathoon**a**

## 23:101

Fai*tha* nufikha fee a**l***ss*oori fal*a* ans*a*ba baynahum yawmai*th*in wal*a* yatas*a*aloon**a**

## 23:102

Faman thaqulat maw*a*zeenuhu faol*a*ika humu almufli*h*oon**a**

## 23:103

Waman khaffat maw*a*zeenuhu faol*a*ika alla*th*eena khasiroo anfusahum fee jahannama kh*a*lidoon**a**

## 23:104

Talfa*h*u wujoohahumu a**l**nn*a*ru wahum feeh*a* k*a*li*h*oon**a**

## 23:105

Alam takun *a*y*a*tee tutl*a* AAalaykum fakuntum bih*a* tuka*thth*iboon**a**

## 23:106

Q*a*loo rabban*a* ghalabat AAalayn*a* shiqwatun*a* wakunn*a* qawman *da*lleen**a**

## 23:107

Rabban*a* akhrijn*a* minh*a* fain AAudn*a* fainn*a* **th***a*limoon**a**

## 23:108

Q*a*la ikhsaoo feeh*a* wal*a* tukallimoon**i**

## 23:109

Innahu k*a*na fareequn min AAib*a*dee yaqooloona rabban*a* *a*mann*a* fa**i**ghfir lan*a* wa**i**r*h*amn*a* waanta khayru a**l**rr*ah*imeen**a**

## 23:110

Fa**i**ttakha*th*tumoohum sikhriyyan *h*att*a* ansawkum *th*ikree wakuntum minhum ta*dh*akoon**a**

## 23:111

Innee jazaytuhumu alyawma bim*a* *s*abaroo annahum humu alf*a*izoon**a**

## 23:112

Q*a*la kam labithtum fee alar*d*i AAadada sineen**a**

## 23:113

Q*a*loo labithn*a* yawman aw baAA*d*a yawmin fa**i**sali alAA*a*ddeen**a**

## 23:114

Q*a*la in labithtum ill*a* qaleelan law annakum kuntum taAAlamoon**a**

## 23:115

Afa*h*asibtum annam*a* khalaqn*a*kum AAabathan waannakum ilayn*a* l*a* turjaAAoon**a**

## 23:116

FataAA*a*l*a* All*a*hu almaliku al*h*aqqu l*a* il*a*ha ill*a* huwa rabbu alAAarshi alkareem**i**

## 23:117

Waman yadAAu maAAa All*a*hi il*a*han *a*khara l*a* burh*a*na lahu bihi fainnam*a* *h*is*a*buhu AAinda rabbihi innahu l*a* yufli*h*u alk*a*firoon**a**

## 23:118

Waqul rabbi ighfir wa**i**r*h*am waanta khayru a**l**rr*ah*imeen**a**

## 24:1

Sooratun anzaln*a*h*a* wafara*d*n*a*h*a* waanzaln*a* feeh*a* *a*y*a*tin bayyin*a*tin laAAallakum ta*th*akkaroon**a**

## 24:2

A**l**zz*a*niyatu wa**al**zz*a*nee fa**i**jlidoo kulla w*ah*idin minhum*a* miata jaldatin wal*a* takhu*th*kum bihim*a* rafatun fee deeni All*a*hi in kuntum tuminoona bi**A**ll*a*hi wa**a**lyawmi al*a*khiri walyashhad AAa*tha*bahum*a* *ta*ifatun mina almumineen**a**

## 24:3

A**l**zz*a*nee l*a* yanki*h*u ill*a* z*a*niyatan aw mushrikatan wa**al**zz*a*niyatu l*a* yanki*h*uh*a* ill*a* z*a*nin aw mushrikun wa*h*urrima *tha*lika AAal*a* almumineen**a**

## 24:4

Wa**a**lla*th*eena yarmoona almu*hs*an*a*ti thumma lam yatoo biarbaAAati shuhad*a*a fa**i**jlidoohum tham*a*neena jaldatan wal*a* taqbaloo lahum shah*a*datan abadan waol*a*ika humu alf*a*siqoon**a**

## 24:5

Ill*a* alla*th*eena t*a*boo min baAAdi *tha*lika waa*s*la*h*oo fainna All*a*ha ghafoorun ra*h*eem**un**

## 24:6

Wa**a**lla*th*eena yarmoona azw*a*jahum walam yakun lahum shuhad*a*o ill*a* anfusuhum fashah*a*datu a*h*adihim arbaAAu shah*a*d*a*tin bi**A**ll*a*hi innahu lamina a**l***ssa*diqeen**a**

## 24:7

Wa**a**lkh*a*misatu anna laAAnata All*a*hi AAalayhi in k*a*na mina alk*ath*ibeen**a**

## 24:8

Wayadrao AAanh*a* alAAa*tha*ba an tashhada arbaAAa shah*a*d*a*tin bi**A**ll*a*hi innahu lamina alk*ath*ibeen**a**

## 24:9

Wa**a**lkh*a*misata anna gha*d*aba All*a*hi AAalayh*a* in k*a*na mina a**l***ssa*diqeen**a**

## 24:10

Walawl*a* fa*d*lu All*a*hi AAalaykum wara*h*matuhu waanna All*a*ha taww*a*bun *h*akeem**un**

## 24:11

Inna alla*th*eena j*a*oo bi**a**lifki AAu*s*batun minkum l*a* ta*h*saboohu sharran lakum bal huwa khayrun lakum likulli imriin minhum m*a* iktasaba mina alithmi wa**a**lla*th*ee tawall*a* kibrahu minhum lahu AAa*tha*bun AA&#x61;**th**&#x65;em**un**

## 24:12

Lawl*a* i*th* samiAAtumoohu **th**&#x61;nna almuminoona wa**a**lmumin*a*tu bianfusihim khayran waq*a*loo h*atha* ifkun mubeen**un**

## 24:13

Lawl*a* j*a*oo AAalayhi biarbaAAati shuhad*a*a fai*th* lam yatoo bi**al**shshuhad*a*i faol*a*ika AAinda All*a*hi humu alk*ath*iboon**a**

## 24:14

Walawl*a* fa*d*lu All*a*hi AAalaykum wara*h*matuhu fee a**l**dduny*a* wa**a**l*a*khirati lamassakum fee m*a* afa*d*tum feehi AAa*tha*bun AA&#x61;**th**&#x65;em**un**

## 24:15

I*th* talaqqawnahu bialsinatikum wataqooloona biafw*a*hikum m*a* laysa lakum bihi AAilmun wata*h*saboonahu hayyinan wahuwa AAinda All*a*hi AA&#x61;**th**&#x65;em**un**

## 24:16

Walawl*a* i*th* samiAAtumoohu qultum m*a* yakoonu lan*a* an natakallama bih*atha* sub*ha*naka h*atha* buht*a*nun AA&#x61;**th**&#x65;em**un**

## 24:17

YaAA&#x69;**th**&#x75;kumu All*a*hu an taAAoodoo limithlihi abadan in kuntum mumineen**a**

## 24:18

Wayubayyinu All*a*hu lakumu al*a*y*a*ti wa**A**ll*a*hu AAaleemun *h*akeem**un**

## 24:19

Inna alla*th*eena yu*h*ibboona an tasheeAAa alf*ah*ishatu fee alla*th*eena *a*manoo lahum AAa*tha*bun aleemun fee a**l**dduny*a* wa**a**l*a*khirati wa**A**ll*a*hu yaAAlamu waantum l*a* taAAlamoon**a**

## 24:20

Walawl*a* fa*d*lu All*a*hi AAalaykum wara*h*matuhu waanna All*a*ha raoofun ra*h*eem**un**

## 24:21

Y*a* ayyuh*a* alla*th*eena *a*manoo l*a* tattabiAAoo khu*t*uw*a*ti a**l**shshay*ta*ni waman yattabiAA khu*t*uw*a*ti a**l**shshay*ta*ni fainnahu yamuru bi**a**lfa*h*sh*a*i wa**a**lmunkari walawl*a* fa*d*lu All*a*hi AAalaykum wara*h*matuhu m*a* zak*a* minkum min a*h*adin abadan wal*a*kinna All*a*ha yuzakkee man yash*a*o wa**A**ll*a*hu sameeAAun AAaleem**un**

## 24:22

Wal*a* yatali oloo alfa*d*li minkum wa**al**ssaAAati an yutoo olee alqurb*a* wa**a**lmas*a*keena wa**a**lmuh*a*jireena fee sabeeli All*a*hi walyaAAfoo walya*s*fa*h*oo al*a* tu*h*ibboona an yaghfira All*a*hu lakum wa**A**ll*a*hu ghafoorun ra*h*eem**un**

## 24:23

Inna alla*th*eena yarmoona almu*hs*an*a*ti algh*a*fil*a*ti almumin*a*ti luAAinoo fee a**l**dduny*a* wa**a**l*a*khirati walahum AAa*tha*bun AA&#x61;**th**&#x65;em**un**

## 24:24

Yawma tashhadu AAalayhim alsinatuhum waaydeehim waarjuluhum bim*a* k*a*noo yaAAmaloon**a**

## 24:25

Yawmai*th*in yuwaffeehimu All*a*hu deenahumu al*h*aqqa wayaAAlamoona anna All*a*ha huwa al*h*aqqu almubeen**u**

## 24:26

Alkhabeeth*a*tu lilkhabeetheena wa**a**lkhabeethoona lilkhabeeth*a*ti wa**al***tt*ayyib*a*tu li**l***tt*ayyibeena wa**al***tt*ayyiboona li**l***tt*ayyib*a*ti ol*a*ika mubarraoona mimm*a* yaqooloona lahum maghfiratun warizqun kareem**un**

## 24:27

Y*a* ayyuh*a* alla*th*eena *a*manoo l*a* tadkhuloo buyootan ghayra buyootikum *h*att*a* tastanisoo watusallimoo AAal*a* ahlih*a* *tha*likum khayrun lakum laAAallakum ta*th*akkaroon**a**

## 24:28

Fain lam tajidoo feeh*a* a*h*adan fal*a* tadkhulooh*a* *h*att*a* yu*th*ana lakum wain qeela lakumu irjiAAoo fa**i**rjiAAoo huwa azk*a* lakum wa**A**ll*a*hu bim*a* taAAmaloona AAaleem**un**

## 24:29

Laysa AAalaykum jun*ah*un an tadkhuloo buyootan ghayra maskoonatin feeh*a* mat*a*AAun lakum wa**A**ll*a*hu yaAAlamu m*a* tubdoona wam*a* taktumoon**a**

## 24:30

Qul lilmumineena yaghu*dd*oo min ab*sa*rihum waya*h*f&#x61;**th**&#x6F;o furoojahum *tha*lika azk*a* lahum inna All*a*ha khabeerun bim*a* ya*s*naAAoon**a**

## 24:31

Waqul lilmumin*a*ti yagh*d*u*d*na min ab*sa*rihinna waya*h*f&#x61;**th**&#x6E;a furoojahunna wal*a* yubdeena zeenatahunna ill*a* m*a* **th**&#x61;hara minh*a* walya*d*ribna bikhumurihinna AAal*a* juyoobihinna wal*a* yubdeena zeenatahunna ill*a* libuAAoolatihinna aw *a*b*a*ihinna aw *a*b*a*i buAAoolatihinna aw abn*a*ihinna aw abn*a*i buAAoolatihinna aw ikhw*a*nihinna aw banee ikhw*a*nihinna aw banee akhaw*a*tihinna aw nis*a*ihinna aw m*a* malakat aym*a*nuhunna awi a**l**tt*a*biAAeena ghayri olee alirbati mina a**l**rrij*a*li awi a**l***tt*ifli alla*th*eena lam y&#x61;**th**&#x68;aroo AAal*a* AAawr*a*ti a**l**nnis*a*i wal*a* ya*d*ribna biarjulihinna liyuAAlama m*a* yukhfeena min zeenatihinna watooboo il*a* All*a*hi jameeAAan ayyuh*a* almuminoona laAAallakum tufli*h*oon**a**

## 24:32

Waanki*h*oo alay*a*m*a* minkum wa**al***ssa*li*h*eena min AAib*a*dikum waim*a*ikum in yakoonoo fuqar*a*a yughnihimu All*a*hu min fa*d*lihi wa**A**ll*a*hu w*a*siAAun AAaleem**un**

## 24:33

WalyastaAAfifi alla*th*eena l*a* yajidoona nik*ah*an *h*att*a* yughniyahumu All*a*hu min fa*d*lihi wa**a**lla*th*eena yabtaghoona alkit*a*ba mimm*a* malakat aym*a*nukum fak*a*tiboohum in AAalimtum feehim khayran wa*a*toohum min m*a*li All*a*hi alla*th*ee *a*t*a*kum wal*a* tukrihoo fatay*a*tikum AAal*a* albigh*a*i in aradna ta*h*a*ss*unan litabtaghoo AAara*d*a al*h*ay*a*ti a**l**dduny*a* waman yukrihhunna fainna All*a*ha min baAAdi ikr*a*hihinna ghafoorun ra*h*eem**un**

## 24:34

Walaqad anzaln*a* ilaykum *a*y*a*tin mubayyin*a*tin wamathalan mina alla*th*eena khalaw min qablikum wamawAA&#x69;**th**&#x61;tan lilmuttaqeen**a**

## 24:35

All*a*hu nooru a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i mathalu noorihi kamishk*a*tin feeh*a* mi*s*b*ah*un almi*s*b*ah*u fee zuj*a*jatin a**l**zzuj*a*jatu kaannah*a* kawkabun durriyyun yooqadu min shajaratin mub*a*rakatin zaytoonatin l*a* sharqiyyatin wal*a* gharbiyyatin yak*a*du zaytuh*a* yu*d*eeo walaw lam tamsashu n*a*run noorun AAal*a* noorin yahdee All*a*hu linoorihi man yash*a*o waya*d*ribu All*a*hu alamth*a*la li**l**nn*a*si wa**A**ll*a*hu bikulli shayin AAaleem**un**

## 24:36

Fee buyootin a*th*ina All*a*hu an turfaAAa wayu*th*kara feeh*a* ismuhu yusabbi*h*u lahu feeh*a* bi**a**lghuduwwi wa**a**l*asa*l**i**

## 24:37

Rij*a*lun l*a* tulheehim tij*a*ratun wal*a* bayAAun AAan *th*ikri All*a*hi waiq*a*mi a**l***ss*al*a*ti waeet*a*i a**l**zzak*a*ti yakh*a*foona yawman tataqallabu feehi alquloobu wa**a**lab*sa*r**u**

## 24:38

Liyajziyahumu All*a*hu a*h*sana m*a* AAamiloo wayazeedahum min fa*d*lihi wa**A**ll*a*hu yarzuqu man yash*a*o bighayri *h*is*a*b**in**

## 24:39

Wa**a**lla*th*eena kafaroo aAAm*a*luhum kasar*a*bin biqeeAAatin ya*h*sabuhu a**l****thth**&#x61;m*a*nu m*a*an *h*att*a* i*tha* j*a*ahu lam yajidhu shayan wawajada All*a*ha AAindahu fawaff*a*hu *h*is*a*bahu wa**A**ll*a*hu sareeAAu al*h*is*a*b**i**

## 24:40

Aw k&#x61;**th**&#x75;lum*a*tin fee ba*h*rin lujjiyyin yaghsh*a*hu mawjun min fawqihi mawjun min fawqihi sa*ha*bun **th**&#x75;lum*a*tun baAA*d*uh*a* fawqa baAA*d*in i*tha* akhraja yadahu lam yakad yar*a*h*a* waman lam yajAAali All*a*hu lahu nooran fam*a* lahu min noor**in**

## 24:41

Alam tara anna All*a*ha yusabbi*h*u lahu man fee a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i wa**al***tt*ayru *sa*ff*a*tin kullun qad AAalima *s*al*a*tahu watasbee*h*ahu wa**A**ll*a*hu AAaleemun bim*a* yafAAaloon**a**

## 24:42

Walill*a*hi mulku a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i wail*a* All*a*hi alma*s*eer**u**

## 24:43

Alam tara anna All*a*ha yuzjee sa*ha*ban thumma yuallifu baynahu thumma yajAAaluhu ruk*a*man fatar*a* alwadqa yakhruju min khil*a*lihi wayunazzilu mina a**l**ssam*a*i min jib*a*lin feeh*a* min baradin fayu*s*eebu bihi man yash*a*o waya*s*rifuhu AAan man yash*a*o yak*a*du san*a* barqihi ya*th*habu bi**a**lab*sa*r**i**

## 24:44

Yuqallibu All*a*hu allayla wa**al**nnah*a*ra inna fee *tha*lika laAAibratan liolee alab*sa*r**i**

## 24:45

Wa**A**ll*a*hu khalaqa kulla d*a*bbatin min m*a*in faminhum man yamshee AAal*a* ba*t*nihi waminhum man yamshee AAal*a* rijlayni waminhum man yamshee AAal*a* arbaAAin yakhluqu All*a*hu m*a* yash*a*o inna All*a*ha AAal*a* kulli shayin qadeer**un**

## 24:46

Laqad anzaln*a* *a*y*a*tin mubayyin*a*tin wa**A**ll*a*hu yahdee man yash*a*o il*a* *s*ir*at*in mustaqeem**in**

## 24:47

Wayaqooloona *a*mann*a* bi**A**ll*a*hi wabi**al**rrasooli waa*t*aAAn*a* thumma yatawall*a* fareequn minhum min baAAdi *tha*lika wam*a* ol*a*ika bi**a**lmumineen**a**

## 24:48

Wai*tha* duAAoo il*a* All*a*hi warasoolihi liya*h*kuma baynahum i*tha* fareequn minhum muAAri*d*oon**a**

## 24:49

Wain yakun lahumu al*h*aqqu yatoo ilayhi mu*th*AAineen**a**

## 24:50

Afee quloobihim mara*d*un ami irt*a*boo am yakh*a*foona an ya*h*eefa All*a*hu AAalayhim warasooluhu bal ol*a*ika humu a**l****thth***a*limoon**a**

## 24:51

Innam*a* k*a*na qawla almumineena i*tha* duAAoo il*a* All*a*hi warasoolihi liya*h*kuma baynahum an yaqooloo samiAAn*a* waa*t*aAAn*a* waol*a*ika humu almufli*h*oon**a**

## 24:52

Waman yu*t*iAAi All*a*ha warasoolahu wayakhsha All*a*ha wayattaqhi faol*a*ika humu alf*a*izoon**a**

## 24:53

Waaqsamoo bi**A**ll*a*hi jahda aym*a*nihim lain amartahum layakhrujunna qul l*a* tuqsimoo *ta*AAatun maAAroofatun inna All*a*ha khabeerun bim*a* taAAmaloon**a**

## 24:54

Qul a*t*eeAAoo All*a*ha waa*t*eeAAoo a**l**rrasoola fain tawallaw fainnam*a* AAalayhi m*a* *h*ummila waAAalaykum m*a* *h*ummiltum wain tu*t*eeAAoohu tahtadoo wam*a* AAal*a* a**l**rrasooli ill*a* albal*a*ghu almubeen**a**

## 24:55

WaAAada All*a*hu alla*th*eena *a*manoo minkum waAAamiloo a**l***ssa*li*ha*ti layastakhlifannahum fee alar*d*i kam*a* istakhlafa alla*th*eena min qablihim walayumakkinanna lahum deenahumu alla*th*ee irta*da* lahum walayubaddilannahum min baAAdi khawfihim amnan yaAAbudoonanee l*a* yushrikoona bee shayan waman kafara baAAda *tha*lika faol*a*ika humu alf*a*siqoon**a**

## 24:56

Waaqeemoo a**l***ss*al*a*ta wa*a*too a**l**zzak*a*ta waa*t*eeAAoo a**l**rrasoola laAAallakum tur*h*amoon**a**

## 24:57

L*a* ta*h*sabanna alla*th*eena kafaroo muAAjizeena fee alar*d*i wamaw*a*humu a**l**nn*a*ru walabisa alma*s*eer**u**

## 24:58

Y*a* ayyuh*a* alla*th*eena *a*manoo liyasta*th*inkumu alla*th*eena malakat aym*a*nukum wa**a**lla*th*eena lam yablughoo al*h*uluma minkum thal*a*tha marr*a*tin min qabli *s*al*a*ti alfajri wa*h*eena ta*d*aAAoona thiy*a*bakum mina a**l****thth**&#x61;heerati wamin baAAdi *s*al*a*ti alAAish*a*i thal*a*thu AAawr*a*tin lakum laysa AAalaykum wal*a* AAalayhim jun*ah*un baAAdahunna *t*aww*a*foona AAalaykum baAA*d*ukum AAal*a* baAA*d*in ka*tha*lika yubayyinu All*a*hu lakumu al*a*y*a*ti wa**A**ll*a*hu AAaleemun *h*akeem**un**

## 24:59

Wai*tha* balagha ala*t*f*a*lu minkumu al*h*uluma falyasta*th*inoo kam*a* ista*th*ana alla*th*eena min qablihim ka*tha*lika yubayyinu All*a*hu lakum *a*y*a*tihi wa**A**ll*a*hu AAaleemun *h*akeem**un**

## 24:60

Wa**a**lqaw*a*AAidu mina a**l**nnis*a*i all*a*tee l*a* yarjoona nik*ah*an falaysa AAalayhinna jun*ah*un an ya*d*aAAna thiy*a*bahunna ghayra mutabarrij*a*tin bizeenatin waan yastaAAfifna khayrun lahunna wa**A**ll*a*hu sameeAAun AAaleem**un**

## 24:61

Laysa AAal*a* alaAAm*a* *h*arajun wal*a* AAal*a* alaAAraji *h*arajun wal*a* AAal*a* almaree*d*i *h*arajun wal*a* AAal*a* anfusikum an takuloo min buyootikum aw buyooti *a*b*a*ikum aw buyooti ommah*a*tikum aw buyooti ikhw*a*nikum aw buyooti akhaw*a*tikum aw buyooti aAAm*a*mikum aw buyooti AAamm*a*tikum aw buyooti akhw*a*likum aw buyooti kh*a*l*a*tikum aw m*a* malaktum maf*a*ti*h*ahu aw *s*adeeqikum laysa AAalaykum jun*ah*un an takuloo jameeAAan aw asht*a*tan fai*tha* dakhaltum buyootan fasallimoo AAal*a* anfusikum ta*h*iyyatan min AAindi All*a*hi mub*a*rakatan *t*ayyibatan ka*tha*lika yubayyinu All*a*hu lakumu al*a*y*a*ti laAAallakum taAAqiloon**a**

## 24:62

Innam*a* almuminoona alla*th*eena *a*manoo bi**A**ll*a*hi warasoolihi wai*tha* k*a*noo maAAahu AAal*a* amrin j*a*miAAin lam ya*th*haboo *h*att*a* yasta*th*inoohu inna alla*th*eena yasta*th*inoonaka ol*a*ika alla*th*eena yuminoona bi**A**ll*a*hi warasoolihi fai*tha* ista*th*anooka libaAA*d*i shanihim fa*th*an liman shita minhum wa**i**staghfir lahumu All*a*ha inna All*a*ha ghafoorun ra*h*eem**un**

## 24:63

L*a* tajAAaloo duAA*a*a a**l**rrasooli baynakum kaduAA*a*i baAA*d*ikum baAA*d*an qad yaAAlamu All*a*hu alla*th*eena yatasallaloona minkum liw*ath*an falya*hth*ari alla*th*eena yukh*a*lifoona AAan amrihi an tu*s*eebahum fitnatun aw yu*s*eebahum AAa*tha*bun aleem**un**

## 24:64

Al*a* inna lill*a*hi m*a* fee a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i qad yaAAlamu m*a* antum AAalayhi wayawma yurjaAAoona ilayhi fayunabbiohum bim*a* AAamiloo wa**A**ll*a*hu bikulli shayin AAaleem**un**

## 25:1

Tab*a*raka alla*th*ee nazzala alfurq*a*na AAal*a* AAabdihi liyakoona lilAA*a*lameena na*th*eer*a***n**

## 25:2

Alla*th*ee lahu mulku a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i walam yattakhi*th* waladan walam yakun lahu shareekun fee almulki wakhalaqa kulla shayin faqaddarahu taqdeer*a***n**

## 25:3

Wa**i**ttakha*th*oo min doonihi *a*lihatan l*a* yakhluqoona shayan wahum yukhlaqoona wal*a* yamlikoona lianfusihim *d*arran wal*a* nafAAan wal*a* yamlikoona mawtan wal*a* *h*ay*a*tan wal*a* nushoor*a***n**

## 25:4

Waq*a*la alla*th*eena kafaroo in h*atha* ill*a* ifkun iftar*a*hu waaAA*a*nahu AAalayhi qawmun *a*kharoona faqad j*a*oo **th**&#x75;lman wazoor*a***n**

## 25:5

Waq*a*loo as*at*eeru alawwaleena iktatabah*a* fahiya tuml*a* AAalayhi bukratan waa*s*eel*a***n**

## 25:6

Qul anzalahu alla*th*ee yaAAlamu a**l**ssirra fee a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i innahu k*a*na ghafooran ra*h*eem*a***n**

## 25:7

Waq*a*loo m*a*li h*atha* a**l**rrasooli yakulu a**l***tt*aAA*a*ma wayamshee fee alasw*a*qi lawl*a* onzila ilayhi malakun fayakoona maAAahu na*th*eer*a***n**

## 25:8

Aw yulq*a* ilayhi kanzun aw takoonu lahu jannatun yakulu minh*a* waq*a*la a**l****thth***a*limoona in tattabiAAoona ill*a* rajulan mas*h*oor*a***n**

## 25:9

O&#x6E;**th**&#x75;r kayfa *d*araboo laka alamth*a*la fa*d*alloo fal*a* yasta*t*eeAAoona sabeel*a***n**

## 25:10

Tab*a*raka alla*th*ee in sh*a*a jaAAala laka khayran min *tha*lika jann*a*tin tajree min ta*h*tih*a* alanh*a*ru wayajAAal laka qu*s*oor*a***n**

## 25:11

Bal ka*thth*aboo bi**al**ss*a*AAati waaAAtadn*a* liman ka*thth*aba bi**al**ss*a*AAati saAAeer*a***n**

## 25:12

I*tha* raathum min mak*a*nin baAAeedin samiAAoo lah*a* taghayy&#x75;**th**&#x61;n wazafeer*a***n**

## 25:13

Wai*tha* olqoo minh*a* mak*a*nan *d*ayyiqan muqarraneena daAAaw hun*a*lika thuboor*a***n**

## 25:14

L*a* tadAAoo alyawma thubooran w*ah*idan wa**o**dAAoo thubooran katheer*a***n**

## 25:15

Qul a*tha*lika khayrun am jannatu alkhuldi allatee wuAAida almuttaqoona k*a*nat lahum jaz*a*an wama*s*eer*a***n**

## 25:16

Lahum feeh*a* m*a* yash*a*oona kh*a*lideena k*a*na AAal*a* rabbika waAAdan masool*a***n**

## 25:17

Wayawma ya*h*shuruhum wam*a* yaAAbudoona min dooni All*a*hi fayaqoolu aantum a*d*laltum AAib*a*dee h*a*ol*a*i am hum *d*alloo a**l**ssabeel**a**

## 25:18

Q*a*loo sub*ha*naka m*a* k*a*na yanbaghee lan*a* an nattakhi*th*a min doonika min awliy*a*a wal*a*kin mattaAAtahum wa*a*b*a*ahum *h*att*a* nasoo a**l***thth*ikra wak*a*noo qawman boor*a***n**

## 25:19

Faqad ka*thth*abookum bim*a* taqooloona fam*a* tasta*t*eeAAoona *s*arfan wal*a* na*s*ran waman y&#x61;**th**&#x6C;im minkum nu*th*iqhu AAa*tha*ban kabeer*a***n**

## 25:20

Wam*a* arsaln*a* qablaka mina almursaleena ill*a* innahum layakuloona a**l***tt*aAA*a*ma wayamshoona fee alasw*a*qi wajaAAaln*a* baAA*d*akum libaAA*d*in fitnatan ata*s*biroona wak*a*na rabbuka ba*s*eer*a***n**

## 25:21

Waq*a*la alla*th*eena l*a* yarjoona liq*a*an*a* lawl*a* onzila AAalayn*a* almal*a*ikatu aw nar*a* rabban*a* laqadi istakbaroo fee anfusihim waAAataw AAutuwwan kabeer*a***n**

## 25:22

Yawma yarawna almal*a*ikata l*a* bushr*a* yawmai*th*in lilmujrimeena wayaqooloona *h*ijran ma*h*joor*a***n**

## 25:23

Waqadimn*a* il*a* m*a* AAamiloo min AAamalin fajaAAaln*a*hu hab*a*an manthoor*a***n**

## 25:24

A*s**ha*bu aljannati yawmai*th*in khayrun mustaqarran waa*h*sanu maqeel*a***n**

## 25:25

Wayawma tashaqqaqu a**l**ssam*a*o bi**a**lgham*a*mi wanuzzila almal*a*ikatu tanzeel*a***n**

## 25:26

Almulku yawmai*th*in al*h*aqqu li**l**rra*h*m*a*ni wak*a*na yawman AAal*a* alk*a*fireena AAaseer*a***n**

## 25:27

Wayawma yaAAa*dd*u a**l****thth***a*limu AAal*a* yadayhi yaqoolu y*a* laytanee ittakha*th*tu maAAa a**l**rrasooli sabeel*a***n**

## 25:28

Y*a* waylat*a* laytanee lam attakhi*th* ful*a*nan khaleel*a***n**

## 25:29

Laqad a*d*allanee AAani a**l***thth*ikri baAAda i*th* j*a*anee wak*a*na a**l**shshay*ta*nu lilins*a*ni kha*th*ool*a***n**

## 25:30

Waq*a*la a**l**rrasoolu y*a* rabbi inna qawmee ittakha*th*oo h*atha* alqur*a*na mahjoor*a***n**

## 25:31

Waka*tha*lika jaAAaln*a* likulli nabiyyin AAaduwwan mina almujrimeena wakaf*a* birabbika h*a*diyan wana*s*eer*a***n**

## 25:32

Waq*a*la alla*th*eena kafaroo lawl*a* nuzzila AAalayhi alqur*a*nu jumlatan w*ah*idatan ka*tha*lika linuthabbita bihi fu*a*daka warattaln*a*hu tarteel*a***n**

## 25:33

Wal*a* yatoonaka bimathalin ill*a* jin*a*ka bi**a**l*h*aqqi waa*h*sana tafseer*a***n**

## 25:34

Alla*th*eena yu*h*sharoona AAal*a* wujoohihim il*a* jahannama ol*a*ika sharrun mak*a*nan waa*d*allu sabeel*a***n**

## 25:35

Walaqad *a*tayn*a* moos*a* alkit*a*ba wajaAAaln*a* maAAahu akh*a*hu h*a*roona wazeer*a***n**

## 25:36

Faquln*a* i*th*hab*a* il*a* alqawmi alla*th*eena ka*thth*aboo bi*a*y*a*tin*a* fadammarn*a*hum tadmeer*a***n**

## 25:37

Waqawma noo*h*in lamm*a* ka*thth*aboo a**l**rrusula aghraqn*a*hum wajaAAaln*a*hum li**l**nn*a*si *a*yatan waaAAtadn*a* li**l****thth***a*limeena AAa*tha*ban aleem*a***n**

## 25:38

WaAA*a*dan wathamooda waa*s**ha*ba a**l**rrassi waquroonan bayna *tha*lika katheer*a***n**

## 25:39

Wakullan *d*arabn*a* lahu alamth*a*la wakullan tabbarn*a* tatbeer*a***n**

## 25:40

Walaqad ataw AAal*a* alqaryati allatee om*t*irat ma*t*ara a**l**ssawi afalam yakoonoo yarawnah*a* bal k*a*noo l*a* yarjoona nushoor*a***n**

## 25:41

Wai*tha* raawka in yattakhi*th*oonaka ill*a* huzuwan ah*atha* alla*th*ee baAAatha All*a*hu rasool*a***n**

## 25:42

In k*a*da layu*d*illun*a* AAan *a*lihatin*a* lawl*a* an *s*abarn*a* AAalayh*a&#x20;*&#x77;asawfa yaAAlamoona *h*eena yarawna alAAa*tha*ba man a*d*allu sabeel*a***n**

## 25:43

Araayta mani ittakha*th*a il*a*hahu haw*a*hu afaanta takoonu AAalayhi wakeel*a***n**

## 25:44

Am ta*h*sabu anna aktharahum yasmaAAoona aw yaAAqiloona in hum ill*a* ka**a**lanAA*a*mi bal hum a*d*allu sabeel*a***n**

## 25:45

Alam tara il*a* rabbika kayfa madda a**l****thth**&#x69;lla walaw sh*a*a lajaAAalahu s*a*kinan thumma jaAAaln*a* a**l**shshamsa AAalayhi daleel*a***n**

## 25:46

Thumma qaba*d*n*a*hu ilayn*a* qab*d*an yaseer*a***n**

## 25:47

Wahuwa alla*th*ee jaAAala lakumu allayla lib*a*san wa**al**nnawma sub*a*tan wajaAAala a**l**nnah*a*ra nushoor*a***n**

## 25:48

Wahuwa alla*th*ee arsala a**l**rriy*ah*a bushran bayna yaday ra*h*matihi waanzaln*a* mina a**l**ssam*a*i m*a*an *t*ahoor*a***n**

## 25:49

Linu*h*yiya bihi baldatan maytan wanusqiyahu mimm*a* khalaqn*a* anAA*a*man waan*a*siyya katheer*a***n**

## 25:50

Walaqad *s*arrafn*a*hu baynahum liya*thth*akkaroo faab*a* aktharu a**l**nn*a*si ill*a* kufoor*a***n**

## 25:51

Walaw shin*a* labaAAathn*a* fee kulli qaryatin na*th*eer*a***n**

## 25:52

Fal*a* tu*t*iAAi alk*a*fireena waj*a*hidhum bihi jih*a*dan kabeer*a***n**

## 25:53

Wahuwa alla*th*ee maraja alba*h*rayni h*atha* AAa*th*bun fur*a*tun wah*atha* mil*h*un oj*a*jun wajaAAala baynahum*a* barzakhan wa*h*ijran ma*h*joor*a***n**

## 25:54

Wahuwa alla*th*ee khalaqa mina alm*a*i basharan fajaAAalahu nasaban wa*s*ihran wak*a*na rabbuka qadeer*a***n**

## 25:55

WayaAAbudoona min dooni All*a*hi m*a* l*a* yanfaAAuhum wal*a* ya*d*urruhum wak*a*na alk*a*firu AAal*a* rabbihi **th**&#x61;heer*a***n**

## 25:56

Wam*a* arsaln*a*ka ill*a* mubashshiran wana*th*eer*a***n**

## 25:57

Qul m*a* asalukum AAalayhi min ajrin ill*a* man sh*a*a an yattakhi*th*a il*a* rabbihi sabeel*a***n**

## 25:58

Watawakkal AAal*a* al*h*ayyi alla*th*ee l*a* yamootu wasabbi*h* bi*h*amdihi wakaf*a* bihi bi*th*unoobi AAib*a*dihi khabeer*a***n**

## 25:59

Alla*th*ee khalaqa a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*a wam*a* baynahum*a* fee sittati ayy*a*min thumma istaw*a* AAal*a* alAAarshi a**l**rra*h*m*a*nu fa**i**sal bihi khabeer*a***n**

## 25:60

Wai*tha* qeela lahumu osjudoo li**l**rra*h*m*a*ni q*a*loo wam*a* a**l**rra*h*m*a*nu anasjudu lim*a* tamurun*a* waz*a*dahum nufoor*a***n**

## 25:61

Tab*a*raka alla*th*ee jaAAala fee a**l**ssam*a*i buroojan wajaAAala feeh*a* sir*a*jan waqamaran muneer*a***n**

## 25:62

Wahuwa alla*th*ee jaAAala allayla wa**al**nnah*a*ra khilfatan liman ar*a*da an ya*thth*akkara aw ar*a*da shukoor*a***n**

## 25:63

WaAAib*a*du a**l**rra*h*m*a*ni alla*th*eena yamshoona AAal*a* alar*d*i hawnan wai*tha* kh*at*abahumu alj*a*hiloona q*a*loo sal*a*m*a***n**

## 25:64

Wa**a**lla*th*eena yabeetoona lirabbihim sujjadan waqiy*a*m*a***n**

## 25:65

Wa**a**lla*th*eena yaqooloona rabban*a* i*s*rif AAann*a* AAa*tha*ba jahannama inna AAa*tha*bah*a* k*a*na ghar*a*m*a***n**

## 25:66

Innah*a* s*a*at mustaqarran wamuq*a*m*a***n**

## 25:67

Wa**a**lla*th*eena i*tha* anfaqoo lam yusrifoo walam yaqturoo wak*a*na bayna *tha*lika qaw*a*m*a***n**

## 25:68

Wa**a**lla*th*eena l*a* yadAAoona maAA*a* All*a*hi il*a*han *a*khara wal*a* yaqtuloona a**l**nnafsa allatee *h*arrama All*a*hu ill*a* bi**a**l*h*aqqi wal*a* yaznoona waman yafAAal *tha*lika yalqa ath*a*m*a***n**

## 25:69

Yu*da*AAaf lahu alAAa*tha*bu yawma alqiy*a*mati wayakhlud feehi muh*a*n*a***n**

## 25:70

Ill*a* man t*a*ba wa*a*mana waAAamila AAamalan *sa*li*h*an faol*a*ika yubaddilu All*a*hu sayyi*a*tihim *h*asan*a*tin wak*a*na All*a*hu ghafooran ra*h*eem*a***n**

## 25:71

Waman t*a*ba waAAamila *sa*li*h*an fainnahu yatoobu il*a* All*a*hi mat*a*b*a***n**

## 25:72

Wa**a**lla*th*eena l*a* yashhadoona a**l**zzoora wai*tha* marroo bi**a**llaghwi marroo kir*a*m*a***n**

## 25:73

Wa**a**lla*th*eena i*tha* *th*ukkiroo bi*a*y*a*ti rabbihim lam yakhirroo AAalayh*a* *s*umman waAAumy*a*n*a***n**

## 25:74

Wa**a**lla*th*eena yaqooloona rabban*a* hab lan*a* min azw*a*jin*a* wa*th*urriyy*a*tin*a* qurrata aAAyunin wa**i**jAAaln*a* lilmuttaqeena im*a*m*a***n**

## 25:75

Ol*a*ika yujzawna alghurfata bim*a* *s*abaroo wayulaqqawna feeh*a* ta*h*iyyatan wasal*a*m*a***n**

## 25:76

Kh*a*lideena feeh*a* *h*asunat mustaqarran wamuq*a*m*a***n**

## 25:77

Qul m*a* yaAAbao bikum rabbee lawl*a* duAA*a*okum faqad ka*thth*abtum fasawfa yakoonu liz*a*m*a***n**

## 26:1

*Ta*seenmeem

## 26:2

Tilka *a*y*a*tu alkit*a*bi almubeen**i**

## 26:3

LaAAallaka b*a*khiAAun nafsaka all*a* yakoonoo mumineen**a**

## 26:4

In nasha nunazzil AAalayhim mina a**l**ssam*a*i *a*yatan f&#x61;**th**&#x61;llat aAAn*a*quhum lah*a* kh*ad*iAAeen**a**

## 26:5

Wam*a* yateehim min *th*ikrin mina a**l**rra*h*m*a*ni mu*h*dathin ill*a* k*a*noo AAanhu muAAri*d*een**a**

## 26:6

Faqad ka*thth*aboo fasayateehim anb*a*o m*a* k*a*noo bihi yastahzioon**a**

## 26:7

Awalam yaraw il*a* alar*d*i kam anbatn*a* feeh*a* min kulli zawjin kareem**in**

## 26:8

Inna fee *tha*lika la*a*yatan wam*a* k*a*na aktharuhum mumineen**a**

## 26:9

Wainna rabbaka lahuwa alAAazeezu a**l**rra*h*eem**u**

## 26:10

Wai*th* n*a*d*a* rabbuka moos*a* ani iti alqawma a**l****thth***a*limeen**a**

## 26:11

Qawma firAAawna al*a* yattaqoon**a**

## 26:12

Q*a*la rabbi innee akh*a*fu an yuka*thth*iboon**i**

## 26:13

Waya*d*eequ *s*adree wal*a* yan*t*aliqu lis*a*nee faarsil il*a* h*a*roon**a**

## 26:14

Walahum AAalayya *th*anbun faakh*a*fu an yaqtuloon**i**

## 26:15

Q*a*la kall*a* fa**i***th*hab*a* bi*a*y*a*tin*a* inn*a* maAAakum mustamiAAoon**a**

## 26:16

Fatiy*a* firAAawna faqool*a* inn*a* rasoolu rabbi alAA*a*lameen**a**

## 26:17

An arsil maAAan*a* banee isr*a*eel**a**

## 26:18

Q*a*la alam nurabbika feen*a* waleedan walabithta feen*a* min AAumurika sineen**a**

## 26:19

WafaAAalta faAAlataka allatee faAAalta waanta mina alk*a*fireen**a**

## 26:20

Q*a*la faAAaltuh*a* i*th*an waan*a* mina a**l***dda*lleen**a**

## 26:21

Fafarartu minkum lamm*a* khiftukum fawahaba lee rabbee *h*ukman wajaAAalanee mina almursaleen**a**

## 26:22

Watilka niAAmatun tamunnuh*a* AAalayya an AAabbadta banee isr*a*eel**a**

## 26:23

Q*a*la firAAawnu wam*a* rabbu alAA*a*lameen**a**

## 26:24

Q*a*la rabbu a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i wam*a* baynahum*a* in kuntum mooqineen**a**

## 26:25

Q*a*la liman *h*awlahu al*a* tastamiAAoon**a**

## 26:26

Q*a*la rabbukum warabbu *a*b*a*ikumu alawwaleen**a**

## 26:27

Q*a*la inna rasoolakumu alla*th*ee orsila ilaykum lamajnoon**un**

## 26:28

Q*a*la rabbu almashriqi wa**a**lmaghribi wam*a* baynahum*a* in kuntum taAAqiloon**a**

## 26:29

Q*a*la laini ittakha*th*ta il*a*han ghayree laajAAalannaka mina almasjooneen**a**

## 26:30

Q*a*la awalaw jituka bishayin mubeen**in**

## 26:31

Q*a*la fati bihi in kunta mina a**l***ssa*diqeen**a**

## 26:32

Faalq*a* AAa*sa*hu fai*tha* hiya thuAAb*a*nun mubeen**un**

## 26:33

WanazaAAa yadahu fai*tha* hiya bay*da*o li**l**nn*a***th**&#x69;reen**a**

## 26:34

Q*a*la lilmalai *h*awlahu inna h*atha* las*ah*irun AAaleem**un**

## 26:35

Yureedu an yukhrijakum min ar*d*ikum bisi*h*rihi fam*atha* tamuroon**a**

## 26:36

Q*a*loo arjih waakh*a*hu wa**i**bAAath fee almad*a*ini *ha*shireen**a**

## 26:37

Yatooka bikulli sa*hha*rin AAaleem**in**

## 26:38

FajumiAAa a**l**ssa*h*aratu limeeq*a*ti yawmin maAAloom**in**

## 26:39

Waqeela li**l**nn*a*si hal antum mujtamiAAoon**a**

## 26:40

LaAAallan*a* nattabiAAu a**l**ssa*h*arata in k*a*noo humu algh*a*libeen**a**

## 26:41

Falamm*a* j*a*a a**l**ssa*h*aratu q*a*loo lifirAAawna ainna lan*a* laajran in kunn*a* na*h*nu algh*a*libeen**a**

## 26:42

Q*a*la naAAam wainnakum i*th*an lamina almuqarrabeen**a**

## 26:43

Q*a*la lahum moos*a* alqoo m*a* antum mulqoon**a**

## 26:44

Faalqaw *h*ib*a*lahum waAAi*s*iyyahum waq*a*loo biAAizzati firAAawna inn*a* lana*h*nu algh*a*liboon**a**

## 26:45

Faalq*a* moos*a* AAa*sa*hu fai*tha* hiya talqafu m*a* yafikoon**a**

## 26:46

Faolqiya a**l**ssa*h*aratu s*a*jideen**a**

## 26:47

Q*a*loo *a*mann*a* birabbi alAA*a*lameen**a**

## 26:48

Rabbi moos*a* wah*a*roon**a**

## 26:49

Q*a*la *a*mantum lahu qabla an *ath*ana lakum innahu lakabeerukumu alla*th*ee AAallamakumu a**l**ssi*h*ra falasawfa taAAlamoona laoqa*tt*iAAanna aydiyakum waarjulakum min khil*a*fin walao*s*allibannakum ajmaAAeen**a**

## 26:50

Q*a*loo l*a* *d*ayra inn*a* il*a* rabbin*a* munqaliboon**a**

## 26:51

Inn*a* na*t*maAAu an yaghfira lan*a* rabbun*a* kha*ta*y*a*n*a* an kunn*a* awwala almumineen**a**

## 26:52

Waaw*h*ayn*a* il*a* moos*a* an asri biAAib*a*dee innakum muttabaAAoon**a**

## 26:53

Faarsala firAAawnu fee almad*a*ini *ha*shireen**a**

## 26:54

Inna h*a*ol*a*i lashir*th*imatun qaleeloon**a**

## 26:55

Wainnahum lan*a* lagh*a*&#x69;**th**&#x6F;on**a**

## 26:56

## 26:57

## 26:58

## 26:59

## 26:60

## 26:61

## 26:62

## 26:63

## 26:82

## 26:83

## 26:227

Ill*a* alla*th*eena *a*manoo waAAamiloo a**l***ssa*li*ha*ti wa*th*akaroo All*a*ha katheeran wa**i**nta*s*aroo min baAAdi m*a* **th**&#x75;limoo wasayaAAlamu alla*th*eena **th**&#x61;lamoo ayya munqalabin yanqaliboon**a**

## 27:1

*Ta*seen tilka *a*y*a*tu alqur*a*ni wakit*a*bin mubeen**in**

## 27:2

Hudan wabushr*a* lilmumineen**a**

## 27:3

Alla*th*eena yuqeemoona a**l***ss*al*a*ta wayutoona a**l**zzak*a*ta wahum bi**a**l*a*khirati hum yooqinoon**a**

## 27:4

Inna alla*th*eena l*a* yuminoona bi**a**l*a*khirati zayyann*a* lahum aAAm*a*lahum fahum yaAAmahoon**a**

## 27:5

Ol*a*ika alla*th*eena lahum sooo alAAa*tha*bi wahum fee al*a*khirati humu alakhsaroon**a**

## 27:6

Wainnaka latulaqq*a* alqur*a*na min ladun *h*akeemin AAaleem**in**

## 27:7

I*th* q*a*la moos*a* liahlihi innee *a*nastu n*a*ran sa*a*teekum minh*a* bikhabarin aw *a*teekum bishih*a*bin qabasin laAAallakum ta*st*aloon**a**

## 27:8

Falamm*a* j*a*ah*a* noodiya an boorika man fee a**l**nn*a*ri waman *h*awlah*a* wasub*ha*na All*a*hi rabbi alAA*a*lameen**a**

## 27:9

Y*a* moos*a* innahu an*a* All*a*hu alAAazeezu al*h*akeem**u**

## 27:10

Waalqi AAa*sa*ka falamm*a* ra*a*h*a* tahtazzu kaannah*a* j*a*nnun wall*a* mudbiran walam yuAAaqqib y*a* moos*a* l*a* takhaf innee l*a* yakh*a*fu ladayya almursaloon**a**

## 27:11

Ill*a* man **th**&#x61;lama thumma baddala *h*usnan baAAda sooin fainnee ghafoorun ra*h*eem**un**

## 27:12

Waadkhil yadaka fee jaybika takhruj bay*da*a min ghayri sooin fee tisAAi *a*y*a*tin il*a* firAAawna waqawmihi innahum k*a*noo qawman f*a*siqeen**a**

## 27:13

Falamm*a* j*a*athum *a*y*a*tun*a* mub*s*iratan q*a*loo h*atha* si*h*run mubeen**un**

## 27:14

Waja*h*adoo bih*a* wa**i**stayqanath*a* anfusuhum **th**&#x75;lman waAAuluwwan fa**o**&#x6E;**th**&#x75;r kayfa k*a*na AA*a*qibatu almufsideen**a**

## 27:15

Walaqad *a*tayn*a* d*a*wooda wasulaym*a*na AAilman waq*a*l*a* al*h*amdu lill*a*hi alla*th*ee fa*dd*alan*a* AAal*a* katheerin min AAib*a*dihi almumineen**a**

## 27:16

Wawaritha sulaym*a*nu d*a*wooda waq*a*la y*a* ayyuh*a* a**l**nn*a*su AAullimn*a* man*t*iqa a**l***tt*ayri waooteen*a* min kulli shayin inna h*atha* lahuwa alfa*d*lu almubeen**u**

## 27:17
