Wa*h*ushira lisulaym*a*na junooduhu mina aljinni wa**a**linsi wa**al***tt*ayri fahum yoozaAAoon**a**

## 27:18

*H*att*a* i*tha* ataw AAal*a* w*a*di a**l**nnamli q*a*lat namlatun y*a* ayyuh*a* a**l**nnamlu odkhuloo mas*a*kinakum l*a* ya*ht*imannakum sulaym*a*nu wajunooduhu wahum l*a* yashAAuroon**a**

## 27:19

Fatabassama *dah*ikan min qawlih*a* waq*a*la rabbi awziAAnee an ashkura niAAmataka allatee anAAamta AAalayya waAAal*a* w*a*lidayya waan aAAmala *sa*li*h*an tar*da*hu waadkhilnee bira*h*matika fee AAib*a*dika a**l***ssa*li*h*een**a**

## 27:20

Watafaqqada a**l***tt*ayra faq*a*la m*a* liya l*a* ar*a* alhudhuda am k*a*na mina algh*a*ibeen**a**

## 27:21

LaoAAa*thth*ibannahu AAa*tha*ban shadeedan aw laa*th*ba*h*annahu aw layatiyannee bisul*ta*nin mubeen**in**

## 27:22

Famakatha ghayra baAAeedin faq*a*la a*hat*tu bim*a* lam tu*h*i*t* bihi wajituka min sabain binabain yaqeen**in**

## 27:23

Innee wajadtu imraatan tamlikuhum waootiyat min kulli shayin walah*a* AAarshun AA&#x61;**th**&#x65;em**un**

## 27:24

Wajadtuh*a* waqawmah*a* yasjudoona li**l**shshamsi min dooni All*a*hi wazayyana lahumu a**l**shshay*ta*nu aAAm*a*lahum fa*s*addahum AAani a**l**ssabeeli fahum l*a* yahtadoon**a**

## 27:25

All*a* yasjudoo lill*a*hi alla*th*ee yukhriju alkhabaa fee a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i wayaAAlamu m*a* tukhfoona wam*a* tuAAlinoon**a**

## 27:26

All*a*hu l*a* il*a*ha ill*a* huwa rabbu alAAarshi alAA&#x61;**th**&#x65;em**i**

## 27:27

Q*a*la sana&#x6E;**th**&#x75;ru a*s*adaqta am kunta mina alk*ath*ibeen**a**

## 27:28

I*th*hab bikit*a*bee h*atha* faalqih ilayhim thumma tawalla AAanhum fa**o**&#x6E;**th**&#x75;r m*atha* yarjiAAoon**a**

## 27:29

Q*a*lat y*a* ayyuh*a* almalao innee olqiya ilayya kit*a*bun kareem**un**

## 27:30

Innahu min sulaym*a*na wainnahu bismi All*a*hi a**l**rra*h*m*a*ni a**l**rra*h*eem**i**

## 27:31

All*a* taAAloo AAalayya watoonee muslimeen**a**

## 27:32

Q*a*lat y*a* ayyuh*a* almalao aftoonee fee amree m*a* kuntu q*at*iAAatan amran *h*att*a* tashhadoon**a**

## 27:33

Q*a*loo na*h*nu oloo quwwatin waoloo basin shadeedin wa**a**lamru ilayki fa**o**&#x6E;**th**&#x75;ree m*atha* tamureen**a**

## 27:34

Q*a*lat inna almulooka i*tha* dakhaloo qaryatan afsadooh*a* wajaAAaloo aAAizzata ahlih*a* a*th*illatan waka*tha*lika yafAAaloon**a**

## 27:35

Wainnee mursilatun ilayhim bihadiyyatin fan*a***th**&#x69;ratun bima yarjiAAu almursaloon**a**

## 27:36

Falamm*a* j*a*a sulaym*a*na q*a*la atumiddoonani bim*a*lin fam*a* *a*t*a*niya All*a*hu khayrun mimm*a* *a*t*a*kum bal antum bihadiyyatikum tafra*h*oon**a**

## 27:37

IrjiAA ilayhim falanatiyannahum bijunoodin l*a* qibala lahum bih*a* walanukhrijannahum minh*a* a*th*illatan wahum *sa*ghiroon**a**

## 27:38

Q*a*la y*a* ayyuh*a* almalao ayyukum yateenee biAAarshih*a* qabla an yatoonee muslimeen**a**

## 27:39

Q*a*la AAifreetun mina aljinni an*a* *a*teeka bihi qabla an taqooma min maq*a*mika wainne AAalayhi laqawiyyun ameen**un**

## 27:40

Q*a*la alla*th*ee AAindahu AAilmun mina alkit*a*bi an*a* *a*teeka bihi qabla an yartadda ilayka *t*arfuka falamm*a* ra*a*hu mustaqirran AAindahu q*a*la h*atha* min fa*d*li rabbee liyabluwanee aashkuru am akfuru waman shakara fainnam*a* yashkuru linafsihi waman kafara fainna rabbee ghaniyyun kareem**un**

## 27:41

Q*a*la nakkiroo lah*a* AAarshah*a* na&#x6E;**th**&#x75;r atahtadee am takoonu mina alla*th*eena l*a* yahtadoon**a**

## 27:42

Falamm*a* j*a*at qeela ah*a*ka*tha* AAarshuki q*a*lat kaannahu huwa waooteen*a* alAAilma min qablih*a* wakunn*a* muslimeen**a**

## 27:43

Wa*s*addah*a* m*a* k*a*nat taAAbudu min dooni All*a*hi innah*a* k*a*nat min qawmin k*a*fireen**a**

## 27:44

Qeela lah*a* odkhulee a**l***ss*ar*h*a falamm*a* raathu *h*asibathu lujjatan wakashafat AAan s*a*qayh*a* q*a*la innahu *s*ar*h*un mumarradun min qaw*a*reera q*a*lat rabbi innee **th**&#x61;lamtu nafsee waaslamtu maAAa sulaym*a*na lill*a*hi rabbi alAA*a*lameen**a**

## 27:45

Walaqad arsaln*a* il*a* thamooda akh*a*hum *sa*li*h*an ani oAAbudoo All*a*ha fai*tha* hum fareeq*a*ni yakhta*s*imoon**a**

## 27:46

Q*a*la y*a* qawmi lima tastaAAjiloona bi**al**ssayyiati qabla al*h*asanati lawl*a* tastaghfiroona All*a*ha laAAallakum tur*h*amoon**a**

## 27:47

Q*a*loo i*tt*ayyarn*a* bika wabiman maAAaka q*a*la *ta*irukum AAinda All*a*hi bal antum qawmun tuftanoon**a**

## 27:48

Wak*a*na fee almadeenati tisAAatu rah*t*in yufsidoona fee alar*d*i wal*a* yu*s*li*h*oon**a**

## 27:49

Q*a*loo taq*a*samoo bi**A**ll*a*hi lanubayyitannahu waahlahu thumma lanaqoolanna liwaliyyihi m*a* shahidn*a* mahlika ahlihi wainn*a* la*sa*diqoon**a**

## 27:50

Wamakaroo makran wamakarn*a* makran wahum l*a* yashAAuroon**a**

## 27:51

Fa**o**&#x6E;**th**&#x75;r kayfa k*a*na AA*a*qibatu makrihim ann*a* dammarn*a*hum waqawmahum ajmaAAeen**a**

## 27:52

Fatilka buyootuhum kh*a*wiyatan bim*a* **th**&#x61;lamoo inna fee *tha*lika la*a*yatan liqawmin yaAAlamoon**a**

## 27:53

Waanjayn*a* alla*th*eena *a*manoo wak*a*noo yattaqoon**a**

## 27:54

Waloo*t*an i*th* q*a*la liqawmihi atatoona alf*ah*ishata waantum tub*s*iroon**a**

## 27:55

Ainnakum latatoona a**l**rrij*a*la shahwatan min dooni a**l**nnis*a*i bal antum qawmun tajhaloon**a**

## 27:56

Fam*a* k*a*na jaw*a*ba qawmihi ill*a* an q*a*loo akhrijoo *a*la loo*t*in min qaryatikum innahum on*a*sun yata*t*ahharoon**a**

## 27:57

Faanjayn*a*hu waahlahu ill*a* imraatahu qaddarn*a*h*a* mina algh*a*bireen**a**

## 27:58

Waam*t*arn*a* AAalayhim ma*t*aran fas*a*a ma*t*aru almun*th*areen**a**

## 27:59

Quli al*h*amdu lill*a*hi wasal*a*mun AAal*a* AAib*a*dihi alla*th*eena i*st*af*a* *a*ll*a*hu khayrun amm*a* yushrikoon**a**

## 27:60

Amman khalaqa a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*a waanzala lakum mina a**l**ssam*a*i m*a*an faanbatn*a* bihi *h*ad*a*iqa *tha*ta bahjatin m*a* k*a*na lakum an tunbitoo shajarah*a* ail*a*hun maAAa All*a*hi bal hum qawmun yaAAdiloon**a**

## 27:61

Amman jaAAala alar*d*a qar*a*ran wajaAAala khil*a*lah*a* anh*a*ran wajaAAala lah*a* raw*a*siya wajaAAala bayna alba*h*rayni *ha*jizan ail*a*hun maAAa All*a*hi bal aktharuhum l*a* yaAAlamoon**a**

## 27:62

Amman yujeebu almu*dt*arra i*tha* daAA*a*hu wayakshifu a**l**ssooa wayajAAalukum khulaf*a*a alar*d*i ail*a*hun maAAa All*a*hi qaleelan m*a* ta*th*akkaroon**a**

## 27:63

Amman yahdeekum fee **th**&#x75;lum*a*ti albarri wa**a**lba*h*ri waman yursilu a**l**rriy*ah*a bushran bayna yaday ra*h*matihi ail*a*hun maAAa All*a*hi taAA*a*l*a* All*a*hu AAamm*a* yushrikoon**a**

## 27:64

Amman yabdao alkhalqa thumma yuAAeeduhu waman yarzuqukum mina a**l**ssam*a*i wa**a**lar*d*i ail*a*hun maAAa All*a*hi qul h*a*too burh*a*nakum in kuntum *sa*diqeen**a**

## 27:65

Qul l*a* yaAAlamu man fee a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i alghayba ill*a* All*a*hu wam*a* yashAAuroona ayy*a*na yubAAathoon**a**

## 27:66

Bali idd*a*raka AAilmuhum fee al*a*khirati bal hum fee shakkin minh*a* bal hum minh*a* AAamoon**a**

## 27:67

Waq*a*la alla*th*eena kafaroo ai*tha* kunn*a* tur*a*ban wa*a*b*a*on*a* ainn*a* lamukhrajoon**a**

## 27:68

Laqad wuAAidn*a* h*atha* na*h*nu wa*a*b*a*on*a* min qablu in h*atha* ill*a* as*at*eeru alawwaleen**a**

## 27:69

Qul seeroo fee alar*d*i fa**o**&#x6E;**th**&#x75;roo kayfa k*a*na AA*a*qibatu almujrimeen**a**

## 27:70

Wal*a* ta*h*zan AAalayhim wal*a* takun fee *d*ayqin mimm*a* yamkuroon**a**

## 27:71

Wayaqooloona mat*a* h*atha* alwaAAdu in kuntum *sa*diqeen**a**

## 27:72

Qul AAas*a* an yakoona radifa lakum baAA*d*u alla*th*ee tastaAAjiloon**a**

## 27:73

Wainna rabbaka la*th*oo fa*d*lin AAal*a* a**l**nn*a*si wal*a*kinna aktharahum l*a* yashkuroon**a**

## 27:74

Wainna rabbaka layaAAlamu m*a* tukinnu *s*udooruhum wam*a* yuAAlinoon**a**

## 27:75

Wam*a* min gh*a*ibatin fee a**l**ssam*a*i wa**a**lar*d*i ill*a* fee kit*a*bin mubeen**in**

## 27:76

Inna h*atha* alqur*a*na yaqu*ss*u AAal*a* banee isr*a*eela akthara alla*th*ee hum feehi yakhtalifoon**a**

## 27:77

Wainnahu lahudan wara*h*matun lilmumineen**a**

## 27:78

Inna rabbaka yaq*d*ee baynahum bi*h*ukmihi wahuwa alAAazeezu alAAaleem**u**

## 27:79

Fatawakkal AAal*a* All*a*hi innaka AAal*a* al*h*aqqi almubeen**i**

## 27:80

Innaka l*a* tusmiAAu almawt*a* wal*a* tusmiAAu a**l***ss*umma a**l**dduAA*a*a i*tha* wallaw mudbireen**a**

## 27:81

Wam*a* anta bih*a*dee alAAumyi AAan *d*al*a*latihim in tusmiAAu ill*a* man yuminu bi*a*y*a*tin*a* fahum muslimoon**a**

## 27:82

Wai*tha* waqaAAa alqawlu AAalayhim akhrajn*a* lahum d*a*bbatan mina alar*d*i tukallimuhum anna a**l**nn*a*sa k*a*noo bi*a*y*a*tin*a* l*a* yooqinoon**a**

## 27:83

Wayawma na*h*shuru min kulli ommatin fawjan mimman yuka*thth*ibu bi*a*y*a*tin*a* fahum yoozaAAoon**a**

## 27:84

*H*att*a* i*tha* j*a*oo q*a*la aka*thth*abtum bi*a*y*a*tee walam tu*h*ee*t*oo bih*a* AAilman amm*atha* kuntum taAAmaloon**a**

## 27:85

WawaqaAAa alqawlu AAalayhim bim*a* **th**&#x61;lamoo fahum l*a* yan*t*iqoon**a**

## 27:86

Alam yaraw ann*a* jaAAaln*a* allayla liyaskunoo feehi wa**al**nnah*a*ra mub*s*iran inna fee *tha*lika la*a*y*a*tin liqawmin yuminoon**a**

## 27:87

Wayawma yunfakhu fee a**l***ss*oori fafaziAAa man fee a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti waman fee alar*d*i ill*a* man sh*a*a All*a*hu wakullun atawhu d*a*khireen**a**

## 27:88

Watar*a* aljib*a*la ta*h*sabuh*a* j*a*midatan wahiya tamurru marra a**l**ssa*ha*bi *s*unAAa All*a*hi alla*th*ee atqana kulla shayin innahu khabeerun bim*a* tafAAaloon**a**

## 27:89

Man j*a*a bi**a**l*h*asanati falahu khayrun minh*a* wahum min fazaAAin yawmai*th*in *a*minoon**a**

## 27:90

Waman j*a*a bi**al**ssayyiati fakubbat wujoohuhum fee a**l**nn*a*ri hal tujzawna ill*a* m*a* kuntum taAAmaloon**a**

## 27:91

Innam*a* omirtu an aAAbuda rabba h*ath*ihi albaldati alla*th*ee *h*arramah*a* walahu kullu shayin waomirtu an akoona mina almuslimeen**a**

## 27:92

Waan atluwa alqur*a*na famani ihtad*a* fainnam*a* yahtadee linafsihi waman *d*alla faqul innam*a* an*a* mina almun*th*ireen**a**

## 27:93

Waquli al*h*amdu lill*a*hi sayureekum *a*y*a*tihi fataAArifoonah*a* wam*a* rabbuka bigh*a*filin AAamm*a* taAAmaloon**a**

## 28:1

*Ta*seenmeem

## 28:2

Tilka *a*y*a*tu alkit*a*bi almubeen**i**

## 28:3

Natloo AAalayka min nabai moos*a* wafirAAawna bi**a**l*h*aqqi liqawmin yuminoon**a**

## 28:4

Inna firAAawna AAal*a* fee alar*d*i wajaAAala ahlah*a* shiyaAAan yasta*d*AAifu *ta*ifatan minhum yu*th*abbi*h*u abn*a*ahum wayasta*h*yee nis*a*ahum innahu k*a*na mina almufsideen**a**

## 28:5

Wanureedu an namunna AAal*a* alla*th*eena istu*d*AAifoo fee alar*d*i wanajAAalahum aimmatan wanajAAalahumu alw*a*ritheen**a**

## 28:6

Wanumakkina lahum fee alar*d*i wanuriya firAAawna wah*a*m*a*na wajunoodahum*a* minhum m*a* k*a*noo ya*hth*aroon**a**

## 28:7

Waaw*h*ayn*a* il*a* ommi moos*a* an ar*d*iAAeehi fai*tha* khifti AAalayhi faalqeehi fee alyammi wal*a* takh*a*fee wal*a* ta*h*zanee inn*a* r*a*ddoohu ilayki waj*a*AAiloohu mina almursaleen**a**

## 28:8

Fa**i**ltaqa*t*ahu *a*lu firAAawna liyakoona lahum AAaduwwan wa*h*azanan inna firAAawna wah*a*m*a*na wajunoodahum*a* k*a*noo kh*at*ieen**a**

## 28:9

Waq*a*lati imraatu firAAawna qurratu AAaynin lee walaka l*a* taqtuloohu AAas*a* an yanfaAAan*a* aw nattakhi*th*ahu waladan wahum l*a* yashAAuroon**a**

## 28:10

Waa*s*ba*h*a fu*a*du ommi moos*a* f*a*righan in k*a*dat latubdee bihi lawl*a* an raba*t*n*a* AAal*a* qalbih*a* litakoona mina almumineen**a**

## 28:11

Waq*a*lat liokhtihi qu*ss*eehi faba*s*urat bihi AAan junubin wahum l*a* yashAAuroon**a**

## 28:12

Wa*h*arramn*a* AAalayhi almar*ad*iAAa min qablu faq*a*lat hal adullukum AAal*a* ahli baytin yakfuloonahu lakum wahum lahu n*as*i*h*oon**a**

## 28:13

Faradadn*a*hu il*a* ommihi kay taqarra AAaynuh*a* wal*a* ta*h*zana walitaAAlama anna waAAda All*a*hi *h*aqqun wal*a*kinna aktharahum l*a* yaAAlamoon**a**

## 28:14

Walamm*a* balagha ashuddahu wa**i**staw*a* *a*tayn*a*hu *h*ukman waAAilman waka*tha*lika najzee almu*h*sineen**a**

## 28:15

Wadakhala almadeenata AAal*a* *h*eeni ghaflatin min ahlih*a* fawajada feeh*a* rajulayni yaqtatil*a*ni h*atha* min sheeAAatihi wah*atha* min AAaduwwihi fa**i**stagh*a*thahu alla*th*ee min sheeAAatihi AAal*a* alla*th*ee min AAaduwwihi fawakazahu moos*a* faqa*da* AAalayhi q*a*la h*atha* min AAamali a**l**shshay*ta*ni innahu AAaduwwun mu*d*illun mubeen**un**

## 28:16

Q*a*la rabbi innee **th**&#x61;lamtu nafsee fa**i**ghfir lee faghafara lahu innahu huwa alghafooru a**l**rra*h*eem**u**

## 28:17

Q*a*la rabbi bim*a* anAAamta AAalayya falan akoona **th**&#x61;heeran lilmujrimeen**a**

## 28:18

Faa*s*ba*h*a fee almadeenati kh*a*ifan yataraqqabu fai*tha* alla*th*ee istan*s*arahu bi**a**lamsi yasta*s*rikhuhu q*a*la lahu moos*a* innaka laghawiyyun mubeen**un**

## 28:19

Falamm*a* an ar*a*da an yab*t*isha bi**a**lla*th*ee huwa AAaduwwun lahum*a* q*a*la y*a* moos*a* atureedu an taqtulanee kam*a* qatalta nafsan bi**a**lamsi in tureedu ill*a* an takoona jabb*a*ran fee alar*d*i wam*a* tureedu an takoona mina almu*s*li*h*een**a**

## 28:20

Waj*a*a rajulun min aq*sa* almadeenati yasAA*a* q*a*la y*a* moos*a* inna almalaa yatamiroona bika liyaqtulooka fa**o**khruj innee laka mina a**l**nn*as*i*h*een**a**

## 28:21

Fakharaja minh*a* kh*a*ifan yataraqqabu q*a*la rabbi najjinee mina alqawmi a**l****thth***a*limeen**a**

## 28:22

Walamm*a* tawajjaha tilq*a*a madyana q*a*la AAas*a* rabbee an yahdiyanee saw*a*a a**l**ssabeel**i**

## 28:23

Walamm*a* warada m*a*a madyana wajada AAalayhi ommatan mina a**l**nn*a*si yasqoona wawajada min doonihimu imraatayni ta*th*ood*a*ni q*a*la m*a* kha*t*bukum*a* q*a*lat*a* l*a* nasqee *h*att*a* yu*s*dira a**l**rriAA*a*o waaboon*a* shaykhun kabeer**un**

## 28:24

Fasaq*a* lahum*a* thumma tawall*a* il*a* a**l****thth**&#x69;lli faq*a*la rabbi innee lim*a* anzalta ilayya min khayrin faqeer**un**

## 28:25

Faj*a*athu i*h*d*a*hum*a* tamshee AAal*a* isti*h*y*a*in q*a*lat inna abee yadAAooka liyajziyaka ajra m*a* saqayta lan*a* falamm*a* j*a*ahu waqa*ss*a AAalayhi alqa*s*a*s*a q*a*la l*a* takhaf najawta mina alqawmi a**l****thth***a*limeen**a**

## 28:26

Q*a*lat i*h*d*a*hum*a* y*a* abati istajirhu inna khayra mani istajarta alqawiyyu alameen**u**

## 28:27

Q*a*la innee oreedu an onki*h*aka i*h*d*a* ibnatayya h*a*tayni AAal*a* an tajuranee tham*a*niya *h*ijajin fain atmamta AAashran famin AAindika wam*a* oreedu an ashuqqa AAalayka satajidunee in sh*a*a All*a*hu mina a**l***ssa*li*h*een**a**

## 28:28

Q*a*la *tha*lika baynee wabaynaka ayyam*a* alajalayni qa*d*aytu fal*a* AAudw*a*na AAalayya wa**A**ll*a*hu AAal*a* m*a* naqoolu wakeel**un**

## 28:29

Falamm*a* qa*da* moos*a*alajala was*a*ra biahlihi *a*nasa min j*a*nibi a**l***tt*oori n*a*ran q*a*la liahlihi omkuthoo innee *a*nastu n*a*ran laAAallee *a*teekum minh*a* bikhabarin aw ja*th*watin mina a**l**nn*a*ri laAAallakum ta*st*aloon**a**

## 28:30

Falamm*a* at*a*h*a* noodiya min sh*at*ii alw*a*di alaymani fee albuqAAati almub*a*rakati mina a**l**shshajarati an y*a* moos*a* innee an*a* All*a*hu rabbu alAA*a*lameen**a**

## 28:31

Waan alqi AAa*sa*ka falamm*a* ra*a*h*a* tahtazzu kaannah*a* j*a*nnun wall*a* mudbiran walam yuAAaqqib y*a* moos*a* aqbil wal*a* takhaf innaka mina al*a*mineen**a**

## 28:32

Osluk yadaka fee jaybika takhruj bay*da*a min ghayri sooin wa**o***d*mum ilayka jan*ah*aka mina a**l**rrahbi fa*tha*nika burh*a*n*a*ni min rabbika il*a* firAAawna wamalaihi innahum k*a*noo qawman f*a*siqeen**a**

## 28:33

Q*a*la rabbi innee qataltu minhum nafsan faakh*a*fu an yaqtuloon**i**

## 28:34

Waakhee h*a*roonu huwa af*s*a*h*u minnee lis*a*nan faarsilhu maAAiya ridan yu*s*addiqunee innee akh*a*fu an yuka*thth*iboon**i**

## 28:35

Q*a*la sanashuddu AAa*d*udaka biakheeka wanajAAalu lakum*a* sul*ta*nan fal*a* ya*s*iloona ilaykum*a* bi*a*y*a*tin*a* antum*a* wamani ittabaAAakum*a* algh*a*liboon**a**

## 28:36

Falamm*a* j*a*ahum moos*a* bi*a*y*a*tin*a* bayyin*a*tin q*a*loo m*a* h*atha* ill*a* si*h*run muftaran wam*a* samiAAn*a* bih*atha* fee *a*b*a*in*a* alawwaleen**a**

## 28:37

Waq*a*la moos*a* rabbee aAAlamu biman j*a*a bi**a**lhud*a* min AAindihi waman takoonu lahu AA*a*qibatu a**l**dd*a*ri innahu l*a* yufli*h*u a**l****thth***a*limoon**a**

## 28:38

Waq*a*la firAAawnu y*a* ayyuh*a* almalao m*a* AAalimtu lakum min il*a*hin ghayree faawqid lee y*a* h*a*m*a*nu AAal*a* a**l***tt*eeni fa**i**jAAal lee *s*ar*h*an laAAallee a*tt*aliAAu il*a* il*a*hi moos*a* wainnee la&#x61;**th**&#x75;nnuhu mina alk*ath*ibeen**a**

## 28:39

Wa**i**stakbara huwa wajunooduhu fee alar*d*i bighayri al*h*aqqi w&#x61;**th**&#x61;nnoo annahum ilayn*a* l*a* yurjaAAoon**a**

## 28:40

Faakha*th*n*a*hu wajunoodahu fanaba*th*n*a*hum fee alyammi fa**o**&#x6E;**th**&#x75;r kayfa k*a*na AA*a*qibatu a**l****thth***a*limeen**a**

## 28:41

WajaAAaln*a*hum aimmatan yadAAoona il*a* a**l**nn*a*ri wayawma alqiy*a*mati l*a* yun*s*aroon**a**

## 28:42

WaatbaAAn*a*hum fee h*ath*ihi a**l**dduny*a* laAAnatan wayawma alqiy*a*mati hum mina almaqboo*h*een**a**

## 28:43

Walaqad *a*tayn*a* moos*a* alkit*a*ba min baAAdi m*a* ahlakn*a* alquroona alool*a* ba*sa*ira li**l**nn*a*si wahudan wara*h*matan laAAallahum yata*th*akkaroon**a**

## 28:44

Wam*a* kunta bij*a*nibi algharbiyyi i*th* qa*d*ayn*a* il*a* moos*a* alamra wam*a* kunta mina a**l**shsh*a*hideen**a**

## 28:45

Wal*a*kinn*a* anshan*a* quroonan fata*ta*wala AAalayhimu alAAumuru wam*a* kunta th*a*wiyan fee ahli madyana tatloo AAalayhim *a*y*a*tin*a* wal*a*kinn*a* kunn*a* mursileen**a**

## 28:46

Wam*a* kunta bij*a*nibi a**l***tt*oori i*th* n*a*dayn*a* wal*a*kin ra*h*matan min rabbika litun*th*ira qawman m*a* at*a*hum min na*th*eerin min qablika laAAallahum yata*th*akkaroon**a**

## 28:47

Walawl*a* an tu*s*eebahum mu*s*eebatun bim*a* qaddamat aydeehim fayaqooloo rabban*a* lawl*a* arsalta ilayn*a* rasoolan fanattabiAAa *a*y*a*tika wanakoona mina almumineen**a**

## 28:48

Falamm*a* j*a*ahumu al*h*aqqu min AAindin*a* q*a*loo lawl*a* ootiya mithla m*a* ootiya moos*a* awalam yakfuroo bim*a* ootiya moos*a* min qablu q*a*loo si*h*r*a*ni t&#x61;**th***a*har*a* waq*a*loo inn*a* bikullin k*a*firoon**a**

## 28:49

Qul fatoo bikit*a*bin min AAindi All*a*hi huwa ahd*a* minhum*a* attabiAAhu in kuntum *sa*diqeen**a**

## 28:50

Fain lam yastajeeboo laka fa**i**AAlam annam*a* yattabiAAoona ahw*a*ahum waman a*d*allu mimmani ittabaAAa haw*a*hu bighayri hudan mina All*a*hi inna All*a*ha l*a* yahdee alqawma a**l****thth***a*limeen**a**

## 28:51

Walaqad wa*ss*aln*a* lahumu alqawla laAAallahum yata*th*akkaroon**a**

## 28:52

Alla*th*eena *a*tayn*a*humu alkit*a*ba min qablihi hum bihi yuminoon**a**

## 28:53

Wai*tha* yutl*a* AAalayhim q*a*loo *a*mann*a* bihi innahu al*h*aqqu min rabbin*a* inn*a* kunn*a* min qablihi muslimeen**a**

## 28:54

Ol*a*ika yutawna ajrahum marratayni bim*a* *s*abaroo wayadraoona bi**a**l*h*asanati a**l**ssayyiata wamimm*a* razaqn*a*hum yunfiqoon**a**

## 28:55

Wai*tha* samiAAoo allaghwa aAAra*d*oo AAanhu waq*a*loo lan*a* aAAm*a*lun*a* walakum aAAm*a*lukum sal*a*mun AAalaykum l*a* nabtaghee alj*a*hileen**a**

## 28:56

Innaka l*a* tahdee man a*h*babta wal*a*kinna All*a*ha yahdee man yash*a*o wahuwa aAAlamu bi**a**lmuhtadeen**a**

## 28:57

Waq*a*loo in nattabiAAi alhud*a* maAAaka nutakha*tt*af min ar*d*in*a* awalam numakkin lahum *h*araman *a*minan yujb*a* ilayhi thamar*a*tu kulli shayin rizqan min ladunn*a* wal*a*kinna aktharahum l*a* yaAAlamoon**a**

## 28:58

Wakam ahlakn*a* min qaryatin ba*t*irat maAAeeshatah*a* fatilka mas*a*kinuhum lam tuskan min baAAdihim ill*a* qaleelan wakunn*a* na*h*nu alw*a*ritheen**a**

## 28:59

Wam*a* k*a*na rabbuka muhlika alqur*a* *h*att*a* yabAAatha fee ommih*a* rasoolan yatloo AAalayhim *a*y*a*tin*a* wam*a* kunn*a* muhlikee alqur*a* ill*a* waahluh*a* **th***a*limoon**a**

## 28:60

Wam*a* ooteetum min shayin famat*a*AAu al*h*ay*a*ti a**l**dduny*a* wazeenatuh*a* wam*a* AAinda All*a*hi khayrun waabq*a* afal*a* taAAqiloon**a**

## 28:61

Afaman waAAadn*a*hu waAAdan *h*asanan fahuwa l*a*qeehi kaman mattaAAn*a*hu mat*a*AAa al*h*ay*a*ti a**l**dduny*a* thumma huwa yawma alqiy*a*mati mina almu*hd*areen**a**

## 28:62

Wayawma yun*a*deehim fayaqoolu ayna shurak*a*iya alla*th*eena kuntum tazAAumoon**a**

## 28:63

Q*a*la alla*th*eena *h*aqqa AAalayhimu alqawlu rabban*a* h*a*ol*a*i alla*th*eena aghwayn*a* aghwayn*a*hum kam*a* ghawayn*a* tabarran*a* ilayka m*a* k*a*noo iyy*a*n*a* yaAAbudoon**a**

## 28:64

Waqeela odAAoo shurak*a*akum fadaAAawhum falam yastajeeboo lahum waraawoo alAAa*tha*ba law annahum k*a*noo yahtadoon**a**

## 28:65

Wayawma yun*a*deehim fayaqoolu m*atha* ajabtumu almursaleen**a**

## 28:66

FaAAamiyat AAalayhimu alanb*a*o yawmai*th*in fahum l*a* yatas*a*aloon**a**

## 28:67

Faamm*a* man t*a*ba wa*a*mana waAAamila *sa*li*h*an faAAas*a* an yakoona mina almufli*h*een**a**

## 28:68

Warabbuka yakhluqu m*a* yash*a*o wayakht*a*ru m*a* k*a*na lahumu alkhiyaratu sub*ha*na All*a*hi wataAA*a*l*a* AAamm*a* yushrikoon**a**

## 28:69

Warabbuka yaAAlamu m*a* tukinnu *s*udooruhum wam*a* yuAAlinoon**a**

## 28:70

Wahuwa All*a*hu l*a* il*a*ha ill*a* huwa lahu al*h*amdu fee alool*a* wa**a**l*a*khirati walahu al*h*ukmu wailayhi turjaAAoon**a**

## 28:71

Qul araaytum in jaAAala All*a*hu AAalaykumu allayla sarmadan il*a* yawmi alqiy*a*mati man il*a*hun ghayru All*a*hi yateekum bi*d*iy*a*in afal*a* tasmaAAoon**a**

## 28:72

Qul araaytum in jaAAala All*a*hu AAalaykumu a**l**nnah*a*ra sarmadan il*a* yawmi alqiy*a*mati man il*a*hun ghayru All*a*hi yateekum bilaylin taskunoona feehi afal*a* tub*s*iroon**a**

## 28:73

Wamin ra*h*matihi jaAAala lakumu allayla wa**al**nnah*a*ra litaskunoo feehi walitabtaghoo min fa*d*lihi walaAAallakum tashkuroon**a**

## 28:74

Wayawma yun*a*deehim fayaqoolu ayna shurak*a*iya alla*th*eena kuntum tazAAumoon**a**

## 28:75

WanazaAAn*a* min kulli ommatin shaheedan faquln*a* h*a*too burh*a*nakum faAAalimoo anna al*h*aqqa lill*a*hi wa*d*alla AAanhum m*a* k*a*noo yaftaroon**a**

## 28:76

Inna q*a*roona k*a*na min qawmi moos*a* fabagh*a* AAalayhim wa*a*tayn*a*hu mina alkunoozi m*a* inna maf*a*ti*h*ahu latanooo bi**a**lAAu*s*bati olee alquwwati i*th* q*a*la lahu qawmuhu l*a* tafra*h* inna All*a*ha l*a* yu*h*ibbu alfari*h*een**a**

## 28:77

Wa**i**btaghi feem*a* *a*t*a*ka All*a*hu a**l**dd*a*ra al*a*khirata wal*a* tansa na*s*eebaka mina a**l**dduny*a* waa*h*sin kam*a* a*h*sana All*a*hu ilayka wal*a* tabghi alfas*a*da fee alar*d*i inna All*a*ha l*a* yu*h*ibbu almufsideen**a**

## 28:78

Q*a*la innam*a* ooteetuhu AAal*a* AAilmin AAindee awalam yaAAlam anna All*a*ha qad ahlaka min qablihi mina alqurooni man huwa ashaddu minhu quwwatan waaktharu jamAAan wal*a* yusalu AAan *th*unoobihimu almujrimoon**a**

## 28:79

Fakharaja AAal*a* qawmihi fee zeenatihi q*a*la alla*th*eena yureedoona al*h*ay*a*ta a**l**dduny*a* y*a* layta lan*a* mithla m*a* ootiya q*a*roonu innahu la*th*oo *h*&#x61;**thth**&#x69;n AA&#x61;**th**&#x65;em**in**

## 28:80

Waq*a*la alla*th*eena ootoo alAAilma waylakum thaw*a*bu All*a*hi khayrun liman *a*mana waAAamila *sa*li*h*an wal*a* yulaqq*a*h*a* ill*a* a**l***ssa*biroon**a**

## 28:81

Fakhasafn*a* bihi wabid*a*rihi alar*d*a fam*a* k*a*na lahu min fiatin yan*s*uroonahu min dooni All*a*hi wam*a* k*a*na mina almunta*s*ireen**a**

## 28:82

Waa*s*ba*h*a alla*th*eena tamannaw mak*a*nahu bi**a**lamsi yaqooloona waykaanna All*a*ha yabsu*t*u a**l**rrizqa liman yash*a*o min AAib*a*dihi wayaqdiru lawl*a* an manna All*a*hu AAalayn*a* lakhasafa bin*a* waykaannahu l*a* yufli*h*u alk*a*firoon**a**

## 28:83

Tilka a**l**dd*a*ru al*a*khiratu najAAaluh*a* lilla*th*eena l*a* yureedoona AAuluwwan fee alar*d*i wal*a* fas*a*dan wa**a**lAA*a*qibatu lilmuttaqeen**a**

## 28:84

Man j*a*a bi**a**l*h*asanati falahu khayrun minh*a* waman j*a*a bi**al**ssayyiati fal*a* yujz*a* alla*th*eena AAamiloo a**l**ssayyi*a*ti ill*a* m*a* k*a*noo yaAAmaloon**a**

## 28:85

Inna alla*th*ee fara*d*a AAalayka alqur*a*na lar*a*dduka il*a* maAA*a*din qul rabbee aAAlamu man j*a*a bi**a**lhud*a* waman huwa fee *d*al*a*lin mubeen**in**

## 28:86

Wam*a* kunta tarjoo an yulq*a* ilayka alkit*a*bu ill*a* ra*h*matan min rabbika fal*a* takoonanna **th**&#x61;heeran lilk*a*fireen**a**

## 28:87

Wal*a* ya*s*uddunnaka AAan *a*y*a*ti All*a*hi baAAda i*th* onzilat ilayka wa**o**dAAu il*a* rabbika wal*a* takoonanna mina almushrikeen**a**

## 28:88

Wal*a* tadAAu maAAa All*a*hi il*a*han *a*khara l*a* il*a*ha ill*a* huwa kullu shayin h*a*likun ill*a* wajhahu lahu al*h*ukmu wailayhi turjaAAoon**a**

## 29:1

Alifl*a*mmeem

## 29:2

A*h*asiba a**l**nn*a*su an yutrakoo an yaqooloo *a*mann*a* wahum l*a* yuftanoon**a**

## 29:3

Walaqad fatann*a* alla*th*eena min qablihim falayaAAlamanna All*a*hu alla*th*eena *s*adaqoo walayaAAlamanna alk*ath*ibeen**a**

## 29:4

Am *h*asiba alla*th*eena yaAAmaloona a**l**ssayyi*a*ti an yasbiqoon*a* s*a*a m*a* ya*h*kumoon**a**

## 29:5

Man k*a*na yarjoo liq*a*a All*a*hi fainna ajala All*a*hi la*a*tin wahuwa a**l**ssameeAAu alAAaleem**u**

## 29:6

Waman j*a*hada fainnam*a* yuj*a*hidu linafsihi inna All*a*ha laghaniyyun AAani alAA*a*lameen**a**

## 29:7

Wa**a**lla*th*eena *a*manoo waAAamiloo a**l***ssa*li*ha*ti lanukaffiranna AAanhum sayyi*a*tihim walanajziyannahum a*h*sana alla*th*ee k*a*noo yaAAmaloon**a**

## 29:8

Wawa*ss*ayn*a* alins*a*na biw*a*lidayhi *h*usnan wain j*a*had*a*ka litushrika bee m*a* laysa laka bihi AAilmun fal*a* tu*t*iAAhum*a* ilayya marjiAAukum faonabbiokum bim*a* kuntum taAAmaloon**a**

## 29:9

Wa**a**lla*th*eena *a*manoo waAAamiloo a**l***ssa*li*ha*ti lanudkhilannahum fee a**l***ssa*li*h*een**a**

## 29:10

Wamina a**l**nn*a*si man yaqoolu *a*mann*a* bi**A**ll*a*hi fai*tha* oo*th*iya fee All*a*hi jaAAala fitnata a**l**nn*a*si kaAAa*tha*bi All*a*hi walain j*a*a na*s*run min rabbika layaqoolunna inn*a* kunn*a* maAAakum awalaysa All*a*hu biaAAlama bim*a* fee *s*udoori alAA*a*lameen**a**

## 29:11

WalayaAAlamanna All*a*hu alla*th*eena *a*manoo walayaAAlamanna almun*a*fiqeen**a**

## 29:12

Waq*a*la alla*th*eena kafaroo lilla*th*eena *a*manoo ittabiAAoo sabeelan*a* walna*h*mil kha*ta*y*a*kum wam*a* hum bi*ha*mileena min kha*ta*y*a*hum min shayin innahum lak*ath*iboon**a**

## 29:13

Walaya*h*milunna athq*a*lahum waathq*a*lan maAAa athq*a*lihim walayusalunna yawma alqiy*a*mati AAamm*a* k*a*noo yaftaroon**a**

## 29:14

Walaqad arsaln*a* noo*h*an il*a* qawmihi falabitha feehim alfa sanatin ill*a* khamseena AA*a*man faakha*th*ahumu a**l***tt*oof*a*nu wahum **th***a*limoon**a**

## 29:15

Faanjayn*a*hu waa*s**ha*ba a**l**ssafeenati wajaAAaln*a*h*a* *a*yatan lilAA*a*lameen**a**

## 29:16

Waibr*a*heema i*th* q*a*la liqawmihi oAAbudoo All*a*ha wa**i**ttaqoohu *tha*likum khayrun lakum in kuntum taAAlamoon**a**

## 29:17

Innam*a* taAAbudoona min dooni All*a*hi awth*a*nan watakhluqoona ifkan inna alla*th*eena taAAbudoona min dooni All*a*hi l*a* yamlikoona lakum rizqan fa**i**btaghoo AAinda All*a*hi a**l**rrizqa wa**o**AAbudoohu wa**o**shkuroo lahu ilayhi turjaAAoon**a**

## 29:18

Wain tuka*thth*iboo faqad ka*thth*aba omamun min qablikum wam*a* AAal*a* a**l**rrasooli ill*a* albal*a*ghu almubeen**u**

## 29:19

Awalam yaraw kayfa yubdio All*a*hu alkhalqa thumma yuAAeeduhu inna *tha*lika AAal*a* All*a*hi yaseer**un**

## 29:20

Qul seeroo fee alar*d*i fa**o**&#x6E;**th**&#x75;roo kayfa badaa alkhalqa thumma All*a*hu yunshio a**l**nnashata al*a*khirata inna All*a*ha AAal*a* kulli shayin qadeer**un**

## 29:21

YuAAa*thth*ibu man yash*a*o wayar*h*amu man yash*a*o wailayhi tuqlaboon**a**

## 29:22

Wam*a* antum bimuAAjizeena fee alar*d*i wal*a* fee a**l**ssam*a*i wam*a* lakum min dooni All*a*hi min waliyyin wal*a* na*s*eer**in**

## 29:23

Wa**a**lla*th*eena kafaroo bi*a*y*a*ti All*a*hi waliq*a*ihi ol*a*ika yaisoo min ra*h*matee waol*a*ika lahum AAa*tha*bun aleem**un**

## 29:24

Fam*a* k*a*na jaw*a*ba qawmihi ill*a* an q*a*loo oqtuloohu aw *h*arriqoohu faanj*a*hu All*a*hu mina a**l**nn*a*ri inna fee *tha*lika la*a*y*a*tin liqawmin yuminoon**a**

## 29:25

Waq*a*la innam*a* ittakha*th*tum min dooni All*a*hi awth*a*nan mawaddata baynikum fee al*h*ay*a*ti a**l**dduny*a* thumma yawma alqiy*a*mati yakfuru baAA*d*ukum bibaAA*d*in wayalAAanu baAA*d*ukum baAA*d*an wamaw*a*kumu a**l**nn*a*ru wam*a* lakum min n*as*ireen**a**

## 29:26

Fa*a*mana lahu loo*t*un waq*a*la innee muh*a*jirun il*a* rabbee innahu huwa alAAazeezu al*h*akeem**u**

## 29:27

Wawahabn*a* lahu is*ha*qa wayaAAqooba wajaAAaln*a* fee *th*urriyyatihi a**l**nnubuwwata wa**a**lkit*a*ba wa*a*tayn*a*hu ajrahu fee a**l**dduny*a* wainnahu fee al*a*khirati lamina a**l***ssa*li*h*een**a**

## 29:28

Waloo*t*an i*th* q*a*la liqawmihi innakum latatoona alf*ah*ishata m*a* sabaqakum bih*a* min a*h*adin mina alAA*a*lameen**a**

## 29:29

Ainnakum latatoona a**l**rrij*a*la wataq*t*aAAoona a**l**ssabeela watatoona fee n*a*deekumu almunkara fam*a* k*a*na jaw*a*ba qawmihi ill*a* an q*a*loo itin*a* biAAa*tha*bi All*a*hi in kunta mina a**l***ssa*diqeen**a**

## 29:30

Q*a*la rabbi on*s*urnee AAal*a* alqawmi almufsideen**a**

## 29:31

Walamm*a* j*a*at rusulun*a* ibr*a*heema bi**a**lbushr*a* q*a*loo inn*a* muhlikoo ahli h*ath*ihi alqaryati inna ahlah*a* k*a*noo **th***a*limeen**a**

## 29:32

Q*a*la inna feeh*a* loo*t*an q*a*loo na*h*nu aAAlamu biman feeh*a* lanunajjiyannahu waahlahu ill*a* imraatahu k*a*nat mina algh*a*bireen**a**

## 29:33

Walamm*a* an j*a*at rusulun*a* loo*t*an seea bihim wa*da*qa bihim *th*arAAan waq*a*loo l*a* takhaf wal*a* ta*h*zan inn*a* munajjooka waahlaka ill*a* imraataka k*a*nat mina algh*a*bireen**a**

## 29:34

Inn*a* munziloona AAal*a* ahli h*ath*ihi alqaryati rijzan mina a**l**ssam*a*i bim*a* k*a*noo yafsuqoon**a**

## 29:35

Walaqad tarakn*a* minh*a* *a*yatan bayyinatan liqawmin yaAAqiloon**a**

## 29:36

Wail*a* madyana akh*a*hum shuAAayban faq*a*la y*a* qawmi oAAbudoo All*a*ha wa**o**rjoo alyawma al*a*khira wal*a* taAAthaw fee alar*d*i mufsideen**a**

## 29:37

Faka*thth*aboohu faakha*th*athumu a**l**rrajfatu faa*s*ba*h*oo fee d*a*rihim j*a*thimeen**a**

## 29:38

WaAA*a*dan wathamooda waqad tabayyana lakum min mas*a*kinihim wazayyana lahumu a**l**shshay*ta*nu aAAm*a*lahum fa*s*addahum AAani a**l**ssabeeli wak*a*noo mustab*s*ireen**a**

## 29:39

Waq*a*roona wafirAAawna wah*a*m*a*na walaqad j*a*ahum moos*a* bi**a**lbayyin*a*ti fa**i**stakbaroo fee alar*d*i wam*a* k*a*noo s*a*biqeen**a**

## 29:40

Fakullan akha*th*n*a* bi*th*anbihi faminhum man arsaln*a* AAalayhi *has*iban waminhum man akha*th*athu a**l***ss*ay*h*atu waminhum man khasafn*a* bihi alar*d*a waminhum man aghraqn*a* wam*a* k*a*na All*a*hu liy&#x61;**th**&#x6C;imahum wal*a*kin k*a*noo anfusahum y&#x61;**th**&#x6C;imoon**a**

## 29:41

Mathalu alla*th*eena ittakha*th*oo min dooni All*a*hi awliy*a*a kamathali alAAankabooti ittakha*th*at baytan wainna awhana albuyooti labaytu alAAankabooti law k*a*noo yaAAlamoon**a**

## 29:42

Inna All*a*ha yaAAlamu m*a* yadAAoona min doonihi min shayin wahuwa alAAazeezu al*h*akeem**u**

## 29:43

Watilka alamth*a*lu na*d*ribuh*a* li**l**nn*a*si wam*a* yaAAqiluh*a* ill*a* alAA*a*limoon**a**

## 29:44

Khalaqa All*a*hu a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*a bi**a**l*h*aqqi inna fee *tha*lika la*a*yatan lilmumineen**a**

## 29:45

Otlu m*a* oo*h*iya ilayka mina alkit*a*bi waaqimi a**l***ss*al*a*ta inna a**l***ss*al*a*ta tanh*a* AAani alfa*h*sh*a*i wa**a**lmunkari wala*th*ikru All*a*hi akbaru wa**A**ll*a*hu yaAAlamu m*a* ta*s*naAAoon**a**

## 29:46

Wal*a* tuj*a*diloo ahla alkit*a*bi ill*a* bi**a**llatee hiya a*h*sanu ill*a* alla*th*eena **th**&#x61;lamoo minhum waqooloo *a*mann*a* bi**a**lla*th*ee onzila ilayn*a* waonzila ilaykum wail*a*hun*a* wail*a*hukum w*ah*idun wana*h*nu lahu muslimoon**a**

## 29:47

Waka*tha*lika anzaln*a* ilayka alkit*a*ba fa**a**lla*th*eena *a*tayn*a*humu alkit*a*ba yuminoona bihi wamin h*a*ol*a*i man yuminu bihi wam*a* yaj*h*adu bi*a*y*a*tin*a* ill*a* alk*a*firoon**a**

## 29:48

Wam*a* kunta tatloo min qablihi min kit*a*bin wal*a* takhu*tt*uhu biyameenika i*th*an la**i**rt*a*ba almub*t*iloon**a**

## 29:49

Bal huwa *a*y*a*tun bayyin*a*tun fee *s*udoori alla*th*eena ootoo alAAilma wam*a* yaj*h*adu bi*a*y*a*tin*a* ill*a* a**l****thth***a*limoon**a**

## 29:50

Waq*a*loo lawl*a* onzila AAalayhi *a*y*a*tun min rabbihi qul innam*a* al*a*y*a*tu AAinda All*a*hi wainnam*a* an*a* na*th*eerun mubeen**un**

## 29:51

Awalam yakfihim ann*a* anzaln*a* AAalayka alkit*a*ba yutl*a* AAalayhim inna fee *tha*lika lara*h*matan wa*th*ikr*a* liqawmin yuminoon**a**

## 29:52

Qul kaf*a* bi**A**ll*a*hi baynee wabaynakum shaheedan yaAAlamu m*a* fee a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i wa**a**lla*th*eena *a*manoo bi**a**lb*at*ili wakafaroo bi**A**ll*a*hi ol*a*ika humu alkh*a*siroon**a**

## 29:53

WayastaAAjiloonaka bi**a**lAAa*tha*bi walawl*a* ajalun musamman laj*a*ahumu alAAa*tha*bu walayatiyannahum baghtatan wahum l*a* yashAAuroon**a**

## 29:54

YastaAAjiloonaka bi**a**lAAa*tha*bi wainna jahannama lamu*h*ee*t*atun bi**a**lk*a*fireen**a**

## 29:55

Yawma yaghsh*a*humu alAAa*tha*bu min fawqihim wamin ta*h*ti arjulihim wayaqoolu *th*ooqoo m*a* kuntum taAAmaloon**a**

## 29:56

Y*a* AAib*a*diya alla*th*eena *a*manoo inna ar*d*ee w*a*siAAatun faiyy*a*ya fa**o**AAbudoon**i**

## 29:57

Kullu nafsin *tha*iqatu almawti thumma ilayn*a* turjaAAoon**a**

## 29:58

Wa**a**lla*th*eena *a*manoo waAAamiloo a**l***ssa*li*ha*ti lanubawwiannahum mina aljannati ghurafan tajree min ta*h*tih*a* alanh*a*ru kh*a*lideena feeh*a* niAAma ajru alAA*a*mileen**a**

## 29:59

Alla*th*eena *s*abaroo waAAal*a* rabbihim yatawakkaloon**a**

## 29:60

Wakaayyin min d*a*bbatin l*a* ta*h*milu rizqah*a* All*a*hu yarzuquh*a* waiyy*a*kum wahuwa a**l**ssameeAAu alAAaleem**u**

## 29:61

Walain saaltahum man khalaqa a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*a wasakhkhara a**l**shshamsa wa**a**lqamara layaqoolunna All*a*hu faann*a* yufakoon**a**

## 29:62

All*a*hu yabsu*t*u a**l**rrizqa liman yash*a*o min AAib*a*dihi wayaqdiru lahu inna All*a*ha bikulli shayin AAaleem**un**

## 29:63

Walain saaltahum man nazzala mina a**l**ssam*a*i m*a*an faa*h*y*a* bihi alar*d*a min baAAdi mawtih*a* layaqoolunna All*a*hu quli al*h*amdu lill*a*hi bal aktharuhum l*a* yaAAqiloon**a**

## 29:64

Wam*a* h*ath*ihi al*h*ay*a*tu a**l**dduny*a* ill*a* lahwun walaAAibun wainna a**l**dd*a*ra al*a*khirata lahiya al*h*ayaw*a*nu law k*a*noo yaAAlamoon**a**

## 29:65

Fai*tha* rakiboo fee alfulki daAAawoo All*a*ha mukhli*s*eena lahu a**l**ddeena falamm*a* najj*a*hum il*a* albarri i*tha* hum yushrikoon**a**

## 29:66

Liyakfuroo bim*a* *a*tayn*a*hum waliyatamattaAAoo fasawfa yaAAlamoon**a**

## 29:67

Awalam yaraw ann*a* jaAAaln*a* *h*araman *a*minan wayutakha*tt*afu a**l**nn*a*su min *h*awlihim afabi**a**lb*at*ili yuminoona wabiniAAmati All*a*hi yakfuroon**a**

## 29:68

Waman &#x61;**th**&#x6C;amu mimmani iftar*a* AAal*a* All*a*hi ka*th*iban aw ka*thth*aba bi**a**l*h*aqqi lamm*a* j*a*ahu alaysa fee jahannama mathwan lilk*a*fireen**a**

## 29:69

Wa**a**lla*th*eena j*a*hadoo feen*a* lanahdiyannahum subulan*a* wainna All*a*ha lamaAAa almu*h*sineen**a**

## 30:1

Alifl*a*mmeem

## 30:2

Ghulibati a**l**rroom**u**

## 30:3

Fee adn*a* alar*d*i wahum min baAAdi ghalabihim sayaghliboon**a**

## 30:4

Fee bi*d*AAi sineena lill*a*hi alamru min qablu wamin baAAdu wayawmai*th*in yafra*h*u almuminoon**a**

## 30:5

Bina*s*ri All*a*hi yan*s*uru man yash*a*o wahuwa alAAazeezu a**l**rra*h*eem**u**

## 30:6

WaAAda All*a*hi l*a* yukhlifu All*a*hu waAAdahu wal*a*kinna akthara a**l**nn*a*si l*a* yaAAlamoon**a**

## 30:7

YaAAlamoona **th***a*hiran mina al*h*ay*a*ti a**l**dduny*a* wahum AAani al*a*khirati hum gh*a*filoon**a**

## 30:8

Awalam yatafakkaroo fee anfusihim m*a* khalaqa All*a*hu a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*a wam*a* baynahum*a* ill*a* bi**a**l*h*aqqi waajalin musamman wainna katheeran mina a**l**nn*a*si biliq*a*i rabbihim lak*a*firoon**a**

## 30:9

Awalam yaseeroo fee alar*d*i faya&#x6E;**th**&#x75;roo kayfa k*a*na AA*a*qibatu alla*th*eena min qablihim k*a*noo ashadda minhum quwwatan waath*a*roo alar*d*a waAAamarooh*a* akthara mimm*a* AAamarooh*a* waj*a*athum rusuluhum bi**a**lbayyin*a*ti fam*a* k*a*na All*a*hu liy&#x61;**th**&#x6C;imahum wal*a*kin k*a*noo anfusahum y&#x61;**th**&#x6C;imoon**a**

## 30:10

Thumma k*a*na AA*a*qibata alla*th*eena as*a*oo a**l**ssoo*a* an ka*thth*aboo bi*a*y*a*ti All*a*hi wak*a*noo bih*a* yastahzioon**a**

## 30:11

All*a*hu yabdao alkhalqa thumma yuAAeeduhu thumma ilayhi turjaAAoon**a**

## 30:12

Wayawma taqoomu a**l**ss*a*AAatu yublisu almujrimoon**a**

## 30:13

Walam yakun lahum min shurak*a*ihim shufaAA*a*o wak*a*noo bishurak*a*ihim k*a*fireen**a**

## 30:14

Wayawma taqoomu a**l**ss*a*AAatu yawmai*th*in yatafarraqoon**a**

## 30:15

Faamm*a* alla*th*eena *a*manoo waAAamiloo a**l***ssa*li*ha*ti fahum fee raw*d*atin yu*h*baroon**a**

## 30:16

Waamm*a* alla*th*eena kafaroo waka*thth*aboo bi*a*y*a*tin*a* waliq*a*i al*a*khirati faol*a*ika fee alAAa*tha*bi mu*hd*aroon**a**

## 30:17

Fasub*ha*na All*a*hi *h*eena tumsoona wa*h*eena tu*s*bi*h*oon**a**

## 30:18

Walahu al*h*amdu fee a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i waAAashiyyan wa*h*eena t&#x75;**th**&#x68;iroon**a**

## 30:19

Yukhriju al*h*ayya mina almayyiti wayukhriju almayyita mina al*h*ayyi wayu*h*yee alar*d*a baAAda mawtih*a* waka*tha*lika tukhrajoon**a**

## 30:20

Wamin *a*y*a*tihi an khalaqakum min tur*a*bin thumma i*tha* antum basharun tantashiroon**a**

## 30:21

Wamin *a*y*a*tihi an khalaqa lakum min anfusikum azw*a*jan litaskunoo ilayh*a* wajaAAala baynakum mawaddatan wara*h*matan inna fee *tha*lika la*a*y*a*tin liqawmin yatafakkaroon**a**

## 30:22

Wamin *a*y*a*tihi khalqu a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i wa**i**khtil*a*fu alsinatikum waalw*a*nikum inna fee *tha*lika la*a*y*a*tin lilAA*a*limeen**a**

## 30:23

Wamin *a*y*a*tihi man*a*mukum bi**a**llayli wa**al**nnah*a*ri wa**i**btigh*a*okum min fa*d*lihi inna fee *tha*lika la*a*y*a*tin liqawmin yasmaAAoon**a**

## 30:24

Wamin *a*y*a*tihi yureekumu albarqa khawfan wa*t*amaAAan wayunazzilu mina a**l**ssam*a*i m*a*an fayu*h*yee bihi alar*d*a baAAda mawtih*a* inna fee *tha*lika la*a*y*a*tin liqawmin yaAAqiloon**a**

## 30:25

Wamin *a*y*a*tihi an taqooma a**l**ssam*a*o wa**a**lar*d*u biamrihi thumma i*tha* daAA*a*kum daAAwatan mina alar*d*i i*tha* antum takhrujoon**a**

## 30:26

Walahu man fee a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i kullun lahu q*a*nitoon**a**

## 30:27

Wahuwa alla*th*ee yabdao alkhalqa thumma yuAAeeduhu wahuwa ahwanu AAalayhi walahu almathalu alaAAl*a* fee a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i wahuwa alAAazeezu al*h*akeem**u**

## 30:28

*D*araba lakum mathalan min anfusikum hal lakum mi mm*a* malakat aym*a*nukum min shurak*a*a fee m*a* razaqn*a*kum faantum feehi saw*a*on takh*a*foonahum kakheefatikum anfusakum ka*tha*lika nufa*ss*ilu al*a*y*a*ti liqawmin yaAAqiloon**a**

## 30:29

Bali ittabaAAa alla*th*eena **th**&#x61;lamoo ahw*a*ahum bighayri AAilmin faman yahdee man a*d*alla All*a*hu wam*a* lahum min n*as*ireen**a**

## 30:30

Faaqim wajhaka li**l**ddeeni *h*aneefan fi*t*rata All*a*hi allatee fa*t*ara a**l**nn*a*sa AAalayh*a* l*a* tabdeela likhalqi All*a*hi *tha*lika a**l**ddeenu alqayyimu wal*a*kinna akthara a**l**nn*a*si l*a* yaAAlamoon**a**

## 30:31

Muneebeena ilayhi wa**i**ttaqoohu waaqeemoo a**l***ss*al*a*ta wal*a* takoonoo mina almushrikeen**a**

## 30:32

Mina alla*th*eena farraqoo deenahum wak*a*noo shiyaAAan kullu *h*izbin bim*a* ladayhim fari*h*oon**a**

## 30:33

Wai*tha* massa a**l**nn*a*sa *d*urrun daAAaw rabbahum muneebeena ilayhi thumma i*tha* a*tha*qahum minhu ra*h*matan i*tha* fareequn minhum birabbihim yushrikoon**a**

## 30:34

Liyakfuroo bim*a* *a*tayn*a*hum fatamattaAAoo fasawfa taAAlamoon**a**

## 30:35

Am anzaln*a* AAalayhim sul*ta*nan fahuwa yatakallamu bim*a* k*a*noo bihi yushrikoon**a**

## 30:36

Wa**i***tha* a*th*aqn*a* a**l**nn*a*sa ra*h*matan fari*h*oo bih*a* wain tu*s*ibhum sayyiatun bim*a* qaddamat aydeehim i*tha* hum yaqna*t*oon**a**

## 30:37

Awalam yaraw anna All*a*ha yabsu*t*u a**l**rrizqa liman yash*a*o wayaqdiru inna fee *tha*lika la*a*y*a*tin liqawmin yuminoon**a**

## 30:38

Fa*a*ti *tha* alqurb*a* *h*aqqahu wa**a**lmiskeena wa**i**bna a**l**ssabeeli *tha*lika khayrun lilla*th*eena yureedoona wajha All*a*hi waol*a*ika humu almufli*h*oon**a**

## 30:39

Wam*a* *a*taytum min riban liyarbuwa fee amw*a*li a**l**nn*a*si fal*a* yarboo AAinda All*a*hi wam*a* *a*taytum min zak*a*tin tureedoona wajha All*a*hi faol*a*ika humu almu*d*AAifoon**a**

## 30:40

All*a*hu alla*th*ee khalaqakum thumma razaqakum thumma yumeetukum thumma yu*h*yeekum hal min shurak*a*ikum man yafAAalu min *tha*likum min shayin sub*ha*nahu wataAA*a*l*a* AAamm*a* yushrikoon**a**

## 30:41

**Th**&#x61;hara alfas*a*du fee albarri wa**a**lba*h*ri bim*a* kasabat aydee a**l**nn*a*si liyu*th*eeqahum baAA*d*a alla*th*ee AAamiloo laAAallahum yarjiAAoon**a**

## 30:42

Qul seeroo fee alar*d*i fa**o**&#x6E;**th**&#x75;roo kayfa k*a*na AA*a*qibatu alla*th*eena min qablu k*a*na aktharuhum mushrikeen**a**

## 30:43

Faaqim wajhaka li**l**ddeeni alqayyimi min qabli an yatiya yawmun l*a* maradda lahu mina All*a*hi yawmai*th*in ya*ss*addaAAoon**a**

## 30:44

Man kafara faAAalayhi kufruhu waman AAamila *sa*li*h*an falianfusihim yamhadoon**a**

## 30:45

Liyajziya alla*th*eena *a*manoo waAAamiloo a**l***ssa*li*ha*ti min fa*d*lihi innahu l*a* yu*h*ibbu alk*a*fireen**a**

## 30:46

Wamin *a*y*a*tihi an yursila a**l**rriy*ah*a mubashshir*a*tin waliyu*th*eeqakum min ra*h*matihi walitajriya alfulku biamrihi walitabtaghoo min fa*d*lihi walaAAallakum tashkuroon**a**

## 30:47

Walaqad arsaln*a* min qablika rusulan il*a* qawmihim faj*a*oohum bi**a**lbayyin*a*ti fa**i**ntaqamn*a* mina alla*th*eena ajramoo wak*a*na *h*aqqan AAalayn*a* na*s*ru almumineen**a**

## 30:48

All*a*hu alla*th*ee yursilu a**l**rriy*ah*a fatutheeru sa*ha*ban fayabsu*t*uhu fee a**l**ssam*a*i kayfa yash*a*o wayajAAaluhu kisafan fatar*a* alwadqa yakhruju min khil*a*lihi fai*tha* a*sa*ba bihi man yash*a*o min AAib*a*dihi i*tha* hum yastabshiroon**a**

## 30:49

Wain k*a*noo min qabli an yunazzala AAalayhim min qablihi lamubliseen**a**

## 30:50

Fa**o**&#x6E;**th**&#x75;r il*a* *a*th*a*ri ra*h*mati All*a*hi kayfa yu*h*yee alar*d*a baAAda mawtih*a* inna *tha*lika lamu*h*yee almawt*a* wahuwa AAal*a* kulli shayin qadeer**un**

## 30:51

Walain arsaln*a* ree*h*an faraawhu mu*s*farran l&#x61;**th**&#x61;lloo min baAAdihi yakfuroon**a**

## 30:52

Fainnaka l*a* tusmiAAu almawt*a* wal*a* tusmiAAu a**l***ss*umma a**l**dduAA*a*a i*tha* wallaw mudbireen**a**

## 30:53

Wam*a* anta bih*a*di alAAumyi AAan *d*al*a*latihim in tusmiAAu ill*a* man yuminu bi*a*y*a*tin*a* fahum muslimoon**a**

## 30:54

All*a*hu alla*th*ee khalaqakum min *d*aAAfin thumma jaAAala min baAAdi *d*aAAfin quwwatan thumma jaAAala min baAAdi quwwatin *d*aAAfan washaybatan yakhluqu m*a* yash*a*o wahuwa alAAaleemu alqadeer**u**

## 30:55

Wayawma taqoomu a**l**ss*a*AAatu yuqsimu almujrimoona m*a* labithoo ghayra s*a*AAatin ka*tha*lika k*a*noo yufakoon**a**

## 30:56

Waq*a*la alla*th*eena ootoo alAAilma wa**a**leem*a*na laqad labithtum fee kit*a*bi All*a*hi il*a* yawmi albaAAthi fah*atha* yawmu albaAAthi wal*a*kinnakum kuntum l*a* taAAlamoon**a**

## 30:57

Fayawmai*th*in l*a* yanfaAAu alla*th*eena **th**&#x61;lamoo maAA*th*iratuhum wal*a* hum yustaAAtaboon**a**

## 30:58

Walaqad *d*arabn*a* li**l**nn*a*si fee h*atha* alqur*a*ni min kulli mathalin walain jitahum bi*a*yatin layaqoolanna alla*th*eena kafaroo in antum ill*a* mub*t*iloon**a**

## 30:59

Ka*tha*lika ya*t*baAAu All*a*hu AAal*a* quloobi alla*th*eena l*a* yaAAlamoon**a**

## 30:60

Fa**i***s*bir inna waAAda All*a*hi *h*aqqun wal*a* yastakhiffannaka alla*th*eena l*a* yooqinoon**a**

## 31:1

Alifl*a*mmeem

## 31:2

Tilka *a*y*a*tu alkit*a*bi al*h*akeem**i**

## 31:3

Hudan wara*h*matan lilmu*h*sineen**a**

## 31:4

Alla*th*eena yuqeemoona a**l***ss*al*a*ta wayutoona a**l**zzak*a*ta wahum bi**a**l*a*khirati hum yooqinoon**a**

## 31:5

Ol*a*ika AAal*a* hudan min rabbihim waol*a*ika humu almufli*h*oon**a**

## 31:6

Wamina a**l**nn*a*si man yashtaree lahwa al*h*adeethi liyu*d*illa AAan sabeeli All*a*hi bighayri AAilmin wayattakhi*th*ah*a* huzuwan ol*a*ika lahum AAa*tha*bun muheen**un**

## 31:7

Wai*tha* tutl*a* AAalayhi *a*y*a*tun*a* wall*a* mustakbiran kaan lam yasmaAAh*a* kaanna fee o*th*unayhi waqran fabashshirhu biAAa*tha*bin aleem**in**

## 31:8

Inna alla*th*eena *a*manoo waAAamiloo a**l***ssa*li*ha*ti lahum jann*a*tu a**l**nnaAAeem**i**

## 31:9

Kh*a*lideena feeh*a* waAAda All*a*hi *h*aqqan wahuwa alAAazeezu al*h*akeem**u**

## 31:10

Khalaqa a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti bighayri AAamadin tarawnah*a* waalq*a* fee alar*d*i raw*a*siya an tameeda bikum wabaththa feeh*a* min kulli d*a*bbatin waanzaln*a* mina a**l**ssam*a*i m*a*an faanbatn*a* feeh*a* min kulli zawjin kareem**in**

## 31:11

H*atha* khalqu All*a*hi faaroonee m*atha* khalaqa alla*th*eena min doonihi bali a**l****thth***a*limoona fee *d*al*a*lin mubeen**in**

## 31:12

Walaqad *a*tayn*a* luqm*a*na al*h*ikmata ani oshkur lill*a*hi waman yashkur fainnam*a* yashkuru linafsihi waman kafara fainna All*a*ha ghaniyyun *h*ameed**un**

## 31:13

Wai*th* q*a*la luqm*a*nu li**i**bnihi wahuwa yaAA&#x69;**th**&#x75;hu y*a* bunayya l*a* tushrik bi**A**ll*a*hi inna a**l**shshirka l&#x61;**th**&#x75;lmun AA&#x61;**th**&#x65;em**un**

## 31:14

Wawa*ss*ayn*a* alins*a*na biw*a*lidayhi *h*amalathu ommuhu wahnan AAal*a* wahnin wafi*sa*luhu fee AA*a*mayni ani oshkur lee waliw*a*lidayka ilayya alma*s*eer**u**

## 31:15

Wain j*a*had*a*ka AAal*a* an tushrika bee m*a* laysa laka bihi AAilmun fal*a* tu*t*iAAhum*a* wa*sah*ibhum*a* fee a**l**dduny*a* maAAroofan wa**i**ttabiAA sabeela man an*a*ba ilayya thumma ilayya marjiAAukum faonabbiokum bim*a* kuntum taAAmaloon**a**

## 31:16

Y*a* bunayya innah*a* in taku mithq*a*la *h*abbatin min khardalin fatakun fee *s*akhratin aw fee a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti aw fee alar*d*i yati bih*a* All*a*hu inna All*a*ha la*t*eefun khabeer**un**

## 31:17

Y*a* bunayya aqimi a**l***ss*al*a*ta wamur bi**a**lmaAAroofi wa**i**nha AAani almunkari wa**i***s*bir AAal*a* m*a* a*sa*baka inna *tha*lika min AAazmi alomoor**i**

## 31:18

Wal*a* tu*s*aAAAAir khaddaka li**l**nn*a*si wal*a* tamshi fee alar*d*i mara*h*an inna All*a*ha l*a* yu*h*ibbu kulla mukht*a*lin fakhoor**in**

## 31:19

Wa**i**q*s*id fee mashyika wa**o**gh*d*u*d* min *s*awtika inna ankara ala*s*w*a*ti la*s*awtu al*h*ameer**i**

## 31:20

Alam taraw anna All*a*ha sakhkhara lakum m*a* fee a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wam*a* fee alar*d*i waasbagha AAalaykum niAAamahu **th***a*hiratan wab*at*inatan wamina a**l**nn*a*si man yuj*a*dilu fee All*a*hi bighayri AAilmin wal*a* hudan wal*a* kit*a*bin muneer**in**

## 31:21

Wai*tha* qeela lahumu ittabiAAoo m*a* anzala All*a*hu q*a*loo bal nattabiAAu m*a* wajadn*a* AAalayhi *a*b*a*an*a* awalaw k*a*na a**l**shshay*ta*nu yadAAoohum il*a* AAa*tha*bi a**l**ssaAAeer**i**

## 31:22

Waman yuslim wajhahu il*a* All*a*hi wahuwa mu*h*sinun faqadi istamsaka bi**a**lAAurwati alwuthq*a* wail*a* All*a*hi AA*a*qibatu alomoor**i**

## 31:23

Waman kafara fal*a* ya*h*zunka kufruhu ilayn*a* marjiAAuhum fanunabbiohum bim*a* AAamiloo inna All*a*ha AAaleemun bi*tha*ti a**l***ss*udoor**i**

## 31:24

NumattiAAuhum qaleelan thumma na*dt*arruhum il*a* AAa*tha*bin ghale&#x65;**th****in**

## 31:25

Walain saaltahum man khalaqa a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*a layaqoolunna All*a*hu quli al*h*amdu lill*a*hi bal aktharuhum l*a* yaAAlamoon**a**

## 31:26

Lill*a*hi m*a* fee a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i inna All*a*ha huwa alghaniyyu al*h*ameed**u**

## 31:27

Walaw annam*a* fee alar*d*i min shajaratin aql*a*mun wa**a**lba*h*ru yamudduhu min baAAdihi sabAAatu ab*h*urin m*a* nafidat kalim*a*tu All*a*hi inna All*a*ha AAazeezun *h*akeem**un**

## 31:28

M*a* khalqukum wal*a* baAAthukum ill*a* kanafsin w*ah*idatin inna All*a*ha sameeAAun ba*s*eer**un**

## 31:29

Alam tara anna All*a*ha yooliju allayla fee a**l**nnah*a*ri wayooliju a**l**nnah*a*ra fee allayli wasakhkhara a**l**shshamsa wa**a**lqamara kullun yajree il*a* ajalin musamman waanna All*a*ha bim*a* taAAmaloona khabeer**un**

## 31:30

*Tha*lika bianna All*a*ha huwa al*h*aqqu waanna m*a* yadAAoona min doonihi alb*at*ilu waanna All*a*ha huwa alAAaliyyu alkabeer**u**

## 31:31

Alam tara anna alfulka tajree fee alba*h*ri biniAAmati All*a*hi liyuriyakum min *a*y*a*tihi inna fee *tha*lika la*a*y*a*tin likulli *s*abb*a*rin shakoor**in**

## 31:32

Wai*tha* ghashiyahum mawjun ka**al****thth**&#x75;lali daAAawoo All*a*ha mukhli*s*eena lahu a**l**ddeena falamm*a* najj*a*hum il*a* albarri faminhum muqta*s*idun wam*a* yaj*h*adu bi*a*y*a*tin*a* ill*a* kullu khatt*a*rin kafoor**in**

## 31:33

Y*a* ayyuh*a* a**l**nn*a*su ittaqoo rabbakum wa**i**khshaw yawman l*a* yajzee w*a*lidun AAan waladihi wal*a* mawloodun huwa j*a*zin AAan w*a*lidihi shayan inna waAAda All*a*hi *h*aqqun fal*a* taghurrannakumu al*h*ay*a*tu a**l**dduny*a* wal*a* yaghurrannakum bi**A**ll*a*hi algharoor**u**

## 31:34

Inna All*a*ha AAindahu AAilmu a**l**ss*a*AAati wayunazzilu alghaytha wayaAAlamu m*a* fee alar*ha*mi wam*a* tadree nafsun m*atha* taksibu ghadan wam*a* tadree nafsun biayyi ar*d*in tamootu inna All*a*ha AAaleemun khabeer**un**

## 32:1

Alifl*a*mmeem

## 32:2

Tanzeelu alkit*a*bi l*a* rayba feehi min rabbi alAA*a*lameen**a**

## 32:3

Am yaqooloona iftar*a*hu bal huwa al*h*aqqu min rabbika litun*th*ira qawman m*a* at*a*hum min na*th*eerin min qablika laAAallahum yahtadoon**a**

## 32:4

All*a*hu alla*th*ee khalaqa a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*a wam*a* baynahum*a* fee sittati ayy*a*min thumma istaw*a* AAal*a* alAAarshi m*a* lakum min doonihi min waliyyin wal*a* shafeeAAin afal*a* tata*th*akkaroon**a**

## 32:5

Yudabbiru alamra mina a**l**ssam*a*i il*a* alar*d*i thumma yaAAruju ilayhi fee yawmin k*a*na miqd*a*ruhu alfa sanatin mimm*a* taAAuddoon**a**

## 32:6

*Tha*lika AA*a*limu alghaybi wa**al**shshah*a*dati alAAazeezu a**l**rra*h*eem**u**

## 32:7

Alla*th*ee a*h*sana kulla shayin khalaqahu wabadaa khalqa alins*a*ni min *t*een**in**

## 32:8

Thumma jaAAala naslahu min sul*a*latin min m*a*in maheen**in**

## 32:9

Thumma saww*a*hu wanafakha feehi min roo*h*ihi wajaAAala lakumu a**l**ssamAAa wa**a**lab*sa*ra wa**a**lafidata qaleelan m*a* tashkuroon**a**

## 32:10

Waq*a*loo ai*tha* *d*al*a*ln*a* fee alar*d*i ainn*a* lafee khalqin jadeedin bal hum biliq*a*i rabbihim k*a*firoon**a**

## 32:11

Qul yatawaff*a*kum malaku almawti alla*th*ee wukkila bikum thumma il*a* rabbikum turjaAAoon**a**

## 32:12

Walaw tar*a* i*th*i almujrimoona n*a*kisoo ruoosihim AAinda rabbihim rabban*a* ab*s*arn*a* wasamiAAn*a* faarjiAAn*a* naAAmal *sa*li*h*an inn*a* mooqinoon**a**

## 32:13

Walaw shin*a* la*a*tayn*a* kulla nafsin hud*a*h*a* wal*a*kin *h*aqqa alqawlu minnee laamlaanna jahannama mina aljinnati wa**al**nn*a*si ajmaAAeen**a**

## 32:14

Fa*th*ooqoo bim*a* naseetum liq*a*a yawmikum h*atha* inn*a* naseen*a*kum wa*th*ooqoo AAa*tha*ba alkhuldi bim*a* kuntum taAAmaloon**a**

## 32:15

Innam*a* yuminu bi*a*y*a*tin*a* alla*th*eena i*tha* *th*ukkiroo bih*a* kharroo sujjadan wasabba*h*oo bi*h*amdi rabbihim wahum l*a* yastakbiroon**a**

## 32:16

Tataj*a*f*a* junoobuhum AAani alma*da*jiAAi yadAAoona rabbahum khawfan wa*t*amaAAan wamimm*a* razaqn*a*hum yunfiqoon**a**

## 32:17

Fal*a* taAAlamu nafsun m*a* okhfiya lahum min qurrati aAAyunin jaz*a*an bim*a* k*a*noo yaAAmaloon**a**

## 32:18

Afaman k*a*na muminan kaman k*a*na f*a*siqan l*a* yastawoon**a**

## 32:19

Amm*a* alla*th*eena *a*manoo waAAamiloo a**l***ssa*li*ha*ti falahum jann*a*tu almaw*a* nuzulan bim*a* k*a*noo yaAAmaloon**a**

## 32:20

Waamm*a* alla*th*eena fasaqoo famaw*a*humu a**l**nn*a*ru kullam*a* ar*a*doo an yakhrujoo minh*a* oAAeedoo feeh*a* waqeela lahum *th*ooqoo AAa*tha*ba a**l**nn*a*ri alla*th*ee kuntum bihi tuka*thth*iboon**a**

## 32:21

Walanu*th*eeqannahum mina alAAa*tha*bi aladn*a* doona alAAa*tha*bi alakbari laAAallahum yarjiAAoon**a**

## 32:22

Waman &#x61;**th**&#x6C;amu mimman *th*ukkira bi*a*y*a*ti rabbihi thumma aAAra*d*a AAanh*a* inn*a* mina almujrimeena muntaqimoon**a**

## 32:23

Walaqad *a*tayn*a* moos*a* alkit*a*ba fal*a* takun fee miryatin min liq*a*ihi wajaAAaln*a*hu hudan libanee isr*a*eel**a**

## 32:24

WajaAAaln*a* minhum aimmatan yahdoona biamrin*a* lamm*a* *s*abaroo wak*a*noo bi*a*y*a*tin*a* yooqinoon**a**

## 32:25

Inna rabbaka huwa yaf*s*ilu baynahum yawma alqiy*a*mati feem*a* k*a*noo feehi yakhtalifoon**a**

## 32:26

Awalam yahdi lahum kam ahlakn*a* min qablihim mina alqurooni yamshoona fee mas*a*kinihim inna fee *tha*lika la*a*y*a*tin afal*a* yasmaAAoon**a**

## 32:27

Awalam yaraw ann*a* nasooqu alm*a*a il*a* alar*d*i aljuruzi fanukhriju bihi zarAAan takulu minhu anAA*a*muhum waanfusuhum afal*a* yub*s*iroon**a**

## 32:28

Wayaqooloona mat*a* h*atha* alfat*h*u in kuntum *sa*diqeen**a**

## 32:29

Qul yawma alfat*h*i l*a* yanfaAAu alla*th*eena kafaroo eem*a*nuhum wal*a* hum yu&#x6E;**th**&#x61;roon**a**

## 32:30

FaaAAri*d* AAanhum wa**i**nt&#x61;**th**&#x69;r innahum munt&#x61;**th**&#x69;roon**a**

## 33:1

Y*a* ayyuh*a* a**l**nnabiyyu ittaqi All*a*ha wal*a* tu*t*iAAi alk*a*fireena wa**a**lmun*a*fiqeena inna All*a*ha k*a*na AAaleeman *h*akeem*a***n**

## 33:2

Wa**i**ttabiAA m*a* yoo*ha* ilayka min rabbika inna All*a*ha k*a*na bim*a* taAAmaloona khabeer*a***n**

## 33:3

Watawakkal AAal*a* All*a*hi wakaf*a* bi**A**ll*a*hi wakeel*a***n**

## 33:4

M*a* jaAAala All*a*hu lirajulin min qalbayni fee jawfihi wam*a* jaAAala azw*a*jakumu all*a*ee t&#x75;**th***a*hiroona minhunna ommah*a*tikum wam*a* jaAAala adAAiy*a*akum abn*a*akum *tha*likum qawlukum biafw*a*hikum wa**A**ll*a*hu yaqoolu al*h*aqqa wahuwa yahdee a**l**ssabeel**a**

## 33:5

OdAAoohum li*a*b*a*ihim huwa aqsa*t*u AAinda All*a*hi fain lam taAAlamoo *a*b*a*ahum faikhw*a*nukum fee a**l**ddeeni wamaw*a*leekum walaysa AAalaykum jun*ah*un feem*a* akh*t*atum bihi wal*a*kin m*a* taAAammadat quloobukum wak*a*na All*a*hu ghafooran ra*h*eem*a***n**

## 33:6

A**l**nnabiyyu awl*a* bi**a**lmumineena min anfusihim waazw*a*juhu ommah*a*tuhum waoloo alar*ha*mi baAA*d*uhum awl*a* bibaAA*d*in fee kit*a*bi All*a*hi mina almumineena wa**a**lmuh*a*jireena ill*a* an tafAAaloo il*a* awliy*a*ikum maAAroofan k*a*na *tha*lika fee alkit*a*bi mas*t*oor*a***n**

## 33:7

Wai*th* akha*th*n*a* mina a**l**nnabiyyeena meeth*a*qahum waminka wamin noo*h*in waibr*a*heema wamoos*a* waAAees*a* ibni maryama waakha*th*n*a* minhum meeth*a*qan ghale&#x65;**th***a***n**

## 33:8

Liyasala a**l***ssa*diqeena AAan *s*idqihim waaAAadda lilk*a*fireena AAa*tha*ban aleem*a***n**

## 33:9

Y*a* ayyuh*a* alla*th*eena *a*manoo o*th*kuroo niAAmata All*a*hi AAalaykum i*th* j*a*atkum junoodun faarsaln*a* AAalayhim ree*h*an wajunoodan lam tarawh*a* wak*a*na All*a*hu bim*a* taAAmaloona ba*s*eer*a***n**

## 33:10

I*th* j*a*ookum min fawqikum wamin asfala minkum wai*th* z*a*ghati alab*sa*ru wabalaghati alquloobu al*h*an*a*jira wat&#x61;**th**&#x75;nnoona bi**A**ll*a*hi a**l****thth**&#x75;noon*a*

## 33:11

Hun*a*lika ibtuliya almuminoona wazulziloo zilz*a*lan shadeed*a***n**

## 33:12

Wai*th* yaqoolu almun*a*fiqoona wa**a**lla*th*eena fee quloobihim mara*d*un m*a* waAAadan*a* All*a*hu warasooluhu ill*a* ghuroor*a***n**

## 33:13

Wai*th* q*a*lat *ta*ifatun minhum y*a* ahla yathriba l*a* muq*a*ma lakum fa**i**rjiAAoo wayasta*th*inu fareequn minhumu a**l**nnabiyya yaqooloona inna buyootan*a* AAawratun wam*a* hiya biAAawratin in yureedoona ill*a* fir*a*r*a***n**

## 33:14

Walaw dukhilat AAalayhim min aq*ta*rih*a* thumma suiloo alfitnata la*a*tawh*a* wam*a* talabbathoo bih*a* ill*a* yaseer*a***n**

## 33:15

Walaqad k*a*noo AA*a*hadoo All*a*ha min qablu l*a* yuwalloona aladb*a*ra wak*a*na AAahdu All*a*hi masool*a***n**

## 33:16

Qul lan yanfaAAakumu alfir*a*ru in farartum mina almawti awi alqatli wai*th*an l*a* tumattaAAoona ill*a* qaleel*a***n**

## 33:17

Qul man *tha* alla*th*ee yaAA*s*imukum mina All*a*hi in ar*a*da bikum sooan aw ar*a*da bikum ra*h*matan wal*a* yajidoona lahum min dooni All*a*hi waliyyan wal*a* na*s*eer*a***n**

## 33:18

Qad yaAAlamu All*a*hu almuAAawwiqeena minkum wa**a**lq*a*ileena liikhw*a*nihim halumma ilayn*a* wal*a* yatoona albasa ill*a* qaleel*a***n**

## 33:19

Ashi*hh*atan AAalaykum fai*tha* j*a*a alkhawfu raaytahum ya&#x6E;**th**&#x75;roona ilayka tadooru aAAyunuhum ka**a**lla*th*ee yughsh*a* AAalayhi mina almawti fai*tha* *th*ahaba alkhawfu salaqookum bialsinatin *h*id*a*din ashi*hh*atan AAal*a* alkhayri ol*a*ika lam yuminoo faa*h*ba*t*a All*a*hu aAAm*a*lahum wak*a*na *tha*lika AAal*a* All*a*hi yaseer*a***n**

## 33:20

Ya*h*saboona ala*h*z*a*ba lam ya*th*haboo wain yati ala*h*z*a*bu yawaddoo law annahum b*a*doona fee alaAAr*a*bi yasaloona AAan anb*a*ikum walaw k*a*noo feekum m*a* q*a*taloo ill*a* qaleel*a***n**

## 33:21

Laqad k*a*na lakum fee rasooli All*a*hi oswatun *h*asanatun liman k*a*na yarjoo All*a*ha wa**a**lyawma al*a*khira wa*th*akara All*a*ha katheer*a***n**

## 33:22

Walamm*a* ra*a* almuminoona ala*h*z*a*ba q*a*loo h*atha* m*a* waAAadan*a* All*a*hu warasooluhu wa*s*adaqa All*a*hu warasooluhu wam*a* z*a*dahum ill*a* eem*a*nan watasleem*a***n**

## 33:23

Mina almumineena rij*a*lun *s*adaqoo m*a* AA*a*hadoo All*a*ha AAalayhi faminhum man qa*da* na*h*bahu waminhum man yant&#x61;**th**&#x69;ru wam*a* baddaloo tabdeel*a***n**

## 33:24

Liyajziya All*a*hu a**l***ssa*diqeena bi*s*idqihim wayuAAa*thth*iba almun*a*fiqeena in sh*a*a aw yatooba AAalayhim inna All*a*ha k*a*na ghafooran ra*h*eem*a***n**

## 33:25

Waradda All*a*hu alla*th*eena kafaroo bigha&#x79;**th**&#x69;him lam yan*a*loo khayran wakaf*a* All*a*hu almumineena alqit*a*la wak*a*na All*a*hu qawiyyan AAazeez*a***n**

## 33:26

Waanzala alla*th*eena **th***a*haroohum min ahli alkit*a*bi min *s*ay*as*eehim waqa*th*afa fee quloobihimu a**l**rruAAba fareeqan taqtuloona watasiroona fareeq*a***n**

## 33:27

Waawrathakum ar*d*ahum wadiy*a*rahum waamw*a*lahum waar*d*an lam ta*t*aooh*a* wak*a*na All*a*hu AAal*a* kulli shayin qadeer*a***n**

## 33:28

Y*a* ayyuh*a* a**l**nnabiyyu qul liazw*a*jika in kuntunna turidna al*h*ay*a*ta a**l**dduny*a* wazeenatah*a* fataAA*a*layna omattiAAkunna waosarri*h*kunna sar*ah*an jameel*a***n**

## 33:29

Wain kuntunna turidna All*a*ha warasoolahu wa**al**dd*a*ra al*a*khirata fainna All*a*ha aAAadda lilmu*h*sin*a*ti minkunna ajran AA&#x61;**th**&#x65;em*a***n**

## 33:30

Y*a* nis*a*a a**l**nnabiyyi man yati minkunna bif*ah*ishatin mubayyinatin yu*da*AAaf lah*a* alAAa*tha*bu *d*iAAfayni wak*a*na *tha*lika AAal*a* All*a*hi yaseer*a***n**

## 33:31

Waman yaqnut minkunna lill*a*hi warasoolihi wataAAmal *sa*li*h*an nutih*a* ajrah*a* marratayni waaAAtadn*a* lah*a* rizqan kareem*a***n**

## 33:32

Y*a* nis*a*a a**l**nnabiyyi lastunna kaa*h*adin mina a**l**nnis*a*i ini ittaqaytunna fal*a* takh*d*aAAna bi**a**lqawli faya*t*maAAa alla*th*ee fee qalbihi mara*d*un waqulna qawlan maAAroof*a***n**

## 33:33

Waqarna fee buyootikunna wal*a* tabarrajna tabarruja alj*a*hiliyyati alool*a* waaqimna a**l***ss*al*a*ta wa*a*teena a**l**zzak*a*ta waa*t*iAAna All*a*ha warasoolahu innam*a* yureedu All*a*hu liyu*th*hiba AAankumu a**l**rrijsa ahla albayti wayu*t*ahhirakum ta*t*heer*a***n**

## 33:34

Wa**o***th*kurna m*a* yutl*a* fee buyootikunna min *a*y*a*ti All*a*hi wa**a**l*h*ikmati inna All*a*ha k*a*na la*t*eefan khabeer*a***n**

## 33:35

Inna almuslimeena wa**a**lmuslim*a*ti wa**a**lmumineena wa**a**lmumin*a*ti wa**a**lq*a*niteena wa**a**lq*a*nit*a*ti wa**al***ssa*diqeena wa**al***ssa*diq*a*ti wa**al***ssa*bireena wa**al***ssa*bir*a*ti wa**a**lkh*a*shiAAeena wa**a**lkh*a*shiAA*a*ti wa**a**lmuta*s*addiqeena wa**a**lmuta*s*addiq*a*ti wa**al***ssa*imeena wa**al***ssa*im*a*ti wa**a**l*ha*f&#x69;**th**&#x65;ena furoojahum wa**a**l*ha*f&#x69;**th***a*ti wa**al***ththa*kireena All*a*ha katheeran wa**al***ththa*kir*a*ti aAAadda All*a*hu lahum maghfiratan waajran AA&#x61;**th**&#x65;em*a***n**

## 33:36

Wam*a* k*a*na limuminin wal*a* muminatin i*tha* qa*da* All*a*hu warasooluhu amran an yakoona lahumu alkhiyaratu min amrihim waman yaAA*s*i All*a*ha warasoolahu faqad *d*alla *d*al*a*lan mubeen*a***n**

## 33:37

Wai*th* taqoolu lilla*th*ee anAAama All*a*hu AAalayhi waanAAamta AAalayhi amsik AAalayka zawjaka wa**i**ttaqi All*a*ha watukhfee fee nafsika m*a* All*a*hu mubdeehi watakhsh*a* a**l**nn*a*sa wa**A**ll*a*hu a*h*aqqu an takhsh*a*hu falamm*a* qa*da* zaydun minh*a* wa*t*aran zawwajn*a*kah*a* likay l*a* yakoona AAal*a* almumineena *h*arajun fee azw*a*ji adAAiy*a*ihim i*tha* qa*d*aw minhunna wa*t*aran wak*a*na amru All*a*hi mafAAool*a***n**

## 33:38

M*a* k*a*na AAal*a* a**l**nnabiyyi min *h*arajin feem*a* fara*d*a All*a*hu lahu sunnata All*a*hi fee alla*th*eena khalaw min qablu wak*a*na amru All*a*hi qadaran maqdoor*a***n**

## 33:39

Alla*th*eena yuballighoona ris*a*l*a*ti All*a*hi wayakhshawnahu wal*a* yakhshawna a*h*adan ill*a* All*a*ha wakaf*a* bi**A**ll*a*hi *h*aseeb*a***n**

## 33:40

M*a* k*a*na mu*h*ammadun ab*a* a*h*adin min rij*a*likum wal*a*kin rasoola All*a*hi wakh*a*tama a**l**nnabiyyeena wak*a*na All*a*hu bikulli shayin AAaleem*a***n**

## 33:41

Y*a* ayyuh*a* alla*th*eena *a*manoo o*th*kuroo All*a*ha *th*ikran katheer*a***n**

## 33:42

Wasabbi*h*oohu bukratan waa*s*eel*a***n**

## 33:43

Huwa alla*th*ee yu*s*allee AAalaykum wamal*a*ikatuhu liyukhrijakum mina a**l****thth**&#x75;lum*a*ti il*a* a**l**nnoori wak*a*na bi**a**lmumineena ra*h*eem*a***n**

## 33:44

Ta*h*iyyatuhum yawma yalqawnahu sal*a*mun waaAAadda lahum ajran kareem*a***n**

## 33:45

Y*a* ayyuh*a* a**l**nnabiyyu inn*a* arsaln*a*ka sh*a*hidan wamubashshiran wana*th*eer*a***n**

## 33:46

Wad*a*AAiyan il*a* All*a*hi bii*th*nihi wasir*a*jan muneer*a***n**

## 33:47

Wabashshiri almumineena bianna lahum mina All*a*hi fa*d*lan kabeer*a***n**

## 33:48

Wal*a* tu*t*iAAi alk*a*fireena wa**a**lmun*a*fiqeena wadaAA a*tha*hum watawakkal AAal*a* All*a*hi wakaf*a* bi**A**ll*a*hi wakeel*a***n**

## 33:49

Y*a* ayyuh*a* alla*th*eena *a*manoo i*tha* naka*h*tumu almumin*a*ti thumma *t*allaqtumoohunna min qabli an tamassoohunna fam*a* lakum AAalayhinna min AAiddatin taAAtaddoonah*a* famattiAAoohunna wasarri*h*oohunna sar*ah*an jameel*a***n**

## 33:50

Y*a* ayyuh*a* a**l**nnabiyyu inn*a* a*h*laln*a* laka azw*a*jaka all*a*tee *a*tayta ojoorahunna wam*a* malakat yameenuka mimm*a* af*a*a All*a*hu AAalayka waban*a*ti AAammika waban*a*ti AAamm*a*tika waban*a*ti kh*a*lika waban*a*ti kh*a*l*a*tika all*a*tee h*a*jarna maAAaka wa**i**mraatan muminatan in wahabat nafsah*a* li**l**nnabiyyi in ar*a*da a**l**nnabiyyu an yastanki*h*ah*a* kh*a*li*s*atan laka min dooni almumineena qad AAalimn*a* m*a* fara*d*n*a* AAalayhim fee azw*a*jihim wam*a* malakat aym*a*nuhum likayl*a* yakoona AAalayka *h*arajun wak*a*na All*a*hu ghafooran ra*h*eem*a***n**

## 33:51

Turjee man tash*a*o minhunna watuwee ilayka man tash*a*o wamani ibtaghayta mimman AAazalta fal*a* jun*ah*a AAalayka *tha*lika adn*a* an taqarra aAAyunuhunna wal*a* ya*h*zanna wayar*d*ayna bim*a* *a*taytahunna kulluhunna wa**A**ll*a*hu yaAAlamu m*a* fee quloobikum wak*a*na All*a*hu AAaleeman *h*aleem*a***n**

## 33:52

L*a* ya*h*illu laka a**l**nnis*a*o min baAAdu wal*a* an tabaddala bihinna min azw*a*jin walaw aAAjabaka *h*usnuhunna ill*a* m*a* malakat yameenuka wak*a*na All*a*hu AAal*a* kulli shayin raqeeb*a***n**

## 33:53

Y*a* ayyuh*a* alla*th*eena *a*manoo l*a* tadkhuloo buyoota a**l**nnabiyyi ill*a* an yu*th*ana lakum il*a* *t*aAA*a*min ghayra n*a***th**&#x69;reena in*a*hu wal*a*kin i*tha* duAAeetum fa**o**dkhuloo fai*tha* *t*aAAimtum fa**i**ntashiroo wal*a* mustaniseena li*h*adeethin inna *tha*likum k*a*na yu*th*ee a**l**nnabiyya fayasta*h*yee minkum wa**A**ll*a*hu l*a* yasta*h*yee mina al*h*aqqi wai*tha* saaltumoohunna mat*a*AAan fa**i**saloohunna min war*a*i *h*ij*a*bin *tha*likum a*t*haru liquloobikum waquloobihinna wam*a* k*a*na lakum an tu*th*oo rasoola All*a*hi wal*a* an tanki*h*oo azw*a*jahu min baAAdihi abadan inna *tha*likum k*a*na AAinda All*a*hi AA&#x61;**th**&#x65;em*a***n**

## 33:54

In tubdoo shayan aw tukhfoohu fainna All*a*ha k*a*na bikulli shayin AAaleem*a***n**

## 33:55

L*a* jun*ah*a AAalayhinna fee *a*b*a*ihinna wal*a* abn*a*ihinna wal*a* ikhw*a*nihinna wal*a* abn*a*i ikhw*a*nihinna wal*a* abn*a*i akhaw*a*tihinna wal*a* nis*a*ihinna wal*a* m*a* malakat aym*a*nuhunna wa**i**ttaqeena All*a*ha inna All*a*ha k*a*na AAal*a* kulli shayin shaheed*a***n**

## 33:56

Inna All*a*ha wamal*a*ikatahu yu*s*alloona AAal*a* a**l**nnabiyyi y*a* ayyuh*a* alla*th*eena *a*manoo *s*alloo AAalayhi wasallimoo tasleem*a***n**

## 33:57

Inna alla*th*eena yu*th*oona All*a*ha warasoolahu laAAanahumu All*a*hu fee a**l**dduny*a* wa**a**l*a*khirati waaAAadda lahum AAa*tha*ban muheen*a***n**

## 33:58

Wa**a**lla*th*eena yu*th*oona almumineena wa**a**lmumin*a*ti bighayri m*a* iktasaboo faqadi i*h*tamaloo buht*a*nan waithman mubeen*a***n**

## 33:59

Y*a* ayyuh*a* a**l**nnabiyyu qul liazw*a*jika waban*a*tika wanis*a*i almumineena yudneena AAalayhinna min jal*a*beebihinna *tha*lika adn*a* an yuAArafna fal*a* yu*th*ayna wak*a*na All*a*hu ghafooran ra*h*eem*a***n**

## 33:60

Lain lam yantahi almun*a*fiqoona wa**a**lla*th*eena fee quloobihim mara*d*un wa**a**lmurjifoona fee almadeenati lanughriyannaka bihim thumma l*a* yuj*a*wiroonaka feeh*a* ill*a* qaleel*a***n**

## 33:61

MalAAooneena aynam*a* thuqifoo okhi*th*oo waquttiloo taqteel*a***n**

## 33:62

Sunnata All*a*hi fee alla*th*eena khalaw min qablu walan tajida lisunnati All*a*hi tabdeel*a***n**

## 33:63

Yasaluka a**l**nn*a*su AAani a**l**ss*a*AAati qul innam*a* AAilmuh*a* AAinda All*a*hi wam*a* yudreeka laAAalla a**l**ss*a*AAata takoonu qareeb*a***n**

## 33:64

Inna All*a*ha laAAana alk*a*fireena waaAAadda lahum saAAeer*a***n**

## 33:65

Kh*a*lideena feeh*a* abadan l*a* yajidoona waliyyan wal*a* na*s*eer*a***n**

## 33:66

Yawma tuqallabu wujoohuhum fee a**l**nn*a*ri yaqooloona y*a* laytan*a* a*t*aAAn*a* All*a*ha waa*t*aAAn*a* a**l**rrasool*a*

## 33:67

Waq*a*loo rabban*a* inn*a* a*t*aAAn*a* s*a*datan*a* wakubar*a*an*a* faa*d*alloon*a* a**l**ssabeel*a*

## 33:68

Rabban*a* *a*tihim *d*iAAfayni mina alAAa*tha*bi wa**i**lAAanhum laAAnan kabeer*a***n**

## 33:69

Y*a* ayyuh*a* alla*th*eena *a*manoo l*a* takoonoo ka**a**lla*th*eena *ath*aw moos*a* fabarraahu All*a*hu mimm*a* q*a*loo wak*a*na AAinda All*a*hi wajeeh*a***n**

## 33:70

Y*a* ayyuh*a* alla*th*eena *a*manoo ittaqoo All*a*ha waqooloo qawlan sadeed*a***n**

## 33:71

Yu*s*li*h* lakum aAAm*a*lakum wayaghfir lakum *th*unoobakum waman yu*t*iAAi All*a*ha warasoolahu faqad f*a*za fawzan AA&#x61;**th**&#x65;em*a***n**

## 33:72

Inn*a* AAara*d*n*a* alam*a*nata AAal*a* a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i wa**a**ljib*a*li faabayna an ya*h*milnah*a* waashfaqna minh*a* wa*h*amalah*a* alins*a*nu innahu k*a*na **th**&#x61;looman jahool*a***n**

## 33:73

LiyuAAa*thth*iba All*a*hu almun*a*fiqeena wa**a**lmun*a*fiq*a*ti wa**a**lmushrikeena wa**a**lmushrik*a*ti wayatooba All*a*hu AAal*a* almumineena wa**a**lmumin*a*ti wak*a*na All*a*hu ghafooran ra*h*eem*a***n**

## 34:1

Al*h*amdu lill*a*hi alla*th*ee lahu m*a* fee a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wam*a* fee alar*d*i walahu al*h*amdu fee al*a*khirati wahuwa al*h*akeemu alkhabeer**u**

## 34:2

YaAAlamu m*a* yaliju fee alar*d*i wam*a* yakhruju minh*a* wam*a* yanzilu mina a**l**ssam*a*i wam*a* yaAAruju feeh*a* wahuwa a**l**rra*h*eemu alghafoor**u**

## 34:3

Waq*a*la alla*th*eena kafaroo l*a* tateen*a* a**l**ss*a*AAatu qul bal*a* warabbee latatiyannakum AA*a*limi alghaybi l*a* yaAAzubu AAanhu mithq*a*lu *th*arratin fee a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wal*a* fee alar*d*i wal*a* a*s*gharu min *tha*lika wal*a* akbaru ill*a* fee kit*a*bin mubeen**in**

## 34:4

Liyajziya alla*th*eena *a*manoo waAAamiloo a**l***ssa*li*ha*ti ol*a*ika lahum maghfiratun warizqun kareem**un**

## 34:5

Wa**a**lla*th*eena saAAaw fee *a*y*a*tin*a* muAA*a*jizeena ol*a*ika lahum AAa*tha*bun min rijzin aleem**in**

## 34:6

Wayar*a* alla*th*eena ootoo alAAilma alla*th*ee onzila ilayka min rabbika huwa al*h*aqqa wayahdee il*a* *s*ir*at*i alAAazeezi al*h*ameed**i**

## 34:7

Waq*a*la alla*th*eena kafaroo hal nadullukum AAal*a* rajulin yunabbiokum i*tha* muzziqtum kulla mumazzaqin innakum lafee khalqin jadeed**in**

## 34:8

Aftar*a* AAal*a* All*a*hi ka*th*iban am bihi jinnatun bali alla*th*eena l*a* yuminoona bi**a**l*a*khirati fee alAAa*tha*bi wa**al***dd*al*a*li albaAAeed**i**

## 34:9

Afalam yaraw il*a* m*a* bayna aydeehim wam*a* khalfahum mina a**l**ssam*a*i wa**a**lar*d*i in nasha nakhsif bihimu alar*d*a aw nusqi*t* AAalayhim kisafan mina a**l**ssam*a*i inna fee *tha*lika la*a*yatan likulli AAabdin muneeb**in**

## 34:10

Walaqad *a*tayn*a* d*a*wooda minn*a* fa*d*lan y*a* jib*a*lu awwibee maAAahu wa**al***tt*ayra waalann*a* lahu al*h*adeed**a**

## 34:11

Ani iAAmal s*a*bigh*a*tin waqaddir fee a**l**ssardi wa**i**AAmaloo *sa*li*h*an innee bim*a* taAAmaloona ba*s*eer**un**

## 34:12

Walisulaym*a*na a**l**rree*h*a ghuduwwuh*a* shahrun waraw*ah*uh*a* shahrun waasaln*a* lahu AAayna alqi*t*ri wamina aljinni man yaAAmalu bayna yadayhi bii*th*ni rabbihi waman yazigh minhum AAan amrin*a* nu*th*iqhu min AAa*tha*bi a**l**ssaAAeer**i**

## 34:13

YaAAmaloona lahu m*a* yash*a*o min ma*ha*reeba watam*a*theela wajif*a*nin ka**a**ljaw*a*bi waqudoorin r*a*siy*a*tin iAAmaloo *a*la d*a*wooda shukran waqaleelun min AAib*a*diya a**l**shshakoor**u**

## 34:14

Falamm*a* qa*d*ayn*a* AAalayhi almawta m*a* dallahum AAal*a* mawtihi ill*a* d*a*bbatu alar*d*i takulu minsaatahu falamm*a* kharra tabayyanati aljinnu an law k*a*noo yaAAlamoona alghayba m*a* labithoo fee alAAa*tha*bi almuheen**i**

## 34:15

Laqad k*a*na lisabain fee maskanihim *a*yatun jannat*a*ni AAan yameenin washim*a*lin kuloo min rizqi rabbikum wa**o**shkuroo lahu baldatun *t*ayyibatun warabbun ghafoor**un**

## 34:16

FaaAAra*d*oo faarsaln*a* AAalayhim sayla alAAarimi wabaddaln*a*hum bijannatayhim jannatayni *th*aw*a*tay okulin kham*t*in waathlin washayin min sidrin qaleel**in**

## 34:17

*Tha*lika jazayn*a*hum bim*a* kafaroo wahal nuj*a*zee ill*a* alkafoor**a**

## 34:18

WajaAAaln*a* baynahum wabayna alqur*a* allatee b*a*rakn*a* feeh*a* quran **th***a*hiratan waqaddarn*a* feeh*a* a**l**ssayra seeroo feeh*a* lay*a*liya waayy*a*man *a*mineen**a**

## 34:19

Faq*a*loo rabban*a* b*a*AAid bayna asf*a*rin*a* w&#x61;**th**&#x61;lamoo anfusahum fajaAAaln*a*hum a*ha*deetha wamazzaqn*a*hum kulla mumazzaqin inna fee *tha*lika la*a*y*a*tin likulli *s*abb*a*rin shakoor**in**

## 34:20

Walaqad *s*addaqa AAalayhim ibleesu **th**&#x61;nnahu fa**i**ttabaAAoohu ill*a* fareeqan mina almumineen**a**

## 34:21

Wam*a* k*a*na lahu AAalayhim min sul*ta*nin ill*a* linaAAlama man yuminu bi**a**l*a*khirati mimman huwa minh*a* fee shakkin warabbuka AAal*a* kulli shayin *h*afe&#x65;**th****un**

## 34:22

Quli odAAoo alla*th*eena zaAAamtum min dooni All*a*hi l*a* yamlikoona mithq*a*la *th*arratin fee a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wal*a* fee alar*d*i wam*a* lahum feehim*a* min shirkin wam*a* lahu minhum min **th**&#x61;heer**in**

## 34:23

Wal*a* tanfaAAu a**l**shshaf*a*AAatu AAindahu ill*a* liman a*th*ina lahu *h*att*a* i*tha* fuzziAAa AAan quloobihim q*a*loo m*atha* q*a*la rabbukum q*a*loo al*h*aqqa wahuwa alAAaliyyu alkabeer**u**

## 34:24

Qul man yarzuqukum mina a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i quli All*a*hu wainn*a* aw iyy*a*kum laAAal*a* hudan aw fee *d*al*a*lin mubeen**in**

## 34:25

Qul l*a* tusaloona AAamm*a* ajramn*a* wal*a* nusalu AAamm*a* taAAmaloon**a**

## 34:26

Qul yajmaAAu baynan*a* rabbun*a* thumma yafta*h*u baynan*a* bi**a**l*h*aqqi wahuwa alfatt*ah*u alAAaleem**u**

## 34:27

Qul arooniya alla*th*eena al*h*aqtum bihi shurak*a*a kall*a* bal huwa All*a*hu alAAazeezu al*h*akeem**u**

## 34:28

Wam*a* arsaln*a*ka ill*a* k*a*ffatan li**l**nn*a*si basheeran wana*th*eeran wal*a*kinna akthara a**l**nn*a*si l*a* yaAAlamoon**a**

## 34:29

Wayaqooloona mat*a* h*atha* alwaAAdu in kuntum *sa*diqeen**a**

## 34:30

Qul lakum meeAA*a*du yawmin l*a* tastakhiroona AAanhu s*a*AAatan wal*a* tastaqdimoon**a**

## 34:31

Waq*a*la alla*th*eena kafaroo lan numina bih*atha* alqur*a*ni wal*a* bi**a**lla*th*ee bayna yadayhi walaw tar*a* i*th*i a**l****thth***a*limoona mawqoofoona AAinda rabbihim yarjiAAu baAA*d*uhum il*a* baAA*d*in alqawla yaqoolu alla*th*eena istu*d*AAifoo lilla*th*eena istakbaroo lawl*a* antum lakunn*a* mumineen**a**

## 34:32

Q*a*la alla*th*eena istakbaroo lilla*th*eena istu*d*AAifoo ana*h*nu *s*adadn*a*kum AAani alhud*a* baAAda i*th* j*a*akum bal kuntum mujrimeen**a**

## 34:33

Waq*a*la alla*th*eena istu*d*AAifoo lilla*th*eena istakbaroo bal makru allayli wa**al**nnah*a*ri i*th* tamuroonan*a* an nakfura bi**A**ll*a*hi wanajAAala lahu and*a*dan waasarroo a**l**nnad*a*mata lamm*a* raawoo alAAa*tha*ba wajaAAaln*a* alaghl*a*la fee aAAn*a*qi alla*th*eena kafaroo hal yujzawna ill*a* m*a* k*a*noo yaAAmaloon**a**

## 34:34

Wam*a* arsaln*a* fee qaryatin min na*th*eerin ill*a* q*a*la mutrafooh*a* inn*a* bim*a* orsiltum bihi k*a*firoon**a**

## 34:35

Waq*a*loo na*h*nu aktharu amw*a*lan waawl*a*dan wam*a* na*h*nu bimuAAa*thth*abeen**a**

## 34:36

Qul inna rabbee yabsu*t*u a**l**rrizqa liman yash*a*o wayaqdiru wal*a*kinna akthara a**l**nn*a*si l*a* yaAAlamoon**a**

## 34:37

Wam*a* amw*a*lukum wal*a* awl*a*dukum bi**a**llatee tuqarribukum AAindan*a* zulf*a* ill*a* man *a*mana waAAamila *sa*li*h*an faol*a*ika lahum jaz*a*o a**l***dd*iAAfi bim*a* AAamiloo wahum fee alghuruf*a*ti *a*minoon**a**

## 34:38

Wa**a**lla*th*eena yasAAawna fee *a*y*a*tin*a* muAA*a*jizeena ol*a*ika fee alAAa*tha*bi mu*hd*aroon**a**

## 34:39

Qul inna rabbee yabsu*t*u a**l**rrizqa liman yash*a*o min AAib*a*dihi wayaqdiru lahu wam*a* anfaqtum min shayin fahuwa yukhlifuhu wahuwa khayru a**l**rr*a*ziqeen**a**

## 34:40

Wayawma ya*h*shuruhum jameeAAan thumma yaqoolu lilmal*a*ikati ah*a*ol*a*i iyy*a*kum k*a*noo yaAAbudoon**a**

## 34:41

Q*a*loo sub*ha*naka anta waliyyun*a* min doonihim bal k*a*noo yaAAbudoona aljinna aktharuhum bihim muminoon**a**

## 34:42

Fa**a**lyawma l*a* yamliku baAA*d*ukum libaAA*d*in nafAAan wal*a* *d*arran wanaqoolu lilla*th*eena **th**&#x61;lamoo *th*ooqoo AAa*tha*ba a**l**nn*a*ri allatee kuntum bih*a* tuka*thth*iboon**a**

## 34:43

Wai*tha* tutl*a* AAalayhim *a*y*a*tun*a* bayyin*a*tin q*a*loo m*a* h*atha* ill*a* rajulun yureedu an ya*s*uddakum AAamm*a* k*a*na yaAAbudu *a*b*a*okum waq*a*loo m*a* h*atha* ill*a* ifkun muftaran waq*a*la alla*th*eena kafaroo lil*h*aqqi lamm*a* j*a*ahum in h*atha* ill*a* si*h*run mubeen**un**

## 34:44

Wam*a* *a*tayn*a*hum min kutubin yadrusoonah*a* wam*a* arsaln*a* ilayhim qablaka min na*th*eer**in**

## 34:45

Waka*thth*aba alla*th*eena min qablihim wam*a* balaghoo miAAsh*a*ra m*a* *a*tayn*a*hum faka*thth*aboo rusulee fakayfa k*a*na nakeer**i**

## 34:46

Qul innam*a* aAA&#x69;**th**&#x75;kum biw*ah*idatin an taqoomoo lill*a*hi mathn*a* wafur*a*d*a* thumma tatafakkaroo m*a* bi*sah*ibikum min jinnatin in huwa ill*a* na*th*eerun lakum bayna yaday AAa*tha*bin shadeed**in**

## 34:47

Qul m*a* saaltukum min ajrin fahuwa lakum in ajriya ill*a* AAal*a* All*a*hi wahuwa AAal*a* kulli shayin shaheed**un**

## 34:48

Qul inna rabbee yaq*th*ifu bi**a**l*h*aqqi AAall*a*mu alghuyoob**i**

## 34:49

Qul j*a*a al*h*aqqu wam*a* yubdio alb*at*ilu wam*a* yuAAeed**u**

## 34:50

Qul in *d*alaltu fainnam*a* a*d*illu AAal*a* nafsee waini ihtadaytu fabim*a* yoo*h*ee ilayya rabbee innahu sameeAAun qareeb**un**

## 34:51

Walaw tar*a* i*th* faziAAoo fal*a* fawta waokhi*th*oo min mak*a*nin qareeb**in**

## 34:52

Waq*a*loo *a*mann*a* bihi waann*a* lahumu a**l**ttan*a*wushu min mak*a*nin baAAeed**in**

## 34:53

Waqad kafaroo bihi min qablu wayaq*th*ifoona bi**a**lghaybi min mak*a*nin baAAeed**in**

## 34:54

Wa*h*eela baynahum wabayna m*a* yashtahoona kam*a* fuAAila biashy*a*AAihim min qablu innahum k*a*noo fee shakkin mureeb**in**

## 35:1

Al*h*amdu lill*a*hi f*at*iri a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i j*a*AAili almal*a*ikati rusulan olee ajni*h*atin mathn*a* wathul*a*tha warub*a*AAa yazeedu fee alkhalqi m*a* yash*a*o inna All*a*ha AAal*a* kulli shayin qadeer**un**

## 35:2

M*a* yafta*h*i All*a*hu li**l**nn*a*si min ra*h*matin fal*a* mumsika lah*a* wam*a* yumsik fal*a* mursila lahu min baAAdihi wahuwa alAAazeezu al*h*akeem**u**

## 35:3

Y*a* ayyuh*a* a**l**nn*a*su o*th*kuroo niAAmata All*a*hi AAalaykum hal min kh*a*liqin ghayru All*a*hi yarzuqukum mina a**l**ssam*a*i wa**a**lar*d*i l*a* il*a*ha ill*a* huwa faann*a* tufakoon**a**

## 35:4

Wain yuka*thth*ibooka faqad kut*hth*ibat rusulun min qablika wail*a* All*a*hi turjaAAu alomoor**u**

## 35:5

Y*a* ayyuh*a* a**l**nn*a*su inna waAAda All*a*hi *h*aqqun fal*a* taghurrannakumu al*h*ay*a*tu a**l**dduny*a* wal*a* yaghurrannakum bi**A**ll*a*hi algharoor**u**

## 35:6

Inna a**l**shshay*ta*na lakum AAaduwwun fa**i**ttakhi*th*oohu AAaduwwan innam*a* yadAAoo *h*izbahu liyakoonoo min a*s**ha*bi a**l**ssaAAeer**i**

## 35:7

Alla*th*eena kafaroo lahum AAa*tha*bun shadeedun wa**a**lla*th*eena *a*manoo waAAamiloo a**l***ssa*li*ha*ti lahum maghfiratun waajrun kabeer**un**

## 35:8

Afaman zuyyina lahu sooo AAamalihi fara*a*hu *h*asanan fainna All*a*ha yu*d*illu man yash*a*o wayahdee man yash*a*o fal*a* ta*th*hab nafsuka AAalayhim *h*asar*a*tin inna All*a*ha AAaleemun bim*a* ya*s*naAAoon**a**

## 35:9

Wa**A**ll*a*hu alla*th*ee arsala a**l**rriy*ah*a fatutheeru sa*ha*ban fasuqn*a*hu il*a* baladin mayyitin faa*h*yayn*a* bihi alar*d*a baAAda mawtih*a* ka*tha*lika a**l**nnushoor**u**

## 35:10

Man k*a*na yureedu alAAizzata falill*a*hi alAAizzatu jameeAAan ilayhi ya*s*AAadu alkalimu a**l***tt*ayyibu wa**a**lAAamalu a**l***ssa*li*h*u yarfaAAuhu wa**a**lla*th*eena yamkuroona a**l**ssayyi*a*ti lahum AAa*tha*bun shadeedun wamakru ol*a*ika huwa yaboor**u**

## 35:11

Wa**A**ll*a*hu khalaqakum min tur*a*bin thumma min nu*t*fatin thumma jaAAalakum azw*a*jan wam*a* ta*h*milu min onth*a* wal*a* ta*d*aAAu ill*a* biAAilmihi wam*a* yuAAammaru min muAAammarin wal*a* yunqa*s*u min AAumurihi ill*a* fee kit*a*bin inna *tha*lika AAal*a* All*a*hi yaseer**un**

## 35:12

Wam*a* yastawee alba*h*r*a*ni h*atha* AAa*th*bun fur*a*tun s*a*ighun shar*a*buhu wah*atha* mil*h*un oj*a*jun wamin kullin takuloona la*h*man *t*ariyyan watastakhrijoona *h*ilyatan talbasoonah*a* watar*a* alfulka feehi maw*a*khira litabtaghoo min fa*d*lihi walaAAallakum tashkuroon**a**

## 35:13

Yooliju allayla fee a**l**nnah*a*ri wayooliju a**l**nnah*a*ra fee allayli wasakhkhara a**l**shshamsa wa**a**lqamara kullun yajree liajalin musamman *tha*likumu All*a*hu rabbukum lahu almulku wa**a**lla*th*eena tadAAoona min doonihi m*a* yamlikoona min qi*t*meer**in**

## 35:14

In tadAAoohum l*a* yasmaAAoo duAA*a*akum walaw samiAAoo m*a* istaj*a*boo lakum wayawma alqiy*a*mati yakfuroona bishirkikum wal*a* yunabbioka mithlu khabeer**in**

## 35:15

Y*a* ayyuh*a* a**l**nn*a*su antumu alfuqar*a*o il*a* All*a*hi wa**A**ll*a*hu huwa alghaniyyu al*h*ameed**u**

## 35:16

In yasha yu*th*hibkum wayati bikhalqin jadeed**in**

## 35:17

Wam*a* *tha*lika AAal*a* All*a*hi biAAazeez**in**

## 35:18

Wal*a* taziru w*a*ziratun wizra okhr*a* wain tadAAu muthqalatun il*a* *h*imlih*a* l*a* yu*h*mal minhu shayon walaw k*a*na *tha* qurb*a* innam*a* tun*th*iru alla*th*eena yakhshawna rabbahum bi**a**lghaybi waaq*a*moo a**l***ss*al*a*ta waman tazakk*a* fainnam*a* yatazakk*a* linafsihi wail*a* All*a*hi alma*s*eer**u**

## 35:19

Wam*a* yastawee alaAAm*a* wa**a**lba*s*eer**u**

## 35:20

Wal*a* a**l****thth**&#x75;lum*a*tu wal*a* a**l**nnoor**u**

## 35:21

Wal*a* a**l****thth**&#x69;llu wal*a* al*h*aroor**u**

## 35:22

Wam*a* yastawee ala*h*y*a*o wal*a* alamw*a*tu inna All*a*ha yusmiAAu man yash*a*o wam*a* anta bimusmiAAin man fee alquboor**i**

## 35:23

In anta ill*a* na*th*eer**un**

## 35:24

Inn*a* arsaln*a*ka bi**a**l*h*aqqi basheeran wana*th*eeran wain min ommatin ill*a* khal*a* feeh*a* na*th*eer**un**

## 35:25

Wain yuka*thth*ibooka faqad ka*thth*aba alla*th*eena min qablihim j*a*athum rusuluhum bi**a**lbayyin*a*ti wabi**al**zzuburi wabi**a**lkit*a*bi almuneer**i**

## 35:26

Thumma akha*th*tu alla*th*eena kafaroo fakayfa k*a*na nakeer**i**

## 35:27

Alam tara anna All*a*ha anzala mina a**l**ssam*a*i m*a*an faakhrajn*a* bihi thamar*a*tin mukhtalifan alw*a*nuh*a* wamina aljib*a*li judadun bee*d*un wa*h*umrun mukhtalifun alw*a*nuh*a* waghar*a*beebu sood**un**

## 35:28
