Wamina a**l**nn*a*si wa**al**ddaw*a*bbi wa**a**lanAA*a*mi mukhtalifun alw*a*nuhu ka*tha*lika innam*a* yakhsh*a* All*a*ha min AAib*a*dihi alAAulam*a*o inna All*a*ha AAazeezun ghafoor**un**

## 35:29

Inna alla*th*eena yatloona kit*a*ba All*a*hi waaq*a*moo a**l***ss*al*a*ta waanfaqoo mimm*a* razaqn*a*hum sirran waAAal*a*niyatan yarjoona tij*a*ratan lan taboor**a**

## 35:30

Liyuwaffiyahum ojoorahum wayazeedahum min fa*d*lihi innahu ghafoorun shakoor**un**

## 35:31

Wa**a**lla*th*ee aw*h*ayn*a* ilayka mina alkit*a*bi huwa al*h*aqqu mu*s*addiqan lim*a* bayna yadayhi inna All*a*ha biAAib*a*dihi lakhabeerun ba*s*eer**un**

## 35:32

Thumma awrathn*a* alkit*a*ba alla*th*eena i*st*afayn*a* min AAib*a*din*a* faminhum **th***a*limun linafsihi waminhum muqta*s*idun waminhum s*a*biqun bi**a**lkhayr*a*ti bii*th*ni All*a*hi *tha*lika huwa alfa*d*lu alkabeer**u**

## 35:33

Jann*a*tu AAadnin yadkhuloonah*a* yu*h*allawna feeh*a* min as*a*wira min *th*ahabin waluluan walib*a*suhum feeh*a* *h*areer**un**

## 35:34

Waq*a*loo al*h*amdu lill*a*hi alla*th*ee a*th*haba AAann*a* al*h*azana inna rabban*a* laghafoorun shakoor**un**

## 35:35

Alla*th*ee a*h*allan*a* d*a*ra almuq*a*mati min fa*d*lihi l*a* yamassun*a* feeh*a* na*s*abun wal*a* yamassun*a* feeh*a* lughoob**un**

## 35:36

Wa**a**lla*th*eena kafaroo lahum n*a*ru jahannama l*a* yuq*da* AAalayhim fayamootoo wal*a* yukhaffafu AAanhum min AAa*tha*bih*a* ka*tha*lika najzee kulla kafoor**in**

## 35:37

Wahum ya*st*arikhoona feeh*a* rabban*a* akhrijn*a* naAAmal *sa*li*h*an ghayra alla*th*ee kunn*a* naAAmalu awalam nuAAammirkum m*a* yata*th*akkaru feehi man ta*th*akkara waj*a*akumu a**l**nna*th*eeru fa*th*ooqoo fam*a* li**l****thth***a*limeena min na*s*eer**in**

## 35:38

Inna All*a*ha AA*a*limu ghaybi a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i innahu AAaleemun bi*tha*ti a**l***ss*udoor**i**

## 35:39

Huwa alla*th*ee jaAAalakum khal*a*ifa fee alar*d*i faman kafara faAAalayhi kufruhu wal*a* yazeedu alk*a*fireena kufruhum AAinda rabbihim ill*a* maqtan wal*a* yazeedu alk*a*fireena kufruhum ill*a* khas*a*r*a***n**

## 35:40

Qul araaytum shurak*a*akumu alla*th*eena tadAAoona min dooni All*a*hi aroonee m*atha* khalaqoo mina alar*d*i am lahum shirkun fee a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti am *a*tayn*a*hum kit*a*ban fahum AAal*a* bayyinatin minhu bal in yaAAidu a**l****thth***a*limoona baAA*d*uhum baAA*d*an ill*a* ghuroor*a***n**

## 35:41

Inna All*a*ha yumsiku a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*a an tazool*a* walain z*a*lat*a* in amsakahum*a* min a*h*adin min baAAdihi innahu k*a*na *h*aleeman ghafoor*a***n**

## 35:42

Waaqsamoo bi**A**ll*a*hi jahda aym*a*nihim lain j*a*ahum na*th*eerun layakoonunna ahd*a* min i*h*d*a* alomami falamm*a* j*a*ahum na*th*eerun m*a* z*a*dahum ill*a* nufoor*a***n**

## 35:43

Istikb*a*ran fee alar*d*i wamakra a**l**ssayyii wal*a* ya*h*eequ almakru a**l**ssayyio ill*a* biahlihi fahal ya&#x6E;**th**&#x75;roona ill*a* sunnata alawwaleena falan tajida lisunnati All*a*hi tabdeelan walan tajida lisunnati All*a*hi ta*h*weel*a***n**

## 35:44

Awalam yaseeroo fee alar*d*i faya&#x6E;**th**&#x75;roo kayfa k*a*na AA*a*qibatu alla*th*eena min qablihim wak*a*noo ashadda minhum quwwatan wam*a* k*a*na All*a*hu liyuAAjizahu min shayin fee a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wal*a* fee alar*d*i innahu k*a*na AAaleeman qadeer*a***n**

## 35:45

Walaw yu*a*khi*th*u All*a*hu a**l**nn*a*sa bim*a* kasaboo m*a* taraka AAal*a* **th**&#x61;hrih*a* min d*a*bbatin wal*a*kin yuakhkhiruhum il*a* ajalin musamman fai*tha* j*a*a ajaluhum fainna All*a*ha k*a*na biAAib*a*dihi ba*s*eer*a***n**

## 36:1

Y*a*seen

## 36:2

Wa**a**lqur*a*ni al*h*akeem**i**

## 36:3

Innaka lamina almursaleen**a**

## 36:4

AAal*a* *s*ir*at*in mustaqeem**in**

## 36:5

Tanzeela alAAazeezi a**l**rra*h*eem**i**

## 36:6

Litun*th*ira qawman m*a* on*th*ira *a*b*a*ohum fahum gh*a*filoon**a**

## 36:7

Laqad *h*aqqa alqawlu AAal*a* aktharihim fahum l*a* yuminoon**a**

## 36:8

Inn*a* jaAAaln*a* fee aAAn*a*qihim aghl*a*lan fahiya il*a* ala*th*q*a*ni fahum muqma*h*oon**a**

## 36:9

WajaAAaln*a* min bayni aydeehim saddan wamin khalfihim saddan faaghshayn*a*hum fahum l*a* yub*s*iroon**a**

## 36:10

Wasaw*a*on AAalayhim aan*th*artahum am lam tun*th*irhum l*a* yuminoon**a**

## 36:11

Innam*a* tun*th*iru mani ittabaAAa a**l***thth*ikra wakhashiya a**l**rra*h*m*a*na bi**a**lghaybi fabashshirhu bimaghfiratin waajrin kareem**in**

## 36:12

Inn*a* na*h*nu nu*h*yee almawt*a* wanaktubu m*a* qaddamoo wa*a*th*a*rahum wakulla shayin a*hs*ayn*a*hu fee im*a*min mubeen**in**

## 36:13

Wa**i***d*rib lahum mathalan a*s**ha*ba alqaryati i*th* j*a*ah*a* almursaloon**a**

## 36:14

I*th* arsaln*a* ilayhimu ithnayni faka*thth*aboohum*a* faAAazzazn*a* bith*a*lithin faq*a*loo inn*a* ilaykum mursaloon**a**

## 36:15

Q*a*loo m*a* antum ill*a* basharun mithlun*a* wam*a* anzala a**l**rra*h*m*a*nu min shayin in antum ill*a* tak*th*iboon**a**

## 36:16

Q*a*loo rabbun*a* yaAAlamu inn*a* ilaykum lamursaloon**a**

## 36:17

Wam*a* AAalayn*a* ill*a* albal*a*ghu almubeen**u**

## 36:18

Q*a*loo inn*a* ta*t*ayyarn*a* bikum lain lam tantahoo lanarjumannakum walayamassannakum minn*a* AAa*tha*bun aleem**un**

## 36:19

Q*a*loo *ta*irukum maAAakum ain *th*ukkirtum bal antum qawmun musrifoon**a**

## 36:20

Waj*a*a min aq*sa* almadeenati rajulun yasAA*a* q*a*la y*a* qawmi ittabiAAoo almursaleen**a**

## 36:21

IttabiAAoo man l*a* yasalukum ajran wahum muhtadoon**a**

## 36:22

Wam*a* liya l*a* aAAbudu alla*th*ee fa*t*aranee wailayhi turjaAAoon**a**

## 36:23

Aattakhi*th*u min doonihi *a*lihatan in yuridni a**l**rra*h*m*a*nu bi*d*urrin l*a&#x20;*&#x74;ughni AAannee shaf*a*AAatuhum shayan wal*a* yunqi*th*oon**i**

## 36:24

Innee i*th*an lafee *d*al*a*lin mubeen**in**

## 36:25

Innee *a*mantu birabbikum fa**i**smaAAoon**i**

## 36:26

Qeela odkhuli aljannata q*a*la y*a* layta qawmee yaAAlamoon**a**

## 36:27

Bim*a* ghafara lee rabbee wajaAAalanee mina almukrameen**a**

## 36:28

Wam*a* anzaln*a* AAal*a* qawmihi min baAAdihi min jundin mina a**l**ssam*a*i wam*a* kunn*a* munzileen**a**

## 36:29

In k*a*nat ill*a* *s*ay*h*atan w*ah*idatan fai*tha* hum kh*a*midoon**a**

## 36:30

Y*a* *h*asratan AAal*a* alAAib*a*di m*a* yateehim min rasoolin ill*a* k*a*noo bihi yastahzioon**a**

## 36:31

Alam yaraw kam ahlakn*a* qablahum mina alqurooni annahum ilayhim l*a* yarjiAAoon**a**

## 36:32

Wain kullun lamm*a* jameeAAun ladayn*a* mu*hd*aroon**a**

## 36:33

Wa*a*yatun lahumu alar*d*u almaytatu a*h*yayn*a*h*a* waakhrajn*a* minh*a* *h*abban faminhu yakuloon**a**

## 36:34

WajaAAaln*a* feeh*a* jann*a*tin min nakheelin waaAAn*a*bin wafajjarn*a* feeh*a* mina alAAuyoon**i**

## 36:35

Liyakuloo min thamarihi wam*a* AAamilathu aydeehim afal*a* yashkuroon**a**

## 36:36

Sub*ha*na alla*th*ee khalaqa alazw*a*ja kullah*a* mimm*a* tunbitu alar*d*u wamin anfusihim wamimm*a* l*a* yaAAlamoon**a**

## 36:37

Wa*a*yatun lahumu allaylu naslakhu minhu a**l**nnah*a*ra fai*tha* hum m&#x75;**th**&#x6C;imoon**a**

## 36:38

Wa**al**shshamsu tajree limustaqarrin lah*a* *tha*lika taqdeeru alAAazeezi alAAaleem**i**

## 36:39

Wa**a**lqamara qaddarn*a*hu man*a*zila *h*att*a* AA*a*da ka**a**lAAurjooni alqadeem**i**

## 36:40

L*a* a**l**shshamsu yanbaghee lah*a* an tudrika alqamara wal*a* allaylu s*a*biqu a**l**nnah*a*ri wakullun fee falakin yasba*h*oon**a**

## 36:41

Wa*a*yatun lahum ann*a* *h*amaln*a* *th*urriyyatahum fee alfulki almash*h*oon**i**

## 36:42

Wakhalaqn*a* lahum min mithlihi m*a* yarkaboon**a**

## 36:43

Wain nasha nughriqhum fal*a* *s*areekha lahum wal*a* hum yunqa*th*oon**a**

## 36:44

Ill*a* ra*h*matan minn*a* wamat*a*AAan il*a* *h*een**in**

## 36:45

Wai*tha* qeela lahumu ittaqoo m*a* bayna aydeekum wam*a* khalfakum laAAallakum tur*h*amoon**a**

## 36:46

Wam*a* tateehim min *a*yatin min *a*y*a*ti rabbihim ill*a* k*a*noo AAanh*a* muAAri*d*een**a**

## 36:47

Wai*tha* qeela lahum anfiqoo mimm*a* razaqakumu All*a*hu q*a*la alla*th*eena kafaroo lilla*th*eena *a*manoo anu*t*AAimu man law yash*a*o All*a*hu a*t*AAamahu in antum ill*a* fee *d*al*a*lin mubeen**in**

## 36:48

Wayaqooloona mat*a* h*atha* alwaAAdu in kuntum *sa*diqeen**a**

## 36:49

M*a* ya&#x6E;**th**&#x75;roona ill*a* *s*ay*h*atan w*ah*idatan takhu*th*uhum wahum yakhi*ss*imoon**a**

## 36:50

Fal*a* yasta*t*eeAAoona taw*s*iyatan wal*a* il*a* ahlihim yarjiAAoon**a**

## 36:51

Wanufikha fee a**l***ss*oori fai*tha* hum mina alajd*a*thi il*a* rabbihim yansiloon**a**

## 36:52

Q*a*loo y*a* waylan*a* man baAAathan*a* min marqadin*a* h*atha* m*a* waAAada a**l**rra*h*m*a*nu wa*s*adaqa almursaloon**a**

## 36:53

In k*a*nat ill*a* *s*ay*h*atan w*ah*idatan fai*tha* hum jameeAAun ladayn*a* mu*hd*aroon**a**

## 36:54

Fa**a**lyawma l*a* t&#x75;**th**&#x6C;amu nafsun shayan wal*a* tujzawna ill*a* m*a* kuntum taAAmaloon**a**

## 36:55

Inna a*s**ha*ba aljannati alyawma fee shughulin f*a*kihoon**a**

## 36:56

Hum waazw*a*juhum fee **th**&#x69;l*a*lin AAal*a* alar*a*iki muttakioon**a**

## 36:57

Lahum feeh*a* f*a*kihatun walahum m*a* yaddaAAoon**a**

## 36:58

Sal*a*mun qawlan min rabbin ra*h*eem**in**

## 36:59

Wa**i**mt*a*zoo alyawma ayyuh*a* almujrimoon**a**

## 36:60

Alam aAAhad ilaykum y*a* banee *a*dama an l*a* taAAbudoo a**l**shshay*ta*na innahu lakum AAaduwwun mubeen**un**

## 36:61

Waani oAAbudoonee h*atha* *s*ir*at*un mustaqeem**un**

## 36:62

Walaqad a*d*alla minkum jibillan katheeran afalam takoonoo taAAqiloon**a**

## 36:63

H*ath*ihi jahannamu allatee kuntum tooAAadoon**a**

## 36:64

I*s*lawh*a* alyawma bim*a* kuntum takfuroon**a**

## 36:65

Alyawma nakhtimu AAal*a* afw*a*hihim watukallimun*a* aydeehim watashhadu arjuluhum bim*a* k*a*noo yaksiboon**a**

## 36:66

Walaw nash*a*o la*t*amasn*a* AAal*a* aAAyunihim fa**i**stabaqoo a**l***ss*ir*at*a faann*a* yub*s*iroon**a**

## 36:67

Walaw nash*a*o lamasakhn*a*hum AAal*a* mak*a*natihim fam*a* ista*ta*AAoo mu*d*iyyan wal*a* yarjiAAoon**a**

## 36:68

Waman nuAAammirhu nunakkishu fee alkhalqi afal*a* yaAAqiloon**a**

## 36:69

Wam*a* AAallamn*a*hu a**l**shshiAAra wam*a* yanbaghee lahu in huwa ill*a* *th*ikrun waqur*a*nun mubeen**un**

## 36:70

Liyun*th*ira man k*a*na *h*ayyan waya*h*iqqa alqawlu AAal*a* alk*a*fireen**a**

## 36:71

Awalam yaraw ann*a* khalaqn*a* lahum mimm*a* AAamilat aydeen*a* anAA*a*man fahum lah*a* m*a*likoon**a**

## 36:72

Wa*th*allaln*a*h*a* lahum faminh*a* rakoobuhum waminh*a* yakuloon**a**

## 36:73

Walahum feeh*a* man*a*fiAAu wamash*a*ribu afal*a* yashkuroon**a**

## 36:74

Wa**i**ttakha*th*oo min dooni All*a*hi *a*lihatan laAAallahum yun*s*aroon**a**

## 36:75

L*a* yasta*t*eeAAoona na*s*rahum wahum lahum jundun mu*hd*aroon**a**

## 36:76

Fal*a* ya*h*zunka qawluhum inn*a* naAAlamu m*a* yusirroona wam*a* yuAAlinoon**a**

## 36:77

Awalam yar*a* alins*a*nu ann*a* khalaqn*a*hu min nu*t*fatin fai*tha* huwa kha*s*eemun mubeen**un**

## 36:78

Wa*d*araba lan*a* mathalan wanasiya khalqahu q*a*la man yu*h*yee alAA&#x69;**th***a*ma wahiya rameem**un**

## 36:79

Qul yu*h*yeeh*a* alla*th*ee anshaah*a* awwala marratin wahuwa bikulli khalqin AAaleem**un**

## 36:80

Alla*th*ee jaAAala lakum mina a**l**shshajari alakh*d*ari n*a*ran fai*tha* antum minhu tooqidoon**a**

## 36:81

Awalaysa alla*th*ee khalaqa a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*a biq*a*dirin AAal*a* an yakhluqa mithlahum bal*a* wahuwa alkhall*a*qu alAAaleem**u**

## 36:82

Innam*a* amruhu i*tha* ar*a*da shayan an yaqoola lahu kun fayakoon**u**

## 36:83

Fasub*ha*na alla*th*ee biyadihi malakootu kulli shayin wailayhi turjaAAoon**a**

## 37:1

Wa**al***ssa*ff*a*ti *s*aff*a***n**

## 37:2

Fa**al**zz*a*jir*a*ti zajr*a***n**

## 37:3

Fa**al**tt*a*liy*a*ti *th*ikr*a***n**

## 37:4

Inna il*a*hakum law*ah*id**un**

## 37:5

Rabbu a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i wam*a* baynahum*a* warabbu almash*a*riq**i**

## 37:6

Inn*a* zayyann*a* a**l**ssam*a*a a**l**dduny*a* bizeenatin alkaw*a*kib**i**

## 37:7

Wa*h*i&#x66;**th**&#x61;n min kulli shay*ta*nin m*a*rid**in**

## 37:8

L*a* yassammaAAoona il*a* almalai alaAAl*a* wayuq*th*afoona min kulli j*a*nib**in**

## 37:9

Du*h*ooran walahum AAa*tha*bun w*as*ib**un**

## 37:10

Ill*a* man kha*t*ifa alkha*t*fata faatbaAAahu shih*a*bun th*a*qib**un**

## 37:11

Fa**i**staftihim ahum ashaddu khalqan am man khalaqn*a* inn*a&#x20;*&#x6B;halaqn*a*hum min *t*eenin l*a*zib**in**

## 37:12

Bal AAajibta wayaskharoon**a**

## 37:13

Wai*tha* *th*ukkiroo l*a* ya*th*kuroon**a**

## 37:14

## 37:15

Waq*a*loo in h*atha* ill*a* si*h*run mubeen**un**

## 37:16

Ai*tha* mitn*a* wakunn*a* tur*a*ban waAA&#x69;**th***a*man ainn*a* lamabAAoothoon**a**

## 37:17

Awa*a*b*a*on*a* alawwaloon**a**

## 37:18

Qul naAAam waantum d*a*khiroon**a**

## 37:19

## 37:20

Waq*a*loo y*a* waylan*a* h*atha* yawmu a**l**ddeen**i**

## 37:21

H*atha* yawmu alfa*s*li alla*th*ee kuntum bihi tuka*thth*iboon**a**

## 37:22

O*h*shuroo alla*th*eena **th**&#x61;lamoo waazw*a*jahum wam*a* k*a*noo yaAAbudoon**a**

## 37:23

Min dooni All*a*hi fa**i**hdoohum il*a* *s*ir*at*i alja*h*eem**i**

## 37:24

Waqifoohum innahum masooloon**a**

## 37:25

M*a* lakum l*a* tan*as*aroon**a**

## 37:26

Bal humu alyawma mustaslimoon**a**

## 37:27

Waaqbala baAA*d*uhum AAal*a* baAA*d*in yatas*a*aloon**a**

## 37:28

Q*a*loo innakum kuntum tatoonan*a* AAani alyameen**i**

## 37:29

Q*a*loo bal lam takoonoo mumineen**a**

## 37:30

Wam*a* k*a*na lan*a* AAalaykum min *s*ul*ta*nin bal kuntum qawman *ta*gheen**a**

## 37:31

Fa*h*aqqa AAalayn*a* qawlu rabbin*a* inn*a* la*tha*iqoon**a**

## 37:32

Faaghwayn*a*kum inn*a* kunn*a* gh*a*ween**a**

## 37:33

Fainnahum yawmai*th*in fee alAAa*tha*bi mushtarikoon**a**

## 37:34

Inn*a* ka*tha*lika nafAAalu bi**a**lmujrimeen**a**

## 37:35

Innahum k*a*noo i*tha* qeela lahum l*a* il*a*ha ill*a* All*a*hu yastakbiroon**a**

## 37:36

Wayaqooloona ainn*a* lat*a*rikoo *a*lihatin*a* lish*a*AAirin majnoon**in**

## 37:37

## 37:38

## 37:39

## 37:40

Ill*a* AAib*a*da All*a*hi almukhla*s*een**a**

## 37:41

Ol*a*ika lahum rizqun maAAloom**un**

## 37:42

## 37:43

## 37:44

AAal*a* sururin mutaq*a*bileen**a**

## 37:45

## 37:46

Bay*da*a la*thth*atin li**l**shsh*a*ribeen**a**

## 37:47

## 37:48

WaAAindahum q*as*ir*a*tu a**l***tt*arfi AAeen**un**

## 37:49

Kaannahunna bay*d*un maknoon**un**

## 37:50

## 37:51

## 37:52

Yaqoolu ainnaka lamina almu*s*addiqeen**a**

## 37:53

## 37:54

Q*a*la hal antum mu*tt*aliAAoon**a**

## 37:55

Fa**i***tt*alaAAa fara*a*hu fee saw*a*i alja*h*eem**i**

## 37:56

Q*a*la ta**A**ll*a*hi in kidta laturdeen**i**

## 37:57

Walawl*a* niAAmatu rabbee lakuntu mina almu*hd*areen**a**

## 37:58

Afam*a* na*h*nu bimayyiteen**a**

## 37:59

Ill*a* mawtatan*a* alool*a* wam*a* na*h*nu bimuAAa*thth*abeen**a**

## 37:60

Inna h*atha* lahuwa alfawzu alAA&#x61;**th**&#x65;em**u**

## 37:61

Limithli h*atha* falyaAAmali alAA*a*miloon**a**

## 37:62

A*tha*lika khayrun nuzulan am shajaratu a**l**zzaqqoom**i**

## 37:63

Inn*a* jaAAaln*a*h*a* fitnatan li**l****thth***a*limeen**a**

## 37:64

Innah*a* shajaratun takhruju fee a*s*li alja*h*eem**i**

## 37:65

*T*alAAuh*a* kaannahu ruoosu a**l**shshay*at*een**i**

## 37:66

Fainnahum la*a*kiloona minh*a* fam*a*lioona minh*a* albu*t*oon**a**

## 37:67

## 37:68

## 37:69

Innahum alfaw *a*b*a*ahum *da*lleen**a**

## 37:70

Fahum AAal*a* *a*th*a*rihim yuhraAAoon**a**

## 37:71

## 37:72

Walaqad arsaln*a* feehim mun*th*ireen**a**

## 37:73

Fa**o**&#x6E;**th**&#x75;r kayfa k*a*na AA*a*qibatu almun*th*areen**a**

## 37:74

Ill*a* AAib*a*da All*a*hi almukhla*s*een**a**

## 37:75

Walaqad n*a*d*a*n*a* noo*h*un falaniAAma almujeeboon**a**

## 37:76

Wanajjayn*a*hu waahlahu mina alkarbi alAA&#x61;**th**&#x65;em**i**

## 37:77

WajaAAaln*a* *th*urriyyatahu humu alb*a*qeen**a**

## 37:78

Watarakn*a* AAalayhi fee al*a*khireen**a**

## 37:79

Sal*a*mun AAal*a* noo*h*in fee alAA*a*lameen**a**

## 37:80

Inn*a* ka*tha*lika najzee almu*h*sineen**a**

## 37:81

Innahu min AAib*a*din*a* almumineen**a**

## 37:82

## 37:83

Wainna min sheeAAatihi laibr*a*heem**a**

## 37:84

I*th* j*a*a rabbahu biqalbin saleem**in**

## 37:85

## 37:86

Aifkan *a*lihatan doona All*a*hi tureedoon**a**

## 37:87

Fam*a* **th**&#x61;nnukum birabbi alAA*a*lameen**a**

## 37:88

Fan&#x61;**th**&#x61;ra n&#x61;**th**&#x72;atan fee a**l**nnujoom**i**

## 37:89

Faq*a*la innee saqeem**un**

## 37:90

## 37:91

## 37:92

## 37:93

Far*a*gha AAalayhim *d*arban bi**a**lyameen**i**

## 37:94

Faaqbaloo ilayhi yaziffoon**a**

## 37:95

Q*a*la ataAAbudoona m*a* tan*h*itoon**a**

## 37:96

## 37:97

## 37:98

Faar*a*doo bihi kaydan fajaAAaln*a*humu alasfaleen**a**

## 37:99

## 37:100

Rabbi hab lee mina a**l***ssa*li*h*een**a**

## 37:101

Fabashsharn*a*hu bighul*a*min *h*aleem**in**

## 37:102

Falamm*a* balagha maAAahu a**l**ssaAAya q*a*la y*a* bunayya innee ar*a* fee alman*a*mi annee a*th*ba*h*uka fa**o**&#x6E;**th**&#x75;r m*atha* tar*a* q*a*la y*a* abati ifAAal m*a* tumaru satajidunee in sh*a*a All*a*hu mina a**l***ssa*bireen**a**

## 37:103

## 37:104

## 37:106

## 37:107

Wafadayn*a*hu bi*th*ib*h*in AA&#x61;**th**&#x65;em**in**

## 37:112

## 37:113

Wab*a*rakn*a* AAalayhi waAAal*a* is*ha*qa wamin *th*urriyyatihim*a* mu*h*sinun w&#x61;**th***a*limun linafsihi mubeen**un**

## 37:144

## 37:145

Fanaba*th*n*a*hu bi**a**lAAar*a*i wahuwa saqeem**un**

## 37:146

## 37:147

## 37:148

Fa*a*manoo famattaAAn*a*hum il*a* *h*een**in**

## 37:149

## 37:157

## 37:159

## 37:170

## 37:178

## 37:179

Waab*s*ir fasawfa yub*s*iroon**a**

## 37:180

Wa**a**l*h*amdu lill*a*hi rabbi alAA*a*lameen**a**

## 38:1

*Sa*d wa**a**lqur*a*ni *th*ee a**l***thth*ikr**i**

## 38:2

Bali alla*th*eena kafaroo fee AAizzatin washiq*a*q**in**

## 38:3

Kam ahlakn*a* min qablihim min qarnin fan*a*daw wal*a*ta *h*eena man*as***in**

## 38:4

WaAAajiboo an j*a*ahum mun*th*irun minhum waq*a*la alk*a*firoona h*atha&#x20;*&#x73;*ah*irun ka*ththa*b**un**

## 38:5

AjaAAala al*a*lihata il*a*han w*ah*idan inna h*atha* lashayon AAuj*a*b**un**

## 38:6

Wa**i**n*t*alaqa almalao minhum ani imshoo wa**i***s*biroo AAal*a* *a*lihatikum inna h*atha* lashayon yur*a*d**u**

## 38:7

M*a* samiAAn*a* bih*atha* fee almillati al*a*khirati in h*atha* ill*a* ikhtil*a*q**un**

## 38:8

Aonzila AAalayhi a**l***thth*ikru min baynin*a* bal hum fee shakkin min *th*ikree bal lamm*a* ya*th*ooqoo AAa*tha*b**i**

## 38:9

Am AAindahum khaz*a*inu ra*h*mati rabbika alAAazeezi alwahh*a*b**i**

## 38:10

Am lahum mulku a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i wam*a* baynahum*a* falyartaqoo fee alasb*a*b**i**

## 38:11

Jundun m*a* hun*a*lika mahzoomun mina ala*h*z*a*b**i**

## 38:12

Ka*thth*abat qablahum qawmu noo*h*in waAA*a*dun wafirAAawnu *th*oo alawt*a*d**i**

## 38:13

Wathamoodu waqawmu loo*t*in waa*s**ha*bu alaykati ol*a*ika ala*h*z*a*b**u**

## 38:14

In kullun ill*a* ka*thth*aba a**l**rrusula fa*h*aqqa AAiq*a*b**i**

## 38:15

Wam*a* ya&#x6E;**th**&#x75;ru h*a*ol*a*i ill*a* *s*ay*h*atan w*ah*idatan m*a* lah*a* min faw*a*q**in**

## 38:16

Waq*a*loo rabban*a* AAajjil lan*a* qi*tt*an*a* qabla yawmi al*h*is*a*b**i**

## 38:17

I*s*bir AAal*a* m*a* yaqooloona wa**o***th*kur AAabdan*a* d*a*wooda *tha* alaydi innahu aww*a*b**un**

## 38:18

Inn*a* sakhkharn*a* aljib*a*la maAAahu yusabbi*h*na bi**a**lAAashiyyi wa**a**lishr*a*q**i**

## 38:19

Wa**al***tt*ayra ma*h*shooratan kullun lahu aww*a*b**un**

## 38:20

Washadadn*a* mulkahu wa*a*tayn*a*hu al*h*ikmata wafa*s*la alkhi*ta*b**i**

## 38:21

Wahal at*a*ka nabao alkha*s*mi i*th* tasawwaroo almi*h*r*a*b**a**

## 38:22

Ith dakhaloo AAal*a* d*a*wooda fafaziAAa minhum q*a*loo l*a* takhaf kha*s*m*a*ni bagh*a* baAA*d*un*a* AAal*a* baAA*d*in fa**o***h*kum baynan*a* bi**a**l*h*aqqi wal*a* tush*t*i*t* wa**i**hdin*a* il*a* saw*a*i a**l***ss*ir*at***i**

## 38:23

Inna h*atha* akhee lahu tisAAun watisAAoona naAAjatan waliya naAAjatun w*ah*idatun faq*a*la akfilneeh*a* waAAazzanee fee alkhi*ta*b**i**

## 38:24

Q*a*la laqad **th**&#x61;lamaka bisu*a*li naAAjatika il*a* niAA*a*jihi wainna katheeran mina alkhula*ta*i layabghee baAA*d*uhum AAal*a* baAA*d*in ill*a* alla*th*eena *a*manoo waAAamiloo a**l***ssa*li*ha*ti waqaleelun m*a* hum w&#x61;**th**&#x61;nna d*a*woodu annam*a* fatann*a*hu fa**i**staghfara rabbahu wakharra r*a*kiAAan waan*a*b**a**

## 38:25

Faghafarn*a* lahu *tha*lika wainna lahu AAindan*a* lazulf*a* wa*h*usna ma*a*b**in**

## 38:26

Y*a* d*a*woodu inn*a* jaAAaln*a*ka khaleefatan fee alar*d*i fa**o***h*kum bayna a**l**nn*a*si bi**a**l*h*aqqi wal*a* tattabiAAi alhaw*a* fayu*d*illaka AAan sabeeli All*a*hi inna alla*th*eena ya*d*illoona AAan sabeeli All*a*hi lahum AAa*tha*bun shadeedun bim*a* nasoo yawma al*h*is*a*b**i**

## 38:27

Wam*a* khalaqn*a* a**l**ssam*a*a wa**a**lar*d*a wam*a* baynahum*a* b*at*ilan *tha*lika **th**&#x61;nnu alla*th*eena kafaroo fawaylun lilla*th*eena kafaroo mina a**l**nn*a*r**i**

## 38:28

Am najAAalu alla*th*eena *a*manoo waAAamiloo a**l***ssa*li*ha*ti ka**a**lmufsideena fee alar*d*i am najAAalu almuttaqeena ka**a**lfujj*a*r**i**

## 38:29

Kit*a*bun anzaln*a*hu ilayka mub*a*rakun liyaddabbaroo *a*y*a*tihi waliyata*th*akkara oloo alalb*a*b**i**

## 38:30

Wawahabn*a* lid*a*wooda sulaym*a*na niAAma alAAabdu innahu aww*a*b**un**

## 38:31

I*th* AAuri*d*a AAalayhi bi**a**lAAashiyyi a**l***ssa*fin*a*tu aljiy*a*d**u**

## 38:32

Faq*a*la innee a*h*babtu *h*ubba alkhayri AAan *th*ikri rabbee *h*att*a* taw*a*rat bi**a**l*h*ij*a*b**i**

## 38:33

Ruddooh*a* AAalayya fa*t*afiqa mas*h*an bi**al**ssooqi wa**a**laAAn*a*q**i**

## 38:34

Walaqad fatann*a* sulaym*a*na waalqayn*a* AAal*a* kursiyyihi jasadan thumma an*a*b**a**

## 38:35

Q*a*la rabbi ighfir lee wahab lee mulkan l*a* yanbaghee lia*h*adin min baAAdee innaka anta alwahh*a*b**u**

## 38:36

Fasakhkharn*a* lahu a**l**rree*h*a tajree biamrihi rukh*a*an *h*aythu a*sa*b**a**

## 38:37

Wa**al**shshay*at*eena kulla bann*a*in waghaww*as***in**

## 38:38

Wa*a*khareena muqarraneena fee ala*s*f*a*d**i**

## 38:39

H*atha* AAa*ta*on*a* fa**o**mnun aw amsik bighayri *h*is*a*b**in**

## 38:40

Wainna lahu AAindan*a* lazulf*a* wa*h*usna ma*a*b**in**

## 38:41

Wa**o***th*kur AAabdan*a* ayyooba i*th* n*a*d*a* rabbahu annee massaniya a**l**shshay*ta*nu binu*s*bin waAAa*tha*b**in**

## 38:42

Orku*d* birijlika h*atha* mughtasalun b*a*ridun washar*a*b**un**

## 38:43

Wawahabn*a* lahu ahlahu wamithlahum maAAahum ra*h*matan minn*a&#x20;*&#x77;a*th*ikr*a* liolee alalb*a*b**i**

## 38:44

Wakhu*th* biyadika *d*ighthan fa**i***d*rib bihi wal*a* ta*h*nath inn*a* wajadn*a*hu *sa*biran niAAma alAAabdu innahu aww*a*b**un**

## 38:45

Wa**o***th*kur AAib*a*dan*a* ibr*a*heema wais*ha*qa wayaAAqooba olee alaydee wa**a**lab*sa*r**i**

## 38:46

Inn*a* akhla*s*n*a*hum bikh*a*li*s*atin *th*ikr*a* a**l**dd*a*r**i**

## 38:47

Wainnahum AAindan*a* lamina almu*st*afayna alakhy*a*r**i**

## 38:48

Wa**o***th*kur ism*a*AAeela wailyasaAAa wa*tha* alkifli wakullun mina alakhy*a*r**i**

## 38:49

H*atha* *th*ikrun wainna lilmuttaqeena la*h*usna ma*a*b**in**

## 38:50

Jann*a*ti AAadnin mufatta*h*atan lahumu alabw*a*b**u**

## 38:51

Muttakieena feeh*a* yadAAoona feeh*a* bif*a*kihatin katheeratin washar*a*b**in**

## 38:52

WaAAindahum q*as*ir*a*tu a**l***tt*arfi atr*a*b**un**

## 38:53

H*atha* m*a* tooAAadoona liyawmi al*h*is*a*b**i**

## 38:54

Inna h*atha* larizqun*a* m*a* lahu min naf*a*d**in**

## 38:55

H*atha* wainna li**l***tta*gheena lasharra ma*a*b**in**

## 38:56

Jahannama ya*s*lawnah*a* fabisa almih*a*d**u**

## 38:57

H*atha* falya*th*ooqoohu *h*ameemun waghass*a*q**un**

## 38:58

Wa*a*kharu min shaklihi azw*a*j**un**

## 38:59

H*atha* fawjun muqta*h*imun maAAakum l*a* mar*h*aban bihim innahum *sa*loo a**l**nn*a*r**i**

## 38:60

Q*a*loo bal antum l*a* mar*h*aban bikum antum qaddamtumoohu lan*a* fabisa alqar*a*r**u**

## 38:61

Q*a*loo rabban*a* man qaddama lan*a* h*atha* fazidhu AAa*tha*ban *d*iAAfan fee a**l**nn*a*r**i**

## 38:62

Waq*a*loo m*a* lan*a* l*a* nar*a* rij*a*lan kunn*a* naAAudduhum mina alashr*a*r**i**

## 38:63

Attakha*th*n*a*hum sikhriyyan am z*a*ghat AAanhumu alab*sa*r**u**

## 38:64

Inna *tha*lika la*h*aqqun takh*as*umu ahli a**l**nn*a*r**i**

## 38:65

Qul innam*a* an*a* mun*th*irun wam*a* min il*a*hin ill*a* All*a*hu alw*ah*idu alqahh*a*r**u**

## 38:66

Rabbu a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i wam*a* baynahum*a* alAAazeezu alghaff*a*r**u**

## 38:67

Qul huwa nabaon AA&#x61;**th**&#x65;em**un**

## 38:68

Antum AAanhu muAAri*d*oon**a**

## 38:69

M*a* k*a*na liya min AAilmin bi**a**lmalai alaAAl*a* i*th* yakhta*s*imoon**a**

## 38:70

In yoo*ha* ilayya ill*a* annam*a* an*a* na*th*eerun mubeen**un**

## 38:71

I*th* q*a*la rabbuka lilmal*a*ikati innee kh*a*liqun basharan min *t*een**in**

## 38:72

Fai*tha* sawwaytuhu wanafakhtu feehi min roo*h*ee faqaAAoo lahu s*a*jideen**a**

## 38:73

Fasajada almal*a*ikatu kulluhum ajmaAAoon**a**

## 38:74

Ill*a* ibleesa istakbara wak*a*na mina alk*a*fireen**a**

## 38:75

Q*a*la y*a* ibleesu m*a* manaAAaka an tasjuda lim*a* khalaqtu biyadayya astakbarta am kunta mina alAA*a*leen**a**

## 38:76

Q*a*la an*a* khayrun minhu khalaqtanee min n*a*rin wakhalaqtahu min *t*een**in**

## 38:77

Q*a*la fa**o**khruj minh*a* fainnaka rajeem**un**

## 38:78

Wainna AAalayka laAAnatee il*a* yawmi a**l**ddeen**i**

## 38:79

Q*a*la rabbi faa&#x6E;**th**&#x69;rnee il*a* yawmi yubAAathoon**a**

## 38:80

Q*a*la fainnaka mina almu&#x6E;**th**&#x61;reen**a**

## 38:81

Il*a* yawmi alwaqti almaAAloom**i**

## 38:82

Q*a*la fabiAAizzatika laoghwiyannahum ajmaAAeen**a**

## 38:83

Ill*a* AAib*a*daka minhumu almukhla*s*een**a**

## 38:84

Q*a*la fa**a**l*h*aqqu wa**a**l*h*aqqa aqool**u**

## 38:85

Laamlaanna jahannama minka wamimman tabiAAaka minhum ajmaAAeen**a**

## 38:86

Qul m*a* asalukum AAalayhi min ajrin wam*a* an*a* mina almutakallifeen**a**

## 38:87

In huwa ill*a* *th*ikrun lilAA*a*lameen**a**

## 38:88

WalataAAlamunna nabaahu baAAda *h*een**in**

## 39:1

Tanzeelu alkit*a*bi mina All*a*hi alAAazeezi al*h*akeem**i**

## 39:2

Inn*a* anzaln*a* ilayka alkit*a*ba bi**a**l*h*aqqi fa**o**AAbudi All*a*ha mukhli*s*an lahu a**l**ddeen**a**

## 39:3

Al*a* lill*a*hi a**l**ddeenu alkh*a*li*s*u wa**a**lla*th*eena ittakha*th*oo min doonihi awliy*a*a m*a* naAAbuduhum ill*a* liyuqarriboon*a* il*a* All*a*hi zulf*a* inna All*a*ha ya*h*kumu baynahum fee m*a* hum feehi yakhtalifoona inna All*a*ha l*a* yahdee man huwa k*ath*ibun kaff*a*r**un**

## 39:4

Law ar*a*da All*a*hu an yattakhi*th*a waladan la**i***st*af*a* mimm*a* yakhluqu m*a* yash*a*o sub*ha*nahu huwa All*a*hu alw*ah*idu alqahh*a*r**u**

## 39:5

Khalaqa a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*a bi**a**l*h*aqqi yukawwiru allayla AAal*a* a**l**nnah*a*ri wayukawwiru a**l**nnah*a*ra AAal*a* allayli wasakhkhara a**l**shshamsa wa**a**lqamara kullun yajree liajalin musamman al*a* huwa alAAazeezu alghaff*a*r**u**

## 39:6

Khalaqakum min nafsin w*ah*idatin thumma jaAAala minh*a* zawjah*a* waanzala lakum mina alanAA*a*mi tham*a*niyata azw*a*jin yakhluqukum fee bu*t*ooni ommah*a*tikum khalqan min baAAdi khalqin fee **th**&#x75;lum*a*tin thal*a*thin *tha*likumu All*a*hu rabbukum lahu almulku l*a* il*a*ha ill*a* huwa faann*a* tu*s*rafoon**a**

## 39:7

In takfuroo fainna All*a*ha ghaniyyun AAankum wal*a* yar*da* liAAib*a*dihi alkufra wain tashkuroo yar*d*ahu lakum wal*a* taziru w*a*ziratun wizra okhr*a* thumma il*a* rabbikum marjiAAukum fayunabbiokum bim*a* kuntum taAAmaloona innahu AAaleemun bi*tha*ti a**l***ss*udoor**i**

## 39:8

Wai*tha* massa alins*a*na *d*urrun daAA*a* rabbahu muneeban ilayhi thumma i*tha* khawwalahu niAAmatan minhu nasiya m*a* k*a*na yadAAoo ilayhi min qablu wajaAAala lill*a*hi and*a*dan liyu*d*illa AAan sabeelihi qul tamattaAA bikufrika qaleelan innaka min a*s**ha*bi a**l**nn*a*r**i**

## 39:9

Amman huwa q*a*nitun *a*n*a*a allayli s*a*jidan waq*a*iman ya*hth*aru al*a*khirata wayarjoo ra*h*mata rabbihi qul hal yastawee alla*th*eena yaAAlamoona wa**a**lla*th*eena l*a* yaAAlamoona innam*a* yata*th*akkaru oloo alalb*a*b**i**

## 39:10

Qul y*a* AAib*a*di alla*th*eena *a*manoo ittaqoo rabbakum lilla*th*eena a*h*sanoo fee h*ath*ihi a**l**dduny*a* *h*asanatun waar*d*u All*a*hi w*a*siAAatun innam*a* yuwaff*a* a**l***ssa*biroona ajrahum bighayri *h*is*a*b**in**

## 39:11

Qul innee omirtu an aAAbuda All*a*ha mukhli*s*an lahu a**l**ddeen**a**

## 39:12

Waomirtu lian akoona awwala almuslimeen**a**

## 39:13

Qul innee akh*a*fu in AAa*s*aytu rabbee AAa*tha*ba yawmin AA&#x61;**th**&#x65;em**in**

## 39:14

Quli All*a*ha aAAbudu mukhli*s*an lahu deenee

## 39:15

Fa**o**AAbudoo m*a* shitum min doonihi qul inna alkh*a*sireena alla*th*eena khasiroo anfusahum waahleehim yawma alqiy*a*mati al*a* *tha*lika huwa alkhusr*a*nu almubeen**u**

## 39:16

Lahum min fawqihim **th**&#x75;lalun mina a**l**nn*a*ri wamin ta*h*tihim **th**&#x75;lalun *tha*lika yukhawwifu All*a*hu bihi AAib*a*dahu y*a* AAib*a*di fa**i**ttaqoon**i**

## 39:17

Wa**a**lla*th*eena ijtanaboo a**l***tta*ghoota an yaAAbudooh*a* waan*a*boo il*a* All*a*hi lahumu albushr*a* fabashshir AAib*a*d**i**

## 39:18

Alla*th*eena yastamiAAoona alqawla fayattabiAAoona a*h*sanahu ol*a*ika alla*th*eena had*a*humu All*a*hu waol*a*ika hum oloo alalb*a*b**i**

## 39:19

Afaman *h*aqqa AAalayhi kalimatu alAAa*tha*bi afaanta tunqi*th*u man fee a**l**nn*a*r**i**

## 39:20

L*a*kini alla*th*eena ittaqaw rabbahum lahum ghurafun min fawqih*a* ghurafun mabniyyatun tajree min ta*h*tih*a* alanh*a*ru waAAda All*a*hi l*a* yukhlifu All*a*hu almeeAA*a*d**a**

## 39:21

Alam tara anna All*a*ha anzala mina a**l**ssam*a*i m*a*an fasalakahu yan*a*beeAAa fee alar*d*i thumma yukhriju bihi zarAAan mukhtalifan alw*a*nuhu thumma yaheeju fatar*a*hu mu*s*farran thumma yajAAaluhu *h*u*ta*man inna fee *tha*lika la*th*ikr*a* liolee alalb*a*b**i**

## 39:22

Afaman shara*h*a All*a*hu *s*adrahu lilisl*a*mi fahuwa AAal*a* noorin min rabbihi fawaylun lilq*a*siyati quloobuhum min *th*ikri All*a*hi ol*a*ika fee *d*al*a*lin mubeen**in**

## 39:23

All*a*hu nazzala a*h*sana al*h*adeethi kit*a*ban mutash*a*bihan math*a*niya taqshaAAirru minhu juloodu alla*th*eena yakhshawna rabbahum thumma taleenu julooduhum waquloobuhum il*a* *th*ikri All*a*hi *tha*lika hud*a* All*a*hi yahdee bihi man yash*a*o waman yu*d*lili All*a*hu fam*a* lahu min h*a*d**in**

## 39:24

Afaman yattaqee biwajhihi sooa alAAa*tha*bi yawma alqiy*a*mati waqeela li**l****thth***a*limeena *th*ooqoo m*a* kuntum taksiboon**a**

## 39:25

Ka*thth*aba alla*th*eena min qablihim faat*a*humu alAAa*tha*bu min *h*aythu l*a* yashAAuroon**a**

## 39:26

Faa*tha*qahumu All*a*hu alkhizya fee al*h*ay*a*ti a**l**dduny*a* walaAAa*tha*bu al*a*khirati akbaru law k*a*noo yaAAlamoon**a**

## 39:27

Walaqad *d*arabn*a* li**l**nn*a*si fee h*atha* alqur*a*ni min kulli mathalin laAAallahum yata*th*akkaroon**a**

## 39:28

Qur*a*nan AAarabiyyan ghayra *th*ee AAiwajin laAAallahum yattaqoon**a**

## 39:29

*D*araba All*a*hu mathalan rajulan feehi shurak*a*o mutash*a*kisoona warajulan salaman lirajulin hal yastawiy*a*ni mathalan al*h*amdu lill*a*hi bal aktharuhum l*a* yaAAlamoon**a**

## 39:30

Innaka mayyitun wainnahum mayyitoon**a**

## 39:31

Thumma innakum yawma alqiy*a*mati AAinda rabbikum takhta*s*imoon**a**

## 39:32

Faman &#x61;**th**&#x6C;amu mimman ka*th*aba AAal*a* All*a*hi waka*thth*aba bi**al***ss*idqi i*th* j*a*ahu alaysa fee jahannama mathwan lilk*a*fireen**a**

## 39:33

Wa**a**lla*th*ee j*a*a bi**al***ss*idqi wa*s*addaqa bihi ol*a*ika humu almuttaqoon**a**

## 39:34

Lahum m*a* yash*a*oona AAinda rabbihim *tha*lika jaz*a*o almu*h*sineen**a**

## 39:35

Liyukaffira All*a*hu AAanhum aswaa alla*th*ee AAamiloo wayajziyahum ajrahum bia*h*sani alla*th*ee k*a*noo yaAAmaloon**a**

## 39:36

Alaysa All*a*hu bik*a*fin AAabdahu wayukhawwifoonaka bi**a**lla*th*eena min doonihi waman yu*d*lili All*a*hu fam*a* lahu min h*a*d**in**

## 39:37

Waman yahdi All*a*hu fam*a* lahu min mu*d*illin alaysa All*a*hu biAAazeezin *th*ee intiq*a*m**in**

## 39:38

Walain saaltahum man khalaqa a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*a layaqoolunna All*a*hu qul afaraaytum m*a* tadAAoona min dooni All*a*hi in ar*a*daniya All*a*hu bi*d*urrin hal hunna k*a*shif*a*tu *d*urrihi aw ar*a*danee bira*h*matin hal hunna mumsik*a*tu ra*h*matihi qul *h*asbiya All*a*hu AAalayhi yatawakkalu almutawakkiloon**a**

## 39:39

Qul y*a* qawmi iAAmaloo AAal*a* mak*a*natikum innee AA*a*milun fasawfa taAAlamoon**a**

## 39:40

Man yateehi AAa*tha*bun yukhzeehi waya*h*illu AAalayhi AAa*tha*bun muqeem**un**

## 39:41

Inn*a* anzaln*a* AAalayka alkit*a*ba li**l**nn*a*si bi**a**l*h*aqqi famani ihtad*a* falinafsihi waman *d*alla fainnam*a* ya*d*illu AAalayh*a* wam*a* anta AAalayhim biwakeel**in**

## 39:42

All*a*hu yatawaff*a* alanfusa *h*eena mawtih*a* wa**a**llatee lam tamut fee man*a*mih*a* fayumsiku allatee qa*da* AAalayh*a* almawta wayursilu alokhr*a* il*a* ajalin musamman inna fee *tha*lika la*a*y*a*tin liqawmin yatafakkaroon**a**

## 39:43

Ami ittakha*th*oo min dooni All*a*hi shufaAA*a*a qul awalaw k*a*noo l*a* yamlikoona shayan wal*a* yaAAqiloon**a**

## 39:44

Qul lill*a*hi a**l**shshaf*a*AAatu jameeAAan lahu mulku a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i thumma ilayhi turjaAAoon**a**

## 39:45

Wai*tha* *th*ukira All*a*hu wa*h*dahu ishmaazzat quloobu alla*th*eena l*a* yuminoona bi**a**l*a*khirati wai*tha* *th*ukira alla*th*eena min doonihi i*tha* hum yastabshiroon**a**

## 39:46

Quli all*a*humma f*at*ira a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i AA*a*lima alghaybi wa**al**shshah*a*dati anta ta*h*kumu bayna AAib*a*dika fee m*a* k*a*noo feehi yakhtalifoon**a**

## 39:47

Walaw anna lilla*th*eena **th**&#x61;lamoo m*a* fee alar*d*i jameeAAan wamithlahu maAAahu la**i**ftadaw bihi min sooi alAAa*tha*bi yawma alqiy*a*mati wabad*a* lahum mina All*a*hi m*a* lam yakoonoo ya*h*tasiboon**a**

## 39:48

Wabad*a* lahum sayyi*a*tu m*a* kasaboo wa*ha*qa bihim m*a* k*a*noo bihi yastahzioon**a**

## 39:49

Fai*tha* massa alins*a*na *d*urrun daAA*a*n*a* thumma i*tha* khawwaln*a*hu niAAmatan minn*a* q*a*la innam*a* ooteetuhu AAal*a* AAilmin bal hiya fitnatun wal*a*kinna aktharahum l*a* yaAAlamoon**a**

## 39:50

Qad q*a*lah*a* alla*th*eena min qablihim fam*a* aghn*a* AAanhum m*a* k*a*noo yaksiboon**a**

## 39:51

Faa*sa*bahum sayyi*a*tu m*a* kasaboo wa**a**lla*th*eena **th**&#x61;lamoo min h*a*ol*a*i sayu*s*eebuhum sayyi*a*tu m*a* kasaboo wam*a* hum bimuAAjizeen**a**

## 39:52

Awalam yaAAlamoo anna All*a*ha yabsu*t*u a**l**rrizqa liman yash*a*o wayaqdiru inna fee *tha*lika la*a*y*a*tin liqawmin yuminoon**a**

## 39:53

Qul y*a* AAib*a*diya alla*th*eena asrafoo AAal*a* anfusihim l*a* taqna*t*oo min ra*h*mati All*a*hi inna All*a*ha yaghfiru a**l***thth*unooba jameeAAan innahu huwa alghafooru a**l**rra*h*eem**u**

## 39:54

Waaneeboo il*a* rabbikum waaslimoo lahu min qabli an yatiyakumu alAAa*tha*bu thumma l*a* tun*s*aroon**a**

## 39:55

Wa**i**ttabiAAoo a*h*sana m*a* onzila ilaykum min rabbikum min qabli an yatiyakumu alAAa*tha*bu baghtatan waantum l*a* tashAAuroon**a**

## 39:56

An taqoola nafsun y*a* *h*asrat*a* AAal*a* m*a* farra*t*tu fee janbi All*a*hi wain kuntu lamina a**l**ss*a*khireen**a**

## 39:57

Aw taqoola law anna All*a*ha had*a*nee lakuntu mina almuttaqeen**a**

## 39:58

Aw taqoola *h*eena tar*a* alAAa*tha*ba law anna lee karratan faakoona mina almu*h*sineen**a**

## 39:59

Bal*a* qad j*a*atka *a*y*a*tee faka*thth*abta bih*a* wa**i**stakbarta wakunta mina alk*a*fireen**a**

## 39:60

Wayawma alqiy*a*mati tar*a* alla*th*eena ka*th*aboo AAal*a* All*a*hi wujoohuhum muswaddatun alaysa fee jahannama mathwan lilmutakabbireen**a**

## 39:61

Wayunajjee All*a*hu alla*th*eena ittaqaw bimaf*a*zatihim l*a* yamassuhumu a**l**ssooo wal*a* hum ya*h*zanoon**a**

## 39:62

All*a*hu kh*a*liqu kulli shayin wahuwa AAal*a* kulli shayin wakeel**un**

## 39:63

Lahu maq*a*leedu a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i wa**a**lla*th*eena kafaroo bi*a*y*a*ti All*a*hi ol*a*ika humu alkh*a*siroon**a**

## 39:64

Qul afaghayra All*a*hi tamuroonnee aAAbudu ayyuh*a* alj*a*hiloon**a**

## 39:65

Walaqad oo*h*iya ilayka wail*a* alla*th*eena min qablika lain ashrakta laya*h*ba*t*anna AAamaluka walatakoonanna mina alkh*a*sireen**a**

## 39:66

Bali All*a*ha fa**o**AAbud wakun mina a**l**shsh*a*kireen**a**

## 39:67

Wam*a* qadaroo All*a*ha *h*aqqa qadrihi wa**a**lar*d*u jameeAAan qab*d*atuhu yawma alqiy*a*mati wa**al**ssam*a*w*a*tu ma*t*wiyy*a*tun biyameenihi sub*ha*nahu wataAA*a*l*a* AAamm*a* yushrikoon**a**

## 39:68

Wanufikha fee a**l***ss*oori fa*s*aAAiqa man fee a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti waman fee alar*d*i ill*a* man sh*a*a All*a*hu thumma nufikha feehi okhr*a* fai*tha* hum qiy*a*mun ya&#x6E;**th**&#x75;roon**a**

## 39:69

Waashraqati alar*d*u binoori rabbih*a* wawu*d*iAAa alkit*a*bu wajeea bi**al**nnabiyyeena wa**al**shshuhad*a*i waqu*d*iya baynahum bi**a**l*h*aqqi wahum l*a* y&#x75;**th**&#x6C;amoon**a**

## 39:70

Wawuffiyat kullu nafsin m*a* AAamilat wahuwa aAAlamu bim*a* yafAAaloon**a**

## 39:71

Waseeqa alla*th*eena kafaroo il*a* jahannama zumaran *h*att*a* i*tha* j*a*ooh*a* futi*h*at abw*a*buh*a* waq*a*la lahum khazanatuh*a* alam yatikum rusulun minkum yatloona AAalaykum *a*y*a*ti rabbikum wayun*th*iroonakum liq*a*a yawmikum h*atha* q*a*loo bal*a* wal*a*kin *h*aqqat kalimatu alAAa*tha*bi AAal*a* alk*a*fireen**a**

## 39:72

Qeela odkhuloo abw*a*ba jahannama kh*a*lideena feeh*a* fabisa mathw*a* almutakabbireen**a**

## 39:73

Waseeqa alla*th*eena ittaqaw rabbahum il*a* aljannati zumaran *h*att*a* i*tha* j*a*ooh*a* wafuti*h*at abw*a*buh*a* waq*a*la lahum khazanatuh*a* sal*a*mun AAalaykum *t*ibtum fa**o**dkhulooh*a* kh*a*lideen**a**

## 39:74

Waq*a*loo al*h*amdu lill*a*hi alla*th*ee *s*adaqan*a* waAAdahu waawrathan*a* alar*d*a natabawwao mina aljannati *h*aythu nash*a*o faniAAma ajru alAA*a*mileen**a**

## 39:75

Watar*a* almal*a*ikata *ha*ffeena min *h*awli alAAarshi yusabbi*h*oona bi*h*amdi rabbihim waqu*d*iya baynahum bi**a**l*h*aqqi waqeela al*h*amdu lill*a*hi rabbi alAA*a*lameen**a**

## 40:1

*Ha*meem

## 40:2

Tanzeelu alkit*a*bi mina All*a*hi alAAazeezi alAAaleem**i**

## 40:3

Gh*a*firi a**l***thth*anbi waq*a*bili a**l**ttawbi shadeedi alAAiq*a*bi *th*ee a**l***tt*awli l*a* il*a*ha ill*a* huwa ilayhi alma*s*eer**u**

## 40:4

M*a* yuj*a*dilu fee *a*y*a*ti All*a*hi ill*a* alla*th*eena kafaroo fal*a* yaghrurka taqallubuhum fee albil*a*d**i**

## 40:5

Ka*thth*abat qablahum qawmu noo*h*in wa**a**la*h*z*a*bu min baAAdihim wahammat kullu ommatin birasoolihim liyakhu*th*oohu waj*a*daloo bi**a**lb*at*ili liyud*h*i*d*oo bihi al*h*aqqa faakha*th*tuhum fakayfa k*a*na AAiq*a*b**i**

## 40:6

Waka*tha*lika *h*aqqat kalimatu rabbika AAal*a* alla*th*eena kafaroo annahum a*s**ha*bu a**l**nn*a*r**i**

## 40:7

Alla*th*eena ya*h*miloona alAAarsha waman *h*awlahu yusabbi*h*oona bi*h*amdi rabbihim wayuminoona bihi wayastaghfiroona lilla*th*eena *a*manoo rabban*a* wasiAAta kulla shayin ra*h*matan waAAilman fa**i**ghfir lilla*th*eena t*a*boo wa**i**ttabaAAoo sabeelaka waqihim AAa*tha*ba alja*h*eem**i**

## 40:8

Rabban*a* waadkhilhum jann*a*ti AAadnin allatee waAAadtahum waman *s*ala*h*a min *a*b*a*ihim waazw*a*jihim wa*th*urriyy*a*tihim innaka anta alAAazeezu al*h*akeem**u**

## 40:9

Waqihimu a**l**ssayyi*a*ti waman taqi a**l**ssayyi*a*ti yawmai*th*in faqad ra*h*imtahu wa*tha*lika huwa alfawzu alAA&#x61;**th**&#x65;em**u**

## 40:10

Inna alla*th*eena kafaroo yun*a*dawna lamaqtu All*a*hi akbaru min maqtikum anfusakum i*th* tudAAawna il*a* aleem*a*ni fatakfuroon**a**

## 40:11

Q*a*loo rabban*a* amattan*a* ithnatayni waa*h*yaytan*a* ithnatayni fa**i**AAtarafn*a* bi*th*unoobin*a* fahal il*a* khuroojin min sabeel**in**

## 40:12

*Tha*likum biannahu i*tha* duAAiya All*a*hu wa*h*dahu kafartum wain yushrak bihi tuminoo fa**a**l*h*ukmu lill*a*hi alAAaliyyi alkabeer**i**

## 40:13

Huwa alla*th*ee yureekum *a*y*a*tihi wayunazzilu lakum mina a**l**ssam*a*i rizqan wam*a* yata*th*akkaru ill*a* man yuneeb**u**

## 40:14

Fa**o**dAAoo All*a*ha mukhli*s*eena lahu a**l**ddeena walaw kariha alk*a*firoon**a**

## 40:15

RafeeAAu a**l**ddaraj*a*ti *th*oo alAAarshi yulqee a**l**rroo*h*a min amrihi AAal*a* man yash*a*o min AAib*a*dihi liyun*th*ira yawma a**l**ttal*a*q**i**

## 40:16

Yawma hum b*a*rizoona l*a* yakhf*a* AAal*a* All*a*hi minhum shayon limani almulku alyawma lill*a*hi alw*ah*idi alqahh*a*r**i**

## 40:17

Alyawma tujz*a* kullu nafsin bim*a* kasabat l*a* **th**&#x75;lma alyawma inna All*a*ha sareeAAu al*h*is*a*b**i**

## 40:18

Waan*th*irhum yawma al*a*zifati i*th*i alquloobu lad*a* al*h*an*a*jiri k*a***th**&#x69;meena m*a* li**l****thth***a*limeena min *h*ameemin wal*a* shafeeAAin yu*ta*AA**u**

## 40:19

YaAAlamu kh*a*inata alaAAyuni wam*a* tukhfee a**l***ss*udoor**u**

## 40:20

Wa**A**ll*a*hu yaq*d*ee bi**a**l*h*aqqi wa**a**lla*th*eena yadAAoona min doonihi l*a* yaq*d*oona bishayin inna All*a*ha huwa a**l**ssameeAAu alba*s*eer**u**

## 40:21

Awa lam yaseeroo fee alar*d*i faya&#x6E;**th**&#x75;roo kayfa k*a*na AA*a*qibatu alla*th*eena k*a*noo min qablihim k*a*noo hum ashadda minhum quwwatan wa*a*th*a*ran fee alar*d*i faakha*th*ahumu All*a*hu bi*th*unoobihim wam*a* k*a*na lahum mina All*a*hi min w*a*q**in**

## 40:22

*Tha*lika biannahum k*a*nat tateehim rusuluhum bi**a**lbayyin*a*ti fakafaroo faakha*th*ahumu All*a*hu innahu qawiyyun shadeedu alAAiq*a*b**i**

## 40:23

Walaqad arsaln*a* moos*a* bi*a*y*a*tin*a* wasul*ta*nin mubeen**in**

## 40:24

Il*a* firAAawna wah*a*m*a*na waq*a*roona faq*a*loo s*ah*irun ka*ththa*b**un**

## 40:25

Falamm*a* j*a*ahum bi**a**l*h*aqqi min AAindin*a* q*a*loo oqtuloo abn*a*a alla*th*eena *a*manoo maAAahu wa**i**sta*h*yoo nis*a*ahum wam*a* kaydu alk*a*fireena ill*a* fee *d*al*a*l**in**

## 40:26

Waq*a*la firAAawnu *th*aroonee aqtul moos*a* walyadAAu rabbahu innee akh*a*fu an yubaddila deenakum aw an y&#x75;**th**&#x68;ira fee alar*d*i alfas*a*d**a**

## 40:27

Waq*a*la moos*a* innee AAu*th*tu birabbee warabbikum min kulli mutakabbirin l*a* yuminu biyawmi al*h*is*a*b**i**

## 40:28

Waq*a*la rajulun muminun min *a*li firAAawna yaktumu eem*a*nahu ataqtuloona rajulan an yaqoola rabbiyya All*a*hu waqad j*a*akum bi**a**lbayyin*a*ti min rabbikum wain yaku k*ath*iban faAAalayhi ka*th*ibuhu wain yaku *sa*diqan yu*s*ibkum baAA*d*u alla*th*ee yaAAidukum inna All*a*ha l*a* yahdee man huwa musrifun ka*ththa*b**un**

## 40:29

Y*a* qawmi lakumu almulku alyawma **th***a*hireena fee alar*d*i faman yan*s*urun*a* min basi All*a*hi in j*a*an*a* q*a*la firAAawnu m*a* oreekum ill*a* m*a* ar*a* wam*a* ahdeekum ill*a* sabeela a**l**rrash*a*d**i**

## 40:30

Waq*a*la alla*th*ee *a*mana y*a* qawmi innee akh*a*fu AAalaykum mithla yawmi ala*h*z*a*b**i**

## 40:31

Mithla dabi qawmi noo*h*in waAA*a*din wathamooda wa**a**lla*th*eena min baAAdihim wam*a* All*a*hu yureedu **th**&#x75;lman lilAAib*a*d**i**

## 40:32

Way*a* qawmi innee akh*a*fu AAalaykum yawma a**l**ttan*a*d**i**

## 40:33

Yawma tuwalloona mudbireena m*a* lakum mina All*a*hi min AA*as*imin waman yu*d*lili All*a*hu fam*a* lahu min h*a*d**in**

## 40:34

Walaqad j*a*akum yoosufu min qablu bi**a**lbayyin*a*ti fam*a* ziltum fee shakkin mimm*a* j*a*akum bihi *h*att*a* i*tha* halaka qultum lan yabAAatha All*a*hu min baAAdihi rasoolan ka*tha*lika yu*d*illu All*a*hu man huwa musrifun murt*a*b**un**

## 40:35

Alla*th*eena yuj*a*diloona fee *a*y*a*ti All*a*hi bighayri sul*ta*nin at*a*hum kabura maqtan AAinda All*a*hi waAAinda alla*th*eena *a*manoo ka*tha*lika ya*t*baAAu All*a*hu AAal*a* kulli qalbi mutakabbirin jabb*a*r**in**

## 40:36

Waq*a*la firAAawnu y*a* h*a*m*a*nu ibni lee *s*ar*h*an laAAallee ablughu alasb*a*b**a**

## 40:37

Asb*a*ba a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti faa*tt*aliAAa il*a* il*a*hi moos*a* wainnee la&#x61;**th**&#x75;nnuhu k*ath*iban waka*tha*lika zuyyina lifirAAawna sooo AAamalihi wa*s*udda AAani a**l**ssabeeli wam*a* kaydu firAAawna ill*a* fee tab*a*b**in**

## 40:38

Waq*a*la alla*th*ee *a*mana y*a* qawmi ittabiAAooni ahdikum sabeela a**l**rrash*a*d**i**

## 40:39

Y*a* qawmi innam*a* h*ath*ihi al*h*ay*a*tu a**l**dduny*a* mat*a*AAun wainna al*a*khirata hiya d*a*ru alqar*a*r**i**

## 40:40

Man AAamila sayyiatan fal*a* yujz*a* ill*a* mithlah*a* waman AAamila *sa*li*h*an min *th*akarin aw onth*a* wahuwa muminun faol*a*ika yadkhuloona aljannata yurzaqoona feeh*a* bighayri *h*is*a*b**in**

## 40:41

Way*a* qawmi m*a* lee adAAookum il*a* a**l**nnaj*a*ti watadAAoonanee il*a* a**l**nn*a*r**i**

## 40:42

TadAAoonanee liakfura bi**A**ll*a*hi waoshrika bihi m*a* laysa lee bihi AAilmun waan*a* adAAookum il*a* alAAazeezi alghaff*a*r**i**

## 40:43

L*a* jarama annam*a* tadAAoonanee ilayhi laysa lahu daAAwatun fee a**l**dduny*a* wal*a* fee al*a*khirati waanna maraddan*a* il*a* All*a*hi waanna almusrifeena hum a*s**ha*bu a**l**nn*a*r**i**

## 40:44

Fasata*th*kuroona m*a* aqoolu lakum waofawwi*d*u amree il*a* All*a*hi inna All*a*ha ba*s*eerun bi**a**lAAib*a*d**i**

## 40:45

Fawaq*a*hu All*a*hu sayyi*a*ti m*a* makaroo wa*ha*qa bi*a*li firAAawna sooo alAAa*tha*b**i**

## 40:46

A**l**nn*a*ru yuAAra*d*oona AAalayh*a* ghuduwwan waAAashiyyan wayawma taqoomu a**l**ss*a*AAatu adkhiloo *a*la firAAawna ashadda alAAa*tha*b**i**

## 40:47

Wai*th* yata*ha*jjoona fee a**l**nn*a*ri fayaqoolu a**l***dd*uAAaf*a*o lilla*th*eena istakbaroo inn*a* kunn*a* lakum tabaAAan fahal antum mughnoona AAann*a* na*s*eeban mina a**l**nn*a*r**i**

## 40:48

Q*a*la alla*th*eena istakbaroo inn*a* kullun feeh*a* inna All*a*ha qad *h*akama bayna alAAib*a*d**i**

## 40:49

Waq*a*la alla*th*eena fee a**l**nn*a*ri likhazanati jahannama odAAoo rabbakum yukhaffif AAann*a* yawman mina alAAa*tha*b**i**

## 40:50

Q*a*loo awalam taku tateekum rusulukum bi**a**lbayyin*a*ti q*a*loo bal*a* q*a*loo fa**o**dAAoo wam*a* duAA*a*o alk*a*fireena ill*a* fee *d*al*a*l**in**

## 40:51

Inn*a* lanan*s*uru rusulan*a* wa**a**lla*th*eena *a*manoo fee al*h*ay*a*ti a**l**dduny*a* wayawma yaqoomu alashh*a*d**u**

## 40:52

Yawma l*a* yanfaAAu a**l****thth***a*limeena maAA*th*iratuhum walahumu allaAAnatu walahum sooo a**l**dd*a*r**i**

## 40:53

Walaqad *a*tayn*a* moos*a* alhud*a* waawrathn*a* banee isr*a*eela alkit*a*b**a**

## 40:54

Hudan wa*th*ikr*a* liolee alalb*a*b**i**

## 40:55

Fa**i***s*bir inna waAAda All*a*hi *h*aqqun wa**i**staghfir li*th*anbika wasabbi*h* bi*h*amdi rabbika bi**a**lAAashiyyi wa**a**libk*a*r**i**

## 40:56

Inna alla*th*eena yuj*a*diloona fee *a*y*a*ti All*a*hi bighayri sul*ta*nin at*a*hum in fee *s*udoorihim ill*a* kibrun m*a* hum bib*a*ligheehi fa**i**staAAi*th* bi**A**ll*a*hi innahu huwa a**l**ssameeAAu alba*s*eer**u**

## 40:57

Lakhalqu a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i akbaru min khalqi a**l**nn*a*si wal*a*kinna akthara a**l**nn*a*si l*a* yaAAlamoon**a**

## 40:58

Wam*a* yastawee alaAAm*a* wa**a**lba*s*eeru wa**a**lla*th*eena *a*manoo waAAamiloo a**l***ssa*li*ha*ti wal*a* almuseeo qaleelan m*a* tata*th*akkaroon**a**

## 40:59

Inna a**l**ss*a*AAata la*a*tiyatun l*a* rayba feeh*a* wal*a*kinna akthara a**l**nn*a*si l*a* yuminoon**a**

## 40:60

Waq*a*la rabbukumu odAAoonee astajib lakum inna alla*th*eena yastakbiroona AAan AAib*a*datee sayadkhuloona jahannama d*a*khireen**a**

## 40:61

All*a*hu alla*th*ee jaAAala lakumu allayla litaskunoo feehi wa**al**nnah*a*ra mub*s*iran inna All*a*ha la*th*oo fa*d*lin AAal*a* a**l**nn*a*si wal*a*kinna akthara a**l**nn*a*si l*a* yashkuroon**a**

## 40:62

*Tha*likumu All*a*hu rabbukum kh*a*liqu kulli shayin l*a* il*a*ha ill*a* huwa faann*a* tufakoon**a**

## 40:63

Ka*tha*lika yufaku alla*th*eena k*a*noo bi*a*y*a*ti All*a*hi yaj*h*adoon**a**

## 40:64

All*a*hu alla*th*ee jaAAala lakumu alar*d*a qar*a*ran wa**al**ssam*a*a bin*a*an wa*s*awwarakum faa*h*sana *s*uwarakum warazaqakum mina a**l***tt*ayyib*a*ti *tha*likumu All*a*hu rabbukum fatab*a*raka All*a*hu rabbu alAA*a*lameen**a**

## 40:65

Huwa al*h*ayyu l*a* il*a*ha ill*a* huwa fa**o**dAAoohu mukhli*s*eena lahu a**l**ddeena al*h*amdu lill*a*hi rabbi alAA*a*lameen**a**

## 40:66

Qul innee nuheetu an aAAbuda alla*th*eena tadAAoona min dooni All*a*hi lamm*a* j*a*aniya albayyin*a*tu min rabbee waomirtu an oslima lirabbi alAA*a*lameen**a**

## 40:67

Huwa alla*th*ee khalaqakum min tur*a*bin thumma min nu*t*fatin thumma min AAalaqatin thumma yukhrijukum *t*iflan thumma litablughoo ashuddakum thumma litakoonoo shuyookhan waminkum man yutawaff*a* min qablu walitablughoo ajalan musamman walaAAallakum taAAqiloon**a**

## 40:68

Huwa alla*th*ee yu*h*yee wayumeetu fai*tha* qa*da* amran fainnam*a* yaqoolu lahu kun fayakoon**u**

## 40:69

Alam tara il*a* alla*th*eena yuj*a*diloona fee *a*y*a*ti All*a*hi ann*a* yu*s*rafoon**a**

## 40:70

Alla*th*eena ka*thth*aboo bi**a**lkit*a*bi wabim*a* arsaln*a* bihi rusulan*a* fasawfa yaAAlamoon**a**

## 40:71

I*th*i alaghl*a*lu fee aAAn*a*qihim wa**al**ssal*a*silu yus*h*aboon**a**

## 40:72

Fee al*h*ameemi thumma fee a**l**nn*a*ri yusjaroon**a**

## 40:73

Thumma qeela lahum ayna m*a* kuntum tushrikoon**a**

## 40:74

Min dooni All*a*hi q*a*loo *d*alloo AAann*a* bal lam nakun nadAAoo min qablu shayan ka*tha*lika yu*d*illu All*a*hu alk*a*fireen**a**

## 40:75

*Tha*likum bim*a* kuntum tafra*h*oona fee alar*d*i bighayri al*h*aqqi wabim*a* kuntum tamra*h*oon**a**

## 40:76

Odkhuloo abw*a*ba jahannama kh*a*lideena feeh*a* fabisa mathw*a* almutakabbireen**a**

## 40:77

Fa**i***s*bir inna waAAda All*a*hi *h*aqqun faimm*a* nuriyannaka baAA*d*a alla*th*ee naAAiduhum aw natawaffayannaka failayn*a* yurjaAAoon**a**

## 40:78

Walaqad arsaln*a* rusulan min qablika minhum man qa*s*a*s*n*a* AAalayka waminhum man lam naq*s*u*s* AAalayka wam*a* k*a*na lirasoolin an yatiya bi*a*yatin ill*a* bii*th*ni All*a*hi fai*tha* j*a*a amru All*a*hi qu*d*iya bi**a**l*h*aqqi wakhasira hun*a*lika almub*t*iloon**a**

## 40:79

All*a*hu alla*th*ee jaAAala lakumu alanAA*a*ma litarkaboo minh*a* waminh*a* takuloon**a**

## 40:80

Walakum feeh*a* man*a*fiAAu walitablughoo AAalayh*a* *ha*jatan fee *s*udoorikum waAAalayh*a* waAAal*a* alfulki tu*h*maloon**a**

## 40:81

Wayureekum *a*y*a*tihi faayya *a*y*a*ti All*a*hi tunkiroon**a**

## 40:82

Afalam yaseeroo fee alar*d*i faya&#x6E;**th**&#x75;roo kayfa k*a*na AA*a*qibatu alla*th*eena min qablihim k*a*noo akthara minhum waashadda quwwatan wa*a*th*a*ran fee alar*d*i fam*a* aghn*a* AAanhum m*a* k*a*noo yaksiboon**a**

## 40:83

Falamm*a* j*a*athum rusuluhum bi**a**lbayyin*a*ti fari*h*oo bim*a* AAindahum mina alAAilmi wa*ha*qa bihim m*a* k*a*noo bihi yastahzioon**a**

## 40:84

Falamm*a* raaw basan*a* q*a*loo *a*mann*a* bi**A**ll*a*hi wa*h*dahu wakafarn*a* bim*a* kunn*a* bihi mushrikeen**a**

## 40:85

Falam yaku yanfaAAuhum eem*a*nuhum lamm*a* raaw basan*a* sunnata All*a*hi allatee qad khalat fee AAib*a*dihi wakhasira hun*a*lika alk*a*firoon**a**

## 41:1

*Ha*meem

## 41:2

Tanzeelun mina a**l**rra*h*m*a*ni a**l**rra*h*eem**i**

## 41:3

Kit*a*bun fu*ss*ilat *a*y*a*tuhu qur*a*nan AAarabiyyan liqawmin yaAAlamoon**a**

## 41:4

Basheeran wana*th*eeran faaAAra*d*a aktharuhum fahum l*a* yasmaAAoon**a**

## 41:5

Waq*a*loo quloobun*a* fee akinnatin mimm*a* tadAAoon*a* ilayhi wafee *atha*nin*a* waqrun wamin baynin*a* wabaynika *h*ij*a*bun fa**i**AAmal innan*a* AA*a*miloon**a**

## 41:6

Qul innam*a* an*a* basharun mithlukum yoo*ha* ilayya annam*a* il*a*hukum il*a*hun w*ah*idun fa**i**staqeemoo ilayhi wa**i**staghfiroohu wawaylun lilmushrikeen**a**

## 41:7

Alla*th*eena l*a* yutoona a**l**zzak*a*ta wahum bi**a**l*a*khirati hum k*a*firoon**a**

## 41:8

Inna alla*th*eena *a*manoo waAAamiloo a**l***ssa*li*ha*ti lahum ajrun ghayru mamnoon**in**

## 41:9

Qul ainnakum latakfuroona bi**a**lla*th*ee khalaqa alar*d*a fee yawmayni watajAAaloona lahu and*a*dan *tha*lika rabbu alAA*a*lameen**a**

## 41:10

WajaAAala feeh*a* raw*a*siya min fawqih*a* wab*a*raka feeh*a* waqaddara feeh*a* aqw*a*tah*a* fee arbaAAati ayy*a*min saw*a*an li**l**ss*a*ileen**a**

## 41:11

Thumma istaw*a* il*a* a**l**ssam*a*i wahiya dukh*a*nun faq*a*la lah*a* walilar*d*i itiy*a* *t*awAAan aw karhan q*a*lat*a* atayn*a* *ta*iAAeen**a**

## 41:12

Faqa*da*hunna sabAAa sam*a*w*a*tin fee yawmayni waaw*ha* fee kulli sam*a*in amrah*a* wazayyann*a* a**l**ssam*a*a a**l**dduny*a* bima*sa*bee*h*a wa*h*i&#x66;**th**&#x61;n *tha*lika taqdeeru alAAazeezi alAAaleem**i**

## 41:13

Fain aAAra*d*oo fuqul an*th*artukum *sa*AAiqatan mithla *sa*AAiqati AA*a*din wathamood**a**

## 41:14

I*th* j*a*athumu a**l**rrusulu min bayni aydeehim wamin khalfihim all*a* taAAbudoo ill*a* All*a*ha q*a*loo law sh*a*a rabbun*a* laanzala mal*a*ikatan fainn*a* bim*a* orsiltum bihi k*a*firoon**a**

## 41:15

Faamm*a* AA*a*dun fa**i**stakbaroo fee alar*d*i bighayri al*h*aqqi waq*a*loo man ashaddu minn*a* quwwatan awalam yaraw anna All*a*ha alla*th*ee khalaqahum huwa ashaddu minhum quwwatan wak*a*noo bi*a*y*a*tin*a* yaj*h*adoon**a**

## 41:16

Faarsaln*a* AAalayhim ree*h*an *s*ar*s*aran fee ayy*a*min na*h*is*a*tin linu*th*eeqahum AAa*tha*ba alkhizyi fee al*h*ay*a*ti a**l**dduny*a* walaAAa*tha*bu al*a*khirati akhz*a* wahum l*a* yun*s*aroon**a**

## 41:17

Waamm*a* thamoodu fahadayn*a*hum fa**i**sta*h*abboo alAAam*a* AAal*a* alhud*a* faakha*th*athum *sa*AAiqatu alAAa*tha*bi alhooni bim*a* k*a*noo yaksiboon**a**

## 41:18

Wanajjayn*a* alla*th*eena *a*manoo wak*a*noo yattaqoon**a**

## 41:19

Wayawma yu*h*sharu aAAd*a*o All*a*hi il*a* a**l**nn*a*ri fahum yoozaAAoon**a**

## 41:20

*H*att*a* i*tha* m*a* j*a*ooh*a* shahida AAalayhim samAAuhum waab*sa*ruhum wajulooduhum bim*a* k*a*noo yaAAmaloon**a**

## 41:21

Waq*a*loo lijuloodihim lima shahidtum AAalayn*a* q*a*loo an*t*aqan*a* All*a*hu alla*th*ee an*t*aqa kulla shayin wahuwa khalaqakum awwala marratin wailayhi turjaAAoon**a**

## 41:22

Wam*a* kuntum tastatiroona an yashhada AAalaykum samAAukum wal*a* ab*sa*rukum wal*a* juloodukum wal*a*kin **th**&#x61;nantum anna All*a*ha l*a* yaAAlamu katheeran mimm*a* taAAmaloon**a**

## 41:23

Wa*tha*likum **th**&#x61;nnukumu alla*th*ee **th**&#x61;nantum birabbikum ard*a*kum faa*s*ba*h*tum mina alkh*a*sireen**a**

## 41:24

Fain ya*s*biroo fa**al**nn*a*ru mathwan lahum wain yastaAAtiboo fam*a* hum mina almuAAtabeen**a**

## 41:25

Waqayya*d*n*a* lahum quran*a*a fazayyanoo lahum m*a* bayna aydeehim wam*a* khalfahum wa*h*aqqa AAalayhimu alqawlu fee omamin qad khalat min qablihim mina aljinni wa**a**linsi innahum k*a*noo kh*a*sireen**a**

## 41:26

Waq*a*la alla*th*eena kafaroo l*a* tasmaAAoo lih*atha* alqur*a*ni wa**i**lghaw feehi laAAallakum taghliboon**a**

## 41:27

Falanu*th*eeqanna alla*th*eena kafaroo AAa*tha*ban shadeedan walanajziyannahum aswaa alla*th*ee k*a*noo yaAAmaloon**a**

## 41:28

*Tha*lika jaz*a*o aAAd*a*i All*a*hi a**l**nn*a*ru lahum feeh*a* d*a*ru alkhuldi jaz*a*an bim*a* k*a*noo bi*a*y*a*tin*a* yaj*h*adoon**a**

## 41:29

Waq*a*la alla*th*eena kafaroo rabban*a* arin*a* alla*th*ayni a*d*all*a*n*a* mina aljinni wa**a**linsi najAAalhum*a* ta*h*ta aqd*a*min*a* liyakoon*a* mina alasfaleen**a**

## 41:30

Inna alla*th*eena q*a*loo rabbun*a* All*a*hu thumma istaq*a*moo tatanazzalu AAalayhimu almal*a*ikatu all*a* takh*a*foo wal*a* ta*h*zanoo waabshiroo bi**a**ljannati allatee kuntum tooAAadoon**a**

## 41:31

Na*h*nu awliy*a*okum fee al*h*ay*a*ti a**l**dduny*a* wafee al*a*khirati walakum feeh*a* m*a* tashtahee anfusukum walakum feeh*a* m*a* taddaAAoon**a**

## 41:32

Nuzulan min ghafoorin ra*h*eem**in**

## 41:33

Waman a*h*sanu qawlan mimman daAA*a* il*a* All*a*hi waAAamila *sa*li*h*an waq*a*la innanee mina almuslimeen**a**

## 41:34

Wal*a* tastawee al*h*asanatu wal*a* a**l**ssayyiatu idfaAA bi**a**llatee hiya a*h*sanu fai*tha* alla*th*ee baynaka wabaynahu AAad*a*watun kaannahu waliyyun *h*ameem**un**

## 41:35

Wam*a* yulaqq*a*h*a* ill*a* alla*th*eena *s*abaroo wam*a* yulaqq*a*h*a* ill*a* *th*oo *h*&#x61;**thth**&#x69;n AA&#x61;**th**&#x65;em**in**

## 41:36

Waimm*a* yanzaghannaka mina a**l**shshay*ta*ni nazghun fa**i**staAAi*th* bi**A**ll*a*hi innahu huwa a**l**ssameeAAu alAAaleem**u**

## 41:37

Wamin *a*y*a*tihi allaylu wa**al**nnah*a*ru wa**al**shshamsu wa**a**lqamaru l*a* tasjudoo li**l**shshamsi wal*a* lilqamari wa**o**sjudoo lill*a*hi ala*th*ee khalaqahunna in kuntum iyy*a*hu taAAbudoon**a**

## 41:38

Faini istakbaroo fa**a**lla*th*eena AAinda rabbika yusabbi*h*oona lahu bi**a**llayli wa**al**nnah*a*ri wahum l*a* yasamoon**a**

## 41:39

Wamin *a*y*a*tihi annaka tar*a* alar*d*a kh*a*shiAAatan fai*tha* anzaln*a* AAalayh*a* alm*a*a ihtazzat warabat inna alla*th*ee a*h*y*a*h*a* lamu*h*yee almawt*a* innahu AAal*a* kulli shayin qadeer**un**

## 41:40

Inna alla*th*eena yul*h*idoona fee *a*y*a*tin*a* l*a* yakhfawna AAalayn*a* afaman yulq*a* fee a**l**nn*a*ri khayrun am man yatee *a*minan yawma alqiy*a*mati iAAmaloo m*a* shitum innahu bim*a* taAAmaloona ba*s*eer**un**

## 41:41

Inna alla*th*eena kafaroo bi**al***thth*ikri lamm*a* j*a*ahum wainnahu lakit*a*bun AAazeez**un**

## 41:42

L*a* yateehi alb*at*ilu min bayni yadayhi wal*a* min khalfihi tanzeelun min *h*akeemin *h*ameed**in**

## 41:43

M*a* yuq*a*lu laka ill*a* m*a* qad qeela li**l**rrusuli min qablika inna rabbaka la*th*oo maghfiratin wa*th*oo AAiq*a*bin aleem**in**

## 41:44

Walaw jaAAaln*a*hu qur*a*nan aAAjamiyyan laq*a*loo lawl*a* fu*ss*ilat *a*y*a*tuhu aaAAjamiyyun waAAarabiyyun qul huwa lilla*th*eena *a*manoo hudan washif*a*on wa**a**lla*th*eena l*a* yuminoona fee *atha*nihim waqrun wahuwa AAalayhim AAaman ol*a*ika yun*a*dawna min mak*a*nin baAAeed**in**

## 41:45

Walaqad *a*tayn*a* moos*a* alkit*a*ba fa**i**khtulifa feehi walawl*a* kalimatun sabaqat min rabbika laqu*d*iya baynahum wainnahum lafee shakkin minhu mureeb**in**

## 41:46

Man AAamila *sa*li*h*an falinafsihi waman as*a*a faAAalayh*a* wam*a* rabbuka b&#x69;**th**&#x61;ll*a*min lilAAabeed**i**

## 41:47

Ilayhi yuraddu AAilmu a**l**ss*a*AAati wam*a* takhruju min thamar*a*tin min akm*a*mih*a* wam*a* ta*h*milu min onth*a* wal*a* ta*d*aAAu ill*a* biAAilmihi wayawma yun*a*deehim ayna shurak*a*ee q*a*loo *ath*ann*a*ka m*a* minn*a* min shaheed**in**

## 41:48

Wa*d*alla AAanhum m*a* k*a*noo yadAAoona min qablu w&#x61;**th**&#x61;nnoo m*a* lahum min ma*h*ee*s***in**

## 41:49

L*a* yasamu alins*a*nu min duAA*a*i alkhayri wain massahu a**l**shsharru fayaoosun qanoo*t***un**

## 41:50

Walain a*th*aqn*a*hu ra*h*matan minn*a* min baAAdi *d*arr*a*a massathu layaqoolanna h*atha* lee wam*a* &#x61;**th**&#x75;nnu a**l**ss*a*AAata q*a*imatan walain rujiAAtu il*a* rabbee inna lee AAindahu lal*h*usn*a* falanunabbianna alla*th*eena kafaroo bim*a* AAamiloo walanu*th*eeqannahum min AAa*tha*bin ghale&#x65;**th****in**

## 41:51

Wai*tha* anAAamn*a* AAal*a* alins*a*ni aAAra*d*a wana*a* bij*a*nibihi wai*tha* massahu a**l**shsharru fa*th*oo duAA*a*in AAaree*d***in**

## 41:52

Qul araaytum in k*a*na min AAindi All*a*hi thumma kafartum bihi man a*d*allu mimman huwa fee shiq*a*qin baAAeed**in**

## 41:53

Sanureehim *a*y*a*tin*a* fee al*a*f*a*qi wafee anfusihim *h*att*a* yatabayyana lahum annahu al*h*aqqu awalam yakfi birabbika annahu AAal*a* kulli shayin shaheed**un**

## 41:54

Al*a* innahum fee miryatin min liq*a*i rabbihim al*a* innahu bikulli shayin mu*h*ee*t***un**

## 42:1

*Ha*meem

## 42:2

AAaynseenq*a*f

## 42:3

Ka*tha*lika yoo*h*ee ilayka wail*a* alla*th*eena min qablika All*a*hu alAAazeezu al*h*akeem**u**

## 42:4

Lahu m*a* fee a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wam*a* fee alar*d*i wahuwa alAAaliyyu alAA&#x61;**th**&#x65;em**u**

## 42:5

Tak*a*du a**l**ssam*a*w*a*tu yatafa*tt*arna min fawqihinna wa**a**lmal*a*ikatu yusabbi*h*oona bi*h*amdi rabbihim wayastaghfiroona liman fee alar*d*i al*a* inna All*a*ha huwa alghafooru a**l**rra*h*eem**u**

## 42:6

Wa**a**lla*th*eena ittakha*th*oo min doonihi awliy*a*a All*a*hu *h*afe&#x65;**th**&#x75;n AAalayhim wam*a* anta AAalayhim biwakeel**in**

## 42:7

Waka*tha*lika aw*h*ayn*a* ilayka qur*a*nan AAarabiyyan litun*th*ira omma alqur*a* waman *h*awlah*a* watun*th*ira yawma aljamAAi l*a* rayba feehi fareequn fee aljannati wafareequn fee a**l**ssaAAeer**i**

## 42:8

Walaw sh*a*a All*a*hu lajaAAalahum ommatan w*ah*idatan wal*a*kin yudkhilu man yash*a*o fee ra*h*matihi wa**al****thth***a*limoona m*a* lahum min waliyyin wal*a* na*s*eer**in**

## 42:9

Ami ittakha*th*oo min doonihi awliy*a*a fa**A**ll*a*hu huwa alwaliyyu wahuwa yu*h*yee almawt*a* wahuwa AAal*a* kulli shayin qadeer**un**

## 42:10

Wam*a* ikhtalaftum feehi min shayin fa*h*ukmuhu il*a* All*a*hi *tha*likumu All*a*hu rabbee AAalayhi tawakkaltu wailayhi oneeb**u**

## 42:11

F*at*iru a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i jaAAala lakum min anfusikum azw*a*jan wamina alanAA*a*mi azw*a*jan ya*th*raokum feehi laysa kamithlihi shayon wahuwa a**l**ssameeAAu alba*s*eer**u**

## 42:12

Lahu maq*a*leedu a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i yabsu*t*u a**l**rrizqa liman yash*a*o wayaqdiru innahu bikulli shayin AAaleem**un**

## 42:13

SharaAAa lakum mina a**l**ddeeni m*a* wa*ssa* bihi noo*h*an wa**a**lla*th*ee aw*h*ayn*a* ilayka wam*a* wa*ss*ayn*a* bihi ibr*a*heema wamoos*a* waAAees*a* an aqeemoo a**l**ddeena wal*a* tatafarraqoo feehi kabura AAal*a* almushrikeena m*a* tadAAoohum ilayhi All*a*hu yajtabee ilayhi man yash*a*o wayahdee ilayhi man yuneeb**u**

## 42:14

Wam*a* tafarraqoo ill*a* min baAAdi m*a* j*a*ahumu alAAilmu baghyan baynahum walawl*a* kalimatun sabaqat min rabbika il*a* ajalin musamman laqu*d*iya baynahum wainna alla*th*eena oorithoo alkit*a*ba min baAAdihim lafee shakkin minhu mureeb**in**

## 42:15

Fali*tha*lika fa**o**dAAu wa**i**staqim kam*a* omirta wal*a* tattabiAA ahw*a*ahum waqul *a*mantu bim*a* anzala All*a*hu min kit*a*bin waomirtu liaAAdila baynakum All*a*hu rabbun*a* warabbukum lan*a* aAAm*a*lun*a* walakum aAAm*a*lukum l*a* *h*ujjata baynan*a* wabaynakumu All*a*hu yajmaAAu baynan*a* wailayhi alma*s*eer**u**

## 42:16

Wa**a**lla*th*eena yu*ha*jjoona fee All*a*hi min baAAdi m*a* istujeeba lahu *h*ujjatuhum d*ah*i*d*atun AAinda rabbihim waAAalayhim gha*d*abun walahum AAa*tha*bun shadeed**un**

## 42:17

All*a*hu alla*th*ee anzala alkit*a*ba bi**a**l*h*aqqi wa**a**lmeez*a*ni wam*a* yudreeka laAAalla a**l**ss*a*AAata qareeb**un**

## 42:18

YastaAAjilu bih*a* alla*th*eena l*a* yuminoona bih*a* wa**a**lla*th*eena *a*manoo mushfiqoona minh*a* wayaAAlamoona annah*a* al*h*aqqu al*a* inna alla*th*eena yum*a*roona fee a**l**ss*a*AAati lafee *d*al*a*lin baAAeed**in**

## 42:19

All*a*hu la*t*eefun biAAib*a*dihi yarzuqu man yash*a*o wahuwa alqawiyyu alAAazeez**u**

## 42:20

Man k*a*na yureedu *h*artha al*a*khirati nazid lahu fee *h*arthihi waman k*a*na yureedu *h*artha a**l**dduny*a* nutihi minh*a* wam*a* lahu fee al*a*khirati min na*s*eeb**in**

## 42:21

Am lahum shurak*a*o sharaAAoo lahum mina a**l**ddeeni m*a* lam ya*th*an bihi All*a*hu walawl*a* kalimatu alfa*s*li laqu*d*iya baynahum wainna a**l****thth***a*limeena lahum AAa*tha*bun aleem**un**

## 42:22

Tar*a* a**l****thth***a*limeena mushfiqeena mimm*a* kasaboo wahuwa w*a*qiAAun bihim wa**a**lla*th*eena *a*manoo waAAamiloo a**l***ssa*li*ha*ti fee raw*da*ti aljann*a*ti lahum m*a* yash*a*oona AAinda rabbihim *tha*lika huwa alfa*d*lu alkabeer**u**

## 42:23

*Tha*lika alla*th*ee yubashshiru All*a*hu AAib*a*dahu alla*th*eena *a*manoo waAAamiloo a**l***ssa*li*ha*ti qul l*a* asalukum AAalayhi ajran ill*a* almawaddata fee alqurb*a* waman yaqtarif *h*asanatan nazid lahu feeh*a* *h*usnan inna All*a*ha ghafoorun shakoor**un**

## 42:24

Am yaqooloona iftar*a* AAal*a* All*a*hi ka*th*iban fain yashai All*a*hu yakhtim AAal*a* qalbika wayam*h*u All*a*hu alb*at*ila wayu*h*iqqu al*h*aqqa bikalim*a*tihi innahu AAaleemun bi*tha*ti a**l***ss*udoor**i**

## 42:25

Wahuwa alla*th*ee yaqbalu a**l**ttawbata AAan AAib*a*dihi wayaAAfoo AAani a**l**ssayyiati wayaAAlamu m*a* tafAAaloon**a**

## 42:26

Wayastajeebu alla*th*eena *a*manoo waAAamiloo a**l***ssa*li*ha*ti wayazeeduhum min fa*d*lihi wa**a**lk*a*firoona lahum AAa*tha*bun shadeed**un**

## 42:27

Walaw basa*t*a All*a*hu a**l**rrizqa liAAib*a*dihi labaghaw fee alar*d*i wal*a*kin yunazzilu biqadarin m*a* yash*a*o innahu biAAib*a*dihi khabeerun ba*s*eer**un**

## 42:28

Wahuwa alla*th*ee yunazzilu alghaytha min baAAdi m*a* qana*t*oo wayanshuru ra*h*matahu wahuwa alwaliyyu al*h*ameed**u**

## 42:29

Wamin *a*y*a*tihi khalqu a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i wam*a* baththa feehim*a* min d*a*bbatin wahuwa AAal*a* jamAAihim i*tha* yash*a*o qadeer**un**

## 42:30

Wam*a* a*sa*bakum min mu*s*eebatin fabim*a* kasabat aydeekum wayaAAfoo AAan katheer**in**

## 42:31

Wam*a* antum bimuAAjizeena fee alar*d*i wam*a* lakum min dooni All*a*hi min waliyyin wal*a* na*s*eer**in**

## 42:32

Wamin *a*y*a*tihi aljaw*a*ri fee alba*h*ri ka**a**laAAl*a*m**i**

## 42:33

In yasha yuskini a**l**rree*h*a fay&#x61;**th**&#x6C;alna raw*a*kida AAal*a* **th**&#x61;hrihi inna fee *tha*lika la*a*y*a*tin likulli *s*abb*a*rin shakoor**in**

## 42:34

Aw yoobiqhunna bim*a* kasaboo wayaAAfu AAan katheer**in**

## 42:35

WayaAAlama alla*th*eena yuj*a*diloona fee *a*y*a*tin*a* m*a* lahum min ma*h*ee*s***in**

## 42:36

Fam*a* ooteetum min shayin famat*a*AAu al*h*ay*a*ti a**l**dduny*a* wam*a* AAinda All*a*hi khayrun waabq*a* lilla*th*eena *a*manoo waAAal*a* rabbihim yatawakkaloon**a**

## 42:37

Wa**a**lla*th*eena yajtaniboona kab*a*ira alithmi wa**a**lfaw*ah*isha wai*tha* m*a* gha*d*iboo hum yaghfiroon**a**

## 42:38

Wa**a**lla*th*eena istaj*a*boo lirabbihim waaq*a*moo a**l***ss*al*a*ta waamruhum shoor*a* baynahum wamimm*a* razaqn*a*hum yunfiqoon**a**

## 42:39

Wa**a**lla*th*eena i*tha* a*sa*bahumu albaghyu hum yanta*s*iroon**a**

## 42:40

Wajaz*a*o sayyiatin sayyiatun mithluh*a* faman AAaf*a* waa*s*la*h*a faajruhu AAal*a* All*a*hi innahu l*a* yu*h*ibbu a**l****thth***a*limeen**a**

## 42:41

Walamani inta*s*ara baAAda **th**&#x75;lmihi faol*a*ika m*a* AAalayhim min sabeel**in**

## 42:42

Innam*a* a**l**ssabeelu AAal*a* alla*th*eena y&#x61;**th**&#x6C;imoona a**l**nn*a*sa wayabghoona fee alar*d*i bighayri al*h*aqqi ol*a*ika lahum AAa*tha*bun aleem**un**

## 42:43

Walaman *s*abara waghafara inna *tha*lika lamin AAazmi alomoor**i**

## 42:44

Waman yu*d*lili All*a*hu fam*a* lahu min waliyyin min baAAdihi watar*a* a**l****thth***a*limeena lamm*a* raawoo alAAa*tha*ba yaqooloona hal il*a* maraddin min sabeel**in**

## 42:45

Watar*a*hum yuAAra*d*oona AAalayh*a* kh*a*shiAAeena mina a**l***thth*ulli ya&#x6E;**th**&#x75;roona min *t*arfin khafiyyin waq*a*la alla*th*eena *a*manoo inna alkh*a*sireena alla*th*eena khasiroo anfusahum waahleehim yawma alqiy*a*mati al*a* inna a**l****thth***a*limeena fee AAa*tha*bin muqeem**in**

## 42:46

Wam*a* k*a*na lahum min awliy*a*a yan*s*uroonahum min dooni All*a*hi waman yu*d*lili All*a*hu fam*a* lahu min sabeel**in**

## 42:47

Istajeeboo lirabbikum min qabli an yatiya yawmun l*a* maradda lahu mina All*a*hi m*a* lakum min maljain yawmai*th*in wam*a* lakum min nakeer**in**

## 42:48

Fain aAAra*d*oo fam*a* arsaln*a*ka AAalayhim *h*afe&#x65;**th**&#x61;n in AAalayka ill*a* albal*a*ghu wainn*a* i*tha* a*th*aqn*a* alins*a*na minn*a* ra*h*matan fari*h*a bih*a* wain tu*s*ibhum sayyiatun bim*a* qaddamat aydeehim fainna alins*a*na kafoor**un**

## 42:49

Lill*a*hi mulku a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i yakhluqu m*a* yash*a*o yahabu liman yash*a*o in*a*than wayahabu liman yash*a*o a**l***thth*ukoor**a**

## 42:50

Aw yuzawwijuhum *th*ukr*a*nan wain*a*than wayajAAalu man yash*a*o AAaqeeman innahu AAaleemun qadeer**un**

## 42:51

Wam*a* k*a*na libasharin an yukallimahu All*a*hu ill*a* wa*h*yan aw min war*a*i *h*ij*a*bin aw yursila rasoolan fayoo*h*iya bii*th*nihi m*a* yash*a*o innahu AAaliyyun *h*akeem**un**

## 42:52

Waka*tha*lika aw*h*ayn*a* ilayka roo*h*an min amrin*a* m*a* kunta tadree m*a* alkit*a*bu wal*a* aleem*a*nu wal*a*kin jaAAaln*a*hu nooran nahdee bihi man nash*a*o min AAib*a*din*a* wainnaka latahdee il*a* *s*ir*at*in mustaqeem**in**

## 42:53

*S*ir*at*i All*a*hi alla*th*ee lahu m*a* fee a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wam*a* fee alar*d*i al*a* il*a* All*a*hi ta*s*eeru alomoor**u**

## 43:1

*Ha*meem

## 43:2

Wa**a**lkit*a*bi almubeen**i**

## 43:3

Inn*a* jaAAaln*a*hu qur*a*nan AAarabiyyan laAAallakum taAAqiloona

## 43:4

Wainnahu fee ommi alkit*a*bi ladayn*a* laAAaliyyun *h*akeem**un**

## 43:5

Afana*d*ribu AAankumu a**l***thth*ikra *s*af*h*an an kuntum qawman musrifeen**a**

## 43:6

Wakam arsaln*a* min nabiyyin fee alawwaleen**a**

## 43:7

Wam*a* yateehim min nabiyyin ill*a* k*a*noo bihi yastahzioon**a**

## 43:8

Faahlakn*a* ashadda minhum ba*t*shan wama*da* mathalu alawwaleen**a**

## 43:9

Walain saaltahum man khalaqa a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*a layaqoolunna khalaqahunna alAAazeezu alAAaleem**u**

## 43:10

Alla*th*ee jaAAala lakumu alar*d*a mahdan wajaAAala lakum feeh*a* subulan laAAallakum tahtadoon**a**

## 43:11

Wa**a**lla*th*ee nazzala mina a**l**ssam*a*i m*a*an biqadarin faansharn*a* bihi baldatan maytan ka*tha*lika tukhrajoon**a**

## 43:12

Wa**a**lla*th*ee khalaqa alazw*a*ja kullah*a* wajaAAala lakum mina alfulki wa**a**lanAA*a*mi m*a* tarkaboon**a**

## 43:13

Litastawoo AAal*a* **th**&#x75;hoorihi thumma ta*th*kuroo niAAmata rabbikum i*tha* istawaytum AAalayhi wataqooloo sub*ha*na alla*th*ee sakhkhara lan*a* h*atha* wam*a* kunn*a* lahu muqrineen**a**

## 43:14

Wainn*a* il*a* rabbin*a* lamunqaliboon**a**

## 43:15

WajaAAaloo lahu min AAib*a*dihi juzan inna alins*a*na lakafoorun mubeen**un**

## 43:16

Ami ittakha*th*a mimm*a* yakhluqu ban*a*tin waa*s*f*a*kum bi**a**lbaneen**a**

## 43:17

Wai*tha* bushshira a*h*aduhum bim*a* *d*araba li**l**rra*h*m*a*ni mathalan **th**&#x61;lla wajhuhu muswaddan wahuwa k&#x61;**th**&#x65;em**un**

## 43:18

Awaman yunashshao fee al*h*ilyati wahuwa fee alkhi*sa*mi ghayru mubeen**in**

## 43:19

WajaAAaloo almal*a*ikata alla*th*eena hum AAib*a*du a**l**rra*h*m*a*ni in*a*than ashahidoo khalqahum satuktabu shah*a*datuhum wayusaloon**a**

## 43:20

Waq*a*loo law sh*a*a a**l**rra*h*m*a*nu m*a* AAabadn*a*hum m*a* lahum bi*tha*lika min AAilmin in hum ill*a* yakhru*s*oon**a**

## 43:21

Am *a*tayn*a*hum kit*a*ban min qablihi fahum bihi mustamsikoon**a**

## 43:22

Bal q*a*loo inn*a* wajadn*a* *a*b*a*an*a* AAal*a* ommatin wainn*a* AAal*a* *a*th*a*rihim muhtadoon**a**

## 43:23

Waka*tha*lika m*a* arsaln*a* min qablika fee qaryatin min na*th*eerin ill*a* q*a*la mutrafooh*a* inn*a* wajadn*a* *a*b*a*an*a* AAal*a* ommatin wainn*a* AAal*a* *a*th*a*rihim muqtadoon**a**

## 43:24

Q*a*la awalaw jitukum biahd*a* mimm*a* wajadtum AAalayhi *a*b*a*akum q*a*loo inn*a* bim*a* orsiltum bihi k*a*firoon**a**

## 43:25

Fa**i**ntaqamn*a* minhum fa**o**&#x6E;**th**&#x75;r kayfa k*a*na AA*a*qibatu almuka*thth*ibeen**a**

## 43:26

Wai*th* q*a*la ibr*a*heemu liabeehi waqawmihi innanee bar*a*on mimm*a* taAAbudoon**a**

## 43:27

Ill*a* alla*th*ee fa*t*aranee fainnahu sayahdeen**i**

## 43:28

WajaAAalah*a* kalimatan b*a*qiyatan fee AAaqibihi laAAallahum yarjiAAoon**a**

## 43:29

Bal mattaAAtu h*a*ol*a*i wa*a*b*a*ahum *h*att*a* j*a*ahumu al*h*aqqu warasoolun mubeen**un**

## 43:30

Walamm*a* j*a*ahumu al*h*aqqu q*a*loo h*atha* si*h*run wainn*a* bihi k*a*firoon**a**

## 43:31

Waq*a*loo lawl*a* nuzzila h*atha* alqur*a*nu AAal*a* rajulin mina alqaryatayni AA&#x61;**th**&#x65;em**un**

## 43:32

Ahum yaqsimoona ra*h*mata rabbika na*h*nu qasamn*a* baynahum maAAeeshatahum fee al*h*ay*a*ti a**l**dduny*a* warafaAAn*a* baAA*d*ahum fawqa baAA*d*in daraj*a*tin liyattakhi*th*a baAA*d*uhum baAA*d*an sukhriyyan wara*h*matu rabbika khayrun mimm*a* yajmaAAoon**a**

## 43:33

Walawl*a* an yakoona a**l**nn*a*su ommatan w*ah*idatan lajaAAaln*a* liman yakfuru bi**al**rra*h*m*a*ni libuyootihim suqufan min fi*dd*atin wamaAA*a*rija AAalayh*a* y&#x61;**th**&#x68;aroon**a**

## 43:34

Walibuyootihim abw*a*ban wasururan AAalayh*a* yattakioon**a**

## 43:35

Wazukhrufan wain kullu *tha*lika lamm*a* mat*a*AAu al*h*ay*a*ti a**l**dduny*a&#x20;*&#x77;a**a**l*a*khiratu AAinda rabbika lilmuttaqeen**a**

## 43:36

Waman yaAAshu AAan *th*ikri a**l**rra*h*m*a*ni nuqayyi*d* lahu shay*ta*nan fahuwa lahu qareen**un**

## 43:37

Wainnahum laya*s*uddoonahum AAani a**l**ssabeeli waya*h*saboona annahum muhtadoon**a**

## 43:38

*H*att*a* i*tha* j*a*an*a* q*a*la y*a* layta baynee wabaynaka buAAda almashriqayni fabisa alqareen**u**

## 43:39

Walan yanfaAAakumu alyawma i*th* **th**&#x61;lamtum annakum fee alAAa*tha*bi mushtarikoon**a**

## 43:40

Afaanta tusmiAAu a**l***ss*umma aw tahdee alAAumya waman k*a*na fee *d*al*a*lin mubeen**in**

## 43:41

Faimm*a* na*th*habanna bika fainn*a* minhum muntaqimoon**a**

## 43:42

Aw nuriyannaka alla*th*ee waAAadn*a*hum fainn*a* AAalayhim muqtadiroon**a**

## 43:43

Fa**i**stamsik bi**a**lla*th*ee oo*h*iya ilayka innaka AAal*a* *s*ir*at*in mustaqeem**in**

## 43:44

Wainnahu la*th*ikrun laka waliqawmika wasawfa tusaloon**a**

## 43:45

Wa**i**sal man arsaln*a* min qablika min rusulin*a* ajaAAaln*a* min dooni a**l**rra*h*m*a*ni *a*lihatan yuAAbadoon**a**

## 43:46

Walaqad arsaln*a* moos*a* bi*a*y*a*tin*a* il*a* firAAawna wamalaihi faq*a*la innee rasoolu rabbi alAA*a*lameen**a**

## 43:47

Falamm*a* j*a*ahum bi*a*y*a*tin*a* i*tha* hum minh*a* ya*dh*akoon**a**

## 43:48

Wam*a* nureehim min *a*yatin ill*a* hiya akbaru min okhtih*a* waakha*th*n*a*hum bi**a**lAAa*tha*bi laAAallahum yarjiAAoon**a**

## 43:49

Waq*a*loo y*a* ayyuh*a* a**l**s*ah*iru odAAu lan*a* rabbaka bim*a* AAahida AAindaka innan*a* lamuhtadoon**a**

## 43:50

Falamm*a* kashafn*a* AAanhumu alAAa*tha*ba i*tha* hum yankuthoon**a**

## 43:51

Wan*a*d*a* firAAawnu fee qawmihi q*a*la y*a* qawmi alaysa lee mulku mi*s*ra wah*ath*ihi alanh*a*ru tajree min ta*h*tee afal*a* tub*s*iroon**a**

## 43:52

Am an*a* khayrun min h*atha* alla*th*ee huwa maheenun wal*a* yak*a*du yubeen**u**

## 43:53

Falawl*a* olqiya AAalayhi aswiratun min *th*ahabin aw j*a*a maAAahu almal*a*ikatu muqtarineen**a**

## 43:54

Fa**i**stakhaffa qawmahu faa*ta*AAoohu innahum k*a*noo qawman f*a*siqeen**a**

## 43:55

Falamm*a* *a*safoon*a* intaqamn*a* minhum faaghraqn*a*hum ajmaAAeen**a**

## 43:56

FajaAAaln*a*hum salafan wamathalan lil*a*khireen**a**

## 43:57

Walamm*a* *d*uriba ibnu maryama mathalan i*tha* qawmuka minhu ya*s*iddoon**a**

## 43:58

Waq*a*loo a*a*lihatun*a* khayrun am huwa m*a* *d*araboohu laka ill*a* jadalan bal hum qawmun kha*s*imoon**a**

## 43:59

In huwa ill*a* AAabdun anAAamn*a* AAalayhi wajaAAaln*a*hu mathalan libanee isr*a*eel**a**

## 43:60

Walaw nash*a*o lajaAAaln*a* minkum mal*a*ikatan fee alar*d*i yakhlufoon**a**

## 43:61

Wainnahu laAAilmun li**l**ss*a*AAati fal*a* tamtarunna bih*a* wa**i**ttabiAAooni h*atha* *s*ir*at*un mustaqeem**un**

## 43:62

Wal*a* ya*s*uddannakumu a**l**shshay*ta*nu innahu lakum AAaduwwun mubeen**un**

## 43:63

Walamm*a* j*a*a AAees*a* bi**a**lbayyin*a*ti q*a*la qad jitukum bi**a**l*h*ikmati waliobayyina lakum baAA*d*a alla*th*ee takhtalifoona feehi fa**i**ttaqoo All*a*ha waa*t*eeAAoon**i**

## 43:64

Inna All*a*ha huwa rabbee warabbukum fa**o**AAbudoohu h*atha* *s*ir*at*un mustaqeem**un**

## 43:65

Fa**i**khtalafa ala*h*z*a*bu min baynihim fawaylun lilla*th*eena **th**&#x61;lamoo min AAa*tha*bi yawmin aleem**in**

## 43:66

Hal ya&#x6E;**th**&#x75;roona ill*a* a**l**ss*a*AAata an tatiyahum baghtatan wahum l*a* yashAAuroon**a**

## 43:67

Alakhill*a*o yawmai*th*in baAA*d*uhum libaAA*d*in AAaduwwun ill*a* almuttaqeen**a**

## 43:68

Y*a* AAib*a*di l*a* khawfun AAalaykumu alyawma wal*a* antum ta*h*zanoon**a**

## 43:69

Alla*th*eena *a*manoo bi*a*y*a*tin*a* wak*a*noo muslimeen**a**

## 43:70

Odkhuloo aljannata antum waazw*a*jukum tu*h*baroon**a**

## 43:71

Yu*ta*fu AAalayhim bi*s*i*ha*fin min *th*ahabin waakw*a*bin wafeeh*a* m*a* tashtaheehi alanfusu watala*thth*u alaAAyunu waantum feeh*a* kh*a*lidoon**a**

## 43:72

Watilka aljannatu allatee oorithtumooh*a* bim*a* kuntum taAAmaloon**a**

## 43:73

Lakum feeh*a* f*a*kihatun katheeratun minh*a* takuloon**a**

## 43:74

Inna almujrimeena fee AAa*tha*bi jahannama kh*a*lidoon**a**

## 43:75

L*a* yufattaru AAanhum wahum feehi mublisoon**a**

## 43:76

Wam*a* **th**&#x61;lamn*a*hum wal*a*kin k*a*noo humu a**l****thth***a*limeen**a**

## 43:77

Wan*a*daw y*a* m*a*liku liyaq*d*i AAalayn*a* rabbuka q*a*la innakum m*a*kithoon**a**

## 43:78

Laqad jin*a*kum bi**a**l*h*aqqi wal*a*kinna aktharakum lil*h*aqqi k*a*rihoon**a**

## 43:79

Am abramoo amran fainn*a* mubrimoon**a**

## 43:80

Am ya*h*saboona ann*a* l*a* nasmaAAu sirrahum wanajw*a*hum bal*a* warusulun*a* ladayhim yaktuboon**a**

## 43:81

Qul in k*a*na li**l**rra*h*m*a*ni waladun faan*a* awwalu alAA*a*bideen**a**

## 43:82

Sub*ha*na rabbi a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i rabbi alAAarshi AAamm*a* ya*s*ifoon**a**

## 43:83

Fa*th*arhum yakhoo*d*oo wayalAAaboo *h*att*a* yul*a*qoo yawmahumu alla*th*ee yooAAadoon**a**

## 43:84

Wahuwa alla*th*ee fee a**l**ssam*a*i il*a*hun wafee alar*d*i il*a*hun wahuwa al*h*akeemu alAAaleem**u**

## 43:85

Watab*a*raka alla*th*ee lahu mulku a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i wam*a* baynahum*a* waAAindahu AAilmu a**l**ss*a*AAati wailayhi turjaAAoon**a**

## 43:86

Wal*a* yamliku alla*th*eena yadAAoona min doonihi a**l**shshaf*a*AAata ill*a* man shahida bi**a**l*h*aqqi wahum yaAAlamoon**a**

## 43:87

Walain saaltahum man khalaqahum layaqoolunna All*a*hu faann*a* yufakoon**a**

## 43:88

Waqeelihi y*a*rabbi inna h*a*ol*a*i qawmun l*a* yuminoon**a**

## 43:89

Fa**i***s*fa*h* AAanhum waqul sal*a*mun fasawfa yaAAlamoon**a**

## 44:1

*Ha*meem

## 44:2

Wa**a**lkit*a*bi almubeen**i**

## 44:3

Inn*a* anzaln*a*hu fee laylatin mub*a*rakatin inn*a* kunn*a* mun*th*ireen**a**

## 44:4

Feeh*a* yufraqu kullu amrin *h*akeem**in**

## 44:5

Amran min AAindin*a* inn*a* kunn*a* mursileen**a**

## 44:6

Ra*h*matan min rabbika innahu huwa a**l**ssameeAAu alAAaleem**u**

## 44:7

Rabbi a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*i wam*a* baynahum*a* in kuntum mooqineen**a**

## 44:8

L*a* il*a*ha ill*a* huwa yu*h*yee wayumeetu rabbukum warabbu *a*b*a*ikumu alawwaleen**a**

## 44:9

Bal hum fee shakkin yalAAaboon**a**

## 44:10

Fa**i**rtaqib yawma tatee a**l**ssam*a*o bidukh*a*nin mubeen**in**

## 44:11

Yaghsh*a* a**l**nn*a*sa h*atha* AAa*tha*bun aleem**un**

## 44:12

Rabban*a* ikshif AAann*a* alAAa*tha*ba inn*a* muminoon**a**

## 44:13

Ann*a* lahumu a**l***thth*ikr*a* waqad j*a*ahum rasoolun mubeen**un**

## 44:14

Thumma tawallaw AAanhu waq*a*loo muAAallamun majnoon**un**

## 44:15

Inn*a* k*a*shifoo alAAa*tha*bi qaleelan innakum AA*a*idoon**a**

## 44:16

Yawma nab*t*ishu alba*t*shata alkubr*a* inn*a* muntaqimoon**a**

## 44:17

Walaqad fatann*a* qablahum qawma firAAawna waj*a*ahum rasoolun kareem**un**

## 44:18

An addoo ilayya AAib*a*da All*a*hi innee lakum rasoolun ameen**un**

## 44:19

Waan l*a* taAAloo AAal*a* All*a*hi innee *a*teekum bisul*ta*nin mubeen**in**

## 44:20

Wainnee AAu*th*tu birabbee warabbikum an tarjumoon**i**

## 44:21

Wain lam tuminoo lee fa**i**AAtaziloon**i**

## 44:22

FadaAA*a* rabbahu anna h*a*ol*a*i qawmun mujrimoon**a**

## 44:23

Faasri biAAib*a*dee laylan innakum muttabaAAoon**a**

## 44:24

Wa**o**truki alba*h*ra rahwan innahum jundun mughraqoon**a**

## 44:25

Kam tarakoo min jann*a*tin waAAuyoon**in**

## 44:26

WazurooAAin wamaq*a*min kareem**in**

## 44:27

WanaAAmatin k*a*noo feeh*a* f*a*kiheen**a**

## 44:28

Ka*tha*lika waawrathn*a*h*a* qawman *a*khareen**a**

## 44:29

Fam*a* bakat AAalayhimu a**l**ssam*a*o wa**a**lar*d*u wam*a* k*a*noo mu&#x6E;**th**&#x61;reen**a**

## 44:30

Walaqad najjayn*a* banee isr*a*eela mina alAAa*tha*bi almuheen**i**

## 44:31

Min firAAawna innahu k*a*na AA*a*liyan mina almusrifeen**a**

## 44:32

Walaqadi ikhtarn*a*hum AAal*a* AAilmin AAal*a* alAA*a*lameen**a**

## 44:33

Wa*a*tayn*a*hum mina al*a*y*a*ti m*a* feehi bal*a*on mubeen**un**

## 44:34

Inna h*a*ol*a*i layaqooloon**a**

## 44:35

In hiya ill*a* mawtatun*a* alool*a* wam*a* na*h*nu bimunshareen**a**

## 44:36

Fatoo bi*a*b*a*in*a* in kuntum *sa*diqeen**a**

## 44:37

Ahum khayrun am qawmu tubbaAAin wa**a**lla*th*eena min qablihim ahlakn*a*hum innahum k*a*noo mujrimeen**a**

## 44:38

Wam*a* khalaqn*a* a**l**ssam*a*w*a*ti wa**a**lar*d*a wam*a* baynahum*a* l*a*AAibeen**a**

## 44:39

M*a* khalaqn*a*hum*a* ill*a* bi**a**l*h*aqqi wal*a*kinna aktharahum l*a* yaAAlamoon**a**

## 44:40

Inna yawma alfa*s*li meeq*a*tuhum ajmaAAeen**a**

## 44:41

Yawma l*a* yughnee mawlan AAan mawlan shayan wal*a* hum yun*s*aroon**a**

## 44:42

Ill*a* man ra*h*ima All*a*hu innahu huwa alAAazeezu a**l**rra*h*eem**u**

## 44:43

Inna shajarata a**l**zzaqqoom**i**

## 44:44

*T*aAA*a*mu alatheem**i**

## 44:45
